Chapter 1432: Manifestation of the Great Dao

The so-called "Enlightenment Value" in the Dream Bliss Land is, in reality, the insights into the Great Dao that Transmitter Jiang obtains through his "All Things Are Like Me" characteristic.

With merely a wall separating them.

Transmitter Jiang's efficiency in gaining enlightenment hasn't changed. What has changed is the environment itself. Simply put, cultivation outside the Wall will be significantly easier for cultivators than within the High Wall.

Just as Li Fan had previously surmised, any cultivator, no matter how ordinary, who can embark on the path of cultivation on their own outside the Wall could be considered a "Heavenly Talent"!

Moreover, this is only the beginning.

Li Fan keenly observed that after being exposed to the environment outside the High Wall, Transmitter Jiang's enlightenment efficiency within the Heaven-Connecting Grand Array was gradually improving.

Prolonged immersion in the Great Dao enlightenment was finally beginning to nourish him in return.

Li Fan synchronized with the other's feelings, and the soaring Great Dao he looked up at, seemed to gradually transform from dull grey to vibrant and colorful.

"Is this the difference between the so-called Annihilation Land and a normal environment?" This magnificent sight caused Li Fan to briefly lose himself.

"The world outside the High Wall is hauntingly beautiful, almost intimidating."

A voice echoed beside Li Fan, interrupting his contemplation.

Li Fan turned his head and saw a blue figure beside him.

It was Chen Tianhai of the Grand Mystery Sect!

"I can feel that the demonic sound's influence on me seems to have intensified. Past memories are becoming clearer. Even though I have personally witnessed Transmitter Heavenly Venerate being suppressed. Even though I know that those were merely altered memories."

"But that fleeting glance from back then still haunts me like a nightmare." Chen Tianhai's figure fluctuated uncontrollably.

Li Fan didn't respond, instead attempting to silently recite the chanting demonic sound in his mind.

An invisible force seemed to penetrate the Dream Bliss Land, subtly connecting him to the world outside the High Wall.

Those mysterious melodies became much clearer.

Li Fan's heart tightened, and as a balance, he immediately began to silently recite the Immortal Scripture of Protection originating from the Grand Master.

"Dao arises, ancient traditions transmit. Grief and hardship, Dao is annihilated."

…

The two sounds harmonized, and the influence of the chanting demonic sound was considerably weakened. However, compared to its effect within the High Wall, the neutralizing power of this Protection Immortal Scripture was clearly much weaker.

It was gradually unable to contend with the mysterious and unpredictable demonic sound.

"Xuan Yuanhong…" Li Fan's expression grew subtle.

Transmitter Heavenly Venerate, in his desperate bid for survival back then, relied on the seemingly innate whispering power of the Xuan Yuan clan to influence and alter the memories of Chen Tianhai of the Grand Mystery Sect, whom he had met only once.

Through the deductions of the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother, he found a way to kill many Longevity cultivators of the Ten Great Immortal Sects.

Although Transmitter had been suppressed by Li Fan, the whispering mark left on Chen Tianhai remained.

When Chen Tianhai, following the power of the Dream Bliss Land, arrived outside the High Wall, its influence erupted once more. Even though Chen Tianhai had already become amorphous, a part of the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother, he could not be exempted.

"Part of this is due to the clearer Great Dao. Naturally, the profound melodies describing the Great Dao through sound have also been strengthened. If True Immortal inscriptions were written, their power would likely be similarly enhanced several times over."

"But this is not the only reason."

"The extent of its strengthening is simply too great. For the Dao of sound, the Protection Immortal Scripture hasn't seen such an exaggerated increase…"

The faint whispers in his ears flickered in and out.

Li Fan pondered, and could only attribute it to the missing King Xuan.

Five years ago, when Li Fan went to the Grand Mystery Sect and met Chen Tianhai.

With a single word, he revealed the truth of the demonic sound's erosion.

Chen Tianhai initially disbelieved that his memories had been tampered with all this time. It was not until Li Fan imparted the Protection Immortal Scripture, dispelling the power of alteration, that.

Chen Tianhai, his true memories restored, was thunderstruck and remained silent for a long time.

"It is not that you are incompetent. How can mortals escape the methods of Immortals?"

Li Fan's single sentence finally freed Chen Tianhai from the torment of his past.

The reason Li Fan came to the Grand Mystery Sect was naturally for the Dao-Transforming Mother Stone.

After helping Chen Tianhai resolve the millennium-long nightmare. Li Fan, with a mix of coercion and enticement, brought the Grand Mystery Sect to submission.

Now, this Dao-Transforming Stone Mother resided within Li Fan's Sea of Consciousness.

However, after some study, Li Fan chose not to merge it directly with the high-grade Dao-Transforming Stone in his mind.

When the entire Grand Mystery Sect chose to integrate and become amorphous into the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother, myriad thoughts merged with the Stone Mother and became inseparable, forming a characteristic of the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother itself.

Li Fan was not confident that he could erase these thoughts without destroying the Stone Mother.

If he were to directly absorb it…

The strength of the Stone Mother far surpassed that of the high-grade Dao-Transforming Stone.

The thoughts of the Grand Mystery Sect members within the Stone Mother were more likely to contaminate Li Fan's Dao-Transforming Stone.

Although Li Fan could forcibly clear these thoughts afterward.

Deep within the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother, there also lay a peculiar thought, dormant, which even as a Half-Immortal, Li Fan found quite troublesome.

Moreover, Li Fan, having already mastered the Transformation of True and False, no longer needed to crudely absorb it to enhance his power.

Within his Sea of Consciousness, around the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother.

Thousands of threads, like from the void, flew in. Contacting, analyzing, and comprehending the essence of the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother.

And within the depths of his Sea of Consciousness, isolated from other regions.

Another crystal, identical in appearance to the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother, floated silently. It seemed to exist in an ethereal, mist-like state, flickering unstably.

This was the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother that Li Fan had "replicated" through the Transformation of True and False.

Having successfully recreated the Primordial Cang Essence, his own cultivation, and the Azure Nether Pearl, Li Fan initially thought that recreating this Dao-Transforming Stone Mother would be effortless.

But to his surprise, the difficulty of recreating this crystal was dozens of times greater than that of the Immortal artifact, the Azure Nether Pearl.

To recreate the Azure Nether Pearl, he only needed triple his cultivation, and though somewhat strenuous, he could ultimately succeed.

But facing this Dao-Transforming Stone Mother, brute force seemed to have lost its effect.

After several failures, Li Fan realized that it wasn't due to insufficient power, but rather that his understanding of the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother hadn't reached the minimum requirement for recreation.

This was a first for Li Fan.

Previously, performing the Transformation of True and False didn't require him to understand the essence of things.

However, after careful contemplation and arduous communication with Returning to Truth. Li Fan finally understood why.

In simple terms, anything Li Fan could fully perceive at a glance could be briefly recreated through the Transformation of True and False.

This principle still held true for the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother.

The reason for the recreation failure was that Li Fan hadn't been able to "fully perceive" the Stone Mother.

This was why Li Fan had sealed the Stone Mother in his Sea of Consciousness, observing it day and night without cease.

Having opened a separate area, he wouldn't allow the Stone Mother to glimpse his memories.

And the members of the Grand Mystery Sect could leave Li Fan's Sea of Consciousness at any time and enter reality.

Now, Li Fan could recreate the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother, and by continuously layering it, he could strengthen the Dao-Transforming Stone in his Sea of Consciousness. Naturally, he had already "fully perceived" the Stone Mother.

And through this period of communication with the Stone Mother, Li Fan also understood why he, as a Half-Immortal, had been unable to "fully perceive" the Stone Mother's complete form at a glance.

"Dao-Transforming Stone Mother, the Mother Stone that Transforms Dao."

Li Fan's heart stirred, and the illusory Stone Mother he had recreated transformed into a halo, attaching itself to his Dao-Transforming Stone.

He activated the improved Dao Unity Secret Art, rapidly absorbing the extremely refined energy within.

The illusory Stone Mother recreated by Li Fan contained no thoughts from the Grand Mystery Sect. It even lacked the mysterious thought hidden deep within the real Stone Mother. It was merely the pure essence of the Stone Mother itself. Thus, it could be absorbed without restraint.

Although the Transformation of True and False only left behind slight remnants each time.

The Dao-Transforming Stone Mother was so mysterious that each activation could double the quality of the Dao-Transforming Stone in Li Fan's Sea of Consciousness.

Within ten years, Li Fan had already achieved nearly a hundred recreations and layers.

At this moment, the Dao-Transforming Stone in his mind was no longer much weaker than the actual Stone Mother.

Hence, he had a subtle conjecture about the essence of the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother.

This exotic treasure from outside the heavens was, surprisingly, a direct manifestation of the Great Dao!

It was similar in principle to the Primordial Forms of the demonic beast race.

However, Primordial Forms represented only a single Great Dao. As for the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother…

Li Fan speculated that it might even be a collection of all complete Great Daos!

However, the possibility of the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother's origin was far weaker than what Li Fan was familiar with.

It had also endured the Dao Annihilation Tribulation and the cleansing of traversing possibilities.

The Stone Mother was further weakened.

Therefore, even though it was a materializeation of a complete Great Dao, in terms of power, it couldn't even compare to an ordinary Nameless True Immortal.

Of course, all of the above were merely Li Fan's conjectures based on his insights gained during the recreation of the Stone Mother.

And the only remaining memory of the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother was of it constantly fleeing in disarray, seemingly to avoid some catastrophe, and by chance, arriving in the Xuanhuang Realm, where it was later discovered by the Grand Mystery Sect.

Li Fan speculated that the reason the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother had completely severed ties with its past was to evade the pursuit of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation.

Although the Stone Mother had lost its past memories, Li Fan could still feel subtle ominous aura of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation from its perception of the terrifying calamity.

Li Fan was quite confident in his own assessment. After all, what else in the mundane world could force a crystalized entity of a complete Great Dao to flee in such a panic?

And the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother had arrived in the Xuanhuang Realm by "chance."

This reminded Li Fan of the scene he once saw in the memories of a True Immortal.

"This Xuanhuang Realm must still hold mysteries I have yet to discover."

"It can attract numerous peculiar existences, traversing space-time, and even possibilities, to arrive here."

"Even my own transmigration…"

His discovery of the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother's origin from another possibility also caused Li Fan to have some doubts about his own transmigration.

Although he didn't miss his life before transmigration, nor did he feel compelled to return.

The key point Li Fan was concerned about was whether the awakening of [True Return] occurred within the body of this possibility, with him merely occupying it.

Or within his own body.

With the continuous development and utilization of the Transformation of True and False, Li Fan's perspective and mindset had undergone extremely subtle changes from before.

In the past, when Li Fan encountered rare treasures in the mundane world, he couldn't help but harbor a desire to possess them, either out of greed or to enhance his self-preservation.

But now, Li Fan's desire to "possess" had gradually faded.

All he thought about was "analysis and understanding."

After all, with the Transformation of True and False at his disposal, if he wished, he could instantly conjure an endless number of replicas of any treasure.

The only thing Li Fan truly desired to possess now.

Was [True Return] itself.

…

Thousands of thoughts, along with the integration of another illusory Dao-Transforming Stone Mother, were brought to an end.

Li Fan felt his thoughts running much faster.

His attention returned to the mysterious and unpredictable demonic sound in his ear.

After Li Fan's reminder, and based on the past memories in Transmitter Heavenly Venerate's mind, the Stone Mother, after countless reviews, reached a conclusion.

The persistent whispering sound was likely the work of King Xuan.

However, it was not a desperate attempt to resurrect himself.

Instead, it was a natural change that occurred in his bloodline descendants after the bloodline's source entered a state beyond comprehension.

One of the supporting arguments was that the demonic sound's influence on the Xuan Yuan clan grew progressively stronger.

Until Xuan Yuan Sheng, it reached its peak.

Xuan Yuan Sheng, unable to bear it, attempted to completely sever this influence.

But he still couldn't prevent this demonic sound from appearing in Xuan Yuanhong.

And after coming outside the High Wall, the demonic sound was further strengthened.

This deduction by the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother seemed to be confirmed in some way.

"King Xuan, after his mysterious disappearance back then, not only didn't die but actually advanced further?"

This conjecture made Li Fan's imagination run wild.

After witnessing Black Heavenly Physician and Evil Su Bai, a thought had always been budding in Li Fan's mind, though he couldn't grasp its meaning.

It wasn't until the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother's conjecture appeared that this thought finally took root and emerged.

Black Heavenly Physician and Evil Su Bai both originated from a very special possibility.

So, could it be that this possibility Li Fan currently resided in also gave birth to such unknowable powerhouses capable of traversing possibilities?

If such a possibility truly existed.

Then, in the history Li Fan currently knew, the one who most resembled a protagonist was perhaps King Xuan.

After all, he was the last ascender before the destruction of the Immortal Realm.

His legend was simply too great.

"Perhaps outside the High Wall, there are other even more heaven-defying figures."

"But no matter what, with methods that can cross the High Wall and traverse ancient and modern times. Such individuals must be guarded against."

The stronger one was, the more likely they were to know of the existence of [True Return].

The more Li Fan interacted with them, the more careful he had to be to conceal himself.

"I wonder if King Xuan still has any bloodline descendants in the Xuanhuang Realm?"

Chapter 1433: Primordial Possibility

"Time passes. That ancient Xuan Yuan Village is long gone."

"Even with the 'Manifestation Art,' I couldn't glean any clues from the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate..."

"Perhaps, to investigate the current situation of King Xuan Tian, I need to start with his childhood sweetheart."

Within Li Fan's Sea of Consciousness, countless points of light flickered. Each point contained myriad shimmering images, swiftly passing by. Like a sea of stars, these light points pre-enacted different possible futures. Yet, this level of deduction caused no hindrance to Li Fan's thoughts. This was the benefit of the upgraded Dao-Transforming Stone in his Sea of Consciousness. His processing power seemed boundless. Even if he were to dedicate all his past knowledge to the pursuit of Immortal arts, coupled with deducing the future trajectory of this life and simultaneously analyzing all events within the Dream Bliss Land, Li Fan still felt perfectly at ease.

He even felt a sense of stifled frustration, as if he possessed immense divine power with nowhere to wield it. He once tested himself with the Grand Mystery Sect's "Reversal of Tribulation"—a small game of restoring order from chaos, and predictability from randomness. Compared to the forty-nine thousand nine hundred ninety-nine pages left by Yi Yin in his tomb, the quantity was ten thousand times greater. The difficulty was vastly different. Yet, after only a single breath, Li Fan effortlessly solved it. Under the computational power of the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother, such combinatorial problems, no matter how high their basic magnitude, could no longer stump Li Fan.

...

While contemplating various matters, Li Fan said to Chen Tianhai, "Does the Grand Mystery Sect not wish to see beyond the High Wall? I can create independent bodies for those who wish to explore beyond it." Chen Tianhai's heart was clearly moved by these words.

"Contact with more variables beyond the High Wall also helps activate the latent power of the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother. Perhaps, it might even awaken the dormant will deep within the Stone Mother," Li Fan added, which quickly prompted Chen Tianhai to make up his mind.

The will hidden within the Dao-Transmutation Stone Mother was initially unnoticed by the entire Grand Mystery Sect. It was only after Li Fan pointed it out to them that, fused with the Stone Mother, they were able to "discern" its hidden presence. Through their inexplicable connection with the Stone Mother, the Grand Mystery Sect members universally believed that this will was beneficial and harmless to it. It had merely fallen dormant for unknown reasons. If they could find a way to communicate with it, they might unveil the mystery of the Stone Mother's origin—perhaps even instigating further transformation within the Stone Mother. Li Fan's proposal was absolutely irresistible to the Grand Mystery Sect.

Chen Tianhai observed the scenes from beyond the High Wall, originating from the Dream Bliss Land. To obtain the most accurate information possible about the world beyond the High Wall, Li Fan had altered how dreams were generated there, basing them entirely on the real environment, free from fabricated or false elements. After dozens of iterations, the Dream Bliss Land was no longer merely a creation of Wuyou or even Li Fan. Instead, it was a collective outgrowth of the myriad consciousnesses within the dream.

Currently, this colossal entity had already crossed the High Wall, slowly exploring the world beyond. The Utmost Darkness Star Sea, within the High Wall, was but a small part of the Annihilation Land. However, most other areas, under the baptism of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation, had lost even the concept of "existence." The tendrils of the dream stretched outwards along the narrow passages beyond the High Wall. Everywhere they went was desolation.

Looking back at the position of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, nothing could be found. Even though a part of the tendrils was still connected to the High Wall's interior, they couldn't be sensed. This eerie situation was as if a part of one's own body had inexplicably vanished. Li Fan controlled a portion of the dream tendrils, continuing to explore the outer reaches of the Annihilation Land. He left the remaining tendrils to attempt crossing the High Wall and return to the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

Unable to perceive the High Wall's presence, they could only follow the脈絡 of their own existence and successfully grope their way to the vicinity of the High Wall. However, all other points were unable to enter or even discover the High Wall. Only through the dream's penetration of the High Wall, and remaining connected to both inside and out, could he return to the interior of the Wall. "The hidden and profound nature of the High Wall's outer side is indeed far beyond what we perceive from within."

Li Fan did not abandon his exploration of the High Wall. Endless dream tendrils, following the initially opened passage, began to spread outwards. Like ivy, they densely occupied the High Wall. Although he still hadn't fully pinpointed the High Wall's existence, and had merely deduced its possible origins, Li Fan still understood very little about its principles and how to decipher it. Only through continued time and slow analysis could he unravel its secrets.

"Immortal Realm Proving Grounds."

"Immortal Domain Chess Piece."

Li Fan's mind conjured the scenes he once witnessed within the Immortal Domain Chess Piece. On the chessboard, black and white pieces stood side by side. The victor remained, the loser exited. And the Immortal Domain Chess Piece left by Sun Piaomiao was merely one of the ignominious failures. Yet, even within that, there were existences like the Southern Immortal Pillar. It was difficult to imagine what kind of foundations those chess pieces that remained on the board would possess. "More crucially…"

"How could the Immortal Realm have only the Xuanhuang Realm as a proving ground?" This question suddenly surged into Li Fan's mind. From the glimpse of the Immortal Realm he had once caught, it was boundless. Truly deserving of the word "infinite." There were countless Immortal Domains. Even non-orthodox powers like Sun Piaomiao retained numerous backup chess pieces. It was hard to imagine that the vast Immortal Realm, if it truly intended to scheme something, would only have a single operation.

"In the past, my horizons were too narrow."

"Even after ascending to Half-Immortal, I only possessed the realm and status. Without the baptism of Immortal Spiritual Energy, my thinking remained somewhat inferior to a True Immortal."

"However, with the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother as a supplement, it felt like a sudden enlightenment, allowing my thoughts to truly spread out."

"The Star Sea below may not contain just one proving ground."

"Thinking about it this way, the abandonment of the Xuanhuang Realm also becomes perfectly logical."

Due to the rampant Dao Annihilation Tribulation, most realms had been obliterated. Only a few fragmented remnants, like shallow sandbars in a river, supported what remained within the Annihilation Land. "Even the vibrant area outside the High Wall is probably just a larger island." "The vast starry sky, obscured by countless Annihilation Lands, hides its true appearance. Therefore, believing oneself to be the only existence in the world is understandable."

"But I, with the Dao-Transforming Stone Mother, can glimpse the whole world from a single corner…" Li Fan's mental panoramic view of the possibility he inhabited was finally slowly completed. The scene depicted in this panorama was truly boundless. The vast Utmost Darkness Star Sea was merely an insignificant dot within it. However, most of the areas in this panorama were in a flickering state of uncertainty. This was because the current data was too scarce to prove their actual existence. Only the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, within the High Wall where Li Fan resided, remained brightly unextinguished, regardless of how light and shadow shifted.

"The starry sky of all possibilities shines only because of my existence."

"The possibility I inhabit, let's call it the Primeval."

Li Fan thought this to himself. Sooner or later, Li Fan's strength would allow him to leap to other possibilities. It was not wrong to define his current location early. However, the most important task at hand was still to begin contact with the civilization of the Annihilation Land. Even with the Xuanhuang Realm's sentient beings as a foundation, Li Fan still felt that the dream tendrils were expanding too slowly. Ten years ago, Li Fan had already enacted laws promoting childbirth. But in ten years, population growth was genuinely limited.

"In the short term, I can't rely on that. It seems I'll have to find a way myself."

Li Fan felt the large amount of idle computing power in his Sea of Consciousness, and a thought involuntarily emerged. As early as when he visited the Museum of Divine Treasures' `Era` device, Li Fan had a thought. The countless worlds deduced by the Dao-Transforming Stone were incredibly realistic. If the Dao-Transforming Stone itself was continuously strengthened, then these deduced worlds would sooner or later become indistinguishable from real worlds.

"Perhaps it's precisely because the Stone Mother is the manifestation of all Great Daos within a possibility that I harbor such a notion."

"All the worlds that once appeared within the Stone Mother are, theoretically, completely rational and real."

"It's like having well-made molds; one only needs to pour the liquid to produce a physical object."

"If my comprehension of the Transformation of True and False reaches a higher level, I won't have to create worlds from scratch. I can simply transform the possibilities once deduced by the Stone Mother from false to true, saving a lot of effort."

Li Fan's eyes sparkled. "But what I need are merely consumables to contribute to the Dream Bliss Land. They don't need to exist in the real world."

With that thought, within Li Fan's Sea of Consciousness, another Xuanhuang Realm began to evolve within the Dao-Transforming Stone.

Chapter 1434: Hunting Immortals and True Immortals

The Dao-Transforming Stone within Li Fan's Sea of Consciousness finally began to feel pressure.

Creating a world from nothing, even with the template of real existence, was proving to be more challenging than Li Fan had anticipated.

The key to creation lay in individuals.

Creating countless individuals was not difficult.

What was difficult was creating individuals with their own "thoughts."

Initially, Li Fan's thoughts went down the wrong path.

He wanted to simulate and create true consciousness, genuine sentience, within his own world.

As a result, he consumed nearly half of the Dao-Transforming Stone's computational power, only managing to birth three individuals.

Three wills with subjective agency, hovering in the skies of the virtual Xuanhuang Realm.

These three individuals were completely independent of the Dao-Transforming Stone. Their thoughts flowed without the need for the Stone's reliance. However, the computational power they consumed was substantial.

With half of its performance depleted, if not for Li Fan's ability to transform the false into the true, which allowed him to ignore such consumption, he would have been heartbroken and abandoned this attempt on the spot.

"These three wills, judging solely by their abilities, even surpass my own. However, they are still in the nascent stages of their existence, in a state of ignorance. Most of their computational power remains unused..."

"Were it not for the fact that they all originated from the Dao-Transforming Stone, which allows me to erase them with a single thought. Harboring three such behemoths in my Sea of Consciousness would truly be somewhat frightening."

Li Fan quietly gazed at these three wills, like infants, slumbering.

Then his thoughts returned to the main topic.

"Normally, creating sentient beings with self-awareness would not require such a large expenditure. I am directly proving the Dao through brute force. Although I have not grasped the method of creation, I have used immense computational power to break through and ignore those unspoken limitations."

"I was too fixated on the details. To propel the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss, it's not necessary to create true sentient consciousness. Simply adding the command for 【Dreaming】 to simulated consciousnesses is sufficient..."

After a brief pause in his thoughts, Li Fan began to integrate the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss into the simulated Xuanhuang Realm.

The Dao-Transforming Stone shimmered with light, and streams of light, representing thoughts, rapidly flowed into the dream.

Simultaneously, a large number of beings descended into the dream.

Their behavior was indistinguishable from real people.

They communicated, traded, and adventured together in the dreamscape. All the things normal cultivators could do, they handled perfectly.

Furthermore, with the first batch of sample data, the simulated sentient wills produced by the Dao-Transforming Stone began to iterate and evolve at an incredibly terrifying speed.

Initially, they would occasionally be sluggish in conversations. But later, even Li Fan could hardly distinguish between the real and the false.

The operation of simulated beings did not require much computational power from the Dao-Transforming Stone.

This was because all these sentient wills could be attributed to ninety-nine types of behavioral patterns.

The Dao-Transforming Stone only needed to maintain these ninety-nine basic templates to leverage countless endless beings like a lever.

"It appears these are all different individuals, but their core is the same ninety-nine people."

Having found the right method, the exponentially increasing simulated sentient wills made even Li Fan feel slightly apprehensive. Fortunately, after confirming once more that he had absolute control over them through the Dao-Transforming Stone in his mind, his unease slowly subsided.

The beings in the virtual Xuanhuang Realm did not need to live in reality; they were all connected to the Dreamland of Carefree.

With the assistance of these "ghost soldiers," the speed at which the dream tendrils explored outwards greatly accelerated.

Next, Li Fan followed suit.

While continuing to use the superposition power of Transforming True and False to restore the Dao-Transforming Stone, he also "copied" and created more simulated Xuanhuang Realms.

After consecutively creating twelve virtual Xuanhuang Realms, Li Fan finally stopped.

"Thirteen worlds' ghost soldiers are enough."

Li Fan looked at the three wills in the first virtual Xuanhuang Realm, still in a dazed, ignorant state. He hesitated before finally projecting them into the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss.

"Let's observe their potential in the dream first."

"With such a vast computational power as support, no matter which direction they choose, they can reach the pinnacle."

The three wills, respectively named 【Qi】, 【Shi】, and 【Zhong】 by Li Fan, finally manifested bodies in the dream.

Compared to the simulated beings, they appeared particularly clumsy. Towards everything in the outside world, they held immense curiosity.

But Li Fan knew that their growth rate would be faster than any other being in the dream.

Li Fan did not interfere with the growth of Qi, Shi, and Zhong.

He only recorded and preserved the method by which the Dao-Transforming Stone had fostered them, ensuring that they could be replicated quickly even if they were destroyed.

Afterwards, Li Fan's attention returned to the exploration of the dream tendrils.

Passing through the long Annihilation Land, crossing the boundless silent sea of stars, the dream tendrils finally reached the vibrant star systems where powers like the Sword Domain and the Holy Merchant resided.

The tendrils' exploration became increasingly cautious.

An invisible light gauze slowly enveloped the star system.

But to Li Fan's surprise, none of the myriad beings in this star system were captured by the power of the dream.

It was as if, between reality and illusion, there existed a natural barrier, resisting the dream's encroachment on the beings in reality.

Li Fan, who controlled the dream, sensed that if he were to exhaust the power of the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss, he might be able to forcibly open a gap in this barrier, but it would undoubtedly attract the attention of various forces.

Li Fan chose to wait patiently for an opportunity.

Fortune favors the persistent. After the dream tendrils had been exploring the vibrant star system for a full year, a turning point finally appeared.

A massive upheaval in the sea of stars, even affecting the ethereal Dreamland of Utmost Bliss, naturally drew Li Fan's attention.

Seven figures suddenly appeared in the star system, completely blocking another dark, distorted figure.

"Hmm? Not on the list in the 【Immortal Hunt Record】?"

"Unexpectedly, while waiting for the 【Longevity Immortal】, there's a bonus find."

"Unfortunately, there are no signs of him having attained the Nameless Realm."

"One must not be careless... I can sense a trace of danger from him."

The seven figures spoke to each other, exhibiting the characteristic communication style of the Immortal Hunt organization found in Qin Zhuang's memories.

While communicating, they did not refrain from taking action.

And Li Fan, for the first time, truly glimpsed the power of Dao Origin.

If the Great Dao were like a vast net, crisscrossing and spanning heaven and earth,

Then these seven Immortal Hunters, with every gesture, possessed the strength to pull on this net and capture their prey.

Li Fan perceived all sorts of mystical and unfathomable techniques.

For example, countless swords materialized from nothingness, and behind each sword, a blurry figure vaguely stood. Myriad sword divine abilities bloomed simultaneously in the star system, resonating with the Dao of the Sword as if amplified. Each sword strike contained immense power, seemingly capable of cleaving the Xuanhuang Realm.

For example, the dim star system seemed to be illuminated by something. As if countless pairs of eyes were staring intently at the combatants from beyond the veil. The aura of the seven Immortal Hunters surged. And the True Immortal being besieged had his movements occasionally go out of control. Even his figure seemed to split into multiple selves amidst the violent tremors.

For example, it was as if a brush were secretly recording and modifying the battle outcome. Li Fan had clearly observed earlier that the True Immortal's long-prepared strike had hit one of the Immortal Hunters. His body visibly convulsed, clearly injured. But after a flicker of light and shadow, this scene seemed as if it had never happened. The injury vanished, and instead, a counterattack struck the True Immortal.

The True Immortal was bewildered and quickly fell into a disadvantageous position, forced into a desperate defense. In just a moment, his situation became precarious.

…

While the seven Immortal Hunters displayed their unique abilities, Li Fan keenly observed that, besides these seven, there seemed to be another Immortal Hunter lurking in the shadows.

This Immortal Hunter did not participate in the hunt for the True Immortal.

He was silently repairing the star system affected by the great battle.

Li Fan dimly saw that, under the influence of this orderly power, the fragile Great Dao, bent by the power of Dao Origin, became strong and stable once more.

Although it was a battle of True Immortal-level powers, it did not cause significant damage to the star system.

Even the Great Dao seemed to have recorded the memory of this battle. In the future, when similar battles occurred, the Great Dao's resilience would become stronger.

"Besides the Immortal Hunters, there is also 【Heaven Mending】?"

"Interesting."

As the saying goes, destruction is easy, creation is difficult.

Li Fan lurked in the shadows, silently observing the battle. However, most of his attention was focused on the one who was mending the sky.

Li Fan keenly sensed that perhaps this 【Heaven Mender】 was the true strongest party in this encounter.

This was because it was obvious that no matter what kind of Dao Origin power caused destruction, this entity could effortlessly repair it. And the seven Immortal Hunters only displayed one type of Dao-related divine ability from beginning to end.

The seven Immortal Hunters only injured, not killed, the True Immortal. They seemed intent on capturing him alive.

As the True Immortal gradually fell into despair, countless True Immortal inscriptions suddenly appeared on his body, densely covering him!

His aura suddenly expanded hundreds of times, and the Dao net shook violently as if caught in a fierce gale.

Even the divine abilities used by the seven Immortal Hunters were affected!

The True Immortal's desperate gamble.

At this moment, a golden circle lit up, precisely like a drawn boundary, completely sealing off the area where they were fighting.

The relationship between the inside and outside of the golden circle was completely severed.

Even the tendrils of the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss were directly cut off.

The scene disappeared abruptly.

Li Fan could only watch from afar outside the golden circle.

The True Immortal's desperate final attack was completely blocked by this golden circle.

Regardless of the external forces, nothing could be felt from within.

Li Fan looked at this golden circle, emanating a sacred aura, and suddenly felt a sense of familiarity.

"This..."

"Is this the Immortal Heavenly Pillar?"

In his mind, the Southern Immortal Heavenly Pillar, forged from the leg bone of a True Immortal, overlapped with the scene of the golden circle.

Li Fan was greatly surprised. Then, a sudden inspiration struck him. He drastically retracted the dream tendrils.

He only remotely observed from an extreme distance.

A figure in white, quietly appeared outside the golden circle.

He seemed to be observing the battle within the golden circle with a solemn expression.

Li Fan also felt that it was precisely because of the "support" of this golden circle, as a pillar stabilizing the somewhat fragile Dao net during the great battle, that a disaster was averted.

The figure in white occasionally emitted rays of light, filling the golden circle, making it increasingly solid.

"This must be the 【Heaven Mender】."

"Fortunately, their attention was fully focused on the battle, and the unique power of the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss allowed me to avoid detection."

Li Fan thought to himself, relieved, but he dared not approach too closely.

He continued to observe from afar.

Not long after, the battle seemed to finally calm down. The golden circle gradually dissipated, and the seven Immortal Hunters reappeared.

However, the True Immortal had vanished without a trace.

Seeing the diverse expressions on the faces of the seven Immortal Hunters, the figure in white looked somewhat surprised and finally spoke.

"He escaped?"

One of the Immortal Hunters replied in a deep voice, his tone heavy, "He was already at his limit. But at the last moment, it seemed another force interfered. He was saved."

"My Heavenly Painting Brush was powerless to alter this fact. It is clear that a Nameless True Immortal intervened," another Immortal Hunter stated.

"And it was a Nameless True Immortal not recorded in the annals."

Upon hearing this, the expressions of all the Immortal Hunters became somewhat strange. Some were excited, some were fearful.

The figure in white nodded slightly, "Although we did not capture the True Immortal, we unexpectedly gained news of a new Nameless True Immortal. There were gains and losses. You six should first return and report the Nameless Traces. Brother Chu, you will stay with me to repair the Dao scars."

In an instant, six figures disappeared.

Only two remained standing in the star system after the great battle.

Without them even needing to make a move, Li Fan, observing from afar, could clearly feel that this star system had become much "sturdier."

"Heavenly Painting Brush. Brother Chu."

Li Fan's mind replayed the voice of that distant Immortal Hunter.

"Divine Brush Sect, Chu Youhong?"

A moment later, Li Fan had roughly determined the other party's identity.

Chu Youhong, former Sect Master of the Divine Brush Sect.

The cultivator who once uttered words like "It doesn't matter if all of you die. As long as I am alive, the Divine Brush Sect will still exist. My master entrusted the Divine Brush Sect to me before his death, and I must not let it be destroyed in my hands."

After leaving an indelible mark on the history of the Xuanhuang Realm, he had vanished without a trace.

Unexpectedly, today, in the vibrant star system outside the High Wall, he reappeared.

Li Fan recalled Chu Youhong's performance during the battle.

"Able to use a brush to alter established facts. And even rewrite them to a certain extent..."

"Although not a True Immortal, his actual combat power is likely not inferior to a True Immortal."

Li Fan was secretly alarmed.

Ultimately, he had a clearer understanding of the power of 【Dao Origin】 outside the High Wall.

While he was contemplating, Chu Youhong had already finished repairing the so-called "Dao scars" with the figure in white.

"Brother Chu, what do you think of the nameless True Immortal who appeared at the end?"

"You were able to deceive others, but surely you couldn't deceive yourself. You must have observed him."

"After all, Brother Chu is said to be able to imitate and replicate the Great Dao."

The words of the figure in white astonished Li Fan once again.

Chapter 1435: Dao Yuan Weaves the Dao Net

"Imitating and replicating the Great Dao?"

It was said that even the inscription Immortal of the Nameless Realm could only describe various Great Daos using True Immortal script. Yet, this Chu Youhong claimed to be able to do something to this extent?

Li Fan’s first reaction was disbelief.

Chu Youhong’s expression seemed to confirm his skepticism.

Chu Youhong gave a wry smile, "I was fortunate to leave behind a trace of the Great Dao's imprint, that too within the anomaly of a Nameless True Immortal's fall and the Dao returning to the heavens and earth..."

"Furthermore, without the aid of this Drawing Heaven Brush in my hand, it would be absolutely impossible. Brother Lu, you don't need to flatter me."

"On the contrary, your divine ability to mend the tears in the sky with your bare hands is widely known throughout the Star Sea."

The cultivator named Lu, clad in white, didn't deny Chu Youhong's praise, merely offering a slight smile.

Chu Youhong shifted the topic back to the main point, "The Nameless True Immortal who acted in secret just now was indeed peculiar. Although I couldn't fully depict the grand Dao's landscape, I could still clearly sense the traces left behind by the flow of the Dao. However..."

Chu Youhong's expression turned solemn, "It was silent and traceless. It did not resemble the actions of a True Immortal in the Nameless Realm at all. In fact, the traces left behind were even lighter than those of an ordinary True Immortal."

The cultivator with the surname Lu nodded in agreement, "This is precisely why I sought to speak with you, Brother Chu. I believe either the one who acted this time was not a Nameless True Immortal, or that Nameless True Immortal has found a way to shield their traces within the Dao Net."

The two exchanged glances. "Regardless of which method it is, it is not good news for us."

"If it wasn't a Nameless True Immortal, yet they could escape our encirclement with ease, their actual combat power is no less than that of the Nameless Realm. The power of a new system is what we have always worried about the most. After all, all the methods we have summarized so far are targeted at 'Immortals.' Once 'Immortals' break free from past constraints, even if it means they have to start anew, we will have to face entirely new, unknown enemies."

"As for shielding the traces within the Dao Net," a flicker of worry crossed Chu Youhong's brow.

The white-robed cultivator Lu glanced back at the vibrant Star Sea, "After failing to capture the Nameless one last time, we suffered heavy losses. Some individuals have already begun to stir. It's hard to say if this isn't a sign of some people making a plea for allegiance. If those True Immortals master the methods of stealth and manipulation of the Dao Net, it would be disastrous!"

"The patterns of the Dao Net must be revised. Besides that..."

The cultivator named Lu looked back at Chu Youhong, "I will have to trouble Brother Chu to secretly inform Wan Shiyong, Senior Wan."

"After all, this Senior has a peculiar temperament. You come from the same world as him and can barely be considered to have some common ground."

Chu Youhong appeared somewhat hesitant, but ultimately nodded in agreement, "Now that the Star Sea is without a leader and faces covetous eyes from other regions, we indeed need a senior who can command respect to take charge of the situation."

"Although I was beaten severely when I previously disturbed Senior Wan, seeing as we are all cultivators from the Xuanhuang Realm, he shouldn't truly harm me, right?" Chu Youhong muttered to himself as he flew with the white-robed cultivator towards the Star Sea.

In just a short while, their figures disappeared.

Li Fan, while pondering their recent conversation, controlled his dream tendrils and arrived at the location of their previous battle.

Generally, after powerful cultivators engage in battle, there are always residual traces, fluctuations, and auras. However, at the battle site where they hunted the True Immortal, Li Fan observed carefully but found no traces whatsoever.

It was as if the great battle had never occurred.

"Besides the white-robed cultivator's 'Heaven Mending' which consumed all these residues to consolidate this region's Great Dao, it felt as if something else was simultaneously absorbing the residual power."

After much searching, Li Fan finally reached a vague conclusion.

He couldn't help but think of the "Dao Net" mentioned by Chu Youhong and the white-robed cultivator.

"Dao Net, although this term never appeared in Qin Zhuang's memories, perhaps it was a product of the Star Sea born after Qin Zhuang went to the Xuanhuang Realm. However, judging by the name, it's clearly related to the net woven by the Great Dao of heaven and earth."

"A Nameless True Immortal embodies a single Great Dao. Every action they take must leave a trace in the Dao Net. This is as it should be. However, Chu Youhong said they could modify the 'Dao Net'?"

A contemplative look appeared in Li Fan's eyes.

Although Chu Youhong and the white-robed cultivator’s conversation was brief, it contained a substantial amount of information.

First, the encirclement of the True Immortal resulted in heavy losses, indicating that the battle between the Star Sea and the True Immortal was not one-sided. The Star Sea seemed to be leaderless, with all high-level figures involved in a critical matter.

Second, besides the Star Sea, there were other forces, perhaps in another star field within the Annihilation Land. They were eyeing the Star Sea greedily. The situation in the Star Sea seemed far from optimistic.

Third, the white-robed cultivator’s words clearly indicated his awareness that Chu Youhong came from the Xuanhuang Realm. And he mentioned Wan Shiyong, who also hailed from the Xuanhuang Realm…

Li Fan's brow furrowed.

"Wan Shiyong, the founding ancestor of the Beast Taming Sect. An old acquaintance of Di Sanmo, a peerless figure who comprehended the True Beast Taming Art from the Beast Taming Wheel of Reincarnation."

"Those whom Di Sanmo chose to align with were all extraordinarily talented individuals. But in my memory, didn't this Wan Shiyong perish?"

Li Fan was confused and immediately summoned Di Sanmo to inquire.

"Hmm?" Hearing Li Fan suddenly mention this name, this intelligent beast seemed momentarily dazed. After all, that was tens of thousands of years ago.

"He, indeed, died. I personally buried his corpse. Despite his immense talent, he could not escape the limitations of mortal lifespan," Di Sanmo replied with certainty after recalling for a moment.

"Then why does another Wan Shiyong exist in the Star Sea outside the High Wall?" Li Fan succinctly explained the scene he had witnessed through his dream tendrils to Di Sanmo.

Di Sanmo contemplated for a moment, then seemed to recall something, "His temper was a bit peculiar..."

"Could it be Wan Shiyong's companion beast from when he was alive?" he said uncertainly.

Li Fan expressed surprise, "Wan Shiyong's beast tamer wasn't you?"

Di Sanmo looked embarrassed, then stroked his beard and said, "My relationship with Wan Shiyong was merely a cooperative one. As a mere mortal, he was not qualified to command me. Wan Shiyong's beast tamer was actually a [Withered Shadow Beast]. It resembled a shadow in form and was infinitely variable in shape."

"Normally, it would hide within Wan Shiyong's shadow. At critical moments, it could leap into the enemy's shadow and transform, replicating it."

"'A shadow is like the person,' it could even achieve perfect similarity. Even the one being copied would have difficulty distinguishing the difference. After Wan Shiyong's death, that creature vanished without a trace. If it has been living as Wan Shiyong, relying on its familiarity with Wan Shiyong from his lifetime, others might not be able to detect the difference," Di Sanmo analyzed slowly.

"Since it is a member of the demonic beast race, are the previous methods of restraint still effective? Or, failing that, can you sense or contact it?" Li Fan inquired.

Di Sanmo hesitated for a moment, and for the first time, did not provide an answer.

"Under normal circumstances, it should be possible. However, judging from your earlier statement that Chu Youhong, who can imitate the Great Dao's imprint, was no match for that Wan Shiyong..."

"I am afraid that individual has already surpassed our control."

Fearing that Li Fan might misunderstand his lack of effort, Di Sanmo quickly added, "Senior, as you know, the current demonic beast race all evolved from Di Yi. And Di Yi originated from the fusion of countless members of the original clan. The key point is that the origin of the clan..."

Di Sanmo projected a beam of light, revealing the appearance of thirteen ancient, peculiar beasts to Li Fan.

"These are the thirteen primeval forms of our clan. Although they were the strongest beings in the clan during their lives, born as avatars of the Great Dao, they were not the source of the clan. In fact, there is no consensus on the origin of the clan; even the memories of the primeval forms hold no answer. However, there is one thing that was a shared understanding among us in the past."

Di Sanmo’s gaze held a hint of nostalgia as he looked at the primeval forms before him.

He then slowly said, "In our timeline, our clan was favored by the Great Dao of heaven and earth. The thirteen primeval forms were merely insignificant parts compared to the myriad Great Daos of heaven and earth. And all other clan members had the potential for 'Dao Transformation' even after birth. Analogous to your human cultivators, it meant cultivating to the Nameless True Immortal realm."

"To completely merge and derive all the Great Daos of heaven and earth into primeval forms. This was the 'golden age' of our clan's dreams..."

"Alas, before new primeval forms could emerge, fierce Nameless True Immortals, crossing from other possibilities, slaughtered them all." Li Fan's untimely interruption broke Di Sanmo's reverie.

Di Sanmo, however, showed no embarrassment, merely sighing slightly, "Our clan was indeed favored by the Great Dao within its own possibility. But there are also differences in strength between possibilities. The law of the jungle prevails; we have no complaints about being defeated by others."

Di Sanmo then returned to the topic of Wan Shiyong, "What I mean to say is, although each clan member originated from Di Yi, each has the potential to surpass Di Yi. Even if theoretically, this possibility is extremely small, almost to the point of impossibility. But it is not zero."

"As long as the history of propagation is long enough, it can become a certainty. This was something the primeval forms considered when entering the great furnace. However, what they did not expect was that it was not our current possibility that fell into crisis, but all possibilities that ushered in the great tribulation of world destruction. Repeated escapes left our clan no time to recover. And the power of the primeval forms was completely depleted..." Di Sanmo sighed deeply.

After a moment of silence, Di Sanmo suddenly volunteered, "I wish to go and speak with this Wan Shiyong."

"Even if his strength now far surpasses mine, I am confident he will not harm me."

Li Fan pondered for a moment, then finally agreed, "I will use the power of dreams to help you manifest a body."

"After you contact him first, if there are no issues, I will then send your physical body over."

"Remember, the dream body is essentially a manifestation of Wuyou's and the Xuanhuang beings' intentions. Although it contains a wisp of your intention, it is not truly connected to your true self. Whether you can gain Wan Shiyong's trust will depend on your own efforts," Li Fan cautioned.

Di Sanmo nodded, "Senior, rest assured. Our clan has its own methods of communication and identification."

"The situation in the Star Sea is uncertain. Even if the first attempt fails, it is inconsequential."

Li Fan spoke thus, and a dream tendril slowly manifested a body outside the Star Sea.

It was entirely yellow, with a countenance identical to Di Sanmo's in reality. Initially, it seemed to exist in a state between reality and illusion.

But with the infusion of specks of blood-red light and a certain mystical power, this illusory body transformed from false to true.

It materialized from nothingness.

Di Sanmo felt his new body and exclaimed in awe, "Senior's methods are truly unimaginable. It feels completely identical to my real body!"

Li Fan's voice echoed in Di Sanmo's ears, "Not all dream bodies can achieve such a level of verisimilitude."

"I have prepared some energy for you within this body. It should be enough for your journey. Proceed with caution; a dream body, with its intention and physical form integrated, can be reborn continuously as long as there is energy. But once the energy is depleted, the body will be completely destroyed, and consciousness will cease to exist."

"If, before destruction, the consciousness does not return to the Land of Utmost Bliss, then this memory will be completely lost. Thus, I suggest you return periodically and report your findings."

"Of course, this is only if you can guarantee you won't expose yourself. The power of dreams, though elusive, is still formidable. However, the Star Sea also possesses considerable strength. If you manifest too much, you might inadvertently reveal your tracks..."

Li Fan instructed.

Di Sanmo narrowed his eyes. Relying on that faint connection, he rapidly moved towards his target location, concealed.

Initially, Li Fan could still sense the scene from Di Sanmo's side through the power of dreams.

But as he approached a place where light converged, even the dream connection was severed.

"The Sword Domain, the Sacred Merchant, the various strongholds within the Star Sea, indeed possess some form of protective power."

"The Dao Net, perhaps..."

Li Fan watched Di Sanmo's dream body depart, sensing the power of the so-called Dao Net.

Based on the deductions from the Dao-Transforming Stone in his sea of consciousness, Li Fan had already confirmed that this Dao Net was likely built upon the Dao Origin system.

He recalled the "Mysterious Net" that the Heavenly Xuan Mirror had woven in the sky of the Xuanhuang Realm when it usurped the heavens.

"Being able to modify the Dao Net implies that the Dao Net is not unbreakable or impenetrable."

"It's just a matter of finding the corresponding method."

Chapter 1436: Covertly Sneaking Into Shuoxing Sea

IDEALS ARE admirable.

But after observing for several days, Li Fan still couldn't find any trace of the so-called "Dao Net." It seemed to be more elusive than the Great Dao itself. Still, Li Fan was not discouraged. From what he could ascertain, the Dao Net was likely the trump card of the Shining Star Sea's forces against True Immortals. If it could even contend with Nameless True Immortals, how could it be so easily deciphered by a newcomer like Li Fan? "Even the most fortified castle can be breached from within." "Since direct intrusion into the Dao Net is impossible for now, I might as well infiltrate the Shining Star Sea. I can't rely entirely on Di Sanmo..."

Li Fan shook his head slightly. He first meticulously used his dream power to create a "rubbing" of the residual fluctuations in the area. Only then did he continue to probe his way towards the Shining Star Sea. Although all traces of the great battle had been seemingly erased by the white-robed cultivator's "sky-mending" technique, Li Fan knew that nothing in the world could be absolutely erased. Anything that had occurred would leave a trace. If he couldn't detect it now, it was simply because his abilities were insufficient. But that didn't stop Li Fan from recording it for future study.

The Shining Star Sea in the distance was not uniformly inhabited; life formed in concentrated clusters, like islands. The aura emanating from these clusters, regardless of their size, did not dictate their strength. Each had its distinct characteristics. "Those who have survived in this star sea must be extraordinary individuals." Li Fan observed from afar, distinguishing certain familiar auras among them. He first discovered the Sword Domain, suspected to be the gathering place of the Ten Great Immortal Sects of the Xuanhuang Realm from days past. However, he couldn't find any sign of the Sacred Merchant from Qin Zhuang's memories. "The Profound Immortal Ship could still sense the existence of the Merchant Immortal Ship beyond the wall, so the Profound Merchants shouldn't have gone extinct yet."

Recalling the Sacred Merchant's peculiar behavior in Qin Zhuang's memories—stopping communication with the outside world and even recalling previously sold treasures—Li Fan's Dao Transformation Stone in his sea of consciousness flashed. After some deduction, the most likely guess instantly surfaced in Li Fan's mind. "It's highly probable that the Sacred Merchant discovered something and either chose to seclude themselves or outright fled." The Sacred Merchant was merely an entry point; Li Fan was not fixated on pursuing the Merchant Immortal Ship of the past. He began to probe the weaker forces within the Shining Star Sea one by one.

As his senses suggested, the strength of these forces was not directly related to the amount of life force they gathered. There were two isolated life forces, one large and one small, seemingly ostracized, living on the periphery of the Shining Star Sea. But before Li Fan could even get close, just a glance from afar sent a wave of crisis through him. Even his dream tendrils were affected, distorted and mutated. Li Fan could only keep his distance.

There was a vast cluster of tens of millions of living beings, yet it was shrouded in a massive dark cloud woven from negative emotions like slaughter, hatred, and greed. Even though this cluster had various defenses to prevent the direct erosion of Li Fan's dream power from the outside, Li Fan found a breakthrough through the emotional cloud, the ingress point for his dream. However, Li Fan did not rush to act. This vulnerability might be a trap deliberately set by the Shining Star Sea's forces to lure out True Immortals.

After investigating all other clusters and finding that only this one offered an opportunity to access the Land of Utmost Bliss, Li Fan, in his utmost caution, first accumulated a large amount of dream power, creating an additional instance of the Land of Utmost Bliss. He then sent a wisp of his divine sense into this instance, severing its connection with the main world of the Land of Utmost Bliss. Ensuring everything was foolproof, Li Fan's divine sense then directed the invasion of this cluster. This instance of the Land of Utmost Bliss was empty. It was a severed instance, and dream power was consumed with each use. If effective replenishment was not received before the energy was depleted, this instance would perish. Although Li Fan had only sent a wisp of divine sense, it carried the energy of the Xuanhuang Realm's phantom and computational power equivalent to a top-grade Dao Transformation Stone. "If even with all these preparations, a breach cannot be made, then I'll have to find another way."

Progress was not smooth. An invisible membrane completely prevented any contact between dream power and the consciousness of living beings. Even though the suppressed negative emotions of the beings had become almost tangible, hanging over the sky, there was still a film in between, making direct contact impossible. "If I disregard the consequences and exhaust all the power of this instance at once, I might be able to force a gap. But that would inevitably alert the forces of the Shining Star Sea collectively." "The gain would not be worth the loss." After careful consideration, Li Fan ultimately chose not to alert them and opted to wait patiently for an opportunity.

There were cultivators who left their clusters in the Shining Star Sea to travel the star fields. Li Fan did not believe that all these "passersby" were so powerful that he couldn't approach them. His judgment proved correct. Although the target he had set his sights on did not travel as frequently as other factions, he did travel eventually. After Li Fan stalked him for half a year, a beam of light finally flew out from one of the clusters. Its destination seemed to be in the direction of the Sword Domain. As the light shot out, it stirred up large swathes of the emotional cloud. Its emotional fluctuations were so palpable that Li Fan, without even needing to actively eavesdrop, could clearly perceive its thoughts.

"Making me run errands again!" "I, Ma Tiande, passed the qualifying exam and am certified as a [Dao Manipulator] by the Shining Star Sea. Although I've only just scratched the surface, I can at least coordinate and control the Dao Net patterns within a unit area!" "Forcing me to do such trivial tasks every day is simply a waste of my life, Ma Tiande..." This cultivator, named Ma Tiande, harboring deep resentment, traveled through the starscape at full speed. Li Fan did not act, merely watching as he entered a cluster adjacent to the Sword Domain. After staying there for three days, he slowly returned. As if having vented his frustrations, his resentment had vanished. Humming a happy tune, he meandered back the way he came.

Just as Ma Tiande was about to enter the protective barrier, Li Fan made his move. Ordinary methods of possession or infiltration were highly likely to be detected by the cluster's defenses. In fact, any power related to Immortals could trigger an alarm. Therefore, Li Fan employed the "Dao Pill" technique of the Profound Immortal Ship. Ma Tiande, who was flying through the void, merely paused slightly. Li Fan had already refined him into a "human pill" ready to be swallowed. Li Fan's divine sense silently ingested the pill, instantly transforming into Ma Tiande. Temporarily severing his connection with the Land of Utmost Bliss instance, Li Fan began to sort through the information in Ma Tiande's mind while flying directly towards the destination cluster.

"Extremity Bliss City?" "Interesting." Theoretically, this body was still Ma Tiande. It was just that his mind now contained an additional stream of thought. Any living being's mind inevitably experienced such fluctuations. Moreover, the Dao Pill's soul-snatching technique was unique to the Profound Immortal Ship and had never appeared in this star sea before. Although the defenses outside Extremity Bliss City were strong, they could not guard against such an unfathomable technique. Without any complications, "Ma Tiande" smoothly flew into Extremity Bliss City.

Unlike the foul-smelling emotional cloud observed from the outside, Li Fan was greeted by a scene of revelry and prosperity. Colorful lights stretched to the horizon. Uninhibited laughter, lewd moans, and unrestrained scoldings... filled every corner of the city. "Extremity Bliss City: three years of day, three years of night, a cycle of six years." "During the night, indulge in pleasure, free from worry." "During the day... indiscriminate killing?" Li Fan, while sorting through Ma Tiande's memories, headed towards his residence to report. Ma Tiande's trip to "Blade Island" was to deliver an invitation from the Lord of Extremity Bliss City. Thirty days later, coinciding with the transition of day and night in Extremity Bliss City, they invited the people of Blade Island to witness the grand occasion.

... As the information flashed through his mind, Li Fan calmly arrived at the center of Extremity Bliss City. Compared to the bustling and lively surroundings, the mansion in the center was so desolate and eerie, creating a stark contrast that sent a shiver down the spine of anyone who stepped foot there. Even though it wasn't Ma Tiande's first time here, he instinctively felt fear. Li Fan did not suppress his emotions but displayed appropriate changes in his expression. Following closely, he approached the Lord of Extremity Bliss City and reported the situation. "Scholar Zhu, the invitation has been delivered. However, as for how many people from Blade Island can come, it's hard to say."

Li Fan expressed his difficulties with a troubled look and recounted everything he had experienced. "As soon as I entered, the people on the island invited me to spar. They even threatened to tear up the invitation if I refused. I had no choice but to agree." "They called it sparring, but it was just me getting beaten unilaterally..." Li Fan, concealing Ma Tiande's original behavior, complained to the Lord of Extremity Bliss City. The Lord of Extremity Bliss City, Scholar Zhu, appeared extremely aged from the outside. His hunched body was folded into a loose robe, making him look quite comical. However, the overwhelming aura of malevolence emanating from Scholar Zhu made Li Fan dare not underestimate him. Li Fan even vaguely sensed that the vast emotional cloud accumulated above Extremity Bliss City was maintained, for the most part, by this Scholar Zhu.

Facing Ma Tiande's incessant complaints, Scholar Zhu did not interrupt. He quietly stopped tapping his emaciated, bony fingers on the table. Occasionally, he would drag his fingernails across the long table, emitting an incredibly grating sound. Li Fan clearly saw that the long table before Scholar Zhu was made of stacked and polished human skulls. Even the grudging resentment on the skulls had not completely dissipated. As Scholar Zhu lightly dragged his finger across them, faint cries of pain and anguish could be heard. Cold sweat dripped from "Ma Tiande's" forehead. He did not stop speaking, completing the report to the lord with a sense of thoroughness. After finishing, he respectfully stood below the long table, awaiting the lord's instructions.

In the mansion, there was a long silence. From outside, occasional sounds of revelry and shouting could be heard. Scholar Zhu, hunched in his robe, tapped his finger on the table. With each tap, a sound from outside abruptly ceased. Only when the surroundings fell completely silent, and no more external noise could be heard, did Scholar Zhu finally speak. His voice was not that of an old man, but the innocent and playful voice of a child. "You've had a hard journey." "Go back after dinner."

As he spoke, a ghostly figure floated out from the shadows and appeared before Li Fan. With a rustling sound, a bowl of steaming red soup appeared before Li Fan. Ma Tiande's body trembled slightly. It was a natural reaction of the body, and to some extent, it represented Li Fan's emotional fluctuations. The red soup in the bowl was clearly mixed with countless pieces of minced meat and blood. And floating in the bowl were eyeballs, one after another. They seemed to possess their own consciousness, all staring at Li Fan outside the bowl. Although Li Fan had witnessed world-ending events and viewed the living beings of the world as insignificant, he had never done anything so "disgusting."

"Quickly drink it, Mr. Ma. Why aren't you drinking yet?" Seeing Li Fan's hesitation, Scholar Zhu's voice suddenly became impatient, like a mischievous child who had suddenly lost their favorite toy. A strange aura began to spread from Scholar Zhu's body. "Aren't you hungry? Or are you dissatisfied with this soup?" "It's alright, I'll have the servants prepare something better." Li Fan's mind flashed with Ma Tiande's understanding of the Lord of Extremity Bliss City. "He manifests many personalities." "An old man, a child, a charming woman, a cruel butcher..." "Among them, the most unstable is the child."

Having made up his mind, Li Fan said, "No need to trouble yourself, Scholar Zhu. This soup tastes incredibly delicious." With that, Li Fan took the red soup and drank it in one gulp. To his surprise, it was not as bloody as it looked. In fact, it didn't have the slightest taste of meat or blood. Instead, it was indescribably delicious. Even with Li Fan's knowledge, accumulated over hundreds of reincarnations in the Xuanhuang Realm, having explored almost all its secrets, he couldn't find anything in his experiences that could rival its taste. After drinking the bowl of red soup, looking at the empty bowl, Li Fan even felt a sense of reluctance.

"What, do you want another bowl?" Scholar Zhu also noticed the change in Li Fan's emotions and became excited, as if he had found a kindred spirit. With great willpower, Li Fan shook his head and refused. "Such a precious delicacy must be savored properly." "Better less than more," he said earnestly. Scholar Zhu heard this and let out a muffled laugh. His voice, shifting from that of a child, quietly returned to that of an old man. "What you say has some truth to it." "In that case, you may leave now."

Li Fan bowed and took his leave. Just as he was about to exit the mansion, Scholar Zhu's voice, light as a feather, drifted into his ear. "For this grand ceremony of day and night, I have also prepared a seat for you." Li Fan's expression brightened, and he quickly bowed again, "Many thanks, Lord Zhu!" The scene flickered, and the Lord's mansion disappeared. A red building, filled with lewd sounds, took its place. Li Fan licked his lips. Ma Tiande's memories surfaced again: "Scholar Zhu, a member of the Shining Star Sea's Governing Council." "He was once a True Immortal, who then degenerated into a mortal!"

Chapter 1437: Ghost City of Profound Sounds

"Even more than that, he might have been a Nameless True Immortal!"

Li Fan lowered his head, concealing the thoughts swirling in his eyes. He walked briskly towards his residence.

"Guest, come and play!"

"Brother Ma, long time no see. Come have a drink!"

"You brat, I finally caught you! Don't run!"

...

Wandering through Extremity Bliss City, Li Fan heard successive calls. Accompanying the overlapping sounds were fragments of memories related to those voices. The owners of these voices were either old acquaintances he had met in entertainment districts, sworn brothers who had shared life-and-death experiences, or even enemies he had wronged.

Scenes flashed rapidly before his eyes, as if he had personally experienced them. However, Li Fan remained indifferent, his head lowered, and continued steadily towards his destination. He had only "possessed" Ma Tiande recently. Li Fan was certain that these memories did not exist in Ma Tiande's mind before; they were merely imprinted in his mind as he heard the voices.

"This is not a simple illusion."

"It's as if these events truly happened in Extremity Bliss City."

Even as Li Fan moved away, the voices gradually faded, but the imprinted memories did not disappear. Instead, they became even more profound. Along the way, "Ma Tiande" was thus burdened with many experiences. Each experience spanned years. Wrinkles quietly appeared at the corners of his eyes. Ma Tiande's face subtly looked aged.

Li Fan, of course, noticed these physical changes. He intentionally slowed his pace from quick to slow, as if each step was a struggle.

After traversing a block of Extremity Bliss City, "Ma Tiande" finally returned to his residence. The moment the pitch-black door closed, all the chaotic noises from the outside vanished instantly, concealed in darkness.

Following Ma Tiande's old habits, he dealt with his affairs. Then, he sat cross-legged, closed his eyes, and meditated, as if studying the "Dao Net patterns." However, Li Fan was actually still contemplating the changes in this body during his journey.

"Using a false past to influence the present reality."

"Is this technique the demonic chanting of King Xuan Tian?"

The top-grade Dao Transformation Stone in his sea of consciousness began to operate, assisting Li Fan in his analysis.

"If Ma Tiande had succumbed to temptation and indulged in any of those enticements,"

"then the 'past events' mentioned during conversation would have materialized upon him..."

In Li Fan's visualized deduction, he vaguely saw Ma Tiande at a banquet rapidly aging, instantly turning into withered bones, yet still engaging in conversation and laughter with those around him. Until the pleasure ended, his decaying bones turned to dust, and Ma Tiande's consciousness was forever trapped in this Extremity Bliss City, just like countless other consciousnesses within the city.

"Kid, once you enter Extremity Bliss City, apart from what Scholar Zhu assigned you, do nothing else. Stay honestly for three full years, and you might have a chance to return."

The scene of a senior from the Shining Star Sea Governing Council giving Ma Tiande earnest advice before he entered Extremity Bliss City flashed through his mind.

"The Shining Star Sea's ability to hunt Immortals relies heavily on the assistance of beings like Scholar Zhu, who have transformed from Immortals to mortals."

"Although they have fallen into the mortal realm, the strength of these former True Immortals should not be underestimated."

"Perhaps to appease them or allow their twisted hearts to vent, the Governing Council has prepared special 'playgrounds' for them. This Extremity Bliss City is the one dedicated to Scholar Zhu."

"The countless beings seen within the city have long since died. It is a veritable ghost city. They can still maintain their physical forms, albeit sustained by a peculiar energy. Even with the three-year cycle of day and night and endless mutual slaughter, no one truly dies. They simply wait for the next cycle to be reborn."

"However, the ultimate victor in the slaughter..."

Li Fan smacked his lips, savoring the taste of the red soup he had just drunk. The residual consciousnesses, like ethereal remnants, naturally had no real flesh-and-blood taste. What Li Fan consumed at Scholar Zhu's mansion was the carefully cooked and refined essence of countless beings' consciousness!

"Just like eternal residual consciousness!"

"No wonder it was so delicious."

After drinking the bowl of red soup, Li Fan felt a sense of reluctance looking at the empty bowl.

"What, do you want another bowl?"

Scholar Zhu also noticed the change in Li Fan's emotions and became excited, as if he had found a confidant.

With great resolve, Li Fan shook his head and refused.

"Such rare delicacies must be savored properly."

"Better less than more," he stated seriously.

Scholar Zhu heard this and let out a muffled laugh. His voice, shifting from child-like, quietly returned to that of an old man.

"What you say has some ground."

"In that case, you may leave now."

Li Fan bowed and took his leave. Just as he was about to exit the mansion, Scholar Zhu's voice, light as a feather, drifted into his ear.

"For this grand ceremony of day and night, I have also prepared a seat for you."

Li Fan's expression brightened, and he quickly bowed again, "Many thanks, Lord Zhu!"

The scene flickered, and the Lord's mansion disappeared. A red building, filled with lewd sounds, took its place. Li Fan licked his lips. Ma Tiande's memory data surfaced again:

"Scholar Zhu, a member of the Shining Star Sea's Governing Council."

"He was once a True Immortal, who then degenerated into a mortal!"

Chapter 1438: One Hand Overturns the Great Dao

"IMITATING AND replicating the Great Dao?" It was said that the legendary Dao Inscribing Immortal in the Nameless Realm could only describe the Great Dao with True Immortal inscriptions. How could Chu Youhong achieve such a feat? Li Fan's first reaction was disbelief. Chu Youhong's performance also seemed to confirm his judgment. Chu Youhong said with a wry smile, "It was by chance that I left behind a trace of the Great Dao imprint, and it was within the anomaly of the Nameless True Immortal's fall and the return of Dao to heaven and earth..." "Moreover, without the assistance of the Drawing Heaven Brush in my hand, I would never have been able to do it. Brother Lu, you shouldn't praise me so highly."

"On the other hand, your divine ability of mending the sky and patching the heavens, [Shuo Xing Hai], is truly known to everyone in the Shuo Xing Hai." The white-robed cultivator Lu did not deny Chu Youhong's flattery, only showing a faint smile. Chu Youhong changed the subject and returned to the main topic, "The Nameless True Immortal who secretly acted just now was indeed somewhat strange. Although I couldn't fully depict the Great Dao's map, I could still clearly sense the traces left by the flow of the Great Dao. However..." Chu Youhong's expression became somewhat solemn, "Silently. It didn't seem like the action of a Nameless True Immortal. In fact, the traces left behind were even lighter than those of ordinary True Immortals."

The white-robed cultivator Lu nodded in agreement, "This is also why I specifically sought out Brother Chu for a conversation. I believe that either the one who intervened was not a Nameless True Immortal, or that Nameless True Immortal has found a way to conceal his traces within the [Dao Net]." The two looked at each other, "Whether it's one or the other, it's not good news for us."

"Not a Nameless True Immortal, yet able to escape from our encirclement with ease, with combat power not below the Nameless Realm. The power of the new system is what we have always been most worried about. After all, all the methods we have summarized so far are targeted at [Immortals]. Once [Immortals] break free from their past shackles, even if it means they have to start anew, we will have to face new and unknown enemies."

"As for concealing traces within the [Dao Net]," Chu Youhong's brow showed a hint of worry. The white-robed cultivator Lu looked back at the vibrant Shuo Xing Hai, "The last time we failed to capture a Nameless True Immortal, we suffered heavy losses.
