Some people have already started to stir restlessly. It's hard to say if this is a declaration of loyalty from some people. If those True Immortals master the methods of stealth and manipulation of the Dao Net, it will be a disaster!"

"The patterns of the Dao Net must be modified simultaneously. Besides that..." The robed cultivator Lu looked at Chu Youhong again, "I will have to trouble Brother Chu to secretly inform Elder Wan Shiyong, Senior Wan." "After all, this senior has eccentric temperaments. You are from the same world as him, and can barely speak to him."

Chu Youhong looked troubled, but finally nodded and agreed, "Now that the Shuo Xing Hai is leaderless, and facing covetousness from other places, it is indeed necessary for a senior who can command the crowd to come forward and take charge." "Although I was beaten severely when I disturbed Senior Wan before, considering we are all Xuanhuang Realm cultivators, he probably won't really do anything to me." Chu Youhong muttered to himself while flying towards the Shuo Xing Hai with the white-robed cultivator. In a moment, their figures disappeared.

Li Fan pondered their conversation while controlling the dream tendrils to approach the battle site after the great battle. Generally, after experts clash, there are always traces, fluctuations, or auras left behind. But after Li Fan's careful observation of the battle of hunting True Immortals, there were absolutely no signs of residue. It was as if the great battle had never happened.

"Besides the actions of the white-robed cultivator [Sky Mender], which consumed all these residues to consolidate this Great Dao, somehow, something also absorbed the residual power in sync." After searching for a long time, Li Fan vaguely reached a conclusion. He then thought of the [Dao Net] mentioned by Chu Youhong and the white-robed cultivator.

"Dao Net, this term did not appear in Qin Zhuang's mind, perhaps it was a product of the Shuo Xing Hai after Qin Zhuang went to the Xuanhuang Realm. But judging by the name, it is clearly related to the net of heaven and earth Great Dao." "Nameless True Immortals merge with a single Great Dao. Every action they take must leave traces in the Dao Net. This is as it should be. However, Chu Youhong said they could modify the [Dao Net]?" Li Fan's eyes showed contemplation.

Although Chu Youhong and the white-robed cultivator only spoke a few words, the information conveyed was substantial. First, the encirclement of True Immortals resulted in heavy losses, indicating that the battle between the Shuo Xing Hai and True Immortals was not one-sided. The Shuo Xing Hai was leaderless, and it seemed all its high-level figures were occupied with a crucial matter. Second, besides the Shuo Xing Hai, there were other forces, perhaps in another star space within the Annihilation Land, who were coveting the Shuo Xing Hai. The situation of the Shuo Xing Hai did not seem optimistic. Third, the white-robed cultivator's words clearly indicated that Chu Youhong was from the Xuanhuang Realm, and the mentioned Wan Shiyong, who also came from the Xuanhuang Realm... Li Fan's brow furrowed.

"Wan Shiyong, the founding ancestor of the Beast Taming Sect. An old acquaintance of Di San Mo, a peerless figure who comprehended the True Beast Taming Art from the Beast Taming Reincarnation." "Those who Di San Mo chose to ally with were all exceptionally talented individuals. But in my memory, didn't Wan Shiyong already perish?" Li Fan was confused and immediately summoned Di San Mo to ask him.

"Hmm?" Hearing Li Fan suddenly mention this name, the intelligent beast was momentarily dazed. After all, this was tens of thousands of years ago. "Yes, he is dead. I personally buried his body. Even with his talents, he couldn't escape the limitations of mortal lifespan," Di San Mo replied with great certainty after recalling for a while. "Then why is there another Wan Shiyong outside the High Wall in the Shuo Xing Hai?" Li Fan immediately explained the scene he saw through the dream tendrils to Di San Mo.

Di San Mo pondered for a while, then seemed to recall something, "His temper was a bit eccentric..." "Could it be Wan Shiyong's companion beast?" he said uncertainly. Li Fan was somewhat surprised, "Wan Shiyong's beast master wasn't you?"

Di San Mo looked embarrassed, then stroked his beard and said, "Wan Shiyong and I were merely collaborators. He, a mortal, was certainly not qualified to command me. Wan Shiyong's beast master was actually a [Desiccated Shadow Beast]. It looked like a shadow and could change its form infinitely." "Normally, it would hide in Wan Shiyong's shadow. When necessary, it could leap into the enemy's shadow, transform, and replicate." "The shadow was like the person, even achieving complete similarity. Even the replicated person could hardly distinguish the difference. After Wan Shiyong's death, the whereabouts of that child became unknown. If he had been living as Wan Shiyong, given his familiarity with Wan Shiyong during his lifetime, others might not have discovered the difference," Di San Mo analyzed slowly.

"Since it is a member of the demonic beast race, can the previous containment method still be used? Or, as a fallback, can he be sensed or contacted?" Li Fan asked. Di San Mo hesitated for a moment, and surprisingly, did not give an answer. "Under normal circumstances, it should be possible. But based on what Senior just said, even Chu Youhong, who can imitate the Great Dao imprint, was no match for that Wan Shiyong..." "I'm afraid he has already surpassed our control."

Fearing Li Fan might misunderstand that he was not making an effort, Di San Mo quickly explained, "Senior, as you know, the current demonic beast race is all derived from Di Yi's evolution." "And Di Yi originated from the fusion of countless members of the original clan. The key is, the original origin of the clan..." Di San Mo projected a beam of light, revealing the appearances of thirteen strange ancient beasts to Li Fan. "These are the Thirteen Primordial Dao Forms of our clan. Although they were the strongest beings in the clan since birth, the embodiment of the Great Dao, they were not the origin of the clan. In fact, there is no consensus on the origin of the clan, and even the memories of the Primordial Dao Forms hold no answer. But there is one thing that was once a consensus among us."

Di San Mo's expression showed a hint of nostalgia as he looked at the Primordial Dao Forms before him. Only then did he slowly say, "In our timeline, the clan was favored by the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth. The Thirteen Primordial Dao Forms were merely an insignificant part of the myriad Great Daos of Heaven and Earth. As for all other clan members, they had the possibility of post-natal [Dao Transformation]. Analogous to your human cultivators, it was equivalent to cultivating to the Nameless True Immortal realm." "To completely fuse and evolve all the Great Daos of Heaven and Earth into Primordial Dao Forms. This was the 'Golden Age' that the clan dreamed of..." "Unfortunately, before the new Primordial Dao Forms could emerge, fierce Nameless True Immortals crossed over possibilities and slaughtered you all."

Li Fan's untimely interruption shattered Di San Mo's reverie. Di San Mo, however, showed no embarrassment, only sighing slightly, "Our clan was indeed favored by the Great Dao in our own possibility. But there are also differences in strength between possibilities. The strong prey on the weak, and we have no complaints about being defeated by others."

Di San Mo shifted the topic back to Wan Shiyong, "What I mean to express is that although we all originate from Di Yi, each clan member has the potential to surpass Di Yi. Even if, theoretically, this possibility is extremely small, almost impossible. But it is not zero." "As long as the history of reproduction is long enough, it can become a certainty. This was something the Primordial Dao Forms considered when they entered the great furnace. However, what they did not expect was that it was not their own possibility that was in crisis, but all possibilities that faced the world-ending tribulation. Repeated escapes left our clan no time to recuperate, and the power of the Primordial Dao Forms was completely depleted..." Di San Mo sighed deeply.

After a moment of silence, Di San Mo suddenly volunteered, "I wish to go and have a talk with this Wan Shiyong." "Even if his current strength far surpasses mine, I am confident that he will not harm me." Li Fan pondered for a moment and finally agreed, "I will use the power of the dream to help you evolve a body." "After you contact him first, if there are no problems, I will help you send your actual body over."

"Remember, the dream body is essentially a manifestation of Wuyou and the intentions of the Xuanhuang beings. Besides a wisp of your intention being included, it is actually not closely related to your true self. Whether you can gain Wan Shiyong's trust still depends on you finding your own way," Li Fan added. Di San Mo nodded, "Senior, rest assured. Our clan has its own methods for communication and identification." "The situation in the Shuo Xing Hai is unclear. Even if the first attempt fails, it's fine."

As Li Fan said this, dream tendrils slowly evolved a body outside the Shuo Xing Hai. It was entirely golden-yellow, with an appearance identical to the real Di San Mo. Initially, it seemed to exist between reality and illusion. But with the influx of wisps of blood-red light and some mysterious and ultimate power, this illusory body actually transformed from false to true. It emerged out of thin air from the void. Di San Mo felt his new body and exclaimed, "Senior's methods are truly unimaginable. It feels exactly the same as my real body in reality!"

Li Fan's voice sounded in Di San Mo's ear at this moment, "Not all dream avatars can achieve such an extreme level of transforming the false into the true." "I have prepared some energy for you within this body. It should be enough for you to travel. Proceed with caution. In a dream avatar, intention and body are integrated. As long as there is energy, you can be reborn continuously. But if the energy is completely depleted, the body will be completely destroyed, and consciousness will cease to exist." "If your consciousness does not return to the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss before being destroyed, then this memory will be completely lost. Therefore, I suggest you return periodically to report the information." "Of course, as long as you ensure your identity is not exposed. The power of dreams, although mysterious and difficult to detect, is still formidable. Showing too much might inadvertently reveal flaws..." Li Fan instructed.

Di San Mo narrowed his eyes and, relying on the faint connection, rapidly moved towards the target location, cloaked in stealth. Initially, Li Fan could still sense the scene from Di San Mo's side through the power of the dream. But as he approached a place where light converged, even the connection through the dream was severed.

"Sword Domain, Sacred Merchant, the residences of many forces in the Shuo Xing Hai indeed have some protective forces." "Dao Net..." Li Fan watched Di San Mo's dream avatar leave, sensing the power of the so-called Dao Net. Based on the deductions of the Dao-Transforming Stone in his Sea of Consciousness, Li Fan had already confirmed that this Dao Net should be based on the Dao Origin system. He thought of the "Xuan Net" that the Heavenly Xuan Mirror had woven on the Xuanhuang Realm's sky in the past, replacing the sky. "Being able to modify the Dao Net means that the Dao Net is not indestructible or impenetrable." "It's just a matter of finding the corresponding method."

Chapter 1439: Manifestation of the Mind

LI FAN faintly sensed something similar to the Southern Immortal Heavenly Pillar within several key nodes of the Dao Net. Before he could ponder further, the magnificent "Dao Net" before his eyes suddenly vanished, disappearing from his sight.

In Extremity Bliss City, the noisy clamor seemed to vanish collectively for a moment, then instantly resumed its normal state. It was likely that only Li Fan, the person responsible for overseeing the Dao Net inspection, or perhaps the Lord of Extremity Bliss City, would be able to perceive the changes that occurred above Extremity Bliss City.

If the Dao Net was equivalent to a white paper inscribed and overlaid on the surface of the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth, then the inspection of the Dao Net was akin to splashing ink on this white paper and then pressing down forcefully. "The traces of the Dao Net are becoming clearer. Those within the net are tightly bound and cannot escape."

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, seemingly seeing Scholar Zhu's sinister face. He did not interfere with the Dao Net's erosion of Extremity Bliss City, but silently watched, allowing his "toys" to sink deeper into this net.

After the roaring of the Dao Net subsided, Scholar Zhu finally cast a glance towards Li Fan's location. Li Fan bowed slightly, feigning a nervous expression. Only after a full three breaths did Scholar Zhu avert his gaze and his figure faded into the city.

Li Fan paid no mind to the other's threat, instead temporarily clearing all extraneous thoughts to recall every detail he had seen within the Dao Net moments prior.

Ma Tiande, as one of the grassroots operators of the "Dao Net," was not merely a disposable pawn. In fact, being able to connect to and observe the "Dao Net" up close was itself a supreme opportunity that all cultivators yearned for!

The Dao is formless and invisible. Cultivators seek it ceaselessly, striving to approach the Dao, the origin of all things. Although Ma Tiande was a "Dao Manipulator," his actual cultivation was comparable to the Nascent Soul stage. At this level, let alone seeing the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth, even a single strand of the myriad Great Daos was far beyond his comprehension.

However, precisely because of his special identity as a "Dao Manipulator," he could frequently glimpse the Dao Net, which was a reflection of the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth.

"This means Ma Tiande's aptitude is truly mediocre. If he were in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, he might not even reach the Qi Refining stage. Furthermore, the Shining Star Sea's Governing Council intentionally withheld any concepts or knowledge related to cultivation from him. Thus, even after countless lần coming so close to the Great Dao, his cultivation remained mediocre."

"He possessed a great treasure but was unaware of it!" Li Fan exclaimed with a sigh, slowly digesting the profound insights swirling in his mind.

"True Immortal inscriptions are the interpretations of Dao Inscribing Immortals. By studying True Immortal inscriptions, people can glimpse the Great Dao of the world through the eyes of Dao Inscribing Immortals."

"The Dao Net, however, is directly the shadow of the Great Dao, or rather, a replica."

"Compared to True Immortal inscriptions, it is even closer to the 'Dao' itself."

"Incredible!" Li Fan, with his vast experience, offered sincere praise.

Li Fan's comprehension was, of course, far superior to Ma Tiande's. During his first glimpse, inspiration surged unprecedentedly. Li Fan compared and verified the fragmented "Dao" glimpses he had seen from various channels in the past with the real Dao Net. His understanding of the "Dao" escalated rapidly, like waves in a stormy sea, each surpassing the last. This was, in a sense, a culmination of accumulated knowledge, a natural progression.

Although it was only a wisp of divine sense, once it could resonate with the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth, it could transform the mundane into the miraculous. Li Fan's divine sense became like a thin film, upon which countless blurred, crisscrossing lines appeared. It bore a striking resemblance to the Dao Net Li Fan had seen!

In essence, Li Fan had used his divine sense as paper and the Dao Net, a replica of the Great Dao, as a template to create yet another imprint. Although it was a copy of a copy, the original was, after all, the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth!

Even though Li Fan's divine sense film only managed to replicate the most basic shape, it was enough to manifest the true power of the Great Dao. Light flickered on the film, seeming to resonate with the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth. As if imbued with infinite life and power, the flickering light gradually completed Li Fan's "feeble" divine sense.

Slowly, this wisp of divine sense actually nurtured into the complete form of Li Fan! Although the details were still somewhat blurry.

"This is... Divine Manifestation of Thought?" The moment the divine manifestation of thought was born, Li Fan's true body in the Xuanhuang Realm also experienced a drastic change in expression. He sensed everything that had happened in Extremity Bliss City, Shining Star Sea.

Although he had severed all connection with that wisp of divine sense, with the power of the Land of Utmost Bliss no longer connected, and separated by a distance equivalent to dozens of Utmost Darkness Star Seas, with an invisible high wall standing between them, Li Fan could still synchronize with his illusory divine sense.

Li Fan's expression gradually became more profound. "It's not a direct connection between us. Instead, it's through the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth acting as a relay."

"Everything in the world, from top to bottom, is a projection of the Great Dao. My part in the Great Dao's projection is unique."

"Although separated by immense distance and blocked by various means, as long as we both exist under the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth, this synchronization cannot be affected." Li Fan quickly understood the reason behind this seemingly impossible occurrence.

Relying on his profound understanding of the Great Dao, he had, using the Dao Net as a template, constructed another miniature Dao Net within himself! Simultaneously with connecting to the divine sense in the Shining Star Sea, Li Fan's true body's divine sense also underwent corresponding changes. Due to the difference between the true body and the divine sense, the more detailed pattern did not appear on the film. Everything depended on the understanding of the Great Dao.

In his sea of consciousness, after the divine manifestation of thought was born, Li Fan's illusory figure stood tall. The Dao Transformation Stone suddenly emitted a brilliant blue light, which then transformed into myriad rays of light, surging into the illusory figure. This further completed the Great Dao pattern on it!

Some of the Dao Transformation Stone's light rays perfectly integrated into the illusory figure of the divine manifestation of thought. Others, after circulating once, could not find a suitable place to reside and, unable to usurp its position, drifted out from the illusory figure once more. It then reverted into a Dao Transformation Stone. However, due to the absence of the Great Dao it constituted, the quality of this Dao Transformation Stone had fallen from Mother Grade to Middle Grade. But Li Fan did not care about this. As long as he had time, by continuously layering the Transformation of True and False, he could restore the Dao Transformation Stone's quality effortlessly.

"This phenomenon with the Dao Transformation Stone confirms my earlier conjecture."

"The Mother of Dao Transformation Stone was indeed formed from a complete Great Dao of a certain possibility. However, that possibility's Great Dao was not the same as the 'Primordial' one I inhabit, and was even significantly weaker. Thus, only a portion of its Great Dao emerged to complete the Great Dao diagram in my divine manifestation of thought."

"But even so, with the supplement of the Dao Transformation Stone, this miniature Dao Net constructed by me instantly transformed from an unbearable sight to something quite presentable."

Li Fan's mind, immersed in the Great Dao network within his divine sense, was captivated. Because of the substantial external assistance, Li Fan was temporarily unable to achieve the initial feeling of effortless control. This was a matter of both advantage and disadvantage. However, as it was based on Li Fan's divine sense, Li Fan still held absolute control.

After a long period of immersion, Li Fan finally came back to his senses and let out a long sigh, "This is already very close to the theoretical stage of Divine Manifestation of Thought."

"Using one's own thoughts to embody the shadow of the Great Dao."

"By chance, I have skipped several steps before the new method and directly reached this stage."

"Although there are some flaws..." If it were the perfect state described in the new method's theory, Li Fan's divine sense illusion would not just be a distorted and bent copy. Instead, the divine sense would be like a mirror, reflecting the entire Great Dao of Heaven and Earth within it.

"The divine sense, from bottom to top, traces back to the origin of the Great Dao. Every thought and intention can invoke the power of the Great Dao."

"Unfortunately, what I am reflecting is merely an incomplete replica." Li Fan felt a slight regret. However, he knew that even at his current Half-Immortal stage, attempting to glimpse the true Great Dao of this world was still wishful thinking.

"Having a powerful being help create a fake is a temporary Substitute method." After the divine manifestation of thought created the miniature Dao Net, its benefits were not limited to instantaneous long-distance communication. At the very least, Li Fan now possessed the ability to directly invoke the power of the Great Dao to fight, akin to the Immortal Hunters of the Shining Star Sea.

"However, my miniature Dao Net's power is incomparable to the 'Dao Net' constructed by the Shining Star Sea."

"But its efficiency is still more than a hundred times higher than directly using True Immortal inscriptions." Now that Li Fan had mastered his own Dao Net, he naturally understood the difference in operation compared to conventional methods.

"Perhaps only now, with the destruction of the Immortal Realm and the absence of many Immortals, is this method risk-free."

"If in ancient times, several Nameless True Immortals merged with the Great Dao, and I used the Dao Net to invoke the power of the Great Dao, they would surely sense me from within the Great Dao."

"Essentially becoming the public enemy of all Nameless True Immortals... In the initial stages of proving the Dao, I would likely face a concerted pursuit. I wouldn't even know how I died."

After integrating the Great Dao contained within the Dao Transformation Stone, even though the quality of his own Dao Transformation Stone had declined, Li Fan's thinking speed was not affected. In an instant, he considered many possibilities.

"Now, who knows how many Nameless True Immortals remain. And with another larger Dao Net acting as a cover and drawing fire..."

"It's impossible to attract the attention of Nameless True Immortals."

"Even..." A confidence suddenly surged within Li Fan. Now that he had achieved divine manifestation of thought and replicated his own Dao Net, he felt he was no longer completely defenseless against Nameless True Immortals.

"A Nameless True Immortal fully masters one Great Dao of Heaven and Earth."

"My divine manifestation of thought, although merely an incomplete replica of the Great Dao's shadow, can only invoke a limited amount of Great Dao power."

"But its advantage lies in its quantity. And ultimately, it is still the power of the Great Dao. Theoretically, it's the same power used by Nameless True Immortals, just significantly weaker." Li Fan understood this with clarity. This was not just a fleeting arrogance after a temporary breakthrough, but a rational deduction based on his understanding of the Great Dao.

"This is still a rudimentary stage of divine manifestation of thought."

"If it were the ideal state of the new method, perhaps divine manifestation of thought could truly contend with Nameless True Immortals."

"If the Manifestation realm is already like this, what about Star Sea Merging and Dao Resonance Longevity?"

"Could they be the realms where the Black Heavenly Physician and Evil Su Bai reside?" Li Fan could almost not suppress his speculation.

After a long while, the surging thoughts subsided.

"The reason I could achieve divine manifestation of thought was a matter of chance."

"Throughout my past hundred reincarnations, I not only witnessed numerous True Immortal inscriptions but also glimpsed complete Immortal Domains, the leg bone of a True Immortal, and even scenes of black energy descending and the Great Dao annihilating. The birth and death of the Dao have allowed my understanding of the Great Dao to accumulate to an unimaginable level compared to ordinary people."

"Simply relying on these is far from enough. With the 'Dao Net' of the Shining Star Sea as a stepping stone, I could finally transform my past accumulations into reality. A copy of a copy, though far from the original, is the best way for a 'newbie' like me to achieve imitation."

"In addition, and more importantly..." Li Fan's divine sense figure meticulously examined himself. For the first time, he faintly sensed the existence of "True Return." It was as elusive as the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth, and in Li Fan's perception, it was merely an indescribable, blurry presence. But Li Fan, who had been accompanied by True Return for a long time, was certain in his heart. That, indeed, was "True Return."

"The Transformation of True and False contained within True Return seems to encompass all the Great Daos of Heaven and Earth."

"My comprehension of the Transformation of True and False continuously deepens, and in a sense, it's a deepening of my perception of the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth."

"Now, I can briefly maintain the existence of 'False becomes True.' This might be the fundamental reason why my divine sense can accept a complete Great Dao of a possibility."

"As for others..." Li Fan pondered for a moment, then slightly shook his head. "Only those with extraordinary talent, the right time, place, and people, might be able to achieve it."

"I originally thought about pioneering a new path with the new method." To his surprise, he ended up cheating with "True Return," directly skipping the earlier stages. It was an isolated case, not replicable. However, Li Fan was not concerned about whether others could cultivate; as long as it was effective for himself, that was sufficient.

"Even though this is only a half-baked divine manifestation of thought, it has inadvertently pointed me towards my next course of action."

"Maximize contact with the 'Dao Net,' allowing my imitation to become more perfect."

"The Transformation of True and False and the comprehension of the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth, advancing hand in hand, will allow me to approximate the Great Dao's essence by reflecting the Dao Net..." Li Fan's heart rejoiced. The Immortal path was broken, but with the enlightenment from the civilization outside the High Wall, he had found a new potential path in such a short time.

"This is not just the achievement of mortals in a single lifetime."

"Not to mention the participation of True Immortals, but between the inside and outside of the wall, there is a difference in time flow..." Li Fan frowned slightly, calculating.

Chapter 1440: The Death of the Nameless Immortal

THE flow of time in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea was already inconsistent due to the existence of the Immortal Ruins. Therefore, Li Fan compared the Xuanhuang Realm with Extremity Bliss City in the Shining Star Sea. Under normal circumstances, it was a hundred and twenty times faster!

This meant that over a hundred and twenty years in the Shining Star Sea, only one year had passed in the Xuanhuang Realm.

"A time flow rate of over a hundred times is also why the gap between the inside and outside of the High Wall is so vast."

"Even the current situation in the Shining Star Sea must be vastly different from when Qin Zhuang left. It can be said that times have changed."

Having initially established a Great Dao projection and a miniature Dao Net within himself, Li Fan's understanding of the "Dao" had reached a new C. Therefore, faced with this unbelievable time discrepancy, Li Fan naturally began to harbor doubts.

"Theoretically, when the 'Hunger' mantra is understood to its peak, it can indeed achieve such an effect. But..."

"This is the performance that should be exhibited by one who has attained the Nameless realm by proving the Dao with 'Hunger'."

"From the performances of the Hunger Immortals I've seen, she clearly hasn't reached that level."

Images of the Hunger Immortal Li Fan had seen in the past flashed through his mind. When the Cat Treasure appeared, she was in a sorry state and captured; even before the Dao Annihilation Tribulation itself, but merely its precursor, the great tide of black energy, she visibly paled. It seemed she could only escape the calamity with the Southern Immortal Heavenly Pillar; even when Evil Su Bai was extremely close, stepping on her face, she remained oblivious...

"Perhaps only one step away from the Nameless realm, but this one step's difference manifests externally as an enormous disparity!"

"The temporal anomaly in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea was likely not caused by the Hunger Immortal. Or rather, only a small part of it was due to the Hunger Immortal's enlightenment."

"The greater reason seems to stem from the 'Immortal Ruins' themselves."

Li Fan recalled the scenes he had witnessed within the Immortal Ruins. Besides the vast ruins, the most striking feature was the colossal character "Hunger" inscribed on the ground. Li Fan had previously speculated that this Hunger character might have been personally written by a Dao Inscribing Immortal. Now, it seemed this character held a deeper mystery.

"The Hunger Immortal could break free from her shackles at any time; the golden chains were clearly for self-restraint. The Immortal Ruins were once the Ascension channel to the Immortal Realm. When the Immortal Realm suffered the Dao Annihilation Tribulation, the Great Dao collapsed, and all things crumbled. The surviving Immortals fled from the Immortal Realm's channel to the lower realms in a desperate manner."

Li Fan deduced and retraced the events of that time.

"The Dao Annihilation Tribulation could destroy even the Immortal Realm. At that time, who could guarantee that the terrifying tribulation would not spread through the Ascension channel? Theoretically, it would be better to escape as far as possible. Yet, the Hunger Immortal stopped in such a dangerous place, even meditating to achieve enlightenment without regard for the danger..."

"In the past, I overlooked the illogical aspects."

Li Fan's gaze shifted again towards the Immortal Ruins above.

"If the Hunger Immortal insisted on achieving enlightenment using the True Immortal inscription carved on the land, she could have simply taken the entire land, along with the characters, to a safe place for secluded cultivation."

"However, she did not do so."

"The Dao Annihilation Tribulation ceased abruptly and did not affect the lower realms. The True Immortal inscription on the Immortal Ruins land, causing anomalies, even reached the peak of enlightenment, the realm of a Nameless Immortal. The leg bone of the Nameless Immortal, serving as an Immortal Heavenly Pillar..."

These numerous clues flashed through Li Fan's mind, finally connecting to form the most plausible conclusion.

"The Hunger Immortal did not move the 'Hunger' character, not out of unwillingness, but inability. Because, beneath the Hunger character, or perhaps the Hunger character itself, was transformed from the remains of a Nameless True Immortal!"

"This Nameless Immortal, whether willingly or unwillingly, returned to the Great Dao after death, becoming a 'Heavenly Pillar,' temporarily holding up the collapsing sky of the Immortal Realm!"

"And it was precisely because of the death of the Nameless Immortal who proved the Dao through Hunger that the one within the Immortal Ruins had the intention to comprehend the Hunger character and re-attain the Nameless realm!"

Li Fan's heart trembled, and his thoughts drifted again. Given the immensity of the Immortal Realm and the lower star seas, the so-called Ascension channels likely were not limited to just one. From the current state of the lower star seas, although most regions had been annihilated by the Dao Annihilation Tribulation, several surviving lands still existed.

"Perhaps this is the protection of other Nameless True Immortals!"

"By using themselves as pillars, they withstood the overwhelming tribulation."

Li Fan let out a long breath.

"If the High Wall represents the ruins of a collapsed structure, then Nameless Immortals are the pillars above."

"With the protection of Nameless True Immortals, even the Utmost Darkness Star Sea is in such a desolate state..."

"Perhaps the lower star seas could continue to survive, thanks undeniably to the sacrifices of Nameless True Immortals."

Nameless True Immortals, by merging with the Dao, were no longer the same species as mortals, or even True Immortals. But this was Li Fan's perspective. Perhaps, among these Nameless True Immortals, there were noble individuals like Su Bai, willing to sacrifice themselves to save the beings of heaven and earth, even if only temporarily.

Or perhaps, the Immortals who fled downwards had foreseen that the Dao Annihilation Tribulation would pursue them. For their own survival, some had to step forward and "sacrifice themselves" to buy enough time for others to escape.

In summary, some Nameless True Immortals became pillars standing between heaven and earth, temporarily holding back the Dao Annihilation Tribulation. However, this method could only guarantee temporary survival, not eternal protection. The Dao Annihilation Tribulation would only be delayed, not disappear.

"The Dao Net is subtly influenced by these Immortals."

"Furthermore, some of the Dao Net nodes I glimpsed even bear the aura of the remains of Nameless True Immortals."

However, Li Fan was not surprised by this. Li Fan's miniature Dao Net within his divine sense was merely a projection. He deeply understood how difficult it was to affix a real creation to the ethereal Great Dao.

"The Dao Net operates unstably."

"The giant hand I glimpsed outside the Dao Net, only serves a supplementary role. It is clear that the hand does not manifest at all times. What truly anchors the Dao Net..."

Li Fan seemed to see the Dao Net spanning heaven and earth again. All the irrelevant lines disappeared, leaving only a few crucial nodes. They belonged to the Dao Net, and simultaneously, existed within the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth!

It was precisely because of the unique nature of these nodes that the "Dao Net" could adhere tightly to the formless and intangible Great Dao of Heaven and Earth!

"Nameless True Immortals!"

"Even more likely, they are *living* Nameless True Immortals!"

After achieving divine manifestation of thought, Li Fan peered into the hidden secrets of the Dao Net again. The few remaining nodes in his vision vaguely revealed blurry human figures. Then, they stared intently at Li Fan and, without warning, suddenly opened their eyes!

One by one, Nameless True Immortals seemed to reveal their true forms. All of them looked towards Li Fan!

A sudden sense of dread surged within Li Fan, and startled, he broke free from the illusion. The figures vanished, seemingly just ordinary nodes.

However, Li Fan was not calm. Was it just an illusion? Li Fan did not think so. With his current level of cultivation, even sophisticated Immortal-level illusion formations could hardly affect him. He would certainly not hallucinate for no reason.

"The most likely explanation is..."

"The Nameless True Immortal nodes exist simultaneously in the Dao Net and the Great Dao."

"My Great Dao projection in my divine manifestation of thought has also mirrored these nodes."

"Therefore, in a sense, I have indeed seen them!"

With a shift in his thoughts, Li Fan reached a conclusion. Soon, a question arose in his mind. Since Li Fan could see them, could these Nameless True Immortals see Li Fan?

Inevitably, Li Fan felt a wave of agitation. While he believed he could contend with Nameless True Immortals, it did not mean he could remain calm under the gaze of several Nameless True Immortals. Although his intuition, which had always been accurate, did not issue a warning of danger, and although he had become a "stake" node nailed into the Dao Net, the existence of these Nameless True Immortals still made him feel like he was sitting on pins and needles, with his back crawling with unease.

However, it was utterly impossible for Li Fan to give up the power of divine manifestation of thought he had obtained out of fear of this impending danger. Li Fan's true body's thoughts spun rapidly as he pondered countermeasures.

Meanwhile, in Extremity Bliss City of the Shining Star Sea, Li Fan's divine sense, disguised as Ma Tiande, was already preparing for the Extremity Bliss City's grand ceremony. The long-range communication ability of divine manifestation of thought allowed the divine sense to ignore spatial blockades and know everything Li Fan's true body had deduced. However, these troubles were for the true body to bear. The divine sense's current task was to remain hidden in Extremity Bliss City and further observe the Dao Net. But first, he had to get through the Extremity Bliss City grand ceremony.

Scholar Zhu clearly disliked the intrusion of the Dao Net. However, for some reason, he would not directly retaliate, but would only vent his anger on Ma Tiande, who was directly responsible for the operation. To Scholar Zhu, a cultivator like Ma Tiande, although wearing the guise of a Dao Net operator, was still an ant.

Li Fan sat quietly in Ma Tiande's residence, contemplating escape strategies.

"For this grand ceremony, the Blade Island faction did not honor Scholar Zhu's request, sending no one. However, the Sword Domain sent three cultivators."

"The identities of these three are currently unknown, but as representatives of the top forces in the Shining Star Sea, their lives should not be as precarious as mine." Li Fan thought self-deprecatingly.

"Only the Sword Domain participating in the entire Shining Star Sea. Calling it a grand ceremony is essentially Scholar Zhu's self-entertainment. And we are his playthings."

In Ma Tiande's memories, there were scenes of past grand ceremonies. In Extremity Bliss City, beings who had indulged in pleasure for three years began indiscriminate slaughter. Only when the last few survivors remained would this slaughter cease. These survivors might rejoice in having escaped an endless purgatory, but they would never know they were merely tempting fruits for Scholar Zhu's consumption.

"All those invited to the grand ceremony can consume these fruits of slaughter."

"They are indeed extremely precious divine medicines. Even though my true body has reached the realm of divine manifestation of thought, I would still benefit greatly. But for the weak, it is undoubtedly a potent poison!"

Li Fan knew Scholar Zhu's intentions clearly. However, he did not harbor petty thoughts of ensuring Ma Tiande's demise. It was merely a reward of a treasure that could truly be called heavenly and earthly. Who could have known he wouldn't be able to handle it himself?

"With my current divine sense strength, which has been enhanced, consuming the fruits of slaughter should not be a problem."

"But the difficulty lies in how to safely consume the fruits without arousing the suspicion of Scholar Zhu and the Sword Domain cultivators attending the ceremony. After all, based on Ma Tiande's apparent strength, he should have no reason to survive the fruits of slaughter."

Although abandoning Ma Tiande's identity would not result in significant loss, Li Fan's divine sense was unwilling to disappear so ignominiously.

"Perhaps the opportunity lies within Extremity Bliss City's Dao Net."

"Ma Tiande" looked up at the invisible dark cloud covering Extremity Bliss City, a strange expression on his face.

Shortly after, three sword lights descended from the sky.

"Junior Ji Xingdao!"

"Junior Situ Tiantian!"

"Junior Zhao Xing!"

"Greetings, Scholar Zhu!"

Three clear voices echoed through the sky. two males and one female. While their voices still resonated in the air, these three had already flown into Extremity Bliss City.

The Lord's mansion appeared out of thin air, drawing the three from the Sword Domain in. At the same time, Li Fan's ear heard Scholar Zhu's somewhat coquettish voice, "Come quickly, let's entertain our guests."

Li Fan felt a chill run down his spine. Moreover, based on Ma Tiande's past habitual behavior, he did not disguise his reaction and displayed it directly on his face. Knowing this was Scholar Zhu's most twisted and unpredictable state, Li Fan cautiously hurried towards the Lord's mansion.

By the time he entered the mansion, the three from the Sword Domain were already seated. Li Fan glanced at them; the three disciples appeared very young, even "naive." Their eyes were clear and foolish, showing almost no guile. Clearly, the Sword Domain intended to use the fruits of slaughter refined by Extremity Bliss City to "temper" these three young ones.

"It's through such a hasty method, even if they can withstand it, they'll likely become somewhat mentally twisted and erratic."

"Three good seedlings, even in our Xuanhuang Realm, they could be considered prodigies. Is the Sword Domain wasting them like this?"

Li Fan remained impassive, first bowing to Scholar Zhu. Then, with an arrogant expression, he merely nodded slightly at the three from the Sword Domain. Theoretically, the status of a Dao Net operator from the Governing Council was no lower than that of the three from the Sword Domain. But in reality... Pawns could be replaced indefinitely, while direct disciples required painstaking cultivation. The two clearly were not on the same level.

The three disciples from the Sword Domain seemed to understand this too and did not show annoyance at Ma Tiande's attitude, merely smiling at each other nonchalantly. They first merrily drank the three bowls of red soup before them. Compared to what Li Fan had tasted before, it looked even more terrifying. It contained not only eyeballs but also remnants of various non-human monsters. However, the three from the Sword Domain looked at it as if it were nothing, savoring it with relish.

Chapter 1441

THE flow of time in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea was already inconsistent due to the existence of the Immortal Ruins. Therefore, Li Fan compared the Xuanhuang Realm with Extremity Bliss City in the Shining Star Sea. Under normal circumstances, it was a hundred and twenty times faster!

Li Fan felt a chill run down his spine. Moreover, based on Ma Tiande's past habitual behavior, he did not disguise his reaction and displayed it directly on his face. Knowing this was Scholar Zhu's most twisted and unpredictable state, Li Fan cautiously hurried towards the Lord's mansion.

By the time he entered the mansion, the three from the Sword Domain were already seated. Li Fan glanced at them; the three disciples appeared very young, even "naive." Their eyes were clear and foolish, showing almost no guile. Clearly, the Sword Domain intended to use the fruits of slaughter refined by Extremity Bliss City to "temper" these three young ones.

"It's through such a hasty method, even if they can withstand it, they'll likely become somewhat mentally twisted and erratic."

"Three good seedlings, even in our Xuanhuang Realm, they could be considered prodigies. Is the Sword Domain wasting them like this?"

Li Fan remained impassive, first bowing to Scholar Zhu. Then, with an arrogant expression, he merely nodded slightly at the three from the Sword Domain. Theoretically, the status of a Dao Net operator from the Governing Council was no lower than that of the three from the Sword Domain. But in reality... Pawns could be replaced indefinitely, while direct disciples required painstaking cultivation. The two clearly were not on the same level.

The three disciples from the Sword Domain seemed to understand this too and did not show annoyance at Ma Tiande's attitude, merely smiling at each other nonchalantly. They first merrily drank the three bowls of red soup before them. Compared to what Li Fan had tasted before, it looked even more terrifying. It contained not only eyeballs but also remnants of various non-human monsters. However, the three from the Sword Domain looked at it as if it were nothing, savoring it with relish.

Chapter 1441: Audience Desire Fruit

A bowl of red soup entered the stomach, and the expressions on the faces of the three from the Sword Domain began to change drastically.

Clearly, not everyone could enjoy the marvelous benefits of the desires of all beings like Li Fan could, and find it pleasant from the first taste.

Ji Xingdao's eyes widened, his aura fluctuating like waves.

Situ Tiantian's brows furrowed, her face as cold as frost. Countless ice crystals seemed to dance around her, and upon closer inspection, these white ice crystals were actually tiny flying swords!

Zhao Xing was the best among the three, only appearing as if he had drunk a bowl of extremely spicy wine. A strange look flashed across his face and he quickly recovered.

Regardless of how the three from the Sword Domain reacted, Scholar Zhu, still clad in his robe, slowly descended from his main seat.

His hunched body, hidden within the robe, emitted a strange creaking sound of growth and soon became slender.

A woman's singing voice, filled with sorrow and lament, echoed through the hall.

"The Rainbow Skirt and Feathered Coat Pleasure Palace, where the golden goblets and jade wine flow endlessly. The drums and music resound, the dances are graceful, and the lights are dim as the night goes on..."

Scholar Zhu sang and danced softly.

Li Fan stared intently at the graceful, unseen figure, his gaze unwavering.

As Scholar Zhu's singing continued, the gates of the City Lord's mansion seemed to suddenly swing open. The previously silent place was instantly plunged into a boiling cauldron. Ten thousand voices of the beings of Bliss City, coming from all directions, converged in the mansion.

Li Fan, in a daze, saw everything that was happening in Bliss City.

Laughter, indulgence, fighting, lust, joy, pleasure, drunkenness, delight.

Scenes of countless beings reveling in pleasure exploded before Li Fan's eyes simultaneously.

"Bliss City, ultimate bliss."

However, all of this abruptly changed with Scholar Zhu's tone.

"Joy turns to sorrow, as heaven and earth witness; swords flash and blood flows like a river. Ghosts and spirits emerge in the dark night, heads become rammed earth, and bones form the beams..."

His voice grew chilling, filled with murderous intent.

"Ding!" A sound like a sword falling to the ground startled the endless beings in Bliss City, waking them from their dream of pleasure.

The bright lights extinguished, and Bliss City was suddenly plunged into darkness.

However, the darkness did not last long.

A blood-red sun slowly rose from the horizon. Its crimson light cast into the city.

The slaughter had begun.

During the long night of pleasure, those who were once intimate lovers by their side, now suddenly drew their blades against each other, fighting to the death.

All friendship, kinship, and love...

Lost all meaning in the long night that followed.

Only survival was the sole and eternal topic.

...

"Die, die, die, die!"

"Kill!"

"Ah!"

The sounds of screams and frenzied slaughter played out like a grand symphony in the City Lord's mansion.

Scholar Zhu had transformed from a dancer back into a hunched old man. He watched the slaughter in the city with great enjoyment.

And the three young cultivators from the Sword Domain, who had gradually regained consciousness from the hallucination induced by the red soup, began to tremble and their faces turned pale as they faced the terrifying scenes of human evil unfolding in Bliss City.

Li Fan also feigned an appearance of extreme discomfort.

"What a pity, such a scene should have been enjoyed by more people."

"Only a few juniors like you have come."

Scholar Zhu's voice sounded lonely, tinged with melancholy.

But the slaughter in Bliss City did not stop because of this.

"It also must not seem boring, lest it disgrace me."

Scholar Zhu's demonic voice echoed in everyone's ears.

In Bliss City, another variable manifested.

Those beings who had already died were miraculously reborn, though not in a living state, but as incorporeal ghosts.

At this moment, they had two choices. One was to directly take revenge on their enemies as ghosts, which would cause their own spectral form to vanish.

The second was to possess the survivors and use them to exact their revenge. The possessed would have the combined strength of two, greatly increasing the chances of success.

However, the one who was killed would also transform into a spectral form.

Under the spectral form, they could attack each other, but the outcome would only be mutual destruction. Thus, they would likely seek other survivors for possession.

As the fighting continued, only survivors possessed by ghosts gradually remained in Bliss City.

If a ghost-possessed survivor was defeated, no new ghost would be born, and the possessing ghost would vanish along with them.

The battle was gradually approaching its climax.

When only one hundred survivors remained, the possessed could detect the presence of the possessing ghost.

They could choose coexistence or initiate a never-ending mental attack.

The victor over the ghost would absorb all of its power, making it their own.

"What do you think, will more ghosts or humans survive in the end?"

Scholar Zhu suddenly asked the people present.

"For this grand ceremony, ten winners will ultimately emerge. You four will each receive a fruit. If you guess correctly, I will give you an extra reward."

The three from the Sword Domain were overjoyed at this. The fear and reluctance they had felt witnessing the slaughter in Bliss City were instantly cast aside.

"I guess more ghosts will survive," Situ Tiantian said loudly, full of confidence.

The other two from the Sword Domain also made their judgments.

Some guessed ghosts, some guessed humans.

When it was Li Fan's turn, he pondered for a moment and replied earnestly, "Among the ten winners, I think there will be an equal number of humans and ghosts."

The three from the Sword Domain looked surprised.

Scholar Zhu glanced at Li Fan meaningfully but did not reply.

As the sun reached its zenith, the slaughter in Bliss City continued.

Those who survived the initial massacre had already gained some survival experience. Lurking, hiding, and striking secretly, they gradually slowed the pace of the slaughter.

However, as Bliss City continued to shrink, they were forced to concentrate, and the pace of the game sped up again.

Repetitive viewing led to aesthetic fatigue. After seeing too much, even the most gruesome and bizarre scenes felt ordinary.

The three from the Sword Domain had already become numb. No unusual expressions appeared on their faces, and they even began to feel impatient.

Only Li Fan continued to diligently observe every being in Bliss City, their different behaviors and choices when facing life and death.

The promised three-year cycle of Bliss City.

This battle truly lasted for three full years.

It seemed as if a mysterious power from behind the scenes was manipulating the progress of this game.

Over the three years, the three from the Sword Domain had drunk bowl after bowl of red soup. Now, it was like drinking plain water, leaving them with no sensation.

Li Fan's treatment was not as good.

He was only rewarded with six bowls in the first year. After that, Scholar Zhu deliberately ignored him.

Li Fan knew that Scholar Zhu was gradually increasing the endurance of the three from the Sword Domain to prevent them from being unable to bear it when they finally consumed the fruits, and be driven insane by the infinite killing intent contained within the fruits.

After all, they were from the Sword Domain, and Scholar Zhu had to show them some respect.

As for "Ma Tiande"...

His fate was purely in the hands of heaven.

The three-year period had arrived. The blood-red sun finally disappeared below the horizon.

Bliss City, with only a small area remaining, was once again plunged into darkness.

At this moment, it was as if time had frozen. All the survivors were motionless, as if encased in ice.

Light and shadow contracted and flew directly into the City Lord's mansion.

The survivors, glowing with luminescence, flew out from the phantom of Bliss City.

Ghosts and humans separated.

"Five ghosts, five people? You guessed it, you brat!" Situ Tiantian said to Li Fan with some shock.

The three from the Sword Domain were dejected that their additional servings were gone, but Li Fan knew that Scholar Zhu was saving their lives.

With the strength of these young people, swallowing one fruit might be barely manageable. But swallowing two would leave them no chance of survival.

"It seems this Scholar Zhu is truly petty."

Li Fan sneered inwardly.

From the fact that the slaughter in Bliss City's duration could be precisely controlled, one could tell.

The entire process was merely going through the motions.

The final outcome was entirely at Scholar Zhu's whim.

Because Li Fan guessed that the final outcome would be an equal number of humans and ghosts.

Therefore, the final survivors would inevitably be in equal numbers of humans and ghosts.

"Not bad. These two fruits will be yours!"

The survivors, emitting a soft white glow, curled up like being in the womb, forming fruit-like shapes.

Scholar Zhu selected the two most robust ones and personally handed them to Li Fan.

Li Fan bowed in thanks.

The three from the Sword Domain looked displeased but did not dare to act presumptuously. They could only unconventionally swallow their respective fruits, filled with dissatisfaction.

Li Fan sensed that Scholar Zhu's gaze was always focused on him.

He also followed suit and swallowed one fruit first.

There was no taste of it. The fruits of sentient beings melted upon entering the mouth.

The superposition of countless thoughts, memories, and emotions then exploded in Li Fan's mind.

As if a terrible storm capable of destroying everything suddenly arose from nothingness.

Li Fan's original thoughts were swept away by this gale, his body unable to resist, precariously endangered.

"This is what is meant by: 'The thoughts of all beings can refine gods'."

"If it were my divine sense, which has reincarnated a hundred times and reflected the Great Dao, even the strongest storm could not shake me. But Ma Tiande... does not have such an ability..."

"If one does not use the Dao Net."

Hiding within the storm of sentient thoughts, Li Fan gloated inwardly as he observed Scholar Zhu.

He had already planned his countermeasure.

"Within the Dao Net, there are nodes of Nameless True Immortals."

"From one of those nodes, I faintly sensed an aura extremely similar to Scholar Zhu's..."

Li Fan's thoughts raced.

And in reality, Ma Tiande was already weeping, his face contorted.

His face could simultaneously display several different expressions. His limbs flailed uncontrollably, as if a drowning person searching for any possible lifesaver.

Scholar Zhu gazed with enjoyment at Ma Tiande, who was struggling.

However, his peripheral vision could not help but turn towards the heavens.

When a Dao Net operator dies, a signal is generated and transmitted through the Dao Net to the Governing Council.

Within the Shining Star Sea, there are surviving forces from various cultivation realms, and even other star seas. There are also former True Immortals. Various devious and hidden methods are endless. Only the Dao Net can ignore all of them and transmit the status of the Dao Net operator to the Governing Council in real-time.

This is a means by which the Shining Star Sea maintains its stability.

However, it became the phenomenon that Scholar Zhu had anticipated and awaited.

This was also the true reason why he had always wanted "Ma Tiande" to die.

However, what Scholar Zhu had envisioned did not occur.

The Dao Net operator, who had fallen into a desperate struggle, seemed to have truly found something to grasp.

Even with his face contorted, Scholar Zhu could see that his inner divine sense had not dissipated.

"Hm?"

This sparked Scholar Zhu's interest.

"This is..."

Squinting, Scholar Zhu's expression suddenly changed.

He saw, within the consciousness sea.

Ma Tiande, facing the threat of death and on the verge of perishing, instinctively wrote a large number of meaningless Yuan Dao symbols.

These Yuan Dao symbols could not form Dao Net commands, and thus did not trigger any anomaly in the Dao Net.

However, they inexplicably formed a long dike, blocking the storm formed by the Fruit of Sentient Thoughts from the outside.

"By chance, without a formal Dao Net connection, he also managed to invoke the power of the Dao Net?"

Scholar Zhu had a deep understanding of the Dao Net.

He could already see the fundamental reason why Ma Tiande could survive.

The Dao Net was already a tangible entity.

Although it was under the manipulation of some individuals, the controller of the Dao Net could only regulate the behaviors and commands of the Dao Net.

But they could not control all the instinctive reactions of the Dao Net itself.

After all, the Dao Net imitated all the Great Daos of heaven and earth.

"The Yuan Dao command activated the Dao Net."

"Theoretically, it should have triggered an anomaly in the Dao Net. However, the anomaly was intercepted by the Governing Council."

"Among infinite combinations, he happened to form such a life-saving one."

"Is it a coincidence?"

Scholar Zhu remained silent.

He did not intervene, allowing Li Fan to swallow and digest the first Fruit of Sentient Thoughts.

The storm of thoughts gradually subsided.

Li Fan emerged from his confusion and pain.

Before he could even savor the effects of consuming the fruit, Scholar Zhu said coldly, "Continue. There's still one more."

Li Fan was slightly stunned, seemingly unable to comprehend the reason for Scholar Zhu's indifference.

However, he gritted his teeth and swallowed the second fruit.

In his consciousness sea, the storm raged again.

This time, it seemed even more violent than the last.

It once again engulfed Li Fan's consciousness.

"Let's see if you can get lucky a second time!"

This time, Scholar Zhu focused on Ma Tiande's consciousness sea from the very beginning.

As expected, after struggling fruitlessly and gradually losing consciousness, Ma Tiande's dying instinctual actions once again summoned countless Yuan Dao symbols.

The command formed this time was different from the previous one.

"It seems luck will not strike twice," Scholar Zhu said with some satisfaction.

Waiting for the storm of sentient thoughts to completely devour Ma Tiande.

But soon, his expression became somewhat strange.

This time, the Yuan Dao symbols did not form a dike.

Instead, they transformed into another storm.

The two storms canceled each other out.

Thus, Ma Tiande remained unharmed!

Chapter 1442: Immortal Skin Covers New Life

Once, extreme survival could be attributed to a fluke.

But a second time doing so...

At this moment, countless thoughts flashed through Scholar Zhu's mind. He even considered feeding the third Fruit of Sentient Thoughts to "Ma Tiande."

However, Scholar Zhu ultimately did not act. He merely recalled the two Yuan Dao commands that appeared in Ma Tiande's consciousness sea.

Clearly, among the numerous flying Yuan Dao symbols, only a small portion was effective, making it impossible for an observer to accurately replicate them.

Scholar Zhu was not interested in the Yuan Dao commands themselves. Even though he had transformed from an Immortal to a mortal, the methods he could employ were by no means comparable to these two commands.

What Scholar Zhu truly cared about was the "possibility" represented by Ma Tiande's performance.

The "hidden commands" that could still invoke the power of the Dao Net, existing outside the current control system of the Dao Net.

The gloom on his face gradually receded. From a hunched old man, he instantly transformed into an energetic scholar.

Scholar Zhu's expression turned benevolent as he waited for the four people present to recover from consuming the Fruits of Sentient Thoughts.

With Scholar Zhu's special care, although the three from the Sword Domain suffered some torment, they ultimately emerged unharmed. The childishness on their faces had long since faded after absorbing the memories of countless beings and personally experiencing boundless slaughter.

They first expressed their gratitude to Scholar Zhu, and then they all turned to look at Ma Tiande, who was sitting on the other side. There was no longer any contempt.

No one who had personally experienced the storm of sentient thoughts would understand the horror of it better than they.

Regardless of their origin or the methods they used, as long as they could swallow a fruit and remain unharmed, they were absolutely not to be underestimated.

If one could swallow two fruits and still maintain their sanity...

"A sight not to be missed!"

The three from the Sword Domain had already reached a consensus through their exchanged glances. If they could bring such talent back to the Sword Domain, the merit would even surpass that of completing this trial.

Now, it all depended on whether this "Ma Tiande" could truly maintain his sanity and not fall into madness.

Under the watchful eyes of everyone present, the contorted and twitching expression on Li Fan's face slowly calmed down. After closing his eyes for a long time, he suddenly opened them and met the gazes of everyone present.

His eyes, bright like stars, spoke of his current state.

Scholar Zhu lightly applauded, seemingly overjoyed, "It seems you have gained quite a lot this time!"

"I must also thank Scholar Zhu for your fulfillment," Li Fan said neither subserviently nor obsequiously.

After swallowing two Fruits of Sentient Thoughts, his words and actions no longer needed to follow Ma Tiande's past habits. All changes could be attributed to the countless sentient thoughts contained within the fruits.

"Senior Brother Ma, I wonder if you're interested in coming to our Sword Domain? I, Situ Tiantian, guarantee that you will receive the highest tier of cultivation resources. If you agree, we don't even need to apply to the Governing Council. You can return to the Sword Domain with us directly, and we'll handle the paperwork once we get there..." Situ Tiantian glanced at Scholar Zhu, showing only a momentary hesitation. But she quickly made up her mind and directly extended the invitation to Li Fan in front of Scholar Zhu.

Ji Xingdao and Zhao Xing also echoed Situ Tiantian's invitation with playful banter, further promising various wonderful conditions.

"Although I have long heard of the Sword Domain's great name, my ambition lies not in the way of the sword."

Before Scholar Zhu could react, Li Fan directly declined.

"Don't be in such a hurry to refuse, consider it further..." Scholar Zhu smiled faintly.

"My lifelong ambition lies only in [Immortal Hunting]! Previously, due to my weak strength, it was impossible to realize. Thus, I kept it deep in my heart and never mentioned it to anyone. But today, thanks to Scholar Zhu's grace, after swallowing two fruits, my destiny has been reversed, and anything is possible in the future!" Li Fan spoke with great solemnity, his voice like thunder.

Scholar Zhu's smile froze upon hearing this.

The three from the Sword Domain were also full of surprise.

"Immortal Hunting..."

The significance of this term in the current Shining Star Sea was immense.

Immortal Hunting was directly under the Shining Star Sea Governing Council, and its members were selected from various forces in the star sea. Once a cultivator joined Immortal Hunting, regardless of their past identity or status in their original faction, they had to cast it aside.

Everything was secondary to "Immortal Hunting."

The price paid was supreme authority.

In the name of Immortal Hunting, they could not only enter and exit major forces in the Shining Star Sea at will but also directly carry out punishments and executions in special circumstances. More importantly, by becoming a member of Immortal Hunting, one could get closer to the Dao Net.

Living with the Dao Net day and night, their progress would be rapid.

As soon as Li Fan uttered these words, the scene fell into an eerie silence.

Scholar Zhu's face darkened as he scrutinized Li Fan, contemplating something.

Situ Tiantian, breaking the awkward silence, managed a difficult smile, "Members of Immortal Hunting are all carefully selected. Although Senior Brother Ma is extraordinary, it is not easy to join."

Li Fan was unfazed, exuding confidence, "My entry into Immortal Hunting is certain! If I remember correctly, the next recruitment is in five years. At that time, I ask Scholar Zhu to recommend me."

"I will certainly not disappoint Scholar Zhu!"

Seeing Li Fan's determination, the three from the Sword Domain stopped trying to persuade him.

After some pleasantries at the banquet and drinking a few more bowls of red soup, they took their leave. Before departing, they maintained the demeanor of the Sword Domain, stating that the Sword Domain would reciprocate their hospitality soon.

Only Li Fan and Scholar Zhu remained in the City Lord's mansion.

Outside the mansion, the revelry of Bliss City resumed its noise. The two said nothing, silently watching the bustling night outside.

"Creak, creak..."

A terrifying chewing sound came from Scholar Zhu's mouth. He had swallowed the remaining five Fruits of Sentient Thoughts in one go.

Unlike Li Fan and the others, whose fruits melted upon entering the mouth,

The five fruits in Scholar Zhu's mouth emitted the desperate screams of countless beings facing death.

The sounds from purgatory rose to the heavens, even momentarily overpowering the sounds of revelry in Bliss City.

Scholar Zhu, like an old man on the verge of death, chewed slowly. Listening to the continuous, fluctuating cries, he showed an expression of enjoyment.

Li Fan did not even frown, his expression perfectly calm, silently watching.

After a while, Scholar Zhu also grew bored. He swallowed the fruits in just a few bites.

The sounds of despair and wailing abruptly ceased.

"Do you know why I built Bliss City in the Shining Star Sea?"

"Simply to torment?"

"These Fruits of Sentient Thoughts may have the effect of reversing fate for you. But for me, they are tasteless."

"I have experienced all sorts of things, despair, cruelty, far surpassing those in Bliss City by a hundredfold."

Scholar Zhu cackled, his appearance shifting from a scholar to a hunched old man without notice.

"The net of the Great Dao envelops heaven and earth. All things in the world are within it. Although mortal beings are weak, the condensed thoughts of countless beings can perhaps resonate with a certain Great Dao in the unseen depths." Li Fan replied after pondering for a moment.

"Hehehe..." Scholar Zhu let out another sinister laugh.

"You are mistaken."

"The main purpose of creating Bliss City is to torment these ants when I am bored."

Li Fan was slightly taken aback by this.

"Of course, if any unexpected delights are born in the process, that would be even better."

"However, if not, there is no need to force it."

Scholar Zhu's skull-like head slowly emerged from his wide robe, looking towards Bliss City outside the mansion. His expression was dazed, as if lost in memory.

"In the past Immortal Realm, bliss was even greater than in this city. It was a scene of prosperity, with infinite possibilities for the future. Who would have thought that one day, the grand palace would collapse..." Scholar Zhu mumbled in a daze.

Li Fan remained silent. Scholar Zhu then turned the topic back, "You said you wanted me to recommend you for Immortal Hunting?"

"I request Scholar Zhu's fulfillment," Li Fan nodded.

"Certainly. However, I have a condition," Scholar Zhu agreed very readily.

"No problem," Li Fan replied even more readily, without even asking what the condition was.

Scholar Zhu burst into laughter, his external form changing again.

The hunched old man within melted into a pool of blood and merged into his robe.

The robe writhed, transforming into a human skin!

It floated before Li Fan and said sternly, "One day, no matter what method you use, bring my physical body back for me!"

The human skin had no facial features.

Only five sinister holes stared silently at Li Fan.

Li Fan remained silent for a moment, then nodded in agreement.

"Good."

As if having fulfilled a wish, the human skin lost its buoyancy and fell to the ground.

Then, it writhed again, crawling like a person on the ground, eventually returning to the main seat.

It transformed back into a robe.

Scholar Zhu's aged voice came from within, "To help me achieve liberation, to my knowledge, there are several methods."

"First, successfully capture a Nameless True Immortal and exchange bodies."

"Second..."

Li Fan felt Scholar Zhu's gaze sweeping over his face.

"Completely tear apart the Dao Net. Then I can regain my freedom."

"Third, reflect on the unknown regions of the Great Dao and redeem myself with merit."

"..."

Scholar Zhu paused, then asked, "May I know which method you intend to use?"

Li Fan carefully considered his words, and after a while, he said in a low voice, "Perhaps all three."

Scholar Zhu remained silent.

After a long pause, he finally said, "Whatever you need, just tell me."

"Five years is the deadline. Before the Immortal Hunting assessment, I will first test your mettle."

"If you disappoint me..."

"Hehehe..."

Scholar Zhu's calm tone was filled with boundless killing intent.

Li Fan, however, remained impassive, "Scholar Zhu, please wait and see."

...

After the grand ceremony concluded, Li Fan returned to Ma Tiande's residence.

He brought with him a gift from Scholar Zhu.

"This is..."

Li Fan examined the item in his hand with great interest.

A piece of skin, extremely similar to Scholar Zhu's "human skin" state.

It looked as if it had just been peeled off a body. Li Fan could still smell the strong scent of blood. Having a good understanding of human anatomy, Li Fan unfolded the skin and examined it thoroughly.

He confirmed that it was indeed a human skin.

However, unlike Scholar Zhu, it did not possess its own consciousness.

After careful study, Li Fan tried various methods but could not elicit any special properties from this piece of skin. It seemed to be just ordinary human skin.

But when Scholar Zhu handed this piece of skin to Li Fan before, Li Fan clearly saw a complex emotion in his eyes.

There was nostalgia, reluctance, and also hatred.

After examining the skin back and forth again, Li Fan recalled the scene when Scholar Zhu revealed his true form.

After a moment of contemplation, he made up his mind.

He sat upright, took a deep breath, and then put on the human skin like a piece of clothing.

It did not initially fit his body size or shape, as it was not compatible with "Ma Tiande."

But under Li Fan's arrangement, the human skin automatically contracted, becoming incredibly form-fitting, as if this skin had been peeled from Ma Tiande's own body!

Feeling the constricting force surrounding him and the changes in his physique and features,

Li Fan suddenly had a premonition.

He seemed to be transforming into someone else.

An irresistible sense of fear of the unknown arose in his heart, but sensing the miniature Dao Net reflected in his divine sense, Li Fan's fear subsided.

His mind was calm, and he simply experienced the changes brought about by wearing this skin.

Once the outer skin perfectly conformed to his body,

Li Fan seemed to truly become someone else.

Vast amounts of scenes and memories surged into his mind inexplicably.

Even...

Li Fan looked at his hands.

"This realm..."

"The True Immortal realm?"

It was not merely an illusion.

Li Fan pointed his fingertip forward.

A radiant light, like the birth of a starry sea, bloomed at his fingertip.

The light seemed to contain the infinity of the world.

"Immortal Spiritual Energy."

"This is... Immortal Spiritual Energy?"

Li Fan had experienced the existence of Immortal Spiritual Energy in the Immortal Separation Disc before.

Now, this strange and magnificent power surged within his body, and he immediately recognized its essence.

Li Fan's gaze was fixed on the point at his fingertip, not daring to look away.

In a trance, he seemed to have passed through this point and arrived in a boundless ocean.

In this ocean, all things and beings, all life and spirits, were presented together.

It was indescribably strange.

Even with Li Fan's knowledge, accumulated over hundreds of reincarnations in the Xuanhuang Realm and having explored almost all its secrets, he could not find anything in his experiences that could rival its taste.

After drinking the bowl of red soup, Li Fan felt a sense of reluctance as he looked at the empty bowl.

"What, do you want another bowl?" Scholar Zhu also noticed the change in Li Fan's emotions and became excited, as if he had found a confidant.

With great willpower, Li Fan shook his head and refused.

"Such rare delicacies must be savored properly."

"Better less than more," he said earnestly.

Scholar Zhu heard this and let out a muffled laugh. His voice, shifting from child-like, quietly returned to that of an old man.

"What you say has some ground."

"In that case, you may leave now."

Li Fan bowed and took his leave. Just as he was about to exit the mansion, Scholar Zhu's voice, light as a feather, drifted into his ear.

"For this grand ceremony of day and night, I have also prepared a seat for you."

Li Fan's expression brightened, and he quickly bowed again, "Many thanks, Lord Zhu!"

The scene flickered, and the Lord's mansion disappeared. A red building, filled with lewd sounds, took its place. Li Fan licked his lips. Ma Tiande's memory data surfaced again: "Scholar Zhu, a member of the Shining Star Sea's Governing Council." "He was once a True Immortal, who then degenerated into a mortal!"

Chapter 1443: Infinite Immortal Power

INSIDE the faint light, it contained an infinite ocean of all possibilities in the world. But at this moment, the Immortal Spiritual Energy light at Li Fan's fingertip was as fragile as a candle in the wind. It flickered, uncertain, and trembled incessantly.

To Li Fan's shock, after ninety-nine breaths, the Immortal Spiritual Energy light constructing the fingertip suddenly extinguished without warning, as if an unknown invisible entity had aimed at it and gently blown it out.

"Only the external manifestation of the Immortal Spiritual Energy has inexplicably disappeared. This body... or rather, the skin, still possesses Immortal Spiritual Energy," Li Fan concluded after sensing his internal state.

He tried again. This time, Li Fan was no longer satisfied with merely using Immortal Spiritual Energy to form a single point. Instead, he attempted to construct an Immortal Formation using Immortal Spiritual Energy. Of course, to prevent detection by those in the Shining Star Sea, Li Fan did not intend to create too much of a disturbance. He only meant to probe and decipher the formation "[Boundless, Primordial Square]," which could observe and analyze everything. The formation was no different from the one deployed by the Immortal Dissolution Disc, and Li Fan even felt a stronger sense of effortless control. There was no need for the Dissolution Disc to perform a conversion; all information encountered and analyzed by the Primordial Square formation appeared directly in Li Fan's mind, as if he had deduced it himself.

Li Fan looked towards the city outside the mansion. What his eyes saw now was not the bustling Extremity Bliss City, but merely a giant, rapidly spinning vortex. Countless specks of thoughts floated, spun, and settled within this vortex. Occasionally, a few emitted a distinct blue light during their rotation, and then, ignoring the vortex's own power, they slowly sank to the very bottom from the upper edge. Li Fan vaguely saw a huge shadow, like a predator, lurking there. As the blue dots from above approached, it suddenly turned its head towards Li Fan. The shadow rippled, seemingly emitting a meaningful smile.

While maintaining the operation of the Primordial Square formation, Li Fan also kept track of time in his heart. As expected, upon reaching ninety-nine breaths, the Immortal Formation constructed by Immortal Spiritual Energy vanished like melting snow, disappearing in an instant. The pathway connecting Li Fan to the Immortal Formation within his body also seemed to be blocked, preventing further support. He could only watch the Immortal Formation dissipate. The vortex scene Li Fan observed also vanished with it.

"That feeding shadow..."

"It must be Scholar Zhu."

"It seems that selecting suitable targets among the collective thoughts is happening simultaneously within the operation of Extremity Bliss City."

"The Extremity Bliss Grand Ceremony, held every three years, and those fruits of thought are more of a guise," Li Fan faintly understood in his heart.

Although he had reached a certain cooperative agreement with this former Nameless True Immortal, there was no trust between them. Scholar Zhu was merely making a desperate investment after Li Fan had shown some potential. He did not care about Li Fan's identity or background, nor how he had quietly infiltrated Extremity Bliss City and replaced Ma Tiande. He also did not care about Li Fan's goals. As long as Li Fan could help him escape the Dao Net, Scholar Zhu was willing to provide support.

"In fact, he probably doesn't truly expect me to help him escape. As long as I can infiltrate Immortal Hunting and cause some trouble or variable for the Governing Council and the Dao Net, increasing his chances of escape, this deal is worthwhile..."

As Li Fan was contemplating, a feeling of rejection suddenly arose from within this body.

"Get out! Get out of here!"

"Scram, scram, scram, scram!"

"Ant! How dare you desecrate!"

...

The feeling of rejection grew stronger, and the voices echoing in Li Fan's ears became louder, like roaring thunder, making it unbearable. And it was Li Fan's own voice. Yelling at himself made it even more peculiar.

Finally, Li Fan was forced to detach himself from that Immortal Skin. Returning to his original body, Li Fan carefully examined the treasured item in his hand. Being able to grant a mortal the power comparable to a True Immortal in an instant, calling this layer of human skin a treasure was no exaggeration.

"Based on the scenes that appeared in my mind after putting on the Immortal Skin, the original owner of this skin should have been close to the Nameless realm in cultivation."

"However, before he could merge with the Great Dao, the Dao Annihilation Tribulation, which destroys all things, had already descended."
