"The Immortal Realm was shattered, and True Immortals, even Nameless True Immortals, all died in the tribulation. The manifestations and dissolutions of the Dao, the scenes of the creation of heaven and earth coexisting with the end times, caused this person to suddenly have an epiphany. He directly took the final step!"

"It's just a pity that his breakthrough was at the most inopportune time. Originally, that Immortal Region could have held on for a while longer. His transcendence was akin to directly pulling out a crucial supporting pillar at the most critical moment..."

...

The subsequent memories became blurred and even somewhat delirious. Memories from different periods, even contradictory ones, appeared simultaneously. Li Fan could only vaguely deduce that this Nameless True Immortal, although he escaped the tribulation at that time, was eventually captured by someone and pinned into the Dao Net, serving as a key node connecting to the Great Dao.

"Unlike Scholar Zhu."

"This Nameless one has truly perished."

"And the day of his death was the time the Dao Net was constructed."

"The Great Dao he had merged with did not have time to return to heaven and earth; instead, it was captured and utilized by some mysterious power, existing as the most stable nodes of the Dao Net..."

Li Fan tried to reconstruct the scene from the fragmented memories. The opening of the Dao Net, what a magnificent event it was. However, it was accompanied by the curses of the Nameless True Immortal filled with resentment.

"Nameless True Immortals like the owner of this Immortal Skin, who were sacrificed to construct the Dao Net..."

"There are three more!"

"A total of four major nodes, plus that invisible giant hand, are what initially stabilized the Dao Net."

Li Fan took a deep breath. Even after death, a residual layer of skin could instantly grant mortals the power comparable to a True Immortal. Moreover, the Immortal Skin contained residual thoughts and memories, enough to demonstrate the power of its owner. Yet, such a powerful being cruelly became the raw material for the Dao Net's living stakes, with even their names and life stories not being left behind after death.

"Nameless ants die."

"In the face of the great tribulation, those who cannot hold the dominant position are essentially no different from mortals." Li Fan sighed inwardly.

After one round of possession, the Immortal Skin clearly became thinner, and also showed a strange pale color. This was also the reason why it forcefully expelled Li Fan. But after Li Fan studied it, he discovered that the Immortal Skin had not been consumed; it regained its rosy and full appearance at a speed visible to the naked eye. However, Li Fan was still unable to put it on again. Only after waiting for a full incense stick of time did Li Fan sense that he could use this Immortal Skin again.

"It's not due to the nature of the Immortal Skin itself."

"It's a restriction imposed by other existences. Unless my strength surpasses theirs, I must follow this rule." Li Fan seemed to have an epiphany.

"It must be the constraints set by those experts who built the Dao Net in the Shining Star Sea back then. After all, a Nameless True Immortal's skin that can instantly grant any living being power comparable to a True Immortal is definitely a powerful weapon."

Li Fan put on the Immortal Skin again. This time, he wanted to verify if he could increase the effective duration of wearing the Immortal Skin according to his own adaptability. Immortal Spiritual Energy enveloped him again, and Li Fan's consciousness dived into it, as if he were seeing the infinite ocean once more.

"They say the Immortal Realm is vast and boundless."

"This place is a thousand times, even ten thousand times vaster than the Immortal Realm."

Even seeing it for the second time, Li Fan still felt a trace of lostness.

"Immortal Spiritual Energy originates from here. No wonder it possesses the nature of [Infinity]." Wandering, Li Fan thought of the Star Sea again. Although the power of the Star Sea was inferior to Immortal Spiritual Energy in terms of energy level, it also possessed the nature of [Infinity].

"Does this mean that the energy source of the Star Sea also originates from here?" Li Fan suddenly thought of a crucial question. Did the infinite nature of the Star Sea exist since ancient times, or did it arise after the destruction of the Immortal Realm? Li Fan scanned the infinite ocean, lost in thought for a long time. Recalling the appearance of the Immortal Realm he had seen in the memories of True Immortals, Li Fan had a vague guess for the answer.

"Perhaps [Infinity] was originally a characteristic of the Immortal Realm."

"However, due to the destruction of the Immortal Realm, this characteristic then spread to the lower Star Seas."

"Scholar Zhu once said that the bliss of the Immortal Realm was even greater than that of Extremity Bliss City. I guess it's all thanks to this infinite aspect. There's no need to worry about energy consumption anymore; only pure pleasure remains. If not for the sudden descent of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation, the Immortal Realm could have continued to be 'blissful' forever."

Since achieving Nascent Soul with the Five Elements Great Cave Heaven, Li Fan had deeply understood the various benefits of not having to worry about consumption. The Five Elements Cave Heaven was a projection of the Xuanhuang Realm. Although it far surpassed ordinary cultivators, it was clearly incomparable to the nature of [Infinity].

"This is also the most crucial aspect of the difference between Immortals and mortals."

"A continuous supply of energy, no longer considering consumption. Any magical abilities or divine powers can be infinitely amplified in their destructive power..." Even an ordinary punch from a mortal, if repeatedly swung upon the Xuanhuang Great Earth, would cause no harm to the world. However, if the action were repeated enough times, even a mortal could pound the Xuanhuang Realm to dust.

"Ultimately, even the weakest power, when multiplied by infinity, will possess unimaginable power." Li Fan's thoughts were interrupted by the disappearance of Immortal Spiritual Energy. The difference between Immortal and mortal power caused a faint sense of loss to arise in Li Fan's heart.

While waiting for the restriction to disappear, Li Fan suddenly thought of another question.

"Infinity is indeed wonderful. But, what is the price?" The existence of infinite power was somewhat contrary to Li Fan's original understanding. He could understand the power of Immortal Spiritual Energy, but the infinity of Immortal Spiritual Energy was something he could not fathom no matter what.

"What exactly is that infinite ocean?"

"A beautiful thing that seems to exist only in fantasy..."

"Are there really no negative side effects?" The naturally arising concern disappeared as he re-established contact with the infinite Immortal Spiritual Energy. Nothing was worse than knowing the exact end of the mortal world. Li Fan dismissed all other distractions and immersed himself in the study of the Immortal Skin and Immortal Spiritual Energy.

Time passed quickly. This time, the duration of wearing the Immortal Skin was exactly the same as the first time. Though Li Fan did not draw immediate conclusions. After the cooldown period passed, he continued to wear the Immortal Skin. This process repeated. Three years passed in the blink of an eye. Li Fan finally confirmed that the duration of wearing the Immortal Skin each time was fixed and would not increase with "proficiency." However, Li Fan had not been without gains during these three years of research.

The Immortal Spiritual Energy at his fingertip lit up again, like a flame. This time, Li Fan looked at the Immortal Spiritual Energy within "himself" and felt a strange sense of familiarity. It was as if it were a part of his own body. Here, "his own body" did not refer to the Immortal Skin or Ma Tiande, but to the core that directed all thoughts and actions, the divine sense that reflected the Great Dao.

"The reason I am stagnant at the Half-Immortal stage is because the Immortal Realm was destroyed, and I could not receive the infusion of Immortal Spiritual Energy."

"And the remaining Immortal Spiritual Energy in the world seems to have specific identification markers, making it impossible to usurp."

"Only by going through the process of ascension from the Xuanhuang Realm can this marker be washed away to a certain extent. The infinite Immortal Spiritual Energy of the Immortal Dissolution Disc is derived this way."

"But the Immortal Artifact's function cannot be applied to True Immortals."

With a thought from Li Fan, the Immortal Spiritual Energy surged like a tide throughout his body. It seemed to form a miniature infinite ocean. And the owner of this ocean was once a Nameless True Immortal who had turned into a living stake for the Dao Net, completely unknown. But now... this miniature infinite ocean was gradually beginning to bear Li Fan's mark.

"It's still far from a complete takeover."

"It's just that a bit of my mark has been added."

"But I have only been in contact and familiarized myself for three years. If you give me more time..." Li Fan's eyes flashed. The Immortal Spiritual Energy covering his body instantly vanished due to the Immortal Skin's restriction.

"Could it be that Immortal Spiritual Energy can also be inherited?" Immortal Spiritual Energy originated from the unknowable infinite ocean. And that infinite ocean was not something that an individual could contact and utilize. Not even True Immortals could.

"The Ascension Platform in the past, the process of infusing Immortal Energy, should be the key to allowing an individual to connect to the infinite ocean."

"If every True Immortal needs a unique identifier to wield infinite power, then by mastering these unique identifiers, perhaps one could control Immortal Spiritual Energy." Li Fan suddenly noticed that the infinite ocean and the Dao Net, in a certain sense, were somewhat similar. Just like the miniature infinite ocean appearing on Li Fan, it was similar to the miniature Dao Net reflected in his divine sense.

Chapter 1444: Connecting to the Infinite Sea

"The Great Dao of Heaven and Earth, projected by a single thought. However, a projection is merely a projection. To wield the power of the Great Dao at will in reality is not easy."

"Accessing the Infinite Ocean, with its endless energy supply, makes it possible."

The Dao projection provides a theoretical foundation, while the Infinite Ocean provides practical support.

"Achieving either one can lead to extraordinary strength far beyond the ordinary. If both are combined..."

Wearing the True Immortal's skin, with his divine sense projecting the Great Dao, Li Fan looked at Bliss City and felt as if he could turn it into dust with a wave of his hand.

It was not an illusion.

"I have a premonition that my current development of the infinite nature of Immortal Spiritual Energy is still too superficial."

"The Infinite Ocean is an existence comparable to the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth..."

Li Fan squinted his eyes, summoned Immortal Spiritual Energy from his fingertip again, and immersed his consciousness in that wondrous, infinite ocean.

Unfortunately, the fragmented memory snippets contained within the Immortal Skin were mostly from the experiences of its former owner, with no parts related to Immortal arts or divine abilities.

"I wonder, if I were to absorb this Immortal Skin with the Azure Nether Pearl, could I decipher the divine abilities of its former owner?"

"After all, he was once a being who attained the Nameless realm..."

Although this thought flashed through Li Fan's mind, he firmly filed it away, intending to try it when the opportunity arose.

In the blink of an eye, another year passed.

Li Fan became increasingly familiar with the Immortal Spiritual Energy within the Immortal Skin.

However, he soon encountered a bottleneck.

No matter how many times he wore the Immortal Skin, in the "True Immortal" state, it seemed he could transform the Immortal Spiritual Energy within the skin into his own energy.

But as soon as he took off the Immortal Skin, his familiarity with the Immortal Spiritual Energy immediately dropped back to the previous bottleneck level.

He could not advance any further.

"It seems I was being too optimistic. If there weren't some limitations in place, how could Scholar Zhu have so easily lent me this Immortal Skin?"

Li Fan chuckled wryly.

However, he did not give up on the idea of acquiring Immortal Spiritual Energy.

"As the saying goes, if heaven does not grant it, I shall take it myself..."

A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

In the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan's true body caressed a stone slab.

This was the key method left behind by King Xuan Yuan in the Ascension Platform of the former Immortal Realm for cultivators to ascend.

Although it was merely a replica left by King Xuan Yuan, it still seemed to emanate infinite power.

"If my guess is correct, this stone slab must contain the method for newly ascended cultivators to access the Infinite Ocean, thereby obtaining the infinite Immortal Spiritual Energy."

"However, it can only be achieved with official permission from the Immortal Realm."

"Even though King Xuan Yuan was fortunate enough to ascend to the Immortal Realm, the administrator of the Ascension Platform had long since perished. Without guidance from the Immortal Realm, even someone like King Xuan Yuan could not obtain Immortal Spiritual Energy from this stone slab..."

Li Fan called this stone slab the "Key of the Dao," and only by using the corresponding True Immortal inscriptions could its true function be activated.

"In addition to True Immortal inscriptions, other methods might be needed to unlock the method of infinite connection to the ocean."

Li Fan pondered.

Li Fan's divine sense clone in the Shining Star Sea, wearing the Immortal Skin, sent a wisp of Immortal Spiritual Energy through the miniature Dao Net to Li Fan's true body.

However, this wisp of Immortal Spiritual Energy, after traversing the star sea, seemed to have been filtered layer by layer. Its originally faint starlight color became even thinner, appearing milky white.

Furthermore, Li Fan's true body did not have the blessing of the Immortal Skin. It was not the owner of this Immortal Spiritual Energy.

As soon as this Immortal Spiritual Energy appeared in this foreign space-time, it ran wild like an untamed horse, trying to escape from Li Fan's grasp.

Li Fan's true body maintained his focus, using the familiarity with this Immortal Spiritual Energy, honed over four years, as a reins to barely control it.

In the surrounding Immortal Formation, Immortal Spiritual Energy released by the Separation Disc assisted him.

This helped Li Fan subdue this unruly Immortal Spiritual Energy.

After more than half a day of arduous effort, this berserk Immortal Spiritual Energy was finally barely under control.

"Next, we will use this Immortal Spiritual Energy to disguise our identity."

"Through the Key of the Dao stone slab, we will enter that Infinite Ocean."

Although the goal was clear, its actual implementation was far from easy.

After all, it was something that even King Xuan Yuan of the past could not achieve.

The first problem to face was how to activate the stone slab.

Li Fan used the Immortal Formation as a knife, dividing the wisp of Immortal Spiritual Energy transmitted by his divine sense clone into tens of thousands of portions for experimentation.

If he simply used this Immortal Spiritual Energy to touch the stone slab, a faint halo would appear on the slab, and then there would be no further reaction. It seemed to be waiting for Li Fan to take the next step.

Recalling the process of using the Key of the Dao stone slab to help the Xuanhuang Realm ascend to immortality, Li Fan knew that it was necessary to use True Immortal inscriptions for corresponding activation.

"Could it be, the inscription of 'Transformation of Immortals and Mortals' again?"

Li Fan had a thought and guided one portion of the Immortal Spiritual Energy to write on the stone slab.

The stone slab did erupt with a strong energy fluctuation, but after searching the surroundings and finding no suitable candidate, the fluctuation eventually dissipated on its own after a long time.

Eliminating this option, Li Fan began other experiments.

He tested each True Immortal inscription he knew.

Unfortunately, none of them matched.

"It must be an unknown True Immortal inscription."

Li Fan's true body frowned slightly.

...

His attempts to access the Infinite Ocean were blocked, so Li Fan turned his attention to Scholar Zhu.

Directly asking was impossible. Not only would it expose his true identity, but it might also attract the attention of the Shining Star Sea Governing Council.

Li Fan's divine sense clone continued to familiarize himself with the power of Immortal Spiritual Energy while waiting for an opportunity.

Soon, only seven days remained until the recruitment for Immortal Hunting.

This time, the Governing Council announced a recruitment of twice the usual number of cultivators, causing a stir throughout the Shining Star Sea, with mixed feelings of joy and apprehension.

Joy stemmed from the increased probability of joining Immortal Hunting.

Fear arose from the rumor that the increased recruitment was due to heavy losses sustained in the previous operation to hunt True Immortals. It was a forced measure. Clearly, joining Immortal Hunting, while granting immense power, also entailed risks far greater than imagined.

However, regardless of the risks, becoming a member of Immortal Hunting was the lifelong pursuit of the young elites from the various powers of the Shining Star Sea, thus attracting numerous applicants.

In Bliss City, Li Fan received a message from Scholar Zhu.

"In seven days, I will, as promised, recommend you for the selection."

"However, as we agreed beforehand, I need to test you first!"

Li Fan straightened his clothes and slowly walked into the City Lord's mansion.

He pushed open the door but did not encounter Scholar Zhu.

Instead, he stepped into emptiness, as if falling into an endless abyss.

Falling rapidly downwards, surrounded by infinite darkness.

In the darkness, points of light flashed intermittently, as if embedded in the cliff walls of the abyss.

Scholar Zhu's rumbling voice echoed in Li Fan's ears.

"The Immortal Hunting assessment places the utmost importance on understanding the Dao Net."

"The points of light you see are Dao Net commands that may be involved in the test. Try to replicate them."

"This is the first hurdle. If you cannot pass this..."

"Then never leave!"

Scholar Zhu's cackling laughter echoed throughout the abyss.

Li Fan ignored him, focusing instead on carefully observing the Dao Net command points of light around him.

The endless rapid descent and floating techniques were rendered useless here.

Each Dao Net command flashed by in an instant. It was extremely difficult to observe and replicate these commands in such a short time.

Fortunately, Li Fan had a miniature Dao Net projection in his divine sense.

His divine sense acted as a screen, projecting all the rapidly flashing points of light into the surrounding area.

If there was a corresponding Dao Net command in his own projection, it would spontaneously flash in response.

If it fell outside Li Fan's cognitive blind spot, it would be simply ignored.

There was no need for Li Fan's consciousness to identify and replicate them; his miniature Dao Net did it for him.

Both the reaction speed and the accuracy of replication were significantly improved.

Li Fan sensed that with each successful replication, it was as if he were being pulled by a rope, and his descent speed slowed down slightly.

As one point of light after another was replicated and permanently illuminated above in the endless abyss,

Li Fan finally stopped descending.

The darkness gradually dissipated, and leaving the endless abyss, Li Fan arrived in a desolate wilderness.

A figure stood in the void.

Although Li Fan did not recognize the face, he felt a sense of familiarity with its aura. It was Scholar Zhu!

Indeed, Scholar Zhu's voice emanated from the figure, "The second test is martial prowess."

"Immortal Hunting, Immortal Hunting. Its objective is to hunt True Immortals."

"Can you... do it?"

Before he could finish speaking, Scholar Zhu pointed at Li Fan from a distance.

"True Immortals wield the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth as their blade and command infinite power."

The boundless wilderness suddenly seemed to curl up like a sphere with this single point from Scholar Zhu.

Li Fan felt as if he were in a confined space, watching the earth rise around him, with no escape.

It was not just the ground, but all the laws of heaven and earth transformed into oppressive forces, threatening to crush him like a cage, as if facing the entire world!

Li Fan's expression remained unchanged; he did not put on the Immortal Skin.

Instead, countless arms materialized behind him in an instant.

Each arm seemed to be rapidly writing something.

With each completed writing, a point of light appeared before Li Fan.

Slowly, these points of light wove into a net.

Li Fan lightly placed his hands on this net, as if playing a zither, plucking the strings of the net.

With each movement, a large portion of the surrounding rolling wilderness vanished inexplicably.

As the plucking sounds continued, the wilderness was quickly eaten away, forming holes.

By the time it reached Li Fan, there was no longer any threat!

Returning to the void, Li Fan and Scholar Zhu faced each other from afar.

Scholar Zhu stared at the miniature Dao Net woven before Li Fan, deep in thought.

"With the strength of your current body, joining Immortal Hunting is more than enough."

"However... I still need to probe your true capabilities!"

Scholar Zhu let out a cold laugh.

In the darkness, rolling clouds accompanied by roaring thunder descended.

In an instant, they completely enveloped Li Fan.

Li Fan squinted, and within these black clouds, he seemed to see countless figures standing tall and imposing.

"These are all my former servants."

"Let me see how far you can go."

Scholar Zhu's figure suddenly disappeared.

And terrifying creatures with grotesque faces emerged from the black clouds like a tide,

Rushing towards Li Fan.

Li Fan seemed to be so terrified that he stood frozen, not reacting for a long time.

But these immortal creatures had no intention of holding back.

Just as they were about to reach Li Fan,

"Disperse!"

Li Fan uttered a soft command.

All the creatures simultaneously froze in place, as if frozen in ice.

And then...

Like the rolling black clouds, they vanished into thin air!

Scholar Zhu, hidden behind the black clouds, revealed his true face.

He scrutinized Li Fan, filled with disbelief.

"I also had countless servants in the past. What do you think, Scholar Zhu?"

Li Fan smiled faintly.

And as he spoke, countless more gloomy black clouds pressed down from the void.

Figures moved within the clouds.

These were precisely the immortal servants that Li Fan had dispersed with a single word!

However, now they had a new master.

They turned towards Scholar Zhu and attacked him.

"Presumptuous!"

Scholar Zhu was furious.

The heavens and earth seemed to be struck by an invisible giant, and a void appeared out of nowhere.

And all the beings within this collapsed area vanished into nothingness, turning to dust.

Bang bang bang.

Strange sounds continued to erupt, as if countless beings were being crushed like flies.

In a short while, the creatures attacking Scholar Zhu were all annihilated.

But compared to Li Fan's effortless destruction with a single word, he clearly fell short.

Li Fan did not manifest countless immortal creatures again, but merely smiled as he watched the other party.

"Interesting. Very interesting."

"I believe you will bring some surprises to these fellows."

"Go!"

After a long period of gazing at each other, Scholar Zhu finally spoke.

The scene around Li Fan instantly disappeared.

He returned to the outside of the City Lord's mansion.

Before him was the door, which had not yet been opened.

Li Fan bowed towards the front and turned to leave.

"Trapped in Bliss City for so long, how could he still have these immortal servants?"

"If he hadn't insisted on summoning them, I wouldn't have been able to see through the truth."

"It's just a scene similar to the 'Eternal Remnants,' where illusions appear real. In such a situation, even a powerful being like Evil Su Bai would not be my match, let alone a mere discarded Nameless True Immortal."

Li Fan sneered, having already returned to his own residence.

The next step was to infiltrate Immortal Hunting and steal the core secrets of the Shining Star Sea.

"The essence of the test just now was a clash of Dao and consciousness."

"Although I suppressed Scholar Zhu with the 'Transformation of True and False,' his method of forcefully crushing with a force like an invisible giant was indeed not to be underestimated."

Chapter 1445: Ants Besiege and Kill Immortals

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, recalling the divine abilities and techniques of Scholar Zhu in the illusion just now.

The miniature Dao Net in his divine sense flickered, searching for corresponding Great Dao laws. Scholar Zhu, having entered the Dao Net, naturally became one of its foundational roots.

Li Fan's replica in his divine sense also contained its reflection.

The moment it corresponded, a strand of the Dao Net emitted a uniquely deep light.

Li Fan's divine sense vibrated slightly, "This is... the character 'Grind'!"

Before his eyes, a square grinding stone seemed to appear, continuously pounding and crushing targets in the world. With the continuous flow of light from this strand in the miniature Dao Net, Li Fan's understanding of this Dao advanced by leaps and bounds in a short period.

However, after only a few breaths, Li Fan actively withdrew from this Dao comprehension.

"Although Scholar Zhu has been cast into the Dao Net and serves as a living stake, he is still alive. This 'Grind' Dao still has an owner."

"The deeper the research, the easier it is for its owner to sense it."

Even though there were myriad Great Daos in the world, Li Fan only needed to focus on the Transformation of True and False. As for other Dao principles, they were merely tools to be used conveniently before reaching the highest peak.

This deliberate exposure of the Transformation of True and False before Scholar Zhu was not Li Fan showing off his temporary prowess before a former Nameless True Immortal. It was a test.

"Now it seems that the Transformation of True and False is profound and mysterious. Even if there were hidden observers in the Immortal Realm in the past, not everyone knew of its existence. Even though Scholar Zhu has reached the realm of Nameless True Immortal, he could not recognize it when I displayed it before him. He was merely astonished by my unfathomable methods."

Although this trial was somewhat risky, Scholar Zhu himself was a prisoner within the net. Li Fan's true body was far away in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea behind the High Wall, with the concealment of the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss. Even if any accidents occurred, he could still calmly revert to true form.

In fact, with Black Heavenly Physician crossing possibilities to arrive, Li Fan was still able to successfully activate his reversion ability. In this current "Primal" possibility, there were truly few beings who could pose a real threat to Li Fan.

In the blink of an eye, seven days passed.

As promised, Scholar Zhu recommended "Ma Tiande" to the Governing Council.

Ma Tiande was originally sent by the Governing Council to Bliss City to operate the Dao Net and conduct surveillance. Now, the Governing Council assumed that Scholar Zhu and Ma Tiande had an unpleasant relationship and wanted to find an excuse to transfer Ma Tiande.

Through verification via the Dao Net, Ma Tiande's identity was confirmed. After also seeking Ma Tiande's personal opinion, the Governing Council agreed to the recommendation.

The Immortal Hunting selection process was concentrated within half a day.

When the selection officially began, the ethereal Dao Net seemed to reveal its true form, manifesting physically from illusion.

A faintly visible great net covered the entire Shining Star Sea.

It encompassed every faction within the star sea.

The shadow of the Dao Net spanned across heaven and earth, extending beyond the world.

Such a magnificent and miraculous sight inspired awe and reverence in the hearts of all who witnessed it.

Ordinary mortals knelt in worship.

Even cultivators lowered their heads in submission.

As the Dao Net spanned the heavens, Li Fan did not draw attention to himself, merely lowering his head and observing quietly.

Due to the presence of the miniature Dao Net in his divine sense, his vision differed from that of ordinary people.

Four figures exuding a divine and majestic aura stood like pillars behind the Dao Net. In addition, other phantoms, stern and imposing, seemed to stand in layers within the Dao Net. The invisible giant hand that was pressing down on the Dao Net was nowhere to be seen.

In reality, Li Fan felt a chilling fear every time his gaze swept over these Nameless True Immortal nodes. However, his divine sense projection, due to this close-range, more detailed observation, became even clearer.

Therefore, Li Fan did not stop his prying gaze.

A ray of light traversed through the Dao Net.

Wherever it passed, all participants in the Immortal Hunting selection were illuminated by this light.

Their bodies, beyond their control, floated upwards uncontrollably.

Li Fan also floated up, observing the nearly a thousand cultivators rising with him throughout the Shining Star Sea, remaining expressionless. While being caught, he observed the real-world operation of the Dao Net.

"Spanning the entire Shining Star Sea and simultaneously and precisely locking onto a thousand targets, lifting them into the air... in terms of the breadth and precision of power, the Dao Net's action is no less than that of a True Immortal."

Moreover, Li Fan vaguely sensed that these participants in Immortal Hunting were not simply being lifted into the air. They seemed to have entered a parallel space-time, completely separated from the real Shining Star Sea.

The beings in the Shining Star Sea below could look up and see them in the sky, while they gradually lost sight of what was below, as if entering a completely isolated area.

"This is likely to ensure the fairness and justice of the Immortal Hunting selection, a public test conducted before all life forms in the Shining Star Sea," Li Fan understood.

The surrounding scene turned dim, as if immersed in endless void. The thousand cultivators floated within, awaiting the start of the selection.

A rumbling sound soon reverberated.

Without any preamble, it went straight to the point.

"First trial: Dao."

The Dao Net, spanning heaven and earth, seemed to have descended into this selection space, appearing abruptly and then continuously pressing down and constricting.

What was originally a celestial phenomenon was now approaching, right before their eyes.

Facing the trial of a thousand people, before the majestic Dao Net, they were like ants caught in a net.

The oppressive feeling originating from the Great Dao caused one-third of the thousand people to tremble involuntarily.

A flash of light, and these trembling individuals were instantly eliminated and teleported out of the trial space.

The remaining cultivators steadied their minds and focused on confronting the Dao Net, which was pressing down upon them as if it would crush them entirely.

The Dao Net continued to descend as if to completely crush them from above.

Facing the imminent danger of being ground to dust, not everyone could maintain a calm demeanor. Even though they had prepared extensively beforehand, the Dao Net they had imagined and the actual Dao Net were worlds apart. During this process, anyone who showed the slightest change in expression was eliminated.

The Dao Net pressed down, and their bodies and souls felt as if they were being ruthlessly ground. Then, they merged into the Dao Net.

When Li Fan could see again, he found himself in a labyrinth-like area.

The true form of the Dao Net was nowhere to be seen.

Hum hum hum...

A strange sound came from not far away.

Li Fan turned his head and saw that the silvery-white labyrinth path was inexplicably evaporating and disappearing from the edges.

Furthermore, this disappearance was rapidly spreading towards him.

"Dao Annihilation Tribulation?"

Naturally, the words "Dao Annihilation Tribulation" appeared in Li Fan's mind.

Of course, it was not the true Dao Annihilation Tribulation, but a simulated disaster scenario based on its essence.

"So, what needs to be done now is to escape from this Dao Net labyrinth." Li Fan seemed to understand.

He tried to take a step towards the depths of the labyrinth, but habitually exerting force, he found himself completely immobile.

Looking down, Li Fan discovered that his feet were inexplicably stuck to the Dao Net labyrinth.

The path forward, though seemingly smooth, was covered in uneven bumps. Under normal circumstances, it would be a difficult journey.

After observing for a while, Li Fan understood the intention of this first trial.

By extending tentacle-like sensors from his feet, Li Fan perceived the raised bumps of the Dao Net ahead.

"I need to issue a Dao Net command to fill this gap."

Li Fan did not act personally. Instead, he resorted to his usual tactic, just as he had in Scholar Zhu's trial. He used the miniature Dao Net in his divine sense to respond directly.

In an instant, a dim light emerged from Li Fan's body and, through his feet, transmitted to the ground.

Filling the gap.

The path ahead became smooth, and Li Fan took a step forward with ease.

"This method of testing is quite interesting."

The miniature Dao Net and the various gaps on the path ahead quickly corresponded.

Li Fan walked slowly and unhurriedly.

His mind was not burdened by pressure, allowing Li Fan to observe his surroundings. He controlled his walking speed to be slightly behind the leading group.

Not the very top, not the most conspicuous, but still in the first tier.

The Dao Net behind him continued to evaporate and close in.

In this round, about four hundred people were eliminated.

When only over three hundred cultivators remained, the first trial ended.

The Dao Net labyrinth silently disappeared, and a great announcement voice resonated again.

Still straightforward.

"Second trial: Martial prowess."

As the voice echoed in the space, an inexplicable aura descended.

Li Fan's pupils contracted.

"True Immortal?"

Standing alongside the three hundred cultivators was a tall figure clad in golden armor.

However, shackles bound his hands and feet, and his armor was severely damaged and covered in scars.

His beard and hair seemed to have not been trimmed for many years, messy and obscuring his face.

But Li Fan could still see a faint sinister smile flash across the figure's face.

"Rain!"

A somewhat hoarse voice, tinged with a faint killing intent, resounded in everyone's ears.

Suddenly, raindrops began to fall from the sky.

At first, only a few scattered drops, then increasing in intensity, until it became a torrential downpour.

Each drop was as heavy as a mountain.

As it rained down, many cultivators, caught off guard, let out screams.

They were smashed into bloody pulp by the raindrops.

A flash of light, and upon reaching the brink of death, they were teleported out of the trial space.

However, a small number of unfortunate souls, before they could be teleported away, died in this downpour.

"They're serious."

Li Fan watched as a cultivator beside him died tragically.

He, however, showed no panic. He had countless methods to defend against this Immortal Rain.

"Since it's an Immortal Hunting selection, I should make the most of the Dao Net's power."

As the True Immortal appeared, Li Fan sensed that he had somehow gotten closer to the Dao Net. It seemed to facilitate the convenience of the Immortal Hunting participants in invoking the power of the Dao Net.

"Rain..."

"Umbrella!"

With a thought from Li Fan, an umbrella materialized in his hand.

Its circular canopy sheltered him from the falling rain, blocking the torrent.

However, this trial was not so easily passed.

While protecting himself, Li Fan looked to his sides. He discovered that a considerable number of Shining Star Sea cultivators had adapted immediately.

They unleashed their unique abilities; some, like Li Fan, used umbrellas or protective gear to shield themselves. Others used invisible forces to divert the falling raindrops, or directly swallowed the downpour...

After they were able to stand firm in the rain, they began to surround and attack the golden-armored True Immortal, who was assisted by chains.

Various divine abilities and spells were unleashed.

Among them, the most striking was a gust of wind and three swords.

A great wind roared, blowing the torrential rain backward. A divine ability initially used by the True Immortal to torment the testers was now being used against himself.

Three swords belonged to the same person. They stood behind a female cultivator in purple robes. This female cultivator seemed blind, her eyes always closed. However, in the pouring rain that obscured vision, she could accurately lock onto the True Immortal's location. The three swords behind her were held by a broken arm, a severed head, and a circular vortex.

Sword light crisscrossed, cutting through wind and rain, and relentlessly struck the True Immortal.

...

Amidst the raging wind and rain, energy surged like a tidal wave, fluctuating unstantly.

Li Fan hid in the shadows, observing quietly, not making any rash moves. At the same time, he used the miniature Dao Net in his divine sense to record all the fluctuations of spells and divine abilities around him.

Evidently, the participant in this trial was a True Immortal.

Although controlled by the Governing Council, unable to unleash his full power, his protective capabilities were still intact.

The divine abilities of the numerous cultivators continuously bombarded his golden armor.

But it only caused minor tremors. It couldn't even inflict superficial wounds.

The golden-armored True Immortal laughed maniacally, looking at the swarm of ants attacking him.

"Rain! Rain! Rain!"

As the True Immortal chanted, the rain intensified.

The shackles on the True Immortal's hands and feet clanged, seemingly on the verge of breaking and falling off under the impact of the True Immortal's surge.

And the rain that was invading the cultivators began to exhibit its original divine effect.

Not only was it as heavy as a mountain, but it also began to erode the cultivators' souls and spirits.

Even the Great Dao of this realm was activated.

As the cultivators began to show signs of defeat under the True Immortal's counterattack,

Li Fan, who had been watching from the sidelines, finally spoke.

"Shed armor!"

Li Fan, hidden behind all the cultivators, pointed towards the arrogant golden-armored True Immortal from afar.

His voice, though soft, pierced through the wind and rain, reaching the ears of everyone present.

The wind and rain paused.

As if a profoundly mysterious power had descended, the armor on the golden-armored True Immortal's body, irresistibly, trembled slightly.

"No!"

The golden-armored True Immortal, whose face had been filled with ferocity moments ago, was now utterly terrified.

He roared, as if trying to prevent his armor from falling off.

But the power of the Dao Net roughly stripped the protective gear from his body.

In just a moment, the former True Immortal stood before everyone, completely naked.

Although his messy hair provided some covering, it was still an unbearable humiliation!

The cultivators participating in the trial, now realizing what had happened,

Resumed their attack on the True Immortal.

The True Immortal roared, allowing these attacks to wear down his flesh and blood.

His pair of blood-red eyes, however, pierced through the crowd, fixedly staring at Li Fan!

Chapter 1446: First Hunt for a True Immortal

ANGER burned in the True Immortal's eyes, causing the rain to intensify. The raindrops pierced through the void like layers of curtains, dividing the battlefield into small sections.

In the midst of the downpour, Li Fan, through the gaps, saw that among the cultivators who seized this critical opportunity to attack the True Immortal, more than ten could not withstand the immense pressure of the rain and were instantly crushed into powder.

Their remains, mixed with rainwater, writhed and transformed into "Rainmen"! These Rainmen, using the ubiquitous downpour in the battlefield, instantly converged from all directions, attacking Li Fan.

Li Fan feigned a dramatic change in expression and, holding his umbrella, transformed into a beam of light, rapidly escaping the encirclement. His speed was even faster than the falling rain! Thus it was: "Through the torrential rain, a body passes, yet not a single drop adheres."

Escaping to a distant, temporarily safe location, Li Fan looked at the True Immortal who was still staring at him intently, and with a cold laugh, he pointed again: "Shave!" His voice seemed to possess a peculiar magic, causing everyone present to stiffen slightly. The encirclement attack faltered.

The True Immortal, his eyes bloodshot, let out another earth-shattering roar. "Kill you! Kill you! Kill you..." Resentment surged, and anger boiled.

The rain, which had been falling evenly, now seemed to be drawn by some force, and like a waterspout, it all roared towards Li Fan.

However, the True Immortal's retaliatory actions could not stop the Dao Net commands Li Fan had already issued. The invisible fluctuations of the Dao Net instantly spanned the battlefield, descending upon the True Immortal once more. It was as if countless scissors were trimming the True Immortal's hair and beard simultaneously.

As the obscured covering was gradually removed, the True Immortal's true face was finally revealed. Although his face was somewhat gaunt, he was undeniably handsome. His body, however, was covered in deep, unhealable wounds that exposed bone. His flesh writhed continuously, but some inexplicable force prevented it from growing.

The remaining besieging cultivators, their minds in sync, directed their spells and divine abilities towards these wounds. The True Immortal let out a cry of pain.

Not far away, Li Fan, by merely holding his umbrella, could no longer cope with the sky-high waterspouts. Rain fell from all directions, eroding Li Fan's body and mind. The sounds that reached his ears were drowned out by the rain. His vision was shrouded by the dense curtain of rain.

Even with a tightly sealed raincoat, Li Fan slowly felt himself being severed from the world around him. Like the dust of the mortal world, he was being completely washed away by this rain!

"This is the Dao of \[Rain]..."

"If I don't do something, I'll completely disappear from the world. All traces of my existence will be like mud stains washed away by the rain, never to return."

"Even bound by the Dao Net, the True Immortal can still unleash such divine abilities. It seems in his prime, he was no weakling!"

Li Fan, enduring the rain and experiencing the Great Dao's divine abilities at close range, gained considerable insight. Simultaneously, with the flashes of inspiration in his mind, another rain began to form around him. The direction of the raindrops was the opposite of the True Immortal's control.

As the raindrops collided, the wind and rain around Li Fan immediately weakened. Even if it couldn't completely negate the True Immortal's divine abilities, with the raincoat's protection, safety was assured.

Li Fan continued to feel the Dao of Rain around him, watching the discomposed True Immortal facing the cultivators' siege, a sense of alarm suddenly surged in his heart.

"It's just shedding armor and clothes, appearing naked."

"Compared to being captured alive by mortals, such humiliation is not worth mentioning. This Golden-Armored True Immortal's reaction is far too excessive. Screaming and shouting, he has almost completely lost his reason..."

"He doesn't seem like someone who could comprehend such divine abilities."

"No!" Li Fan's heart tightened, and he suddenly realized. He looked at the field; the golden armor and beard that had been removed by his "Shed Armor and Shave" technique had, at some unknown time, inexplicably disappeared!

"His losing control was just a lure, merely to attract everyone's attention. It was so that they could seize the opportunity to escape when everyone was not paying attention."

Li Fan's thoughts raced, and he was about to connect to the Dao Net here and activate the \[Constrain] divine ability. But then he reconsidered; this was not a real True Immortal hunting battlefield, but a test by the Shining Star Sea Governing Council to recruit Immortal Hunters.

With so many people watching, could he really let a mere True Immortal escape?

"It must be an additional test. If I expose it, I will surely attract extra attention from the Governing Council. But if I pretend not to know..."

Li Fan hesitated for only a moment before making the choice to reveal his special abilities. He shouted into the air, "Everyone be careful, don't let him escape stealthily!"

Then he quickly scanned his surroundings, chanting solemn and reverent words: "Constrain!" The Dao Net revealed on the battlefield seemed to be stirred by a gust of wind, rustling. The intersecting Dao strings thus became clearer. With a slight tremor, they emitted a brilliant silver light. The golden armor and beard, which had scattered to the edges of the battlefield, were all simultaneously locked onto and bound!

Buzz! The Dao strings vibrated violently, as if the True Immortal was struggling fiercely.

At this moment, the cultivators on the battlefield finally came to their senses. Some continued to attack the True Immortal's body, while others began to round up the golden armor and beard. The situation was clear: the True Immortal had completely lost any chance of turning the tide. He was about to die at the hands of these ants...

A flash of light passed, and the dying True Immortal disappeared before everyone's eyes. It wasn't that he had escaped again, but that the second test had already concluded.

Li Fan felt the unusual glances from the surrounding cultivators, merely smiling in response.

"Third trial..."

"Life!"

The cold voice had not yet finished when the Dao Net, which had been a mere backdrop, directly descended from above. It seemed as if the heavens were collapsing, Dao strings stretching across, like broken cliffs. In this sudden catastrophe, many cultivators died instantly. Judging by their appearance, they were not teleported away before death, but genuinely died.

The Dao Net, which they could rely on, had now become a murderous weapon. The cultivators participating in the test could only rely on their own abilities to avoid this inexplicable disaster.

But... The cultivators of the Shining Star Sea, especially those participating in the Immortal Hunting selection, had their cultivation and strength almost entirely based on Dao Origin symbols and Dao Net commands. Without the Dao Net's support, the methods they could employ were pitifully few. How could they survive such a catastrophe of falling heavens?

Apart from the elite of the major forces, the rest of the people died within a short period. The remaining individuals, facing the overwhelming catastrophe of the Dao Net's collapse, were merely struggling. As the Dao Net collapsed more and more severely, the places of refuge for them became fewer and fewer. The crowd was gradually being pushed to a dead end.

Li Fan, relying on his Light Escape technique, managed to navigate with relative ease. However, looking at the current situation where only sixteen people remained, including himself, Li Fan could not help but feel a sense of doubt.

"The previous Immortal Hunting tests were not this strict. Could it be that there have been major changes in the Shining Star Sea recently?"

The severity of this assessment had clearly exceeded the expectations of those present. Their faces, no longer calm, now showed uncontrollable panic. All their abilities were used, struggling to survive in this doomsday scenario.

"Ah!" Another person was crushed to death by the falling Dao strings. Right in front of Li Fan. Their soul was annihilated, turning into light spots and merging into the Dao Net.

However, this glimpse allowed Li Fan to discover the anomaly. Li Fan witnessed the extinction of countless beings, but this "death" seemed different from the true demise of a cultivator.

With a shift in his thoughts, Li Fan understood. "So that's how it is. This trial, seemingly testing the candidates, is actually testing their death. Those who can survive such a catastrophe as the collapsing Dao Net without borrowing its power must have reached a divine level in their own cultivation and attainment. The cultivators of the Shining Star Sea, having learned since childhood, all rely on the Dao Net. They have almost no possibility of completing the trial..."

"If someone can last until the end, they are likely lurking criminals from outside regions!"

"Dying is the way to pass the trial. Surviving until the end would likely lead to capture and severe interrogation."

As Li Fan pondered, he quickly understood the essence of this trial.

"Of course, if one dies too quickly, it might still not be acceptable. The first group of people likely died genuinely. However, those who lack the ability to react at all in the face of disaster deserve to die. Only the timing of death, not too early or too late, can lead to selection."

Li Fan, approaching it from the perspective of the examiner rather than the examinee, naturally understood the meaning behind it quickly. Thus, he slowly feigned exhaustion, appearing to be in a precarious situation, and let the Dao strings descend upon him.

It had to be said that even if one understood the truth of this trial, facing the crushing Dao Net strings from above, an ordinary person would absolutely be unable to resist and die calmly. In the face of life and death, there is great terror. And the scene of the Dao Net's collapse could incite instinctive survival and resistance in one's heart.

For someone like Li Fan, who had always walked on the edge of life and death and had narrowly escaped death countless times, upon sensing the silver Dao strings about to press down upon him, he still almost couldn't help but break free and escape its trajectory. Fortunately, he managed to suppress it. He allowed the Dao strings to crush him into powder.

His vision was instantly filled with infinite silver light. Li Fan's divine sense seemed to have lost consciousness. Unknowingly, Li Fan vaguely sensed a vast intention sweeping through his mind. Under instinctive vigilance, Li Fan's mind became utterly still, returning to infinite tranquility.

Instantly, relying on the miniature Dao Net hidden within his own divine sense. He casually projected Ma Tiande's life memories to the surface. The miniature Dao Net and the Dao Net were essentially imprints of the Great Dao, without inherent differences. At this moment, they merged perfectly. Even that vast intention, after a brief scrutiny, did not detect anything. The sense of being stared at by a terrifying monster in the shadows vanished.

Li Fan "resurrected from the dead," his body and consciousness restored. He was no longer in the previous trial space but had arrived at a circular floating platform in the void. Outside the platform, numerous figures stood. Their appearances were indistinct, but they all gazed at the remaining participants in the arena, pointing and laughing, without any malice.

Li Fan scanned his surroundings. He noticed that the other survivors seemed to have not yet recovered from their daze, some still looking bewildered. Occasionally, figures would flash and appear within the circular platform. After about fifteen minutes, all personnel had arrived.

The announcing voice then resounded again. This time, without the previous coldness and seriousness, it carried a hint of warmth. "Final trial: Combat!"

Li Fan understood in his heart: "It seems that reaching this point means completing the trial. The so-called combat is more like determining rankings."

Undeniably, those who reached this stage were already the elite prodigies of the Shining Star Sea. Although they had not yet recovered, upon hearing the order, they instinctively launched sneak attacks on their "enemies" nearby.

Li Fan also, naturally, received attacks. His body moved like lightning, effortlessly dodging all assaults. At the same time, he shouted, "Shed armor!"

The cultivators targeting Li Fan all stiffened slightly, and simultaneously retreated backward. Everyone present were intelligent individuals and understood that this final trial was merely a formality. If one lost in the combat, so be it. The onlookers, who were clearly fellow Immortal Hunters from the Shining Star Sea, would have to interact with each other in the future. If their clothes were stripped off, making them appear naked, how could they continue to interact?

Thus, under the deterrence of the "Shed Armor" technique, everyone tacitly avoided choosing Li Fan as an opponent. They occasionally launched sneak attacks, all of which Li Fan easily dodged. This combat ended with a minimal engagement, as expected.

Not long after, the rankings were finalized. A light screen descended above the circular platform. The names of the people in the arena were all listed. From top to bottom, there were twenty-eight people. Based on their performance in the four trials, their overall rankings were determined. Ma Tiande's name was ranked fifth.

"It must have been his performance in the second trial, the True Immortal capture, that boosted his score."

Li Fan looked at the person ranked first on the list. Theađzes of almost everyone in the arena were focused on him. It was the cultivator who had previously displayed the wind divine ability, reversing the True Immortal's rain. His name was Dao Yuan. He was tall and slender, with deep eyes. Facing the gazes of everyone, he was not intimidated, but smiled and cupped his hands in greeting.

Recalling the information he had seen before, Li Fan remembered this person's origin. He was from the Shining Star Sea, from the Myriad Dao Palace. Since the Myriad Dao Palace dared to take Dao as its name, it naturally had its own backing. They were originally a surviving force from another destroyed star sea, and they had managed to establish a foothold amidst much covetousness. It was said that they had also made outstanding contributions to the establishment of the Dao Net, and were now on par with the Sword Domain and Blade Island.

"Since you have all joined \[Immortal Hunting], you must obey orders from now on."

"Those who disobey will be executed without mercy."

"Next, you will face your first mission."

Everyone present had subtle expressions upon hearing this. They did not expect to be assigned a mission immediately after joining Immortal Hunting, without any training.

"Half a day ago, a True Immortal was lured by our \[Immortal Bait] and crossed the Annihilation Land, entering the area covered by the Dao Net."

"It is not far from the Shining Star Sea."

"This True Immortal is severely injured, and his Dao is \[Eradicate]. He is suitably skilled to be a practice target for your first hunt..."

A figure walked out from among the spectators of the circular platform. Though short, he was muscular, dressed in a blood-colored tunic, and carried a black stone pillar on his shoulder, looking peculiar.

"I hope your first hunt is successful!" the blood-clothed man grinned, patting the stone pillar on his shoulder.

Chapter 1447: Navigating the River Against the Current

BEFORE the blood-clothed man could finish speaking, everyone felt an inexplicable suction force appear above the circular platform. It was like a vortex suddenly forming, drawing them all in.

Before falling into the vortex, Li Fan inadvertently glanced at the stone pillar carried by the blood-clothed man. The moment the latter lightly patted the pillar, Li Fan sensed a faint vibration occurring simultaneously within the Dao Net.

"Pillar of the Great Dao? Or perhaps one of the Great Daos themselves?"

"To be able to carry the Great Dao and look so effortless... this person's strength..."

"He is likely not below the Nameless realm!" Li Fan's heart grew solemn.

The invisible vortex swallowed the twenty-eight new Immortal Hunters collectively.

When they regained their senses, they found themselves in an unfamiliar starscape. Information regarding the mission was transmitted through the Dao Net.

"The True Immortal is expected to arrive here in half an hour."

"Use the remaining time to discuss the hunting strategy."

As everyone digested the information, they all looked at the "Immortal Bait" floating in the void, emitting strange fluctuations. It was a bronze coffin, surrounded by patterns of nine dragons and nine phoenixes.

What was chilling was that a corner of the coffin lid had already been opened by someone, and faint murmurs and whispers emanated from within. Although the sound came from the bronze coffin, it seemed to originate from right behind their ears.

The demonic sounds assaulted their ears, and though they seemed to have no immediate effect on everyone, it was evidently special enough to attract True Immortals to travel across the star sea.

The crowd observed in silence for a moment, and finally, Dao Yuan, who ranked first in the test, spoke first: "I happen to know something about the origin of this Immortal Bait. Let me begin with a humble introduction. If there are any inaccuracies, I hope everyone will forgive me."

Dao Yuan's attitude was humble, and the surrounding spectators nodded one after another.

"As everyone knows, the surviving True Immortals in the star sea today generally seek two things. Firstly, to comprehend the Great Dao and attain the Nameless realm. Secondly..."

"Naturally, it is a method to avoid calamities and seek refuge. When the Immortal Realm suddenly perished that year, countless True Immortals died like ants. The survivors of that group of Immortals subsequently developed a deep obsession with methods of survival. It is said that after the destruction of the Immortal Realm, Nameless True Immortals gathered and researched three divine methods of refuge."

Although Dao Yuan claimed this was common knowledge, the expressions on the faces of these new Immortal Hunters clearly indicated that such secrets were not known to ordinary people. Most were deeply captivated and listened intently. However, some were indifferent to Dao Yuan's boasting and let out cold sneers.

"It is said that these three methods of refuge can protect beings and weather all calamities in the world. Even disasters like the destruction of the Immortal Realm can be survived safely."

"The bronze coffin before us is the [World-Crossing Profound Coffin], one of the three refuge methods. This Profound Coffin seems to connect to other worlds. Once one lies within it, they will completely disappear from this world..."

At this point, someone couldn't help but interrupt Dao Yuan.

"...Completely disappear? In that case, how can we determine if they have perished or truly gone to seek refuge?"

This was clearly the question in everyone else's minds as well.

Dao Yuan smiled slightly and pointed to the nine-dragon, nine-phoenix patterns carved on the bronze coffin. "Have you all seen these dragon and phoenix patterns? After a person lies in the coffin and disappears, the dragons and phoenixes will cry out in unison, finally reflecting the scene of the other world. It is said that all of them are overjoyed and express their thanks with cupped hands. Perhaps communication is still possible when sending the person in the coffin to another world."

"As for the authenticity of these scenes... the eagerness of countless True Immortals, and even Nameless True Immortals, for this [World-Crossing Profound Coffin] already speaks volumes."

Hearing this, everyone gasped in unison.

"Then what about the one before us..."

Dao Yuan smiled. "Naturally, it is a replica."

Although it was an expected answer, everyone couldn't help but sigh.

"The World-Crossing Profound Coffin, since its creation, was meant to help Immortals escape calamities. Therefore, in the beginning, powerful individuals united and announced to all surviving Immortals in the world. They also passed on the Profound Coffin's aura fluctuations and activation method."

"Those with affinities could enter the coffin to avoid calamity," Dao Yuan explained calmly.

At this point, someone among the new Immortal Hunters finally reacted. "This means that the powerful beings who forged the World-Crossing Profound Coffin in the past have already used the Profound Coffin to seek refuge and escape to other worlds?"

Dao Yuan nodded. "Precisely!"

"The Profound Coffin is also their legacy. It is said that the true Profound Coffin floats in the star sea according to a special pattern, constantly emitting announcement fluctuations in all directions. While our Shining Star Sea has never seen the true World-Crossing Profound Coffin, we can already forge its fluctuations..."

Suddenly, a cold sneer interrupted. "Brother Dao, how do you know our Shining Star Sea has never seen the true Profound Coffin? Such a divine object, if one has not seen it with their own eyes, how can they imitate it so perfectly?"

Dao Yuan and the other Immortal Hunter members' expressions changed. However, the voice that had just spoken satirically fell silent, and it was impossible to discern who had spoken. The crowd exchanged surreptitious glances, but seemed to find no suspicious individuals.

Seeing the momentary stalemate, someone stepped forward to smooth things over. "Brother Dao, please continue explaining the other two methods of refuge. Hearing such secret knowledge for the first time, we are extremely curious!"

Others chimed in, and Dao Yuan's expression relaxed. He spoke again.

"As for the other two methods of refuge, I only know one of them."

"It is the [Reverse Time Boat]."

"Reverse Time Boat?"

Everyone savored the meaning of these three words.

Dao Yuan's expression became solemn. "The River of Time flows endlessly, moving forward since ancient times. This Reverse Time Boat is said to be able to carry people upstream in the River of Time, traveling back to a point before any calamity occurred..."

"Ah!"

The shock brought by the Reverse Time Boat was clearly far greater than that of the World-Crossing Profound Coffin. After all, the ability to reverse time was the lifelong dream of all living beings. This ignited the discussions of the crowd, who began to chatter amongst themselves.

"Brother Dao, has this Reverse Time Boat truly been created by those True Immortals?"

"I believe it's impossible. If they had truly returned to the past, why has the fact of the Immortal Realm's destruction not changed at all?"

"Alas, this is where you are mistaken. Returning to the past, if details of history are changed, it is like a river changing its course, naturally forming a different river downstream. But we are still in the original river, so naturally, we cannot perceive it."

"A specious argument! If that's the case, our existence should have vanished with the river's course change. Why do we and all things in the world still exist?"

"This..."

"The principles of time have already surpassed our ability to comprehend and imagine. You two need not be so argumentative."

"However, since Brother Dao speaks so earnestly... the existence of the Reverse Time Boat is likely not false."

...

Everyone exchanged their thoughts.

Finally, Dao Yuan smiled. "Whether the Reverse Time Boat is real or not, I cannot truly confirm. Let alone me, even the seniors in the Shining Star Sea might not truly know. It is merely a fleeting rumor."

Someone else asked, "This second method of refuge can already reverse the flow of time, so what about the third method of refuge...?"

The discussion on the Reverse Time Boat by the new Immortal Hunters instantly ceased, and all eyes were fixed on Dao Yuan, awaiting his explanation.

Dao Yuan gave a wry smile. "The third method of refuge, even among the Immortals of that era, few knew its details. However, all those who knew its true nature were deeply convinced that it was the most perfect method of refuge. If one could master that method, all calamities in the world would be like fleeting clouds. It was true great freedom, great ease, and great liberation!"

As Dao Yuan spoke, a look of longing appeared in his eyes. Everyone present felt the same. However, there was one person whose heart trembled even more profoundly than others at Dao Yuan's words!

It was Li Fan!

Having already learned of the existence of the world-ending calamity from the countdown of True Return, Li Fan initially felt disdain when he first heard of the so-called three methods of refuge. However, this disdain vanished the moment he heard of the first refuge method, the World-Crossing Profound Coffin.

Entering the Profound Coffin and traveling to another world. The world here was clearly not just another lower realm star sea. In an instant, Li Fan thought of the [Primordial Azure Source]. The demonic beast tribe could cross possibilities through it. True Immortals who survived the Dao Annihilation Tribulation might also possess the power to cross possibilities.

"If it's just random jumps between possibilities like the demonic beast tribe, it probably wouldn't be called [World-Crossing]."

"If what Dao Yuan said is true, all survivors who jumped away were overjoyed and expressed their thanks..."

"Could it be that the Profound Coffin can scout and even select the possibilities it reaches in advance?" Li Fan's heart stirred. The entire mortal world had another seventy-three million, six hundred thousand years of lifespan left. This meant there must be possibilities that could still survive for over seven million years. Although this number did not seem very long, compared to Li Fan's current [Primordial] possibility, which was in a deathbed state and could face the Dao Annihilation Tribulation at any time, that was already considered longevity. If they could find such a paradise from the remnants of the Immortal Realm, their joy would be understandable.

...

If the World-Crossing Profound Coffin only managed to surprise Li Fan slightly, then the existence of the Reverse Time Boat made Li Fan's heart tremble immensely. Li Fan believed in the true existence of the [Reverse Time Boat] treasure more than anyone else present. Not to mention Li Fan himself possessing the extraordinary treasure [True Return], just the [Kun Gan Bone Hand] he saw in the Xuanhuang Realm indicated that the Immortals of old had already grasped some divine abilities related to [Time].

"However, even if one can reverse the flow of time, the descent of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation is a general trend. Just like the earth, if the west is higher than the east, then the rivers will mostly flow from west to east into the sea. Even if one can repeatedly return to the source of the river and start anew, they cannot change the outcome of eventually flowing into the sea."

"In reality, it means that if the true cause of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation's outbreak is never found, even repeatedly reversing time will be futile. Moreover, traveling against the River of Time will surely come at a very high price. It is probably possible once or twice, but not three times."

After this period of contemplation, Li Fan also understood the fundamental difference between his [True Return] treasure and the treasure that reverses time.

"When true becomes false, and false becomes true."

"Creating things from nothingness with a single thought."

"Even the concept of time exists because it exists."

"Using water flowing east as an analogy, my [True Return] is like being able to arbitrarily alter the land, and even the sky."

"Not only can it make all rivers flow backward, but it is also possible for the water on the ground to surge upwards towards the heavens."

"Isn't this precisely corresponding to the so-called great freedom, great ease, and great liberation?"

Although Li Fan already knew of the impending doom of the mortal world, he did not feel much fear. This was precisely because he believed that with [True Return], he possessed the power to rewrite everything. After witnessing the scene of the doomsday countdown jumping millions of times, Li Fan became even more certain of his judgment. If there was truly a method of great freedom and escape in the world, it was likely only [True Return].

Dao Yuan's words, however, awakened a hidden worry deep within Li Fan's heart. The scene of True Immortals silently waiting in the Xuanhuang Realm that he saw in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea seemed to indicate that the Immortals of the past already knew of the existence of [True Return]. Just like the Immortal Hunters today, they had set a trap in the Xuanhuang Realm long ago. However, for some unknown reason, True Return was delayed for a long time, allowing Li Fan to ultimately escape a catastrophe.

Although it was just a speculation by Li Fan, after hearing the rumors of the [Reverse Time Boat] and the third refuge method today, Li Fan seemed to have thought of a possibility, and his mind became extremely solemn.

"The mortal world is probably a giant Xuanhuang Realm."

"Just like everything that happened in the Xuanhuang Realm. When disaster strikes, some choose to flee at the first sign, some choose to stand up and resolutely seek a way to save the world."

"And some people just give up and live in vain."

"Indeed, there is nothing new under the sun. The secrets I thought I had, were probably not secrets at all."

"It's just that the people who knew them are no longer around."

Li Fan never underestimated the power of Immortals. Especially True Immortals who could cross possibilities.

"If one day, I leave the [Primordial] possibility and go to another world, I must be even more cautious."

Dao Yuan's words stirred Li Fan's thoughts, making him restless. Fortunately, the reactions of everyone else were not much better, so he did not reveal any flaws.

"Alright, let's get back to the main topic. Just received news, our target, that True Immortal, has attained Dao through [Eradicate]."

"What is [Eradicate]?"

"It is the inability to see. We must guard against it."

Dao Yuan said, his gaze sweeping towards the distance.

Chapter 1448: Xi Yi Enters the Profound Coffin

"PERHAPS that True Immortal has already stealthily lurked nearby..." Dao Yuan's words caused everyone to become nervous, and they quickly snapped back from the ethereal legends of refuge. Unlike the previous trials, this was the first time they were truly facing a True Immortal. People could die. Under the pressure of life and death, the new Immortal Hunters quickly took action, cooperating and preparing. Although it was their first time, and only information transmission and explanation were provided without practical guidance, everyone was an elite among the cultivators of the Shining Star Sea, and they proceeded in an orderly manner.

The first thing Immortal Hunters needed to do to supplement Immortals was to strengthen the local Dao Net and then use the Dao Net to conceal themselves. If the entire Dao Net was fixed onto the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth by an invisible giant hand and four supporting pillars, then in the remote and weak areas of the Dao Net in the Shining Star Sea, the Immortal Hunters needed to act as nails themselves to further stabilize the Dao Net. This would allow the Dao Net to draw upon more power in the upcoming battle.

It was said that the seasoned Immortal Hunters of the organization cooperated skillfully, reinforcing and sealing areas of the Dao Net within moments. Compared to them, these newcomers appeared somewhat flustered. Especially when it came to selecting candidates for the role of temporary "nails," disputes arose. Normally, for efficiency, it would be natural to choose those with the deepest understanding of the Dao Net. However, everyone had only just met and did not know each other. The rankings announced earlier were merely the final results based on comprehensive performance in Dao, martial prowess, and life, not solely based on knowledge of the Dao Net.

Furthermore, by collectively reinforcing the Dao Net and personally entering it, it was like bathing and immersing oneself in the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth, offering infinite benefits. Therefore, who among the ambitious would be willing to yield? Even Dao Yuan, who ranked first, was fine claiming one spot for himself. But to direct and decide all the candidates was impossible. However, there wasn't much time left for the new Immortal Hunters to prepare. With every passing moment, their tension grew.

Finally, someone chose to back down. "Ma Tiande" cupped his fists, his expression at ease. "Everyone, as the saying goes, 'He who knows others is wise, but he who knows himself is enlightened.' The reason I ranked fifth is mostly due to my performance in the martial prowess trial. I will not compete for this!" In this calm manner, he yielded a position as a "nail."

Everyone looked at Li Fan, who was "noble and upright," their expressions changing subtly. Inspired by Li Fan, some cultivators also voluntarily ceded their opportunity. Soon, the candidates for the eight nail positions were decided. To Li Fan's surprise, the second-ranked cultivator among the new Immortal Hunters, the purple-robed female cultivator who wielded three long swords against the True Immortal, also voluntarily gave up the chance to become a Dao Nail. The purple-robed female cultivator was named Jin Changyue. She still kept her eyes closed, saying serenely, "I care more about using my three swords to personally kill the True Immortal." The three long swords, following Jin Changyue's words, emitted buzzing sounds.

With the personnel selected, everyone quickly and solemnly began to reinforce the local Dao Net according to what they had learned. Eight figures formed a circle, facing each other. The other Immortal Hunters surrounded them and sent out Dao Net commands one by one. Each command was like tightening the strings of the Dao, causing the eight figures to gradually dim, as if they were merging into the world. But everyone could feel the imperceptible changes occurring in this world.

A powerful and dark shadow had appeared. Though extremely hidden, it resonated with the Dao Net commands issued by everyone. The entire Dao Net reinforcement and connection process lasted for ninety-nine breaths, strictly speaking, barely meeting the passing standard for beginners' first practice. The figures of the eight cultivators serving as Dao Nails also returned to normal. However, they all appeared somewhat dazed, with a hint of surprise mixed in. They seemed to still be immersed in the experience of entering the Dao Net. Li Fan looked at the eight individuals and sensed that they had become significantly different compared to before.

"Within this small world, these eight individuals can wield Dao Net power equivalent to that of a True Immortal. Eight True Immortals working together..." "It seems the future [Eradicate] Immortal is in dire straits." Li Fan secretly assessed the Dao Nails before him. Although they possessed power comparable to True Immortals, in terms of sensory perception, they were still mortals. Their [Domain] height had not changed. It was merely that a corner of the Great Dao, previously floating in the sky, had descended and was now under their control. The eight Dao Nails acted as the main force for hunting the True Immortal, while the others served as support and supplements.

With the battlefield prepared, the next step was to erect a barrier, allowing the True Immortal to enter but not leave. With the cooperation of the Dao Net, this was incredibly simple. The seemingly ordinary void, in reality, had boundaries that were constantly in a state of potential disappearance. Just like the High Wall that contained the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, the concept of "front" disappeared, and the path ahead was no longer visible.

"This is one of the Immortal Hunter organization's most important trump cards. Its repeated successful hunts of True Immortals owe much to this method, known as the [Immortal Capture Cage]." "The disappearance of existence and concepts, perhaps the inspiration came from the Dao Annihilation Tribulation..." Li Fan muttered instructions, cooperating seamlessly with everyone else, issuing commands and forming the Immortal Capture Cage.

Simultaneously, he secretly recorded the subtle fluctuations of the Dao Net. To others, the Dao Net fluctuations were both imperceptible and extremely complex. Even if one was personally involved as a spellcaster, it would be impossible to record them all at once. The so-called "fluctuations" were strictly speaking, subtle changes like ripples generated by the self-operation of the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth, originating from the Dao Net. Only those with a deep understanding of the "Dao" could sense their existence at close range. The Dao Net commands were composed of countless Dao Origin symbols. The Immortal Hunters present cooperated with each other. In every breath, an unknown number of commands were issued. Such a massive amount of data, even a Nameless True Immortal might not be able to grasp it at a glance.

But Li Fan did not need to identify or memorize them. The miniature Dao Net in his divine sense acted like a mirror, perfectly reflecting the current fluctuations within the Dao Net. Even though Li Fan could not fully decipher the principles of these fluctuations yet, it did not prevent him from "copying" and "pasting" them first. "This is the power of [Spiritual Manifestation of Thought], reflecting the Great Dao." "It can do what the nameless cannot." Stealing a divine ability, Li Fan felt a secret satisfaction in his heart. He looked forward even more to his upcoming infiltration journey into Immortal Hunting.

A great hunting net had been secretly cast. The new Immortal Hunters had completed all preliminary preparations and were hidden around the fabricated World-Crossing Profound Coffin, waiting for the Eradicate Immortal to fall into the trap.

Everyone's spiritual senses were connected to the Dao Net, enabling communication. "Everyone, quickly look! What is that phenomenon?" In the real void, there was no movement whatsoever. However, the reinforced Dao Net in this starscape began to distort inexplicably. And this distortion was rapidly approaching the World-Crossing Profound Coffin! "Although they cannot be seen, they inevitably leave traces in the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth! Just like an invisible monster leaving footprints in the snow.
