Brothers, the True Immortal has taken the bait!" Everyone's hearts were filled with excitement, but also with tension.

"Should we act now?" "No hurry, let's wait. Wait until he fully reveals himself. In any case, this World-Crossing Profound Coffin cannot be moved by him, and he can only lie within its rumored refuge method." Dao Yuan said with great composure. Everyone nodded in agreement. The distorting power, moving within the Dao Net, soon approached the Profound Coffin. After observing it for a while, it seemed to be trying to move the Profound Coffin. However, although the Profound Coffin was a replica from the Shining Star Sea, it still possessed certain mystical characteristics of the true Profound Coffin. It seemed to not exist in this world, and any force applied to it was completely in vain, like drawing water with a bamboo basket. The Profound Coffin remained unmoved.

Although the attempt at the distorting power failed, it did not get angry but instead seemed pleased. It stood in place, and in the distance, larger distorting fluctuations rapidly approached. "No! This power is not from one True Immortal, but two?" Through their actions in the Dao Net, the degree of distortion of the bent Dao strings, the new Immortal Hunters quickly determined that in addition to the Eradicate Immortal, there was another True Immortal who had entered the net! They were together, almost as one. Ordinary methods, even if they were right before their eyes, might not be able to detect them. Only through the traces left in the Dao Net could their existence be discerned.

"Everyone, do not panic. This is a great thing! Capturing one is still capturing, and capturing two is also capturing. I didn't expect us to achieve such merit in our first mission as Immortal Hunters!" The speaker was Jiang Yuming, who ranked third. Empowered by the Dao Net, he was full of confidence. Facing the unexpected two True Immortals, he was unfazed. Dao Yuan also spoke, "However, we cannot be careless. Although this was a weak area of the Dao Net before, they were able to deceive the Dao Net's perception, which shows the extraordinary nature of these two." "To see without seeing, and to hear without hearing. I think the other one mastered the Dao of [Serenity]. Only with Serenity and Eradication together can they deceive the Dao Net."

Although a variable had appeared, everyone was not in a panic. They silently communicated and made tactical adjustments, waiting for the two True Immortals to enter the coffin. Amidst the widespread attention, the Profound Coffin's lid moved, emitting a heavy and decaying sound. Like a bronze gate sealed for a long time, it creaked open. The bent Dao strings instantly returned to normal. The new Immortal Hunters, however, all received notifications simultaneously. Inside the supposed bait Profound Coffin, two figures had indeed entered.

"Act!" Just as Dao Yuan shouted, another voice rang out, interrupting him. "Wait!" It was "Ma Tiande"! Seeing someone opposing him, Dao Yuan frowned slightly. However, Li Fan quickly and solemnly explained, "Brother Dao, you previously said that the Profound Coffin requires a specific method to activate. Let's wait a little longer." "Perhaps they are also bait, who knows?"

Li Fan's words caused everyone to notice something was amiss. They all looked at the Profound Coffin again. After the fluctuations entered the Profound Coffin, there was no further sound. It seemed to be waiting for something. "Indeed, there is something strange." "If it were truly the Serenity and Eradication True Immortals themselves avoiding calamity, they should have eagerly verified it the moment they entered the Profound Coffin. How could there be no movement yet..." Jin Changyue said solemnly. "Won't the fake Profound Coffin show a flaw? If the Serenity and Eradication True Immortals see through it, won't they be alerted and flee?"

"Don't worry. Although the Profound Coffin is fake, it is real. Except for its inability to cross worlds, it is virtually indistinguishable from the real World-Crossing Profound Coffin," said a cultivator who had never spoken before. This cultivator was named Nangong Hongzhao, and his background was somewhat unclear to everyone. However, he spoke with such certainty, implying he had his reasons. Now was not the time to investigate. Everyone held their breath and waited.

At this moment, Nangong Hongzhao spoke again. "It is said that every time the Profound Coffin activates world-crossing, its location changes. This is also why the Serenity and Eradication True Immortals are currently only probing and have not truly activated it yet." "It can be confirmed that what is currently in the coffin is just bait. They are unwilling to waste this great opportunity." As if to confirm Nangong Hongzhao's words, not far away, another cluster of distorted fluctuations appeared in the Dao Net. It was identical to the degree of Dao string distortion caused by the previous crushing. As if replaying the scene, they entered the Profound Coffin again. As soon as they entered the coffin, a supremely mysterious sound emanated from within. It sounded like faint singing, or perhaps some solemn and sacred chanting.

"Act!" Dao Yuan shouted again. The Profound Coffin's lid slammed shut. At the same time, the Immortal Capture Cage silently descended, completely sealing off this star sea. Within the Profound Coffin, it seemed they did not notice the external changes. They likely assumed the closing of the coffin was a normal occurrence. The singing continued unabated.

Li Fan listened, memorizing all the pitch variations. At the same time, a thought crossed his mind: "This rhythm seems somewhat similar to the scriptures for avoiding calamity passed down by the Grand Master." "Could it be that the phantom beside the Grand Master has some connection with the Nameless True Immortals who created the World-Crossing Profound Coffin?" Li Fan suddenly thought. The previously unknown cultivator of the Xuanhuang Realm, listening beside the phantom, gave birth to the Ten Great Sects of the Immortal Path. The Grand Master, already at the Half-Immortal stage, still sat by the phantom without leaving, even clearly imitating the Grand Master's words and actions towards the phantom storyteller. "Could it be that this phantom was left behind by a Nameless True Immortal who departed back then?" "Perhaps it originally possessed other spirituality and divine abilities. But the Nameless True Immortal has already departed to another possibility through the Profound Coffin, hence what remains is merely an empty shell of light and shadow."

While Li Fan's thoughts churned, a strange development occurred within the arena. The Serenity and Eradication True Immortals hid within the Profound Coffin and refused to come out, making it difficult for everyone to break into the coffin. They only intended to wait for them to discover the Profound Coffin was illusory and then ambush them when they emerged. But they never anticipated...

As the singing within the Profound Coffin grew louder, the Profound Coffin also emitted bursts of dazzling seven-colored halos. These halos were elusive and unpredictable, but once they appeared, they showed no sign of extinguishing. The Immortal Hunter crowd gradually became uneasy.

The seven-colored halos suddenly erupted, completely engulfing the Profound Coffin. When the crowd looked again... The fake World-Crossing Profound Coffin, along with the Serenity and Eradication True Immortals, had vanished into thin air!

Chapter 1449: The Case of the Suspicious Saint Merchant

A strange silence descended upon the Immortal Capture scene. The crowd exchanged glances, but no one dared to speak first.

After a long while, someone hesitantly asked, "Brother Dao, the information we received stated that the World-Crossing Profound Coffin... was fake, correct?"

Hearing this, everyone looked at Dao Yuan with uncertainty. Dao Yuan, usually so composed, now showed a flicker of panic in his eyes.

However, he cleared his throat and said grimly, "Don't lose your composure! Perhaps the Profound Coffin was merely concealed by the Serenity and Eradication True Immortals through some unfathomable means, and is still in its original location. We..."

Before he could finish, a panicked voice interrupted him. "How is that possible? The fake Profound Coffin actually managed to achieve world-crossing?!"

As he spoke, this person, disregarding all consequences, flew rapidly towards the Profound Coffin's original location. It was Nangong Hongzhao, who had been so certain of the Profound Coffin's authenticity!

"This is bad!" All the new Immortal Hunters' faces turned pale. If Dao Yuan's judgment was correct, Nangong Hongzhao's actions could potentially expose everyone lying in ambush, not to mention facing the two True Immortals and risking death.

Everyone wanted to stop Nangong Hongzhao's reckless act. However, this person's movements were elusive and incredibly swift. In the blink of an eye, he arrived at his destination.

The crowd held their breath.

Fortunately, the anticipated tragic scene did not occur. However, the expressions of the crowd did not lighten; instead, they grew more distraught.

"The World-Crossing Profound Coffin is genuinely gone."

"Along with it, the two Serenity and Eradication True Immortals have also disappeared."

The gravity of the situation was clearly beyond the control of this group of new Immortal Hunters. Thus, Dao Yuan decisively chose to report the incident through the Dao Net.

The response from the other end of the Dao Net was also beyond his imagination.

"What? The Immortal Bait is gone? This is impossible!"

"According to the Dao Net's observations, it was still in its original location!"

"Where is Yan Xuantai? Why isn't he contacting me!"

The furious voice reached everyone's ears through the ripples of the Dao Net, traveling from the distant center of the Shining Star Sea. By the time the last word was spoken, the owner of the voice had already arrived.

It was a short old man, no more than three feet tall. His silvery beard and hair were even longer than his body, trailing like flowing clouds beneath his feet.

The old man's face was terrifyingly grim, and his gaze swept over everyone. All the new Immortal Hunters instinctively lowered their heads, not daring to meet the old man's eyes.

"Who is this..." Li Fan also felt the power of the old man before him. With the old man's breaths, the invisible Dao strings in the heavens and earth subtly fluctuated. The local Dao Net even became clearer and more stable due to the old man's arrival.

In Ma Tiande's memories, he had seen this old man once from afar. It was this old man who presided over the conference when he received the position of Dao Net operator.

"One of the Directors of the Shining Star Sea Governing Council, Nangong Fusheng."

Nangong Fusheng instantly appeared at the original location of the Immortal Bait Profound Coffin. Seeing Nangong Hongzhao, who was babbling incoherently on the spot, Nangong Fusheng roared, "Useless!

"With a slap, he sent Nangong Hongzhao flying out. Leaving him to drift uncontrollably in the star sea, Nangong Fusheng's rage gradually subsided as he carefully examined his surroundings.

Ripples spread out in circles originating from Nangong Fusheng. The Immortal Hunters watching from afar felt as if the entire world had turned into a raging sea under a violent storm, roaring and surging. The crashing waves seemed capable of swallowing them whole at any moment, and they could only struggle to maintain their stability by relying on the power of the Dao Net.

The Dao Net rippled incessantly.

Finally, Nangong Fusheng concluded by pulling a black, seven-colored, streaming long nail from the void with his right hand.

As the nail was removed, Nangong Fusheng laughed instead of getting angry. "Yan Xuantai, what ingenious means! To be able to deceive the Dao Net and pass undetected!

The new Immortal Hunters stared intently at the black, seven-colored nail in Nangong Fusheng's hand. Their eyes flickered. In their previous understanding, the Dao Net was equivalent to the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth. The power of Heaven and Earth was invincible in the world, and they could only find ways to control it.

But now, in their very first mission after officially joining the Immortal Hunter organization, they encountered someone who could deceive the Dao Net. They even staged a scene of a golden cicada shedding its shell before their very eyes.

"Who exactly is this Yan Xuantai?" The question inevitably arose in everyone's minds. The fake Profound Coffin had actually taken away the two True Immortals who were considered prey. And this involved a conspiracy from within the Shining Star Sea Immortal Hunter organization. This was certainly no small matter.

Soon, in addition to Nangong Fusheng, three other cultivators arrived one after another. Even though they concealed their figures and restrained their auras, their arrival still stirred up huge waves in the local Dao Net. The new Immortal Hunters could only tremble.

When asked, they did not dare to conceal anything and told the truth.

"Let's go back first."

"This matter is not as simple as it seems."

Nangong Fusheng said gravely to the three figures. He no longer bothered to conceal anything from the crowd. His silvery beard grew longer, enveloping all the Immortal Hunters.

As they were about to leave, Li Fan vaguely heard Nangong Hongzhao's anxious cry from outside the silver beard's embrace: "Third Uncle, wait for me!

The silver beard enveloped them and then dispersed. In the blink of an eye, everyone was brought back to the center of the Shining Star Sea. They were then led into pitch-black isolation cells respectively for a second round of questioning.

Since they were genuinely unaware newcomers, the organization did not make things difficult for them. After a few routine questions, it was over. However, there was no intention of releasing them. They were still arranged in countless pitch-black cells, like death rows.

Although everyone's freedom of movement was not restricted, it was limited to this area. They could not leave. Endless darkness gradually consumed the minds of everyone.

Initially, the new Immortal Hunters still held onto hope, believing that the imprisonment would soon end. But as days turned into weeks, the organization seemed to have completely forgotten them. After placing them there, there was not the slightest sound from them.

Gradually, everyone's mindset began to change.

"I understand. Hunting True Immortals, the disappearance of the Profound Coffin, these are all part of the Immortal Hunter assessment. We are still within the assessment! I must pull myself together and not fall into despair!

"I had a bright future, but ended up in such a situation. My life is probably ruined.

"The Profound Coffin disappeared with two True Immortals. Such a major event, someone must be held responsible. Could it be that they are using us as scapegoats?

...

Most people lived in constant fear and uncertainty. In such circumstances, only true prodigies could maintain their composure.

Li Fan sensed the three sword intents from the cell next to him that had not ceased. He nodded slightly. "Since being imprisoned, Jin Changyue has been nurturing this sword intent. Facing unjust imprisonment, her resentment naturally arises. This is the best time to nurture a sword with intent.

"However, for this sword intent to reach perfection, it requires sacrificing someone as the sword's master.

Besides Jin Changyue, Dao Yuan was also quite patient. After some initial fluctuations in his aura, he was like a hidden dragon in the abyss, quietly waiting for his opportunity.

As for Li Fan, he naturally felt no impatience. However, he still pretended to be anxious and desperate, constantly revealing a facade of despair. In reality, he was constantly recalling the scene of the Serenity and Eradication True Immortals activating the World-Crossing Profound Coffin and leaving.

The Profound Xuan music chanted by the Serenity and Eradication True Immortals gradually faded in Li Fan's memory over time. Even the recording by the Dao Transformation Stone faded similarly. Li Fan could only repeat it over and over to deepen his impression. However, the general trend of complete fading was ultimately unchangeable.

Li Fan had also tried to use the miniature Dao Net in his divine sense to replicate the fluctuations at that time. However, the agitation of the Great Dao caused by the Profound Xuan music occurred entirely within the Profound Coffin. Li Fan could only observe it from afar through the Dao Net and could not accurately record it.

"That Profound Coffin, called fake, is actually real."

"Except for its inability to cross worlds, it is virtually indistinguishable from the real Profound Coffin..."

Li Fan remembered Nangong Hongzhao's words and a thought struck him. Although Nangong Hongzhao was not brought back by Nangong Fusheng earlier, after a few days, he was also thrown into this black prison. However, he did not show any anxiety or worry, but instead looked dejected, as if he had botched something.

For the past few days, he had been lying lazily on the ground. Closing his eyes as if in meditation.

Li Fan quietly approached him. "Brother Nangong, there's something I've been wanting to say for a long time.

"It's like a fishbone stuck in my throat; I must say it!

Perhaps because of "Ma Tiande's" previous performance, he had left a slightly positive impression on Nangong Hongzhao's mind. Nangong Hongzhao suddenly opened his eyes and glanced at Li Fan lightly. Then, without saying anything, he closed them again.

Li Fan knew that since he didn't explicitly refuse, it meant he agreed. He immediately transmitted his voice again, asking, "What exactly happened with the fake Profound Coffin suddenly becoming real? Does Brother Nangong know any inside information.

Nangong Hongzhao said exasperatedly, "Don't you see I was swept away for 180,000 li like garbage? What inside information could I possibly know.

Li Fan quickly consoled him, "Brother Nangong, please don't say that. That was Elder Nangong, the Director. Many people wish they could be swept away like that, but they don't have the chance.

Hearing this, Nangong Hongzhao opened his eyes again. He squinted and looked at Li Fan thoughtfully. "I almost forgot, you were originally a Dao Net operator, and somewhat originated from the Governing Council. No wonder you know the power of my Third Uncle.

Li Fan nodded repeatedly. "Of course, of course.

Seeing Nangong Hongzhao's attitude gradually soften, Li Fan quickly got to the point. "These past few days, I've had nothing to do but think. I've come up with a few possibilities regarding this fake coffin incident.

"First, the fake coffin was crafted to imitate the real one. Except for certain necessary conditions, it was indistinguishable from the real World-Crossing Profound Coffin. And the Serenity and Eradication True Immortals who traveled across the star sea happened to possess these necessary conditions. Thus, they naturally used the Profound Coffin to escape to another world.

"But there's one point that doesn't make sense. It was only meant to be bait to lure out True Immortals. As long as it looked convincing, there was no need to make it so real. So, I suspect that Yan Xuantai secretly made some adjustments, or used a trick of replacing the genuine with the fake, replacing it with another coffin that was closer to the real one. And he was hiding inside, waiting for the Serenity and Eradication True Immortals to enter, explain the situation, and then escape with them.

"But..." Li Fan paused. "I don't know who this Yan Xuantai is. Assigning him to secretly monitor and protect the new Immortal Hunters during their first hunt, such a task of moderate importance, his identity and status should not be very high. Yet he possesses such a treasure?

"Also, there's that black seven-colored nail that can deceive the Dao Net. I can't figure it out!

Li Fan sighed. "We seem to be trapped in this black prison indefinitely. Brother Nangong, can you enlighten me? Don't worry, I absolutely won't spread a word.

Li Fan vowed earnestly.

After a long silence, Nangong Hongzhao's voice was faint. "Your thoughts are quite meticulous. In some aspects, they align with my own guesses. However, I know some inside information that you are unaware of.

"It's not really a secret, so I don't mind telling you. Yan Xuantai was originally a member of the [Sacred Merchants] and joined Immortal Hunting. A hundred years ago, the entire Sacred Merchant organization mysteriously vanished from the Shining Star Sea, leaving only some survivors and discarded pawns.

"We originally thought he had severed all ties with the Sacred Merchants long ago. I never expected..." Nangong Hongzhao snorted coldly. "Speaking of which, the Sacred Merchants were once one of the founders of Immortal Hunting. Furthermore, many of their Immortal Hunting techniques were proactively provided by them. And Sacred Merchant members disliked conflict and power, focusing only on the goal of hunting Immortals. Therefore, they held a transcendent status in the early Immortal Hunter organization. After the Sacred Merchants' abrupt departure and unknown whereabouts, Yan Xuantai, as a discarded pawn of the Sacred Merchants, was not excessively targeted. He was even assigned an important position...

Li Fan's heart stirred upon hearing the words [Sacred Merchants]. He continued to ask, "According to Brother Nangong, the Sacred Merchants were a matter of a hundred years ago. In a hundred years, our Dao Net techniques have progressed immensely. Even if Yan Xuantai is a Sacred Merchant, how could he possess a method to deceive the Dao Net? Could it be that the Sacred Merchants were so far ahead of us? Or...

Li Fan seemed to realize something and suddenly lowered his voice. "Could it be that Yan Xuantai secretly re-established contact with the Sacred Merchants recently, and thus found a way to escape?

"But this still doesn't make sense. Unless the fake coffin didn't escape to another world, but to another star sea. Where the Sacred Merchants are located?

Nangong Hongzhao shook his head slightly. "That is beyond my knowledge. This matter is complex and unclear. Yan Xuantai is eccentric and usually acts alone. Investigating him is somewhat difficult.

"However, you can rest assured. We will not be imprisoned forever. When there is a general conclusion to this matter, we will be released.

Nangong Hongzhao comforted him kindly.

Chapter 1450: Great Sun Flame Body Refining

LI FAN was startled at first, then overjoyed. "If anyone else told me this, I would think they were talking nonsense out of prolonged confinement in the black prison. But Brother Nangong, if you say so..." "I will have no fear!"

Facing Li Fan's flattery, Nangong Hongzhao did not overtly respond, but the faint smile that inadvertently appeared on his face betrayed his inner feelings.

Using this chance encounter as an opportunity, Li Fan and Nangong Hongzhao's relationship gradually grew closer. Li Fan quietly inquired about some information regarding the Nangong family. While not top-secret, it was knowledge that individuals below a certain level in the Shining Star Sea would absolutely not have the chance to know.

For instance, Nangong Fusheng's name, "Fusheng," meant that before Nangong Fusheng, the Nangong family indeed had an existence comparable to a "Sage." This person was named Nangong Fusheng, and his contribution included the initial establishment of the Dao Net and the protection of all people. However, Fusheng had long since vanished from the mortal world, and only Fusheng carried out duties on his behalf.

Another example was Nangong family's supreme treasure, rumored to have been obtained from the joint hunt and capture of a Nameless True Immortal. It was the clothing worn by the Nameless True Immortal. Putting aside the preciousness of the material, the divine effect of the Nameless True Immortal's clothes was actually transformed from the Great Dao fused by the Nameless True Immortal. It was just that after the Nameless True Immortal was captured, the clothes were forcibly stripped from him. If a cultivator were fortunate enough to wear these clothes and could withstand it, it would be like falling into the Sea of Great Dao, surrounded by the essence of the Great Dao. The efficiency of comprehending the Great Dao would be even greater than being within the Dao Net. However, the only drawback was that the high efficiency was only reflected in the corresponding Dao path of the Nameless True Immortal.

Nangong Hongzhao also gradually discovered that Li Fan's understanding and cognition of the Dao Net were even superior to his own. In just a few words, he often benefited greatly from Li Fan. After all, most of these new Immortal Hunters came from prominent backgrounds, and none of them were willing to concede to another. And someone like Ma Tiande, who ranked high in the assessment but was extremely humble, was very rare. "This person is worth befriending," Nangong Hongzhao thought to himself.

Time passed as the two conversed day by day.

As if confirming Nangong Hongzhao's words, after being confined in the black prison for a full ninety days, they were finally released. "Everything you said and did in the black prison has been recorded." "This is the final stage of your induction assessment." "The previous rankings will be slightly adjusted." "The official appointments for Immortal Hunting will be based on the new list." "Rest for now and await further notice."

Upon release, the new Immortal Hunters heard these words. Some were overjoyed, glad they had maintained restraint. Others showed changing expressions, regretting their past actions.

Of course, true prodigies like Nangong Hongzhao, Dao Yuan, and Jin Changyue were clearly not fooled by such rhetoric. Jin Changyue let out a cold snort, and the three long swords behind her simultaneously emitted fierce sword cries. It took considerable effort to suppress the overflowing killing intent.

Nangong Hongzhao and Li Fan exchanged glances and quietly left together.

Arriving at Nangong's resting place, it was a courtyard carved out within the Immortal Hunter organization. The Immortal Hunter organization was located within the Dao Net and did not exist in the real world. This courtyard was also manifested by the power of the Dao Net. With the owner's authority, its scope would continuously increase. Furthermore, it could change its appearance at will according to thought. Since it was formed by the power of the Dao Net, living within it allowed one to constantly sense the power of the Dao Net, making cultivation countless times more efficient than in the outer star sea.

The courtyard's appearance, under Nangong Hongzhao's manipulation, transformed into a winding cave in the blink of an eye. Li Fan followed Nangong into the depths of the cave. Below a massive hollow was scorching magma.

"Congratulations, brother. Your ranking has further improved, reaching the top three. It seems you will be assigned an important task." Nangong Hongzhao said with a smile, teasingly.

As he spoke, he actually leaped down into the magma. Immersed in the extremely hot magma, Nangong Hongzhao let out a groan. "I didn't expect Brother Nangong to have such a hobby." Li Fan stared at the scene below, not jumping in.

Unlike the illusions manifested in the Xuanhuang Realm's Heavenly Xuan Mirror's living space, everything in this Dao Net courtyard was real, just like all things in the world, it was a manifestation of the Great Dao. The cultivators of the Shining Star Sea focused only on Dao Net perception and neglected their own cultivation. "Ma Tiande," obviously did not possess the ability to survive in such intense magma.

"Heh heh, you don't understand. This is Great Sun Flame Molten Rock. Theoretically, only by collectively destroying ninety-nine cultivation worlds' Great Suns and then refining them with Lunar power could even a drop be formed." "But now, with the miraculous and unfathomable power of the Dao Net, all the tedious intermediate steps are skipped, and it is created from nothing! This kind of treasure, which was once only enjoyed by True Immortals, can now be freely enjoyed by us mortals!"

As Nangong Hongzhao spoke, he lifted a drop of Great Sun Flame Molten Rock with his hand. Li Fan saw that the crimson viscous liquid was slowly penetrating Nangong Hongzhao's body through his pores. His body turned red, as if ignited. But Nangong Hongzhao acted as if he were fine, even taking a sip with relish.

Li Fan's eyes narrowed. Even observing from afar, he could tell the terrifying destructive power of this so-called Great Sun Flame Molten Rock. The bathwater below, Nangong Hongzhao, could probably turn the Xuanhuang Realm into scorched earth in an instant. "Even if I were the main body, without spiritual energy protection, falling into this Flame Molten Rock would likely result in instant annihilation. Yet Nangong Hongzhao can achieve this with his physical body alone..."

Li Fan suddenly recalled the scene where Nangong Hongzhao was slapped flying by the furious Nangong Fusheng. When Nangong Fusheng descended, the surrounding starscape seemed to immediately fall into a violent tsunami, with waves churning. And that slap, he clearly hadn't held back. Such immense force would likely severely injure even a True Immortal. But Nangong Hongzhao acted as if he were fine and could even keep up and return at high speed. "Body refinement technique." Li Fan thought thoughtfully.

Nangong Hongzhao's subsequent words also confirmed Li Fan's guess. "In the Shining Star Sea, Dao Net power is paramount." "Such a magnificent and great creation allows mortals to manipulate the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth like the Immortals of the past. However, compared to Immortals, we mortals are still too insignificant. Like a child wielding a sharp blade, they might fail to harm the enemy and end up harming themselves. And the methods of Immortals are strictly forbidden by the Governing Council. Therefore..."

Nangong Hongzhao took a deep breath, and all the pores on his body opened, like countless gaping mouths, drawing in all the Great Sun Flame Molten Rock in the pool. "Refreshing!" At this moment, Nangong Hongzhao's face was completely dyed red. He let out a muffled groan and exhaled a long, scorching breath. There was no spiritual energy fluctuation on his body, only by vibrating at an extremely fast speed did he digest the Great Sun Flame Molten Rock. Nangong Hongzhao's complexion slowly returned to normal.

He leaped up, came to Li Fan's side, and then continued, "Dao Yuan, Jin Changyue, and the others, like me, all have unique body refinement methods. Don't be deceived by their apparently frail appearance!" "This is the biggest difference between the esteemed families of the Shining Star Sea and someone like you, brother." Nangong Hongzhao patted Li Fan's shoulder meaningfully. "Being a nail, integrated into the Dao Net. The stronger the body becomes, the more Dao Net strings it can withstand. Dao Yuan and the others have received special training since childhood and are already thoroughly refined. As for Brother Ma..." "Even if you can now wield the power of the Dao Net to a certain extent, what materials and methods should be used for body refinement to be most effective, and yet not harm yourself. You must explore it all on your own. How can you compare to our inherited legacies passed down for generations?"

Nangong Hongzhao had said all he needed to say, and Li Fan understood his meaning. He bowed deeply, his expression stern. "Brother Nangong, please teach me. Whether I succeed or not, I will surely repay you greatly in the future. If you have any commands, I will obey even unto death!"

Nangong Hongzhao helped Li Fan up. "Brother, we are very compatible, please don't say that. However, it's not that I'm being pretentious. You see, every body refinement technique today has been maximally extrapolated and tested with countless lives. It is indeed extremely precious." Li Fan nodded. "I understand this principle."

"You three talked for a long time in the black prison. I also learned quite a bit about you. You have already passed the best age for body tempering. Even with several times the effort, ordinary body refinement methods will have greatly reduced effects. However, your advantage lies in your unparalleled understanding of the Dao Net. Therefore..." Nangong Hongzhao examined Li Fan up and down again, then said softly, "This [Great Dao Descends Upon the Body Technique] is most suitable for you!"

Before Nangong Hongzhao could finish speaking, Li Fan raised his hand and stopped him. Li Fan asked with a solemn expression, "I suddenly thought, body refinement techniques are so precious. Brother Nangong, you are privately passing it to me..." "Will Senior Fusheng blame you?" "If so, I truly cannot accept."

Seeing Li Fan's sincere words, which did not seem like a refusal, Nangong Hongzhao was stunned on the spot. But soon, he recovered and waved his hand. "It's nothing. Although the technique is precious, its confidentiality level is not high. I'm only passing it to you alone, and Third Uncle will certainly not blame me." "Listen carefully..."

The cave formed by the Dao Net courtyard quietly closed off. Within it, Nangong Hongzhao fully imparted the [Great Dao Descends Upon the Body Technique] to Li Fan.

With Li Fan's experience, he quickly understood the origin of this technique. Without a doubt, this technique had the shadow of cultivation techniques. It involved visualizing the Great Dao of the world as a net, suppressing oneself. Using the weight of the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth to temper the physical body. During body refinement, in addition to increasing physical strength, it also deepened the intimacy and comprehension of the Great Dao. As Nangong Hongzhao said, it was an extremely miraculous and precious body refinement profound technique.

However, it also had its drawbacks. That was, the difficulty of cultivation was too high. One could already visualize the Great Dao descending upon their body, clearly indicating that their comprehension of the Great Dao had reached an extremely high realm, even surpassing ordinary Immortals. With such familiarity with the Great Dao, they could directly merge with the Great Dao and ascend to the Nameless realm. Why would they still need to slowly temper their physical bodies? Wasn't that putting the cart before the horse? "Only in the Shining Star Sea, covered by the Dao Net, could such a distorted and strange technique be born." "Firstly, by using the tangible object of the Dao Net to replace the intangible Great Dao of Heaven and Earth, the cultivation threshold was greatly lowered." "Secondly, the Shining Star Sea is a gathering place of the Immortal Realm and lower star seas after the Dao Annihilation Tribulation. True Immortals, and even Nameless True Immortals, gathered here. Only then could this Great Dao Descends Upon the Body Technique be deduced..."

Li Fan's mind was filled with countless thoughts, but it did not delay him from starting to practice this body refinement technique. Since he was already within the Dao Net, it naturally eliminated the complicated process of visualizing the Dao strings descending upon him as before. Suddenly, it felt as if heavy mountains were pressing down on his body. Li Fan stumbled and fell to the ground, his pores instantly erupting with a large amount of blood spray. It almost splashed onto Nangong Hongzhao, who was watching from the side, but he managed to block it in time.

Nangong Hongzhao's mouth twitched. Li Fan struggled to get up from the ground, tidied his disheveled appearance, and cupped his hands to Nangong Hongzhao somewhat weakly, saying, "Brother Nangong, please forgive my clumsiness. I didn't expect practicing this body refinement technique to be so difficult."

Nangong Hongzhao comforted him. "Brother Ma, remember to proceed steadily and not be greedy. It's normal to suffer a little. The hardships I endured in my childhood were a hundred times greater than what you are experiencing now!" "Brother Ma, although I have passed on the Great Dao Descends Upon the Body Technique to you, I cannot tell you how to practice it, related insights, or cultivation experience. All of this must be explored by yourself."

Li Fan clasped his fists. "I am already immensely grateful to receive such a divine technique. How could I dare to ask for more!" "I will not disturb Brother Nangong today. I will return to my courtyard to cultivate."

After some pleasantries, Li Fan bid farewell to Nangong Hongzhao and returned to his own courtyard. His official position was higher than Nangong Hongzhao's, but the area of his courtyard was even smaller than his. Li Fan did not mind and transformed the courtyard into the appearance of a mountain peak. He sat cross-legged and began to formally practice the [Great Dao Descends Upon the Body Technique].

The previous pathetic state in front of Nangong Hongzhao was, of course, intentional on Li Fan's part, merely an excuse to leave. With his exquisite perception of the Great Dao, his cultivation speed of this technique was likely far beyond Nangong's imagination. Moreover, Li Fan was not simply cultivating according to the instructions. Now, Li Fan was capable of modifying techniques based on his own special circumstances. "Great Dao descends upon the body." "And I already have a projection of the Great Dao in my heart." "Therefore..." "There is no need for the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth to descend. Simply by turning the Dao strings in my mind from虚 to 实, I can use the pressure of the Great Dao to temper my body." Li Fan narrowed his eyes, and the miniature Dao Net in his divine sense emitted faint rays of light.

Chapter 1451: Seeking the Creation Furnace Technique Again

"The Great Dao Descends Upon the Body Technique," apart from the comprehension of the Great Dao, the most difficult aspect of its cultivation lies in achieving a delicate balance between tempering the body with the pressure of the Great Dao and ensuring the body is not harmed.

Before the majestic Great Dao, the mortal body is a being far more minuscule than an ant.

While one can refine the body by leveraging the pressure of the Great Dao, the risk of being crushed into powder by the Great Dao is ever-present if one is not careful.

This is also why Nangong Hongzhao repeatedly cautioned Li Fan before imparting the technique, emphasizing the need for caution and gradual progress when cultivating this method.

In fact, for an ordinary person, without the experience and insights of cultivating the "Great Dao Descends Upon the Body Technique" from scratch, step by step, even the initial entry into this art would be exceedingly difficult.

However...

Li Fan is by no means ordinary.

Although the path of body refinement has vanished from the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan had already explored it.

Early on, after obtaining the "Celestial Physician Immortal Scripture" and integrating various texts, he devised a method to mobilize the body's hidden reserves and temper the flesh, naming it the "Fortune Furnace Technique."

This cultivation method was continuously enhanced as Li Fan's experience grew.

The integration of beast cauldrons, flesh and blood factories, and the "Heaven Mending Record" led to several iterations of the Fortune Furnace Technique.

But the limitations of the Xuanhuang Realm's world ultimately made it impossible to achieve the Dao.

Thus, Li Fan eventually turned towards the conventional method of ascending to immortality.

This "Fortune Furnace Technique," with its exceptionally domineering name, stagnated.

"Back then, in the Immortal Eradication Realm, within the Beast Taming Sect scenario, I used the body of Little Black, the Celestial Mandate Black Bird, and received guidance from Mr. Bai."

"The perfect version of the 'Fortune Furnace Technique.'"

"But due to the memory limitations of the Immortal Eradication Realm, I was never able to bring this perfect method back. And by the time my strength rapidly expanded, even surpassing Mr. Bai, whom I once considered merely in the Longevity realm, I became indifferent to this technique. However, I now know the secret history of Mr. Bai being corrupted by the Evil Su Bai from another possibility."

"Having obtained Evil Su Bai's memories, Mr. Bai's strength might still be at the Longevity realm, but his vision is likely beyond anyone trapped in the 'Primal' possibility. The imprinted projections left in the world also confirm this. Thus..."

"When I first encountered the perfect version of the 'Fortune Furnace Technique,' I was deeply shaken, as if I had truly glimpsed the secrets of the Great Dao. This was not due to my shallow understanding at the time due to my weak strength, but because this cultivation method is indeed that wondrous."

"It seems I need to make another trip, to investigate and reference it."

Five years have passed in the Shining Star Sea.

In the Xuanhuang Realm, only a little over ten days have passed.

Li Fan's true body is still deeply contemplating how to avoid the "Mind Manifestation of Divinity" from reflecting the Nameless True Immortal and making eye contact with it.

Sensing the experiences of his clone, his eyes suddenly flickered, revealing a look of surprise.

The Fortune Furnace Technique is a memory from long ago for Li Fan.

He never expected that after ascending to the Half-Immortal realm, he would have a moment to pursue it again.

"This also proves that my choice to give up at the time, and not insist on obtaining it immediately, was the right one. In the Immortal Eradication Realm, the more valuable something is, the harder it is to bring it into the real world. If the Fortune Furnace Technique is as wondrous as I imagine now, it might not be easy for me to take it out even now."

"I just don't know if my method of 'Mind Manifestation of Divinity' can bypass the memory erasure limitations of the Immortal Eradication Realm."

One's perspective on the same matter can yield vastly different conclusions depending on the circumstances.

Li Fan wished to re-explore the perfect version, the true "Fortune Furnace Technique."

However, since he already knew that Mr. Bai and the master of the Immortal Eradication Realm were extraordinary, Li Fan naturally needed to make further preparations.

For a long time, Li Fan was unwilling to personally step into the Immortal Eradication Realm. Even for the illusory trials inherited from the Xuanhuang Great Heavenly Venerable, Li Fan had others act on his behalf.

This was because his treasured item, "Return to Truth," was carried by him, and it seemed that beings from the Immortal Realm were already waiting there.

However, after Li Fan understood the method of "Mind Manifestation of Divinity" in this lifetime, things changed again.

"Initially, I rashly entered the Immortal Eradication Realm out of ignorance and boldness. But now, I have sufficient self-preservation power."

His divine sense retracted, and all converged into that miniature Dao Net.

Then, the Dao Net radiated thousands of lights, and from it, a new divine sense emerged.

However, everything contained within this divine sense was fabricated by Li Fan, used as a disguise.

To say fabricated, it was actually a worldline deduced by the Dao Transformation Stone, appearing almost real.

Apart from the fact that such a person did not exist in the world, everything else was the same as reality.

By adding another layer of disguise to his original identity.

This was Li Fan's temporary solution to reduce the possibility of being discovered by True Immortals within the Great Dao.

As expected, with the emergence of this disguised divine sense, Li Fan clearly felt that the gazes of the Nameless True Immortal projections within his miniature Dao Net, which were being mirrored, significantly decreased for no apparent reason.

The sense of urgent crisis dissipated, and Li Fan, as if hidden behind the scenes, concealed in the darkness, instantly relaxed.

Of course, this was merely a temporary solution, not a fundamental one.

This disguise could still work for now, but as Li Fan's "Mind Manifestation of Divinity" continued to grow, it would inevitably attract the attention of the Nameless True Immortals within the Great Dao again.

If, one day, the scale of Li Fan's projected Great Dao within his mind even surpassed the Dao Net of the Shining Star Sea, and he moved from behind the scenes to the forefront, it would definitely draw the attention of all the existing Nameless True Immortals.

Given Li Fan's caution in his actions, he would absolutely not take this step until he had absolute certainty of dealing with this crisis.

However, all of that was for later. The current Li Fan, after creating a disguise for his mind, had already entered the Immortal Eradication Realm.

As he had predicted, his fabricated life, due to the absence of practicing the "Xuanhuang Heart Refining Incantation," did not show the scene of "Ning Yuan retrieving the Longevity Fruit" when entering the Immortal Eradication Realm.

Li Fan directly committed suicide and exited the Immortal Eradication Realm.

Then, he modified the persona of the disguise.

After changing his life again, he added an experience of his own: "By chance, comprehended the Xuanhuang Heart Refining Incantation in the Body Purifying Spiritual Pool."

In the perception of the Immortal Eradication Realm, this disguise then seemed to truly become another person.

Without the time interval limitation for entering the Immortal Eradication Realm, he arrived again.

And experienced the scene of Ning Yuan retrieving the Longevity Fruit!

With sufficient experience in clearing the level, Li Fan resolved it in the fastest way.

The duration of his stay in the Immortal Eradication Realm was still long. Li Fan directly went to the Beast Taming Sect scenario.

Using the same trick, while waiting for Mr. Bai to arrive, the Celestial Mandate Black Bird soared into the sky and came before him.

The scene from the past replayed.

Mr. Bai observed, shook his head slightly, "My child, why are you practicing so haphazardly?"

Then, he imparted the true "Fortune Furnace Technique" wholeheartedly.

Time seemed to stand still. Although he had already reached the Half-Immortal realm, Li Fan was still immersed in the mysteries of this profound fortune technique.

"My initial premonition was correct. Even a mortal with absolutely no cultivation aptitude can transform and ascend step by step by practicing this method, eventually reaching the Immortal Realm!"

"If there were no various constraints in the world, and if the Immortal Realm still existed."

"As for now..."

Li Fan was no longer the Li Fan of the past.

While marveling and indulging, he also offered his own commentary.

Concurrently.

Outside the Immortal Eradication Realm, Li Fan's true body, hidden behind the miniature Dao Net, was attempting to spy on the true "Fortune Furnace Technique" through synchronized mirroring of the miniature Dao Net.

It had to be said that the Immortal Eradication Realm was truly a remarkable creation.

Existing in the interstice between reality and illusion, even though Li Fan could traverse the distance of countless high walls and star seas through the miniature Dao Net, when sensing the scenes occurring within the Immortal Eradication Realm, it was like looking through a distorted mirror.

Everything seen and felt was distorted to some extent.

And some parts were even completely inaccurate.

But after all, it had broken the boundary between the Immortal Eradication Realm and reality.

Allowing one to gaze upon illusion from reality.

"If I did not have this heaven-defying method of 'Mind Manifestation of Divinity,' I would likely need to surpass the creator of the Immortal Eradication Realm in strength to ignore such limitations."

"'Mind Manifesting Divinity' across the Xuanhuang, and undergoing infinite transformations over countless future years..."

"As I am now, I cannot do that yet."

Li Fan even suspected that the True Immortal who created this Immortal Eradication Realm might have possessed a supreme treasure like the "Dao Transformation Stone Mother," enabling him to achieve such a feat.

Within the Immortal Eradication Realm, Li Fan's disguised divine sense was practicing the perfect "Fortune Furnace Technique" in person.

While in reality, Li Fan was attempting to correct and restore the distorted and inaccurate parts he had spied, based on his insights.

Then, he began to practice the Fortune Furnace Technique himself.

By comparing the different sensations transmitted by his body during cultivation, he recalibrated it once more.

"Mind Manifestation of Divinity," leveraging the omnipresent power of the Great Dao, projecting the illusory objects within the Immortal Eradication Realm into reality.

Through Li Fan's persistent efforts, the "Fortune Furnace Technique" was finally restored in reality!

However, Li Fan did not have the divine sense within the Immortal Eradication Realm withdraw directly.

He remembered that in the next scene, the Sword Forging at the Heavenly Sword Sect, Mr. Bai would also appear. Perhaps he could glean more secrets from him.

Furthermore, the Heavenly Sword Sect had close ties with the Sword Domain of the Shining Star Sea, so it was also necessary to gather some intelligence.

The true body had the calibrated Fortune Furnace Technique synchronized to "Ma Tiande" in the Shining Star Sea.

Because that strand of divine sense had ventured deep alone, and the Shining Star Sea was suspected to have the presence of many Nameless True Immortals.

Thus, Li Fan imposed some restrictions on it.

The true body could not fully sense what was happening to the divine sense.

And the divine sense would not proactively spy on events happening in the Xuanhuang Realm through the miniature Dao Net.

This was to ensure that if things were exposed, Li Fan's true body would have ample time to "Return to Truth."

Although the Shining Star Sea had a time difference of one hundred and twenty times compared to the Xuanhuang Realm, the time flow within the Immortal Eradication Realm also differed from the reality of the Xuanhuang Realm.

Therefore, by the time Li Fan completed the calibration of the Fortune Furnace Technique, only half a day had passed.

In the Shining Star Sea, less than a month had passed.

The holiday for everyone had not even ended yet.

And even without the Fortune Furnace Technique as a reference, Li Fan's "Great Dao Descends Upon the Body Technique" had already achieved preliminary entry.

Within his divine sense, the strings of the Dao Net were as thin as cicada wings.

Emitting a soft, lustrous, pure white light, shining upon this body.

Li Fan seemed to sit in the very center of the Dao Net, enduring immense pressure.

If one were to magnify their mental focus to the extreme, one could see that every piece of flesh and blood in this body was being ground into dust by the oppressive force of the Dao Net.

However, almost at the moment of destruction, they were re-evolved from the miniature Dao Net.

It was Li Fan, combining the transformation of truth and falsehood, along with the function of Dao Net creation.

He was constantly generating and reorganizing all the flesh and blood tissues of this body.

"If I did not have sufficient experience, I would not be able to maintain the vitality of this body."

"This body refinement technique has only just entered the preliminary stage. Although it cannot compare to the time I carried fragments of the Immortal Realm, the pressure is almost akin to carrying an entire cultivation world."

"For ordinary people, let alone cultivation, they would likely be crushed to death on the spot!"

Li Fan knew that his "preliminary entry" was vastly different from the normal "preliminary entry."

However, with the foundation of a hundred reincarnations, Li Fan did not need to cultivate painstakingly from the very beginning.

"The normal cultivation method should be step by step, progressing gradually. If one wants to speed things up, they would at least need to combine it with various heavenly treasures. For someone like me, opting for a simple and crude method is absolutely unattainable for the average person."

Having gained a basic understanding of the Great Dao Descends Upon the Body Technique, this body was renewed.

Li Fan finally understood why the powers within the Shining Star Sea placed such importance on body refinement.

Taking this body as an example.

Compared to his previous frail body, when executing the same number of Dao Net commands, the power of the Dao Net that the new body could mobilize was more than double.

"As the Dao Net flows, it considers the limits that the operator can withstand."

"A person with a strong physique can naturally withstand more."

The same weapon, with an increasingly stronger physique, becomes smoother to control.

"Moreover, this feeling..."

Li Fan moved his stiff body, temporarily stopping the mirroring of the miniature Dao Net.

He walked slowly, back and forth, seemingly just strolling in the courtyard.

In reality, he was roaming within the Dao Net of the Shining Star Sea.

"It feels somewhat familiar."

Li Fan frowned slightly, closing his eyes again, and carefully sensed.

After a few breaths, he finally understood the source of this inexplicable familiarity.

The Great Dao pressed down, continuously grinding and reforming the flesh.

And during this process, the flesh and blood of the body naturally retained the imprint of the Great Dao.

The miniature Dao Net within Li Fan's divine sense and the Dao Net of the Shining Star Sea were both projections of the Great Dao.

Originating from the same source.

Therefore, the sense of familiarity Li Fan cultivated during the practice of the Great Dao Descends Upon the Body Technique.

Naturally extended to the Dao Net.

"This is the 'Postnatal Sacred Body'."

"If cultivated to the extreme according to this method..."

Li Fan's expression suddenly changed.

"'Mind Manifestation of Divinity' is a projection of the Dao Net."

"And the flesh and blood of the body is the mold formed by the continuous grinding and impact of the Dao Net."

"The theoretical perfect limit is to replicate all the Great Daos in the world with one's body."

Chapter 1452: The Great Dao Net Refining Hong Furnace

To have the Great Dao of all heavens as one's physical body.

Even Li Fan found it difficult to imagine what kind of formidable realm this was.

Those called Nameless True Immortals in the present era merely achieved enlightenment through one of the countless Great Daos in the world.

If the realm Li Fan speculated about truly existed, then Nameless True Immortals would be as different as ants and concrete beings when compared to it.

"This individual who proves the Dao through strength, crossing possibilities, would be as easy as stepping over a stream..."

As Li Fan thought this, the scene from his previous life suddenly flashed in his mind: the Black Heavenly Physician, who had suddenly descended from beyond the heavens, breaking through several high walls, and appearing abruptly.

"The Black Heavenly Physician, Evil Su Bai, might be at such a realm."

"However, they likely did not follow the path of becoming a saint through the flesh, but rather through continuously hunting their other selves in different possibilities, pushing a single Dao path beyond its limits and strengthening themselves."

"Making a single Dao path equivalent to the sum of all other Great Daos. This is ultimately the same goal as unifying all laws in the flesh, just through different means."

"But it is truly difficult to imagine how many of their own selves they must have slaughtered..."

Li Fan was momentarily stunned, and a faint chill ran down his spine.

However, this thought quickly passed, sinking deep into his heart. His attention returned to the "Great Dao Descends Upon the Body Technique."

While Li Fan's deductions and speculations might be correct, they were only ideal states in theory.

"If one wishes to cultivate this method to perfection, they must first continuously improve their 'Mind Manifestation of Divinity' until they can simultaneously project all the Great Daos in the world. This step alone is almost impossible."

"If one truly achieves such a realm, they are already invincible in the mortal world. Why then would they still seek to become a saint through the flesh?"

"It's still the same saying, trying to find a distant solution when a close one exists."

Because the realm he had deduced was still too far away, Li Fan inevitably had many doubts in his heart.

However, just like his "Mind Manifestation of Divinity," the body refinement method of the "Great Dao Descends Upon the Body Technique" provided tangible improvements to Li Fan's current strength.

Therefore, Li Fan would not abandon it.

If there were problems in the future, they would be dealt with then.

After all, he had the capital to start over anytime.

"Mind Manifestation projecting the Great Dao is called 'Mind Manifestation of Divinity.' The body containing the Great Dao, isn't that a 'Body Nascent Soul' in a sense?"

"It seems that my new and improved method not only requires reverse cultivation but also simultaneous cultivation of various different realms."

"When all realms are perfected to the extreme simultaneously, perhaps one can glimpse the true path of 'Building the Foundation with Oneself'!"

Li Fan shook his head secretly in his heart.

He was certain that neither Immortal Yin, nor the Sage Emperor, nor Su Bai, nor any of those who contributed to the perfection of the new and improved method had ever considered that the new and improved method could exist in such a peculiar way of cultivation.

Such a strange situation for Li Fan occurred precisely because Li Fan possessed the "Return to Truth" treasure, which had an infinitely high status.

"'Return to Truth' transcends the Great Dao of heaven and earth. To put it crudely, it's like leaping out of the three realms and no longer being bound by the five elements."

"Therefore, the difficulty of building my foundation is even greater than '鸣道' (鳴道). That's why I have to go against the normal path. As for others..."

The difference between Li Fan and others in the Shining Star Sea simultaneously practicing the "Great Dao Descends Upon the Body Technique" could, to some extent, explain something.

Thoughts swirled in his mind, while Li Fan's body slowly transferred the sense of familiarity, constantly refined within his miniature Dao Net, to the Dao Net of the Shining Star Sea.

Like a fish in water, or a bird flying in the sky.

Li Fan even vaguely felt as if he had returned to the Xuanhuang Realm, which he was extremely familiar with.

"Excellent. Excellent."

Moreover, due to this familiarity, Li Fan could also disguise himself at will, preventing his true cultivation progress from being exposed.

"What I am using is purely brute force, a clumsy method. If I were to reference the 'Fortune Furnace Technique' again..."

Within his divine sense, the Fortune Technique transmitted by his true body appeared word by word.

Li Fan took a deep breath, and all the blood and qi in his body seemed to boil and surge incessantly.

His body transformed into a colossal furnace, towering between heaven and earth, refining the aura and flesh and blood within his body.

With a mere thought, this furnace seemed to be located on the illusory Dao Net.

Suddenly, a Dao string flashed with dazzling white light. Then the Dao Net trembled, and the power of the Dao string transformed into a giant hammer, smashing down fiercely upon the colossal furnace.

The furnace roared and bellowed incessantly.

Its outer surface was scarred with faint imprints from the impact, but internally, by leveraging this immense force, the process of refining flesh and blood was accelerated tenfold.

"Ding! Ding! Ding!"

The Dao Net buzzed incessantly. And at an extremely slow pace, the intervals between each strike shortened.

And in reality, Li Fan's complexion visibly turned slightly red.

As if he had suffered a serious injury.

Then, this faint redness quickly turned green, then pale white, and then blood red.

This cycle repeated, becoming increasingly bizarre.

"The Great Dao Descends Upon the Body Technique and the Fortune Furnace Technique can be said to complement each other."

"The Fortune Furnace refines the body using oneself as a furnace, developing all the hidden potential within the human body. Step by step, with each refinement, one's strength grows. The drawback is that it is slow."

"The Great Dao Descends Upon the Body Technique, on the other hand, uses the Great Daos of all heavens to temper and supplement oneself. When all Great Daos are integrated into oneself, the physical body can become a saint. The drawback is that it is difficult and incredibly perilous."

"Combining these two, using the immense power of the Great Dao to strike the Fortune Furnace. Compared to my previous simple breaking and replenishing of flesh and blood, the efficiency is more than a hundred times higher!"

Li Fan's mind visualized the faint imprints appearing on the surface of the Fortune Furnace, precisely the marks left by the Great Dao.

Previously, it took hundreds of thousands of repetitions of flesh and blood shattering and re-forming to leave imprints of a similar degree. However, now, driven by the Fortune Technique, it happened in an instant.

The Dao Net roared, and myriad Dao marks appeared on the Fortune Furnace.

With Li Fan's every breath, the strength of this body increased at a rate of thousands of times.

Furthermore, throughout the entire process, Li Fan never felt any sense of hunger, as if there was truly an infinite source of power within the human body replenishing it.

Li Fan was so immersed in the rapid progress of his physical strength that he was almost unable to extricate himself.

Until Nangong Hongzhao came to visit.

"Brother Ma, how is your cultivation progressing?"

"I have only just entered the preliminary stage. This technique is indeed extraordinary, but it is truly difficult to practice." Li Fan said, his face pale, coughing slightly, sounding somewhat weak.

Nangong Hongzhao saw Li Fan's unstable vitality, seemingly having just been impacted by immense force and suffering a not-light injury. He quickly expressed his concern, "There's no need to rush. The Mysterious Coffin incident is still under investigation. Until a definitive conclusion is reached, our holiday will not end."

"Oh? So much time has passed, and even with the capabilities of the Immortal Hunters, they haven't found out the truth?" Li Fan asked with some surprise.

Nangong Hongzhao lowered his voice and sneered, "If they were to exert their full effort, of course, there would be no problem. However, someone is obstructing them. Before the investigation could even begin, all of Yan Xuantai's records within the Dao Net were inexplicably erased. The one capable of doing this..."

Nangong Hongzhao suddenly fell silent for a moment.

Then he whispered again, "Even more bizarre is that World-Crossing Profound Coffin. Analyzing the records left behind when we captured it, it is said that the coffin at the accident scene was indeed the one planned to be used as 'Immortal Bait'."

"The problem lies in the process of forging the Immortal Bait."

"What was supposed to be just a lure was actually turned into a tool for world-crossing. Most importantly, the one responsible for forging this coffin..."

Li Fan's eyes flickered. Seeing Nangong Hongzhao suddenly stop speaking, he pressed further, "What happened?"

"He died."

"Ah?" Li Fan immediately showed a look of shock.

"It wasn't that he died recently. After forging the nine lure coffins, he ceased to exist in this world. These nine coffins have helped the Immortal Hunters capture Immortals dozens of times, and never encountered an accident. That's why I was so confident back then..."

"Moreover, the coffin we used this time had also been used as bait several times before, yet it never showed any sign of true world-crossing escape..."

As Li Fan listened, he touched his forehead, "The more I hear you say, the more complicated this matter seems. Besides the coffin's forger, it probably involves high-level forces within the Governing Council. After all, one who can modify Dao Net information..."

Li Fan shook his head slightly. "No wonder it has taken so long to get even a rough idea."

"However... I do have a thought."

Nangong Hongzhao was stunned, then said, "It's just the two of us here, Brother Ma. Please speak your mind frankly."

"Let's simplify things and focus on the core of the event. The World-Crossing Profound Coffin is for escaping to other possibilities to avoid disaster. Yan Xuantai has been living in our Shining Star Sea for many years, why would he suddenly go to such great lengths and take such a risk to escape?"

"Yan Xuantai, he belongs to the 'Sacred Merchants'. The Sacred Merchants mysteriously vanished back then. I also heard before that they were collecting various rare treasures from outside before disappearing. Perhaps Yan Xuantai learned something from the Sacred Merchants back then. Was his recent escape a last resort?"

"You mean..." Nangong Hongzhao stared intently at Li Fan.

"Exactly. I suspect that a great catastrophe is about to befall the Shining Star Sea soon..." Li Fan whispered.

"Brother Ma, do not speak rashly!" Nangong Hongzhao interrupted him sternly before he could finish.

However, Li Fan's reasoning was not without merit.

The more Nangong Hongzhao thought about it, the more it seemed like the truth behind the chaos. He also seemed to recall something, and the expression on Nangong Hongzhao's face changed several times within a few breaths.

"It's best if you only tell me this, Brother Ma. Absolutely do not speak of it outside. Otherwise, if an incident occurs, I won't be able to help you." With only this final instruction, Nangong Hongzhao left in a hurry.

Before departing, he left behind a scroll, which contained the Nangong family's records of their predecessors' experiences and insights in cultivating the "Great Dao Descends Upon the Body Technique."

However, it only stopped at the initial stage of comprehending the Great Dao and projecting it onto oneself.

It seemed Nangong Hongzhao intended to use this as bait to continuously increase "Ma Tiande's" favorability.

Li Fan merely glanced at it before discarding the insights aside.

"The Profound Coffin escaped, and there's an insider in the Shining Star Sea. How interesting."

Based on the information known so far, the actual ruling power in the Shining Star Sea should be those True Immortals who have transcended the mortal realm.

As for the mortals in the forefront, they are merely puppets controlled by them.

"However, for True Immortals who have transcended, to allow mortals to serve as figureheads shows that mortals must possess something they fear..."

Li Fan suddenly thought of the invisible giant hand behind the Dao Net.

And the four Nameless True Immortals who were used as living stakes.

"The struggle between transcended Immortals and former Immortals, versus the current group of True Immortals."

"However, in this battlefield, a deserter suddenly appeared."

"Escaping not to any of the existing factions, but to another world outside of possibilities."

According to Nangong Hongzhao's words, the Immortals who survived the Dao Annihilation Tribulation feared this tribulation immensely.

The strongest among them had already escaped and fled far away.

Li Fan believed that the remaining individuals, or Immortals, would still harbor this fear in their hearts.

However, after tens of thousands of years, they had been misled by the false prosperity created by the Dao Net.

It seemed they truly believed they could resist the Dao Annihilation Tribulation with the so-called Dao Net.

However, the Sacred Merchants, and Yan Xuantai's risky escape this time, might just wake them from their dreams.

"Interesting."

"There are no eternal enemies in this world. Perhaps the Shining Star Sea and those True Immortals might actually cooperate again."

"After all, out of the nine Profound Coffins, one was able to escape through world-crossing. Who knows if the others are incapable of doing so?"

Another month passed.

The holiday for the newly recruited Immortal Hunters finally ended.

Li Fan and the others were summoned again. The speaker was the stout man who had previously carried the giant pillar.

This person berated the new Immortal Hunters, saying that regardless of the reason, the failure in their first mission was incompetence.

Therefore, they would now have to "make amends for their mistakes."

"Hunt Immortals again!"

"This time, I will hunt the True Immortal together with you."

"The target is our old adversary in the Immortal Hunters. Previously, this person managed to escape several times. However, this time..."

"Hmph." The stout man sneered, a hint of killing intent flashing in his eyes.

"Senior Qian, who is our target this time..." Dao Yuan was the first to ask.

Dao Yuan apparently knew the stout man, as he addressed him by his surname even before he introduced himself.

"This Immortal's Dao technique can sever all connections with the outside world. It is extremely difficult to track. Even when traversing within the Dao Net, it leaves no trace. We do not know his background, so we simply refer to him as 'Formless'."

"This Immortal, relying on the uniqueness of his Dao path, often infiltrates our Shining Star Sea. Our Immortal Hunter operations to hunt Immortals have been disrupted by this Immortal several times. Therefore, this time we are determined to apprehend him!" the stout man said solemnly, his expression grave.

"Such a difficult mission, assigned to us?" Dao Yuan exclaimed, somewhat taken aback.

Not just Dao Yuan, but all the new Immortal Hunters felt the same.

"Don't worry. Precisely because you are newly recruited and this Immortal does not know you, you have a greater chance of success. All you need to do is obey my command, assist in weaving the Dao Net, and patiently wait for him to come into the net!" the stout man said with extreme confidence.

Li Fan nodded in agreement with the others.

His gaze inadvertently swept over Nangong Hongzhao, who seemed somewhat distracted.

However, Li Fan was more concerned about the target of this immortal hunt.

"Severing all connections with the outside world?"

For some reason, Li Fan's ears suddenly echoed with a wild, defiant laugh.

"What does it matter to me! What does it matter to me!"

Chapter 1453: Ten Thousand Stars Tomb Swallows Bones

The culprit behind the extinction of life in the star sea within the high walls, besides the Immortal Ruins, was also the array of True Immortal inscriptions.

All of them were the work of "He Gan Xian."

During Li Fan's interaction with the True Will of the Star Sea's origin, he had felt the Star Sea's immense hatred for this He Gan Xian.

Although True Immortals viewed all beings as ants, they did not act without reason.

To imitate numerous True Immortal inscriptions, disseminate them, and let them run rampant in the starry sky, and all this while fleeing in disgrace from the upper realm...

Li Fan surmised that this might be He Gan Xian's way of achieving enlightenment.

"First, use this method to generate countless entangled karmic connections out of thin air. When I can completely extricate myself from this karma, it will signify the completion of my Dao comprehension."

"Severing all connections with the outside world..."

Recalling that arrogant and unrestrained laughter, Li Fan's judgment became even more certain.

"If my guess is correct, the 'Formless' Immortal that the Immortal Hunters intend to capture is likely the He Gan Xian I am familiar with."

"However, I cannot yet confirm whether this He Gan Xian is the same as the Faceless Immortal who once saved King Xuan Yuan's life."

Li Fan had previously suspected that He Gan Xian and the Faceless Immortal were the same person. This was because when the Sage Emperor's clone saw the Faceless statue, he felt an aura very similar to that when he spied on He Gan Xian. Li Fan's true body had also experienced the same feeling.

But strangely, this thought only arose the first time he saw it. Now, when Li Fan compared the two again, he felt some hesitation.

...

The stout man named Qian continued to explain the precautions for the Immortal Hunters' hunt.

"Regarding this 'Formless' Immortal, I cannot reveal too much to you."

"His infiltration methods are incredible. Furthermore, he is extremely sensitive to all external connections related to his existence. If I were to tell you his detailed information, with so many people suddenly involved, it would inevitably alert him."

"What you need to do is assist me in weaving a great net, and patiently wait for him to come into our trap!"

The Formless Immortal was clearly more powerful than the previous Xi and Yi Immortals. The newly recruited Immortal Hunters felt both excitement and a bit of trepidation. After all, the previous failure had left them with some psychological trauma.

"Oh, right. My name is Qian Ruochang. You can call me Boss Qian. Hahaha..." With a meaningful laugh, the stout man revealed his name.

Then, everyone was led to participate in the mission.

Traversing through the Dao Net, they soon arrived at their destination.

"Where is this..."

"The Ten Thousand Stars Tomb?"

Unlike the vibrant regions of the Shining Star Sea's various factions, the starry sky ahead was permeated with an aura of decay and death. Even from a distance, everyone instinctively felt discomfort.

Li Fan had been in the Shining Star Sea for some time and was not unfamiliar with the area called the Ten Thousand Stars Tomb.

Although it was also a place where life had been extinguished, there were still some differences between the Ten Thousand Stars Tomb and the Annihilation Lands. The Annihilation Lands were desolate regions created by the Dao Annihilation Tribulation, where even concepts had been erased.

The Ten Thousand Stars Tomb, on the other hand, was a destroyed starfield caused by factors other than the Dao Annihilation Tribulation.

The powers within the Shining Star Sea were not all indigenous to this starry sky; they were refugees from countless star domains who had gathered here.

In the boundless lower star seas, apart from vast stretches of Annihilation Lands, there were the Ten Thousand Stars Tombs and regions of vitality intermingled. The Shining Star Sea was one such region of vitality.

Although the Ten Thousand Stars Tomb was devoid of life, the Dao Net could still cover it.

As for the Annihilation Lands...

Where the Great Dao does not exist, the Dao Net must also halt.

"Boss Qian, could the Formless Immortal be hiding in this place?" someone couldn't help but ask.

Qian Ruochang smiled, "This desolate place in the Ten Thousand Stars Tomb, why would True Immortals hide here? I brought you here to find something good."

Dao Yuan's eyes lit up with curiosity, "I once heard that the Ten Thousand Stars Tomb is filled with dense death qi, accumulated over millions of years. As the saying goes, extremes lead to reversals; perhaps in the midst of infinite death qi, vibrant life might be born..."

"You boy actually have some insight. But our objective this time is not some life force. It's this..."

As he spoke, Qian Ruochang had already led everyone deep into the Ten Thousand Stars Tomb.

Although the Dao Net still covered this area, compared to ordinary vibrant star seas, it felt like progress was heavily hindered. The speed of travel was more than a hundred times slower.

At times, it seemed as if they encountered obstacles ahead, and everyone had to change course.

At this moment, they suddenly stopped. Qian Ruochang pointed towards the front left.

Then, he swung the stone pillar he was carrying fiercely.

All the new Immortal Hunters could feel the Dao Net being pulled by immense force in that instant, shaking violently.

The tremor was even stronger than the one caused by Nangong Fusheng's arrival.

Everyone looked at Qian Ruochang, their faces filled with shock.

They hadn't expected this seemingly amiable Boss Qian to possess such terrifying strength.

Li Fan, however, mused that the phenomenon was not due to Qian Ruochang's strength surpassing Nangong Fusheng.

Rather, they had reached a weak point in the Dao Net.

The Dao Net's power, attached to the Great Dao of heaven and earth, was greatly weakened in this area of the Ten Thousand Stars Tomb. The same amount of force would naturally cause a greater disturbance.

The stone pillar flew out, stirring the darkness and silence of the void.

Li Fan's senses were sharper than everyone else's.

In the pitch-black darkness, he seemed to see several floating, dead worlds that were inadvertently struck by the stone pillar. The immense force stirred and churned, causing them to completely disappear.

Only some almost negligible black dots flew out from the shattered corpses of the dead worlds, drifting along the giant stone pillar towards Qian Ruochang.

Li Fan looked at these black dots, and a sense of familiarity arose.

They were very similar to the black qi produced when True Immortals' flesh and blood were decomposed by the "Descending Mortal Dust" technique!

Li Fan remained expressionless, pretending to be unaware of the danger and actively approaching to observe curiously.

Upon closer inspection, Li Fan discovered the difference between these black dots and black qi.

Black qi was the precursor to the Dao Annihilation Tribulation. For cultivators who had reached a certain realm, observing it would inevitably evoke an inexplicable sense of crisis.

But these black dots before him...

Li Fan observed for a long time but only felt a sense of disgust and discomfort in his heart, without any ominous premonition of impending danger.

And Qian Ruochang's subsequent words provided Li Fan with the answer.

"These can be considered the corpses of the cultivation world."

"Just like after a person dies, their flesh and blood return to heaven and earth in a short time, leaving only white bones to endure. These black dots are the most fundamental and pure part, like the 'bones of the world'. They will not remain in the world for too long, so we must seize the time to collect them," Qian Ruochang said, stirring the stone pillar again.

In a short time, he collected fifteen black dots.

Although it seemed like a simple action, it appeared to be extremely taxing. Qian Ruochang was already panting and sweating profusely.

He had to stop to rest.

"Eat this."

Qian Ruochang渡ed one of the black dots into the air towards Dao Yuan.

Dao Yuan's expression changed slightly, but he showed little hesitation. To the astonishment of everyone, he forced himself to endure the discomfort and swallowed the "world's bone" in one gulp.

From the expression on Dao Yuan's face, it was evident that raw consumption of the "world's bone" was an immense torment.

But the effect after it entered his stomach was also obvious.

"How do I feel, Brother Dao..."

"You've become a bit 'lighter'?"

"Yes, I feel a bit 'blurrier'."
