"This... If you hadn't reminded me, I would have almost overlooked Brother Dao! He's standing right here, yet it's as if he doesn't exist at all!"

Everyone discovered the anomaly and exclaimed in amazement.

Qian Ruochang then smiled and said, "This 'world's bone' is the foundation upon which the cultivation world evolved. It is the lowest layer of the world's mechanisms, closest to the Great Dao itself. After you swallow it, before the 'world's bone' fully returns to heaven and earth, influenced by its power, you will be like ice melting into water, merging into this world."

"The nature of being a 'person' is being concealed by the 'world'. In terms of ordinary sensory perception, it is naturally difficult to distinguish."

Qian Ruochang distributed the "world's bone" to everyone according to the previously planned assessment order.

Li Fan also received his early and swallowed it.

The moment the black dot was absorbed, various illusions appeared before Li Fan's eyes. They were scenes from the cultivation world this black dot belonged to in its former life.

It was not a particularly dramatic story in the lower star sea.

A once prosperous world, one day, a rift appeared in the sky.

Several figures emerged from it.

That powerful oppressive aura caused most of the world's life to die instantly.

And those figures had no intention of restraining their power, or rather, they were too preoccupied to care about such "minor matters."

They themselves...

Were also fleeing in panic and disarray.

Seventeen figures successively emerged from the rift.

Until the last one forcefully closed the rift, the catastrophe was finally halted.

He seemed somewhat dazed in his panic.

His gaze swept over the devastated cultivation world below, affected by the True Immortal's might, and he slightly shook his head.

With a gentle wave of his hand, he erased all the surviving beings on the ground.

Not even their corpses remained.

The cultivation world itself, unable to withstand such pressure, shattered and disintegrated.

As if performing a trivial task, the last figure drifted away.

...

Li Fan awoke from the illusion.

This was one of the sources of the corpses of various worlds in the Ten Thousand Stars Tomb.

"The lower star seas were originally not places for Immortals to survive. When they were forced to come here, they naturally caused immense impact on the original inhabitants, the mortals."

Li Fan did not feel the slightest bit of indignation or rage.

The strong prey on the weak. Moreover, when the doomsday tribulation arrived, the desperate only prioritized survival.

As for other matters...

They were all unimportant.

His mind settled, and he sensed the changes in his body that naturally occurred after swallowing the "world's bone."

As Qian Ruochang had said, like ice melting into water.

Through the connection between the "world's bone" and the Great Dao of heaven and earth, he was slowly "dissolving" into this starscape.

"If I were to communicate with the Star Sea now, I wouldn't need the Great Jia Divine Art. I could effectively connect with the Star Sea's origin consciousness."

"In addition, my connection with the Dao Net has also become closer..."

Within Li Fan's divine sense, the miniature Dao Net shone brightly.

What was originally a faint illusion, now, a part of it seemed to possess a tangible form.

Even though it was only a small part, it brought about a qualitative change.

However, with others around, especially Qian Ruochang, who seemed to be close to the Nameless realm, Li Fan temporarily refrained from careful research.

"The Dao perception that the 'Formless' Immortal comprehended, the so-called karmic connections, were merely directed at beings in the world. He had not yet transcended, thus unable to sever his connection with heaven and earth. By borrowing the 'world's bone' and immersing ourselves within the Great Dao, we should be able to greatly reduce the possibility of him discovering us," Qian Ruochang said, also swallowing a piece of "world's bone."

After collecting enough for all the new Immortal Hunters, he did not stop.

Instead, he continued to explore deeper into the Ten Thousand Stars Tomb.

"Concealing ourselves is merely the first step of the hunt."

"The second step is to prepare traps and weapons capable of severely injuring or even killing the prey," Qian Ruochang's voice gradually turned somewhat somber.

"True Immortals cultivate the Great Dao of heaven and earth, seeking to transcend. The best weapon against them is something that can injure and damage the Great Dao!"

...

Upon hearing this, the faces of all the Immortal Hunters changed.

Li Fan thought Qian Ruochang was about to talk about the "Dao Annihilation Tribulation."

But unexpectedly, he brought up something else.

With a turn of his words, "However, what our Dao Net relies on is still the power of the Great Dao of heaven and earth. Damaging the enemy by a thousand while harming oneself by eight hundred is something that requires extreme caution. However, we can find a similar substitute from this Ten Thousand Stars Tomb."

"As mentioned earlier, in the Ten Thousand Stars Tomb, the corpses and flesh of the cultivation world all dissipate, returning to heaven and earth, leaving only bones."

"This power that catalyzes and devours the flesh and blood of the cultivation world is the weapon we need!"

"The Great Dao, from top to bottom, is a unified entity. The mortal cultivation world, however, is still a manifestation of the Great Dao."

"The ability to cause the Great Dao to revert from its manifested form to nothingness can also inflict heavy damage on True Immortals who cultivate the Dao!"

...

Qian Ruochang spoke incessantly.

Li Fan, however, was lost in thought and suddenly spoke up, "Boss Qian, according to what you said, doesn't this force that annihilates the flesh and blood of the cultivation world also have the potential to severely damage the Dao Net?"

The other Immortal Hunters looked at Li Fan, their expressions showing signs of surprise.

Qian Ruochang, however, clapped his hands vigorously, "Precisely! But you can rest assured. The difference between the Dao Net and True Immortals lies in its comprehensiveness and its ability to self-repair at any time."

"Since we are confident in using it as a weapon, we are not afraid of someone using it to target the Dao Net!"

"Moreover, using this strange force from the Ten Thousand Stars Tomb is a recent achievement of ours..."

Qian Ruochang's words suddenly paused.

His gaze flickered towards the front left, his expression shifting from amusement to solemnity.

"Watch carefully, everyone. That is what I call 'digesting the flesh and blood of the world'..."

Qian Ruochang suddenly threw the stone pillar on his shoulder.

It appeared to be a majestic display.

But as it shuttled through the void, it was utterly silent, causing no disturbance.

After circling back, it simply returned.

However, Li Fan keenly noticed that the stone pillar seemed to have shrunk by a section.

Chapter 1454: Deep Web of Immortal Imprisonment

The part of the stone pillar that appeared to have vanished had not completely dissipated.

Instead, forces from the Dao Net were constantly replenishing it, like regenerating flesh and blood. However, the power to digest flesh and blood from the Ten Thousand Stars Tomb clung stubbornly, like a persistent ailment, entwining around it.

Thus, a very strange scene appeared before everyone: a portion of the giant pillar was rapidly alternating between states of "existence" and "non-existence." It appeared as a transparent shadow.

Qian Ruochang carefully retrieved the pillar from the Ten Thousand Stars Tomb.

Simultaneously, he issued instructions to the new Immortal Hunters who were spectating, "Create a localized Dao Origin Array isolated from the Dao Net, to serve as a breeding ground for the 'Realm Annihilation' power."

Everyone present froze collectively.

Clearly, the Dao Origin commands of this magnitude were beyond their capabilities. After all, since joining the Immortal Hunters, they had only been executing missions or forced into lengthy vacations. They had not yet received formal training.

Fortunately, Qian Ruochang was not foolish.

Before his words could finish, fluctuations emanated from the void, outside the Ten Thousand Stars Tomb.

A seven-colored halo, utilizing the Dao Net, rapidly traversed from the Shining Star Sea, shining brightly and enveloping everyone collectively.

Within the halo was an ocean composed entirely of Dao Origin symbols. It was as if responding to Qian Ruochang's earlier words, tens of millions of symbols surged towards everyone in the center like a relentless tide.

As for other Dao Origin symbols, they suddenly faded into transparency, as if they had never existed.

Caught off guard, everyone was doused by this "tide."

Everyone received an equal share.

Simultaneously, within everyone's minds, the method for executing the "External Dao Manifestation" technique appeared.

External Dao Manifestation: At the boundary of the Dao Net, create a new Dao Net realm. This realm is like a miniature version of the Dao Net; apart from its reduced coverage and power, everything else is identical to the Dao Net. All existing commands within the Dao Net are applicable within it.

This newly created realm, if used for expansion, can significantly reduce the cost of the Dao Net creating new covered areas.

Alternatively, it can be used for certain experiments of an extremely dangerous nature, achieving conditions identical to those within the Dao Net without threatening the Dao Net itself.

To ensure the absolute safety of the Dao Net, only the combined efforts of the three Chief Directors of the Governing Council can access the Dao Net to the newly created "External Dao Manifestation" region. Before that, the new realm will exist in an absolute state of [Isolation].

...

Accompanying the commands were various pieces of information related to "External Dao Manifestation" regions.

Even though the complexity of the commands was unprecedented in their lives, under the illumination of the strange halo, everyone learned and understood them all at once, without any need for learning, memorizing, or mastering the entire process.

Under Qian Ruochang's command, everyone worked together. As commands were constructed one after another, a Dao Net realm was thus "created."

Although building a "mini Dao Net" was this simple, the new Immortal Hunters could not comprehend this incredibly profound process.

They merely felt, as in the past, that commands were generated, and the Dao Net responded accordingly.

Only Li Fan saw a scene that the others could not.

The moment the "External Dao Manifestation" technique was executed, the entire Dao Net seemed to enter a state of stillness. Then, it actually dimmed, as if turning off its light.

Allowing the light from the true Great Dao, from beyond the Dao Net, to pass through.

Projecting the shadow of the Dao Net.

"If the Dao Net is like paper that imitates and covers, then the new realm we are creating is the projection of the Dao Net."

Everyone was still within the scope of the strange halo.

The stone pillar, carrying the power of Realm Annihilation, was thrown into the newly created Dao Net.

As the mini Dao Net continuously supplied Dao laws for "feeding," the formless power of Realm Annihilation was nurtured and grew increasingly strong.

Even though they were outside the realm, everyone inexplicably felt a sense of unease.

At this moment, the stone pillar, which had been completely gnawed down to less than half its original size within the realm, suddenly transformed into a giant hand.

It began to manipulate the surrounding power of Realm Annihilation.

Although the giant hand was continuously being corroded and disappearing, it was also being replenished by the power of the mini Dao Net.

Thus, after repeatedly manipulating for a long time, a black, sharp arrow was forged by this giant hand.

Once the first black arrow of Realm Annihilation was forged, the scene within the realm suddenly changed again, dividing into three distinct areas.

One was for nurturing the power of Realm Annihilation, another for forging black arrows, and the third for storing them.

On each black arrow, a human face appeared.

Corresponding to the new Immortal Hunters present!

"Are these weapons for us?" Dao Yuan asked with some shock.

Qian Ruochang smiled, "Not yet. Once you have properly set up the trap and the Formless Immortal enters the net, it will truly belong to you."

"The power of Realm Annihilation is such that contact with it will inevitably lead to being eroded. Without the support of the Dao Net's power, even I would be instantly drained into dust. Therefore, you must use them only when connected to the Dao Net."

"Let's go!"

Qian Ruochang glanced back at the boundless, deathly silent Ten Thousand Stars Tomb, and led everyone away, whistling back.

"This newly created realm will accompany us throughout this Immortal capture mission. Whether the mission succeeds or fails, we must ensure this realm dissipates. We cannot allow the power of Realm Annihilation to wreak havoc in the true Dao Net."

Moving away from the dark tomb and returning to the realm of vitality in the Shining Star Sea, Qian Ruochang pointed at the halo surrounding everyone and said this.

"This halo is to prevent accidents. If we are all annihilated, the halo will be responsible for reclaiming all our legacies."

Upon hearing this, everyone's expressions became somewhat subtle.

"With Boss Qian leading the team, and with formidable weapons like the Realm Annihilation Black Arrows, coupled with us fighting on home turf within the Dao Net. Even if we fail, can we still be annihilated?" Jiang Yuming frowned and asked, showing some disbelief.

Qian Ruochang's constant faint smile instantly vanished. "The hunter and the prey, the roles can switch in an instant."

"Although our chances of winning are high, our opponent is still an 'Immortal'."

"Especially a True Immortal who has survived the ancient catastrophe and the hunts of the Immortal Hunters..."

Qian Ruochang cast a cold glance at Jiang Yuming.

Jiang Yuming lowered his head and repeatedly said, "Your junior accepts your teachings."

"Your understanding of Immortals is still too shallow. Next, I will take you to truly understand what a True Immortal is."

"And find a suitable bait in the process."

The light and shadow around everyone shifted rapidly.

At this speed, they could traverse the Shining Star Sea multiple times. But for some reason, they kept moving forward, with no end in sight.

The original vibrant light gradually turned dim.

However, it did not disappear but seemed to float above everyone's heads like stars, revolving and hanging overhead.

They were heading towards an unknown realm, constantly delving deeper.

"The place we are going to is the location of the 'Deep Net,' where the Shining Star Sea imprisons various Immortals."

"The so-called Deep Net is the core depths of the Dao Net," Qian Ruochang gave a brief introduction to the 'Deep Net,' seemingly unwilling to say more.

"The Deep Net is a top secret. Ordinary people do not know of its existence, let alone have the fortune to enter it."

"Even I, without this duty of capturing True Immortals in the current mission, could not freely enter and exit."

As they descended, countless tiny points of light flickered on Qian Ruochang and the new Immortal Hunters.

It seemed to be verifying everyone's identities.

When the vital stars above completely disappeared, their journey finally halted.

As if arriving in a vast, dark void, surrounded by nothingness.

Before Qian Ruochang, countless symbols seemed to surge simultaneously.

A single thread of light suddenly illuminated the darkness.

On either side of the thread, rows of squares were distributed.

Like cages, or perhaps like worlds.

The boundaries of the squares were exceptionally thick, as if to completely isolate the beings imprisoned within from the outside.

And within these squares...

Were imprisoned beings!

Or rather, Immortals!

Some were in a state of deep sleep.

Others maintained a vigilant and cold gaze, constantly surveying their surroundings, flying in the void, seemingly searching for a way to escape.

And some were in a state of complete madness, continuously casting immortal arts, bombarding everything in the world. Even though there was nothing else in their prison cages except themselves.

All these imprisoned True Immortals shared one commonality.

That was, various colored threads were inserted into their bodies, extending out from them. Connecting to the outside.

But they did not touch the "boundary" of the cage, but instead disappeared into the void midway.

Clearly, these imprisoned True Immortals could not see these threads attached to themselves. Only observers like Li Fan and the others could see them clearly.

"These... are Immortals?"

After the initial shock, the reverence the crowd felt for Immortals completely dissipated.

After all, no matter who saw the True Immortals of legend and imagination, appearing like this in reality.

Their attitudes would likely change drastically.

"Through the Immortal Cage, you naturally cannot comprehend the terror of True Immortals."

"If we were to put you inside and let you experience it, you would understand what 'True Immortal Might' is." Qian Ruochang saw the disdain arising in the crowd's hearts and sneered.

Then, he swept his gaze over everyone, as if genuinely selecting personnel.

Everyone's hearts tightened, and they immediately adopted serious expressions, not daring to show any abnormal emotions.

They then observed intently.

"Boss Qian, these True Immortals must have been imprisoned for a long time. Why do they all still appear so vigorous and healthy?"

"There's no sign of decay or weakness from prolonged imprisonment?"

In the midst of utter silence, someone suddenly asked.

Qian Ruochang looked at "Ma Tiande," the questioner, and couldn't help but nod in admiration, "I didn't expect you to grasp the core of the issue so quickly."

"You are very good!"

"It's not that we provide energy supplements to these True Immortals after imprisoning them. Rather, as True Immortals, their own energy is inexhaustible!" Qian Ruochang said emphatically.

Clearly, the nature of True Immortals having infinite energy was not something everyone knew.

Upon hearing Qian Ruochang's words, eight or nine out of ten people were greatly astonished.

"Infinite? How is that possible?"

Clearly, the concept of infinity completely contradicted everything they had learned since childhood.

"True Immortals possess infinite immortal spiritual energy, sourced from an unfathomable region called the 'Infinite Sea'."

"It even exists beyond the Great Dao, hence even the core power of the Dao Net cannot sever the connection between True Immortals and the Infinite Sea."

"Being able to freely draw upon the power of the Infinite Sea is the truly terrifying aspect of True Immortals."

Qian Ruochang pointed to a man sitting in meditation with his eyes closed within a square cage.

"This Immortal was among the first batch we captured. He has been imprisoned for nearly fifty thousand years."

"But he still maintains a resolute spirit and has not shown the slightest flaw. Although the cages are 'Dao-severed zones' where cultivation and realm improvement are impossible, this Immortal, solely through inner comprehension, has been silently improving his strength over these years. It is now unknown to what level." Qian Ruochang sighed slightly.

His tone carried both helplessness and admiration.

"Why not simply kill them all!" Jin Changyue, who had remained silent for the most part, suddenly spoke. Her killing intent and desire were unconcealed.

"Heh heh..." Qian Ruochang did not answer but let out a knowing laugh.

Li Fan noticed that when Qian Ruochang laughed, his eyes inadvertently glanced at the various colored threads inserted into the True Immortals' bodies.

Recalling the four Nameless True Immortals used as living stakes, Li Fan pondered, "Perhaps the establishment and stabilization of the Dao Net are also related to these imprisoned True Immortals."

Li Fan turned to look around.

Clearly, what he saw before him was not the entirety of the True Immortals imprisoned within the Dao Net.

In the unseen darkness, there were countless more "squares."

"We can neither kill them nor cut off their energy supply..."

"So we just let them continue to cultivate? What if one day, they manage to escape from these cages?" Dao Yuan frowned deeply.

The eyes of the others also flashed with worry and fear.

True Immortals were hunted and captured one by one.

If so many True Immortals were to lose control simultaneously...

That would be a terrifying scenario beyond imagination.

"You don't need to worry about that."

"Even if they advance further, the 'Deep Net Prison' is not a place they can leave just because they want to." Qian Ruochang was quite confident in the sturdiness of the cages.

"Although I cannot truly let you enter, I can allow you to more concretely and personally experience the might of True Immortals."

"Who should I choose..."

Qian Ruochang scanned everyone, finally selecting a seemingly harmless, perpetually sleeping True Immortal.

With a gentle wave of his hand, various colored threads appeared in front of Qian Ruochang out of thin air.

They seemed to connect to the cages.

"Who wants to try?" Qian Ruochang looked at the crowd.

"I will." Dao Yuan said with great confidence.

Qian Ruochang said nothing, merely motioning to connect the various colored threads to Dao Yuan's body.

The next moment...

This proud prodigy of the Shining Star Sea actually began to tremble uncontrollably, his entire body shaking violently.

Chapter 1455: Dissecting the True Immortal's Corpse

Dao Yuan was currently like someone caught in a terrifying nightmare, his face deathly pale, beads of cold sweat breaking out all over his body.

Fortunately, Qian Ruochang did not let Dao Yuan face the True Immortal's might for too long. After a few breaths, he quickly withdrew the threads. Even so, Dao Yuan still looked terrified, his eyes wide with panic, and it took him quite a while to recover.

"Is it really that exaggerated..." Many people muttered inwardly upon witnessing this.

But after Qian Ruochang connected the threads to their own bodies, not a single person dared to doubt anymore.

Dao Yuan could still manage, showing the best result among them. Some who couldn't endure it collapsed on the spot, trembling uncontrollably. Many suffered psychological breakdowns, crying and wailing.

Seeing these so-called prodigies in such a pathetic state, Qian Ruochang was unfazed.

He had even deliberately chosen a "dangerous element" among the imprisoned True Immortals, precisely to thoroughly intimidate these newcomers.

Unlike the genuine emotional outbursts of others, Li Fan's performance was naturally a pretense.

Let alone a True Immortal, Li Fan had personally witnessed powerhouses who could traverse possibilities. Thus, he was not frightened into losing composure.

However, the True Immortal whom Qian Ruochang made the new Immortal Hunters "face directly" was indeed somewhat peculiar.

He seemed to be able to detect the various colored threads inserted into himself and, through these threads, spy on the outside world.

Therefore, when the new Immortal Hunters connected the threads, they were first met with the True Immortal's gaze.

A pair of indifferent eyes, looking down from above. It seemed capable of seeing through everything in the depths of their souls, leaving no secrets within. Their very life and death could be dictated by the owner of those eyes.

"No wonder these people are in such a state. It's not simply about facing a True Immortal directly, but being constantly under the micro-observation of a True Immortal, a high-ranking being..."

"But isn't he afraid that the imprisoned True Immortal might discover a way to escape by observing the thoughts of those outside?"

Li Fan subtly glanced at Qian Ruochang.

Qian Ruochang, however, maintained a look of relishing the spectacle, showing no such concern.

Thus, Li Fan turned to carefully examine the square cages imprisoning the True Immortals. The so-called 'Dao-severed zones' were indeed prisons.

Although it seemed that the imprisoned True Immortals in the cages were in the same place as everyone else, it was evident that what appeared before them was merely a representation of the cages' existence.

"The only place truly severed from the Dao in the mortal world is the Annihilation Lands, purified by the Dao Annihilation Tribulation. Could it be that the Immortal Hunters of the Shining Star Sea are using the Annihilation Lands as prisons? But how did these threads pass through the Annihilation Lands?"

The core of the Deep Net held too many unknown and top-secret matters.

What Qian Ruochang showed the crowd was only this single, shining thread and the countless surrounding square cages.

In the dim Deep Net, time seemed to be irrelevant. The crowd was merely forced to face one imprisoned True Immortal after another in various ways.

Regardless of the significant difference in power, after such frequent exposure, the crowd gradually became numb.

Only the most dangerous True Immortals among them could still evoke a slight sense of fear.

As for ordinary True Immortals, they could all be treated with indifference.

Qian Ruochang seemed quite pleased with the speed of their progress. One day, he finally stopped the incessant game of inserting and withdrawing threads.

"Very good. It seems you have finally managed to barely adapt to the existence of 'Immortals'."

"Next is the final hurdle here."

"After passing this hurdle, we can officially begin weaving the net to capture Immortals."

Qian Ruochang's face once again revealed that meaningful smile.

The Immortal Hunters present all felt a jolt in their hearts.

And Qian Ruochang's next words made them look incredulous.

"The final test is to personally dismember the corpse of a True Immortal!"

His voice struck like thunder, resonating in everyone's ears.

The threads connected to numerous squares disappeared into the darkness.

After a few breaths, light reappeared.

Along with it, a tall, towering figure emerged.

The figure's aura, like an abyss and a sea, caused the unprepared crowd to cease breathing, not daring to make the slightest sound.

And looking to the sides, Qian Ruochang, who had been with them all along, had mysteriously disappeared!

The crowd then remembered Qian Ruochang's previous words about the test.

To dismember the corpse of a True Immortal...

A strange silence fell upon the scene. Although they understood the objective, no one dared, or could easily, make a move!

The figure standing before them, while called a corpse.

In reality, it was not much different from the imprisoned True Immortals they had faced before.

The True Immortal's face was indistinguishable, but everyone present felt as if they were being lightly stared at by the True Immortal.

This gaze pressed down upon them like a mountain!

Adapting to the existence of a True Immortal, and still being able to act freely under a True Immortal's gaze, let alone drawing a blade against it...

These were completely different concepts.

The True Immortal's corpse was right there. How many people dared to step forward and attempt to dissect it?

Li Fan naturally dared. But he had no intention of being the first to act.

After a long period of silence, finally, someone spoke harshly. "No matter how strong he was in life, in death, he is nothing more than a corpse. What is there to fear!"

Saying this, under everyone's gaze, he charged straight towards the True Immortal's corpse.

Li Fan squinted, inwardly mourning for the cultivator named Feng Zengyuan in advance.

A True Immortal's corpse was vastly different from an ordinary corpse in the mortal world. Even the intention of a True Immortal to survive could instantly kill several Longevity realm powerhouses of the Xuanhuang Realm, let alone a complete True Immortal corpse!

As expected.

Before Feng Zengyuan could even reach the True Immortal's side, the towering figure seemed to suddenly inflate several times.

After engulfing Feng Zengyuan entirely, it returned to its original state in an instant.

The True Immortal's corpse remained silently and majestically standing there.

But Feng Zengyuan was nowhere to be found.

Everyone felt their scalps tingle and instinctively retreated backward.

"Didn't he die? Why did he suddenly attack?"

"Look, hasn't that figure become clearer? It even resembles Feng Zengyuan somewhat!"

"What's happening? We've retreated so far, yet we haven't distanced ourselves from the True Immortal's corpse. Instead, we're getting closer and closer?"

...

Panic spread through the crowd.

Even though they had undergone "adaptation" and theoretical learning, losing Qian Ruochang's protection and truly facing a True Immortal corpse that could attack at any moment, they inevitably descended into chaos.

However, among them, there were still outstanding individuals who remained undaunted in the face of danger.

"We cannot continue to drag this out. Otherwise, who knows who will end up being dissected!" Jiang Yuming said sternly.

"We are all destined to hunt True Immortals in the future. What is there to fear from a mere corpse?" Jin Changyue finally opened her tightly closed eyes.

To be precise, it was triple pupils.

It seemed as if three different personalities existed within Jin Changyue's body: one angry, one compassionate, and one empty.

The three swords behind her also unsheathed with a resonant hum.

Three blinding sword lights illuminated the darkened space.

The previously indistinct True Immortal's corpse revealed its full form.

Its pale face, its features, were actually identical to Qian Ruochang, who had led them here!

Even the sinister smile on its face was exactly the same.

The smiles of the two overlapped in everyone's minds.

"What's going on? Could it be that Boss Qian met with misfortune?"

Qian Ruochang's smile before his disappearance led everyone to indulge in wild speculations.

Their minds in disarray.

"Putting on a show!" Jin Changyue, however, roared, her anger intensifying.

The three sword lights merged into one.

Stabbing into the True Immortal's brow.

A drop of blood seeped from its brow.

Still furious, Jin Changyue was about to unleash another sword technique when a flash of light enveloped her body, and she vanished without a trace.

After a moment of stunned silence, Dao Yuan, Jiang Yuming, and Nangong Hongzhao all came to their senses and unleashed their strongest divine abilities towards the True Immortal's corpse.

Li Fan did the same.

However, while using the power of the Dao Net to conjure a dagger, he did not forget to loudly remind them, "Brothers, do not panic! Jin Changyue has surely completed the test and was safely teleported away. All we need to do is leave a wound on the True Immortal's corpse!"

The illusory dagger, arriving after the others, directly appeared at the True Immortal's face.

With a horizontal slash, it cut open from the corner of its mouth.

The smile, which was identical to the hint left by Qian Ruochang, was instantly disrupted by Li Fan.

The others also broke free from their mental illusions, as if waking from a dream, and unleashed their full might.

Having completed the act of dissecting the True Immortal's corpse, Li Fan was teleported away one step ahead.

He ranked second among the crowd, right behind Jin Changyue.

Not long after, Dao Yuan and the others' figures also emerged successively.

"Brother Ma, how were you able to use the power of the Dao Net just now?" Dao Yuan asked, somewhat confused.

"We couldn't sense the Dao Net's presence at all, which is why we were forced to use our own divine abilities to dissect the corpse," Jiang Yuming also asked, frowning deeply, staring intently at Li Fan.

Li Fan heard this and feigned surprise, "What are you two talking about? We are in the core of the Dao Net, how could there not be the power of the Dao Net around us?"

This counter-question left them both speechless.

As they were about to say more, more people who had completed the test and were teleported out began to appear. It was no longer convenient to speak further.

Li Fan's earlier words of reminder, and his act of disrupting the horrifying appearance of the True Immortal's corpse, had clearly benefited those who came later.

Everyone expressed their gratitude to Li Fan.

It wasn't until Qian Ruochang reappeared that the lively scene was broken.

"You, you, you..."

"You performed well. As for the others, you barely passed." Qian Ruochang pointed at Jin Changyue, Li Fan, Dao Yuan, and the other five who came out first, saying so.

"I hope you can maintain such默契 (mòqì - tacit understanding) and mutual assistance when hunting True Immortals." This statement was directed towards Li Fan.

Li Fan's expression grew solemn, and he cupped his hands, "Your junior will certainly remember."

Qian Ruochang let out a cold snort.

The light and shadow around everyone flickered continuously.

As if rapidly surfacing from deep water to the shore, they instantly transitioned from the Deep Net back to the normal realm of the Shining Star Sea.

"The bait has been chosen."

"Now, I will take you to set up the trap."

Utilizing the power of the Dao Net, they traversed rapidly. In the blink of an eye, everyone arrived at the edge of the Shining Star Sea.

Ahead, the crowd saw only darkness.

A place devoid of life.

It was the direction Li Fan had come from, the Annihilation Land.

After traveling along a narrow strip of vital star field for another half-day, until they were completely outside the Dao Net's coverage, everyone materialized in reality.

"Boss Qian, are we going to act here?"

Even Jin Changyue, who had always been confident, was now filled with doubt.

Qian Ruochang pointed ahead, "No, no. We need to go further!"

"But without the Dao Net, how can we possibly defeat that 'Formless' Immortal?" everyone anxiously asked.

"Who says we don't have the Dao Net? Don't we have the 'External Dao Manifestation' with us?"

Thinking of Qian Ruochang's reminder, everyone suddenly reacted.

Li Fan looked back towards where they came from. Indeed, he saw a faint, illusory Dao Net.

As if the perceived position of light had been distorted, stretching the shadow of this Dao Net infinitely.

It had arrived outside the Dao Net's coverage.

Connected to the true Dao Net by only a single Dao string.

"This Formless Immortal is cunning and treacherous. Capturing him within the Dao Net is truly difficult."

"But outside the Dao Net, in the territory originally belonging to True Immortals, his vigilance will be greatly reduced."

"Let's go. We need to go deeper, to a place where he will feel completely safe," Qian Ruochang said, continuing to lead everyone deeper into the Annihilation Land.

Within the Annihilation Land, there were not many areas of vitality.

The route was almost identical to the one leading to the High Wall of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

This made Li Fan suspect that the destination was within the High Wall.

Fortunately, Qian Ruochang seemed to be very familiar with the area. He bypassed the location of the High Wall and continued deeper into the Annihilation Land.

Finally, in a narrow, circular vital star domain, they stopped.

Three-quarters of the boundary of this place had already been ravaged by the Dao Annihilation Tribulation.

Only a narrow passage formed by the remaining quarter connected to the outside.

Qian Ruochang seemed very familiar with this place and found a patch of floating ruins within this star domain.

"Let me see, it should be here," Qian Ruochang muttered softly, picking up a few broken stones from the ground and observing them.

"First, set up the 'External Dao Manifestation'," he instructed, then continued to collect similar broken stones from the ground of the ruins.

Li Fan appeared to be diligently executing the Dao Net commands along with everyone else, but his attention followed Qian Ruochang as he roamed the ruins.

He was not using the intent of this "Ma Tiande" body.

Instead, he was using the power of the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss, which covered this star domain.

This place was close to the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, Li Fan's current lair, and was naturally covered by the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss.

"It's just ordinary ruins, what could be so mysterious about it that it attracts He Gan Xian?"

Li Fan wondered.

But soon, Qian Ruochang provided the answer.

Because when he returned after circling around and scattered the pile of broken stones on the ground.

A faint aura emanated from them, which Li Fan found somewhat familiar.

"This is... the Ascension Platform of the Immortal Realm?"

"Not the one from the Immortal Ruins above the Xuanhuang Realm."

"But from another star domain's survivor."

Qian Ruochang suddenly clapped his hands in front of the pile of broken stones, and they instantly turned into dust.

Then, under the glow, this cloud of dust transformed into an octagonal, square pavilion.

Chapter 1456: The Immortal Sealing Platform Seals the True Immortal

A scene akin to the ancient Ascension Platform reappeared, a vast and sacred aura radiating from this octagonal pavilion. The onlookers were immediately shaken. Even though they did not understand what this pavilion was, their attention was instinctively drawn to it. As if by a great attraction, everyone present could not shift their gaze. Even the creator of the octagonal Ascension Platform, Qian Ruochang himself, was momentarily stunned.

However, as a strong individual capable of being ordered to capture the Nameless Immortal, he quickly recovered from the illusion. He first integrated this miniature octagonal pavilion into the localized Dao Net that had been following everyone. When the vision of the octagonal pavilion shifted from solid to ethereal, Qian Ruochang took out a ball of bloody light. The blood-red light seemed to be sealed by some power, constantly colliding with an invisible boundary but unable to escape. Li Fan vaguely heard furious roars from within the blood-red ball of light.

Qian Ruochang remained unmoved. With his right hand, he formed a sword with two fingers and stabbed it into the blood-red ball of light. Li Fan keenly felt the localized Dao Net churn like a stormy sea. The freshly built localized Dao Net, not yet large or stable, gave a sense of precariousness. Clearly, Qian Ruochang's stab was not solely from his own strength but borrowed a large amount of the Dao Net's power.

"Everyone, do not be distracted. Quickly help Boss Qian stabilize the situation." Li Fan also wanted to see the method Qian Ruochang used to lure He Gan Xian. Seeing the newly recruited Immortal Hunters still engrossed in the allure of the octagonal Ascension Platform, he spoke up to remind them.

As if awakened from a dream, everyone reluctantly shifted their gaze. Most of them then focused on constructing the localized Dao Net. However, a small number still kept glancing at the Ascension Platform from time to time. The yearning in their eyes flashed and vanished. Coincidentally, these distracted individuals were not the mediocre ones among the group but were elites like Jin Changyue and Dao Yuan.

"It seems that even mortals within the Dao Net still have a fatal innate attraction to ascension," Li Fan understood.

With everyone's help, the swaying localized Dao Net gradually stabilized. Qian Ruochang's two fingers also safely retreated from the blood-red ball of light, though the fingertips were completely stained, turning into a glaring scarlet. It seemed to be the crucial step. To prevent external interference, Qian Ruochang waved his hand and set up defensive measures around himself. Li Fan could feel that at this moment, almost ninety-nine percent of the localized Dao Net's power was being mobilized by Qian Ruochang.

"Poof! Poof!" Amidst the exclamations of the crowd, Qian Ruochang's robust body's flesh and blood repeatedly exploded, revealing bare white bones. This was due to the sudden pressure exceeding his limits. However, what astonished the newly recruited Immortal Hunters present, including Li Fan, was that Qian Ruochang's bones were not ordinary human bones. Instead, they emitted a seven-colored crystalline light, lacking physical form, as if entirely composed of countless Dao Net strings! Under the augmentation of the Dao Net's power, the ethereal flesh and blood rapidly regenerated, covering the Dao string bones.

Qian Ruochang ignored the reactions of the crowd. Using the scarlet on his fingertips as ink and his fingers as a brush, he wrote in the air above the octagonal Ascension Platform. The content of this writing seemed to be some kind of secret. Even though he was exposed to his own Dao string bones, he was unusually concerned about these written symbols. He diverted the power of the surrounding Dao Net into a hazy mist curtain, obscuring the vision of the crowd.

At such a critical moment, there were no more spectacles to see, and the newly recruited Immortal Hunters all showed disappointed expressions. However... Qian Ruochang used the vast majority of the localized Dao Net's power to write this symbol. This obscuring technique could deceive the young Immortal Hunters, and even Li Fan's divine sense clone. But it could not deceive the vast, carefree dream consciousness of this place. As if looking down from above, piercing through the mist, it saw the scene happening within the obstruction clearly.

"This is..."

"Very similar to the 'Immortal and Mortal Transformation' symbol, but it goes in a different direction at several key nodes."

Strictly speaking, the Dao Net's obscuring technique was indeed extraordinary. Even the localized Dao Net was far superior to Li Fan's dreamland, which was built on the foundation of the Xuanhuang beings. However, do not forget that Li Fan himself was one of the builders of this localized Dao Net. He had a profound understanding of its construction, coupled with the miniature projection of the Great Dao within his own divine sense. Deciphering it was naturally much easier than simply using brute force. Without alerting the enemy, Li Fan quietly observed.

When the mysterious symbol was completely written, the octagonal Ascension Platform also erupted with a burst of strong light. Seven-colored auspicious clouds emerged, golden flowers scattered everywhere, and immortal birds chirped auspiciously. It was exactly like the scene of cultivators achieving Dao and ascending in ancient legends!

Before the phenomena dissipated, an aura Li Fan was extremely familiar with was born in this space. True Immortal! From the small Ascension Platform, a palm-sized figure flew out. It was entirely red, as if painted by Qian Ruochang with scarlet blood. Though small, in Li Fan's eyes, it was no different from a True Immortal! Not just in gaining the 'momentum' of an immortal, thereby no longer belonging to the same category as mortals. More so because of the immortal spiritual energy lingering on this little figure!

Li Fan's pupils constricted. What he had previously envisioned but failed to achieve – using the Immortal Realm's Ascension Platform to connect to the Infinite Sea – had now been accomplished by the Shining Star Sea forces. And it was even more comprehensive than he had imagined! Not just in one aspect of immortality. But in all-around creation of immortals!

"Could it be that the Shining Star Sea can now mass-produce True Immortals?" Li Fan stared intently at the small True Immortal figure, his heart churning like a storm. Even more terrifying was that, judging by Qian Ruochang's skilled demeanor, this was clearly not the first time he had done this. While filled with disbelief, Li Fan did not act rashly. He continued to observe. This small figure did not resemble Qian Ruochang. Instead, it bore some resemblance to the vague image Li Fan had seen in the blood-red ball of light, which had continuously tried to break free. After being "created" by Qian Ruochang, it did not dart around. Instead, it quietly sat cross-legged, closed its eyes, and began to rest.

The creation of the immortal was successful, and Qian Ruochang breathed a sigh of relief. The scarlet on his fingertips, which had been present since the appearance of the small immortal figure, had already faded. And the octagonal Ascension Platform before him, having completed its mission, turned to dust. Qian Ruochang showed a look of regret but was powerless to stop it. He bowed respectfully to the small immortal figure before him. The small immortal figure seemed to possess sentience and directly entered Qian Ruochang's body. Qian Ruochang's Dao string bones were no ordinary matter, but a carrier of the Great Dao. Thus, he could actually contain the body of a True Immortal with his mortal body!

After adapting to the new power attached to his body, Qian Ruochang finally withdrew his concealment and appeared before the crowd. Among the young Immortal Hunters, only a few noticed the change in Qian Ruochang. They looked surprised and uncertain. However, they knew better than to ask what they shouldn't. They obediently waited for Boss Qian to speak.

"The bait and the net are both ready. Next, we will formally begin the hunt."

"Are you all ready?"

As Qian Ruochang spoke, he gently took down the pillar he had been carrying on his shoulder. He swung it casually, as if it were a light wooden stick, astonishing the new Immortal Hunters. But they instinctively replied in unison, "We will surely slay the True Immortal!"

Qian Ruochang nodded with great satisfaction. He glanced at this circular area of vitality and whispered, "This place will be the net for the Nameless Immortal."

With that, he swept the giant pillar in his hand across the front of him. Although the giant pillar remained in his hand, an invisible wave of destruction spread across this small vital area. In an instant, it flattened and crushed all the floating ruins that remained. Then, it continued along the narrow channel outside the circular vital area, spreading far out towards the Annihilation Land. Where it finally led, no one knew. Like a stone thrown into the sea, causing ripples in the star sea.

Mortals could not discover the peculiarity of these ripples, only perceiving them as powerful, anomalous energy fluctuations. However, those who had reached the immortal realm, like Li Fan, could perceive information from these ripples. Including the identity of the True Immortal who triggered this ripple, his location, and the reason for his action. Li Fan carefully savored the contents of the ripple, his expression gradually becoming strange. No matter how he looked at it, this so-called trap seemed very clumsy. With such a wide range of dissemination, how could they be sure that He Gan Xian would be the one to fall for it? Moreover, He Gan Xian had survived so many calamities and acted with extreme caution. Could such a simple method of attracting attention truly trick him? Li Fan deeply doubted it. Unless...

"This True Immortal official, the so-called guard official of the Qiong Qu Star Domain, is an old acquaintance of He Gan Xian!"

"And he was captured by the Immortal Hunters not long ago, and He Gan Xian is unaware of this."

"Even more so..."

Recalling the incident where the Xi and Yi Immortals successfully escaped using the World-Crossing Profound Coffin, this guard official lurking near the Shining Star Sea was very likely there for the World-Crossing Profound Coffin!

"In that case, Qian Ruochang must also be genuinely carrying a World-Crossing Profound Coffin."

"Calling it a trap is not entirely false."

"If He Gan Xian is truly capable, and can kill all the ambushing forces here, then he will naturally obtain the Profound Coffin."

"And that small True Immortal..."

Li Fan observed the subtle changes in Qian Ruochang's expression, which had already differed slightly from before. Although the change was generally negligible, Li Fan was certain it was an influence from the small True Immortal possessing him.

"To successfully activate the power of the Ascension Platform, one must use corresponding True Immortal inscription characters. For example, 'Immortal and Mortal Transformation,' and the one Qian Ruochang just wrote. Perhaps, it must be written by a specific True Immortal to be effective."

"Guard official..."

"The Shining Star Sea has mastered the method of imitating True Immortal identities using their essence blood. They can even deceive the identity authentication of the Infinite Sea."

Within Li Fan's mind, he repeatedly recalled that symbol, analyzing its potential usability on the stone tablet left by King Xuan Yuan. After the True Immortal ripple was emitted, it was like a clay ox entering the sea, with no response. Qian Ruochang, however, looked as if he was certain the Nameless Immortal would take the bait, and methodically issued a series of commands to the newly recruited Immortal Hunters. One command after another was activated, and everyone hid within the localized Dao Net. Qian Ruochang then used immortal spiritual energy to conceal them. Even Li Fan, peeking with his dream power, could not find their figures. The Realm Annihilation black arrows were distributed and merged into everyone's bodies, ready to be unleashed at any moment. The Dao string connecting the localized Dao Net to the main Dao Net was also severed at some unknown time. Although the support of the Shining Star Sea's main Dao Net was gone, Li Fan, hidden within the localized Dao Net, did not feel a significant weakening of the Dao Net's power. This was likely due to Qian Ruochang, who was stationed at the center of the localized Dao Net with a body composed of myriad Dao strings.

"It seems that bringing us along for this immortal hunt is completely an encumbrance."

"With the combat power Qian Ruochang is currently displaying, he could directly contend with He Gan Xian. We are completely unnecessary for the fight..."

"Or perhaps, these young Immortal Hunters have other uses."

All the experiences from this training flashed through Li Fan's mind. He pondered the possibilities. In the void of the circular vital area, Qian Ruochang had already taken out a Profound Coffin. Judging by its appearance, it was exactly the same as the one everyone had seen in their first mission. Qian Ruochang stared at the Profound Coffin for a long time, then gently patted its lid. Then he leaped in and lay down inside. However, he did not completely seal the lid, leaving a small gap. The newly recruited Immortal Hunters, hidden within the Dao Net, patiently waited for the prey to appear. Located in the Annihilation Land, there were no other living beings in this starfield except them. Time passed in deathly silence.

After an unknown period, someone suddenly noticed that the calm Dao Net strings seemed to tremble slightly. However, upon closer inspection, it seemed like their own illusion. Within the Dao Net, there was still no other presence.

"It's not an illusion."

"Someone is coming," Dao Yuan said in a deep voice, both nervous and somewhat excited. Since the initial slight tremor, the Nameless Immortal had shown no further trace. Whether he was still within the localized Dao Net at this moment, everyone was unaware. Compared to the invisible and inaudible Xi and Yi Immortals before, this Nameless Immortal was clearly even more unfathomable.

Just as everyone was at a loss, a faint divine chant suddenly arose from the Profound Coffin. The crowd found the sound familiar; it was the same sound they had heard when the Xi and Yi Immortals escaped using the coffin. However, last time they observed from afar, but this time Qian Ruochang was inside the coffin, and they were all within the Dao Net, so they heard it more clearly. Slowly, the way everyone looked at the Profound Coffin subtly changed. Their vision was divided into two parts: on the left, a world-ending calamity of immense destruction; on the right, a new, beautiful world without worries. The stark contrast inevitably made everyone's hearts produce the thought of wanting to flee into the Profound Coffin to avoid disaster.

Chapter 1457: Two Immortals in the Coffin Fight

The chanting from within the World-Crossing Profound Coffin grew more rapid. A transcendent aura also gradually enveloped the Profound Coffin. The gap left in the coffin lid became smaller and smaller, as if Qian Ruochang inside the Profound Coffin was truly going to follow the example of the Xi and Yi Immortals and escape to another world!

The new Immortal Hunters, also enticed by the Profound Coffin and wanting to seize the opportunity to enter it, suddenly found themselves bound by the Dao Net, unable to move. They could only watch helplessly as the situation seemed to spiral out of control.

As panic set in among the crowd, it was Dao Yuan who first stepped forward to stabilize their emotions: "Don't panic, trust Boss Qian!" However, the reality was that besides choosing to trust, they had no other recourse. But their trust seemed to be in vain.

The sealing of the coffin proceeded steadily and, under everyone's despairing gaze, finally closed completely. The Profound Coffin then erupted with dazzling seven-colored light in an instant!

But... the scene they had anticipated, of the Profound Coffin escaping to another world, did not occur. Instead, the chanting abruptly stopped. The seven-colored light seemed to freeze, motionless. The vital area within the Annihilation Land plunged into an eerie silence.

Then, the World-Crossing Profound Coffin suddenly twitched violently. *Bang! Bang! Bang!* Then the commotion grew louder, each tremor seeming to echo in everyone's hearts, as if a ferocious beast was trapped inside, desperately trying to escape!

As everyone was in a state of bewilderment, they suddenly noticed that the Dao Net's restraint had quietly disappeared. It wasn't intentional on anyone's part. It was just that at this moment, almost all the power of the localized Dao Net had been mobilized, and even the portion that had restrained them could no longer be spared.

"This... the Nameless Immortal has entered the coffin, and Boss Qian is fighting him one-on-one inside?" Jin Changyue was the first to react, exclaiming in disbelief. "We didn't even notice his movements? And this is under the coverage of the localized Dao Net!"

"Oh no, Boss Qian is facing the Nameless Immortal alone; could he be in danger?" Everyone then exchanged glances. They were both shocked by the unfathomable strength of the Nameless Immortal and worried about Qian Ruochang's predicament.

But they were powerless. Despite their initial bravado, faced with a True Immortal's battle, they clearly realized that without the Dao Net's power, they couldn't possibly intervene in battles of this caliber. Moreover, the Profound Coffin was now sealed shut. Without knowing how to open it, even if they wished to participate, they had no way in.

"This Nameless Immortal acts so mysteriously. Boss Qian had no choice but to use himself as bait, and staged the event of the Profound Coffin about to close and escape, to force him to reveal himself. With the coffin sealed, even if the Nameless Immortal is skilled at escape, he'll have nowhere to go. Therefore, what we need to do is..." After some thought, everyone quickly reached a consensus.

"Quick! Transport this coffin back to the Immortal Hunter headquarters!"

Even with the suppression of the entire localized Dao Net, the Profound Coffin, which was meant to be bait and had now become a prison, vibrated more and more intensely. Everyone felt their hearts pounding from a distance, fearing that the Nameless Immortal trapped within would break free at any moment.

"This place is far from the Shining Star Sea. Using ordinary flight techniques to return will definitely be too late. Stabilize the localized Dao Net and re-establish the connection with the Shining Star Sea's Dao Net!" Everyone quickly reached an agreement. After training for so long, they finally had some tacit understanding.

Without anyone needing to give orders, commands were issued one after another, and the localized Dao Net, which was precarious in the face of the True Immortal's battle, slowly became stable again. The next step was to reconnect the localized Dao Net to the main Dao Net.

Although the Dao string that previously connected the two had been severed, the location was not too far from the Dao Net's boundary. It only required one person to fly at extreme speed to act as a medium to establish a successful connection.

"I'll go!" Now was not the time for politeness and deferral. Jin Changyue stated directly. She opened her triple pupils again. Perhaps due to the frequency of use in a short period, her strange eyes were filled with bloodshot patterns like scarlet spiderwebs, quite eerie. Two pupils stared into the distance at the target, while the central void pupil strangely looked around.

Sword light like a rainbow, before Jin Changyue finished speaking, she had already vanished from everyone's sight. And only then did her parting words echo back, "The number of people... there's something wrong!"

Everyone was stunned at first, then looked at each other. A few breaths later, a chilling coldness swept over everyone. There were twenty-eight new Immortal Hunters in this batch. Excluding Jin Changyue who left, and Feng Zengyuan who died when dissecting the True Immortal, there should have been twenty-six people remaining. However, the number of people left on site was only twenty-five!

More critically, after recalling and tallying, everyone couldn't even recall the name or information of this mysteriously missing person! It was as if this person had never existed in the world from the beginning.

Everyone looked at the World-Crossing Profound Coffin in unison. A terrifying thought arose in their minds: "That Nameless Immortal... was lurking among us from the start?"

Li Fan's expression was also extremely solemn. Even with his miniature Dao Net in his divine sense, he could only recall a vague shadow, unable to determine the identity of the person. Li Fan's thoughts raced: "Did they infiltrate from the beginning, or replace someone midway?"

"But regardless, since they knew this was a trap, why did they still enter the coffin at the last moment?" Recalling the scene where the World-Crossing Profound Coffin erupted with dazzling seven-colored light, Li Fan suddenly seemed to understand: "Qian Ruochang must have long anticipated the Nameless Immortal's stealthy infiltration."

"His jumping into the coffin was a blatant trap. If the Nameless Immortal hadn't appeared in the end, he would have truly escaped like the Xi and Yi Immortals!" "And seeing an opportunity to completely escape disaster right before his eyes, the Nameless Immortal ultimately couldn't resist the temptation. Moreover, the Nameless Immortal had been secretly observing Qian Ruochang at close range for some time. Perhaps he believed that even if it was a trap, he could suppress the opponent with his strength. That's why he made a desperate gamble..." Li Fan mused, seemingly reconstructing the truth of the matter.

But soon, a new problem presented itself to Li Fan. "Qian Ruochang could actually endure and resist the temptation of escaping to another world, and instead focus on hunting the Nameless Immortal when he appeared... "Capturing this True Immortal was actually more important to Qian Ruochang than escaping to another world?" Li Fan couldn't help but look at Qian Ruochang with newfound respect.

As time passed, the struggle within the Profound Coffin did not cease but intensified. Qian Ruochang seemed to be inevitably falling into a disadvantageous position. Even with everyone's combined efforts, they could barely stabilize the localized Dao Net. Like duckweed in the wind, it was about to be completely blown away and detach from the Great Dao it was attached to.

Just as despair began to set in among the crowd, a beam of sword light appeared from the darkness in the distance. It was Jin Changyue's valiant figure, flying rapidly towards them! Behind her, everyone could vaguely see a Dao string glowing with crystalline white light.

Although the Dao string was only as thin as a thread, it was still as heavy as heaven and earth. Jin Changyue, pulling it, was no longer under the pressure of carrying a cultivation world. Even so, her flight speed did not slow down at all, indicating her extraordinary strength.

As Jin Changyue's figure drew closer, and the Dao Net connection seemed imminent, for some reason, her flight speed suddenly slowed down. Everyone vaguely saw Jin Changyue's triple pupils, her eyelids repeatedly closing and opening.

"This is bad, Jin Changyue must be at her limit. Hurry and go receive her!" Everyone exclaimed. Dao Yuan and most of the others remained to stabilize the Dao Net with great difficulty, while Jiang Yuming led three others to intercept Jin Changyue and the Dao string that was crucial for their survival.

Jin Changyue seemed to have truly exhausted all her strength, her flight speed slowing down further in the dark void, until she completely stopped. Her eyelids closed, and she fell into a deep sleep!

Seeing this, Jiang Yuming's heart grew anxious, and he accelerated his approach. However... before reaching Jin Changyue's side, the four Immortal Hunters who went to intercept her also flew slower and slower. Finally, like Jin Changyue, they quietly fell asleep.

The rhythm of the commands issued by Dao Yuan and the remaining new Immortal Hunters collectively faltered. Although they didn't know what had happened, an ominous feeling welled up in their hearts. Before they could speak, a strange and unfathomable force enveloped them. It felt as if all the fatigue accumulated since birth had erupted at once.

Many Immortal Hunters instantly fell asleep. Even elites like Dao Yuan and Nangong Hongzhao could not persist for long under such intense drowsiness. Soon, they fell into a deep slumber, lost in the dreamland. Li Fan's assumed identity, "Ma Tiande," was no exception.

The entire starscape, aside from the violently trembling Profound Coffin, had no other signs of activity. The new Immortal Hunters slept soundly, while the battle between the two True Immortals in the Profound Coffin, however, showed no signs of concluding for the time being.

One day, two days... When thirty days had passed, the individuals within the coffin finally seemed to sense the potential changes outside, or perhaps the outcome of their battle was finally decided. The commotion within the coffin gradually subsided. However, no one opened the coffin and emerged. The World-Crossing Profound Coffin simply floated silently in the void.

...

In the Xuanhuang Realm. Li Fan, observing the floating Profound Coffin through his dream power, had intervened after careful consideration. He had even prepared to "Return to Truth" at any moment if his true identity was discovered. Whether the Nameless Immortal, the target of the Immortal Hunters, was He Gan Xian or not, both had value for Li Fan to resolve or interact with.

After infiltrating the Shining Star Sea, he had gained a preliminary understanding of its various forces. However, regarding the True Immortal side, which opposed the Shining Star Sea, Li Fan remained in a state of ignorance. Li Fan's true body, besides lacking immortal spiritual energy, was no different from an 'Immortal'. He could barely be considered in the same faction. If he could save this Nameless Immortal and learn something from him, it would undoubtedly be beneficial for Li Fan's plans.

However, Li Fan did not brazenly appear to confront him directly. Instead, he quietly observed the changes within the Profound Coffin. Like a hunter waiting for prey to take the bait, he had plenty of patience.

The silence within the Profound Coffin lasted for a full seven days. Still sensing no external changes, the individuals within seemed to lose patience. The divine chant resumed. It seemed they intended to escape to another world directly, regardless of the external situation!

But the chant did not last long. In the void, another ethereal murmuring voice sounded simultaneously. Unlike the chant, this voice had a completely different tone, causing the chanting from within the coffin to change subtly. The seven-colored light also seemed to be disturbed, flashing continuously but unable to coalesce.

The individuals within the coffin were not resigned. After a brief pause, the colorful light suddenly surged, even doubling the intensity of the chanting. But as the saying goes, "a foot of Dao is a foot of devil," the illusory sounds from the surrounding dreamland, amplified dozens of times, completely suppressed the chanting. The seven-colored light retreated back into the Profound Coffin, leaving no further trace. After completing its interference, the murmuring voice disappeared as mysteriously as it had appeared.

In this void, there was once again only a Profound Coffin. And the newly recruited Immortal Hunters floating silently. Li Fan had personally woven a beautiful dream for them. Of course, out of caution, this dream was independent of the Xuanhuang Realm's dreamland and could be discarded at any time. Coupled with the high wall's obstruction, it would not leave any flaws.

Gathering all the dream power from outside the high wall, along with the demonic sounds from the Xuan Yuan clan's bloodline memory, he could indeed interrupt the World-Crossing Profound Coffin's traversal. Li Fan had previously used the Grand Master's 'Calamity Averting Profound Sound' to counteract the influence of the Heavenly King Xuan Yuan's demonic sounds. Therefore, when he heard the chanting sound of the Profound Coffin activating, which bore some resemblance to the Calamity Averting Profound Sound, this idea arose. Now, it had been proven effective.

"It seems that these two kinds of Great Dao melodies are fundamentally opposed to each other," Li Fan mused.

The Profound Coffin was trapped in this location. The Shining Star Sea Immortal Hunters had not ignored it. Clearly, the Immortal Hunter headquarters had some knowledge of Qian Ruochang's plan. They had dispatched people to the edge of the Dao Net to search for the whereabouts of the missing Profound Coffin and the Immortal Hunter group.

However, to deceive the Nameless Immortal, Qian Ruochang had clearly not revealed too much. The Annihilation Land was still an unknown and dangerous place for the Shining Star Sea. Furthermore, Li Fan had already severed the Dao string, so they would not be able to reach him anytime soon.

"Let's see how long you can last." To capture the Nameless Immortal, this Profound Coffin must have been tampered with, and could only be opened from the outside. Unless their strength was sufficient to shatter the Profound Coffin directly, they could not escape from the sealed coffin. This was originally Qian Ruochang's near-perfect hunting method. But unexpectedly, it had now become Li Fan's reliance to make a move.

Chapter 1458: First Test of True and False

To force the two immortals in the coffin to take further action, and to further study this so-called World-Crossing Profound Coffin, Li Fan unleashed the power of his Demonic Killing Immortal Soul, enveloping the Profound Coffin layer by layer.

The Demonic Killing Immortal Soul possessed power close to the Tribulation of Annihilation, capable of almost completely sealing the Dao Net's power. The faint black mist not only surrounded the Profound Coffin but also seeped into it uncontrollably.

The World-Crossing Profound Coffin, although it claimed to be able to escape all calamities in the world, did so by fleeing to other possibilities. In reality, it could not withstand the Tribulation of Annihilation. It could not even achieve complete isolation between the inside and outside of the coffin.

After a moment of silence, the two immortals in the coffin clearly sensed the destructive aura outside. Violent tremors reappeared within the World-Crossing Profound Coffin. However, this time the commotion was far more intense than before. The previous time was caused by the aftermath of their struggle, but now... it must be that the two immortals were trying to break open the coffin together!

But since the Profound Coffin could be chosen as a cage for the Nameless Immortal, it was not something that could be easily shattered. Even with Qian Ruochang and the Nameless Immortal working together, it was futile. After trying for a while, they quickly discovered that it was completely useless, so they changed their approach.

Under this life-or-death predicament, Li Fan truly witnessed the methods of True Immortals. A divine chant seemed to resume from within the coffin. However, this time, it was almost inaudible. It was only with the help of the Demonic Killing Immortal Soul's power, which enveloped the Profound Coffin, that Li Fan could barely sense it.

The singer appeared to be Qian Ruochang. Li Fan intended to repeat his previous trick, using dream power to weave demonic chanting to interfere. But the two rhythms seemed to exist in different worlds, running parallel and independently, unable to affect each other!

The chanting continued, and the seven-colored light within the coffin grew brighter. "A power is isolating the Profound Coffin from the world. Although I can sense it through the Demonic Killing Immortal Soul, I cannot have any influence on it." "This is the Nameless Immortal making a move." "Since we cannot break out of the coffin, let's choose to join forces and escape to another world."

Li Fan thought coldly. He had expected the reaction of the two immortals in the coffin when he used this life-or-death tactic. "Crossing possibilities..." "Let me see what exactly this entails."

The black mist transformed into countless tentacles, tightly entangled with the World-Crossing Profound Coffin. As an extension of Li Fan's senses, it touched and analyzed the essence of the Profound Coffin.

Without external interference, the World-Crossing Profound Coffin was fully activated. Seven-colored light instantly surged from within the coffin, even forcing back the power of the Demonic Killing Immortal Soul. Li Fan seemed to see countless phantoms appearing and layering upon the Profound Coffin simultaneously. Each phantom of the Profound Coffin was identical, but the scenery surrounding the Profound Coffin differed.

The chanting intensified, and the real Profound Coffin seemed to be drawn into these overlapping shadows, about to detach from reality. At the same time, the number of presenting Profound Coffin phantoms suddenly dropped infinitely. In the fleeting glimpses that intermittently appeared, Li Fan saw only "perfect worlds" that were not currently plagued by the Tribulation of Annihilation.

Although the Profound Coffin was still tightly bound, Li Fan's tactile sensation grew fainter and fainter. The Profound Coffin was about to fade from his grasp and escape. "This World-Crossing Profound Coffin does not unconditionally transfer to other possibilities. Instead, it seems it can only travel to possibilities where a World-Crossing Profound Coffin also exists." "Using the 'Unification' of the Profound Coffin to achieve escape from the current possibility." "So that's how it is..."

Li Fan vaguely understood. If different possibilities of the same entity could consume themselves across possibilities, then certain special items could naturally do the same. The Profound Coffin's so-called "world-crossing" cleverly utilized this characteristic. In fact, Li Fan using "Return to Truth" to retain items from a previous simulation and bring them back to this reality could be seen as a form of "Unification."

However, not all items can strengthen themselves through Unification continuously. Only the "Heaven and Earth Wonders" of the Xuanhuang Realm seem to self-devour each other when appearing simultaneously. As for the Dao Transformation Stone from outside the heavens, it could not. It required Li Fan to actively promote their fusion. "The materials used to forge this World-Crossing Profound Coffin should be similar in nature to the Wonders." "Being exactly identical to the Profound Coffins in other possibilities, only then can the power of Unification be used to jump between possibilities..."

No matter how powerful the entanglement force of the Demonic Killing Immortal Soul was, the World-Crossing Profound Coffin eventually became increasingly ethereal. While Li Fan observed and contemplated, the Profound Coffin was almost escaping from the current possibility. A power transcending everything, imperceptible even to True Immortals, quietly descended. "When true becomes false, and false becomes true."

In Li Fan's eyes, the seven familiar words appeared again. Now at the Half-Immortal realm, he could barely achieve "False becomes True." He could even create energy like the [Primordial Azure Source], which allowed demonic beasts to traverse possibilities, out of nothingness. But he had always been unable to grasp the path of "True becomes False."

Theoretically, destruction should be easier than creation. Li Fan had been pondering for a long time, until just now, by observing the entire process of the Profound Coffin's world-crossing with the Demonic Killing Immortal Soul, he finally realized he had been overthinking it. To turn a real, complete object into nothingness—this ability of "True becomes False"—the difficulty of execution was not determined by the target.

Whether the target was a powerhouse like Evil Su Bai or Black Heavenly Physician, or an insignificant ant on the ground, Li Fan's difficulty would be the same. Because as long as they were subject to "True and False Transformation," they could not resist the concept of "True becomes False." However, turning a complete object from true to false, and correspondingly turning a false object into true, with its existence not disappearing even after the power of true and false disappeared—this great achievement was naturally something the current Li Fan, who had barely entered the threshold, could not accomplish. "The true state of an object can be maintained for a certain period. But once it enters a false state, there is no chance of returning to true." "Once it disappears, it disappears forever."

The reason he suddenly considered this crucial point was that Li Fan observed that the process of the World-Crossing Profound Coffin "disappearing" from the current possibility was not instantaneous. Instead, the countless microscopic particles that constituted the Profound Coffin verified themselves with their counterparts in other possibilities. Then, they entered a state of "Unification" and escaped from the current possibility. It was not the Profound Coffin "itself" traversing, but rather dividing into countless "individuals." After appearing in other possibilities, they would re-form into a whole. "There are inherent constraints between possibilities. Compared to complete individuals, those extremely tiny particles, even beyond my observational capabilities, should be much easier to traverse." "Breaking down the whole into parts." "Similarly, what I need to do is not to turn the entire Profound Coffin from true to false directly." "As long as the verification process of the Profound Coffin is disrupted, making this Profound Coffin different from its original state."

The True-False Transformation instantly enveloped the Profound Coffin. In his mind, Li Fan recalled the feeling of repeatedly simulating rebirth, life after life. "True, becomes, False!" He said each word in his heart. The target was not the macroscopic individual of the Profound Coffin. But any single microscopic particle constituting the Profound Coffin that Li Fan could interact with. It was like gently wiping away a speck of dust.

The Profound Coffin appeared to have no external changes. But... The chanting reached its climax. However, the phantoms of the Profound Coffin within the seven-colored light suddenly extinguished. Although only an insignificant particle was missing, the Profound Coffin was no longer the World-Crossing Profound Coffin. From True to False, world-crossing was difficult to continue.

Qian Ruochang's chanting abruptly stopped. As if unable to accept this reality, the two immortals in the coffin remained motionless for a long time. The Profound Coffin was eerily silent. Qian Ruochang and the Nameless Immortal were as if they had already departed to another world, with no sound at all. They seemed to have accepted their fate and stopped struggling.

Li Fan's attention was not on the two of them. Instead, he was delighted by his successful execution of the True-False Transformation. Theoretically, the degree of "True becomes False" and "False becomes True" that he could achieve should be equivalent. This meant that even if he couldn't completely eliminate an individual for now, it was certainly not limited to wiping away a few particles. "I can now achieve a three-fold power stacking for a short time." "Conversely, I should also be able to achieve a certain degree of weakening."

In Li Fan's understanding, if a part of a complete object was suddenly removed, it would inevitably be weakened accordingly. As for where this weakness manifested... Li Fan instinctively wanted to experiment on himself. However, the moment this thought arose, his heart suddenly pounded. Even "Return to Truth" transmitted a fluctuation, as if issuing a warning. This was unprecedented. "It seems the weakening effect of True-False Transformation is more terrifying than I imagined." "This stab might even sever my own path."

The thought of wielding this terrifying power against himself made Li Fan hesitate. He knew that direct self-experimentation with this power was extremely risky. "This divine ability, capable of severing one's future." "And I vaguely feel that perhaps there's more to it." As if inspiration was within reach, but obscured by a layer of mist, Li Fan could not break through.

After a short rest, Li Fan began his experiment again. The blade of True-False Transformation fell inch by inch. Yin Changshou gradually became inferior to mortals in Li Fan's eyes. Mortals could still forge ahead on the path of cultivation through external resources, but the current Yin Changshou had completely severed his future path. No matter what method was used, he could not progress further.

"His cultivation has regressed in all aspects, which is already a certainty. However, why do I still feel that the true harm has not yet manifested?" Li Fan stared intently at Yin Changshou, gazing for a long time before delivering the final blow. Like repeatedly erasing with an eraser, eventually wiping away the drawing on the canvas. In reality, Yin Changshou did not disappear directly. Instead, some possibility was completely severed. Li Fan sensed something and suddenly looked up towards the heavens.

Chapter 1459: Hidden Secrets Within the Wall

This time, it was not some powerful being crossing possibilities and directly attacking. Instead, Li Fan vaguely sensed that outside the world, a certain existence's gaze had suddenly swept over.
