However, this person did not possess the strength of Black Heavenly Physician or Evil Su Bai, capable of accurately locking onto specific possible locations. Or perhaps Li Fan was within the high wall, protected by it. Regardless, this scan was a random probe, not an indication that the owner of the gaze had truly found Li Fan.

Even so, Li Fan's heart was suddenly filled with a sense of dread, as if being targeted by an ancient ferocious beast. He almost immediately activated "Return to Truth." Fortunately, the feeling of being stared at came and went quickly. In an instant, it completely vanished, as if Li Fan's illusion.

But Li Fan knew that what had just happened was definitely not an illusion.

"That gaze should have come from another Yin Changshou."

"My weakening of Yin Changshou in the current possibility actually attracted the attention of his counterparts in other possibilities..."

Li Fan pondered for a long time. Looking at the extremely dejected young man before him, Li Fan suddenly had a bold idea: "Could my [True-False Transformation] divine ability actually affect all of my counterparts in other possibilities simultaneously?"

This thought indeed excited Li Fan. But after careful consideration, Li Fan negated it. If the True-False Transformation ability operated simultaneously across countless possibilities, then the World-Crossing Profound Coffin would not have failed its verification process simply because a portion of its particles was removed.

Moreover, Li Fan was somewhat self-aware. Perhaps in the future, when his understanding of True-False Transformation deepened further, he might truly be able to act on all targets simultaneously. But with his current nascent level, he absolutely could not achieve such a degree.

Li Fan's thoughts churned, but he quickly guessed the reason why Yin Changshou from another possibility had cast his gaze.

"Based on the actions of Black Heavenly Physician and Evil Su Bai, powerful beings of that level seem to need to constantly devour their counterparts in other possibilities to grow stronger."

"This can be considered a form of cultivation, the so-called [All Selves Unite]."

"Theoretically, reaching this stage in one possibility implies that this person's talent is absolutely not weak. His counterparts in other possibilities might have different cultivation levels. But these are merely divergences caused by different opportunities. There will never be..."

"A situation where the path ahead is completely severed."

"Even a complete invalid who cannot cultivate, for powerhouses who can traverse possibilities, handling them should not be difficult. Treasures are innumerable throughout the star sea, and there are always ways to defy fate. Devouring them can also increase one's own strength. But the current Yin Changshou is an undeniable, completely anomalous 'poisonous pill'."

"Consuming it yields more harm than good."

"Among countless 'selves,' one suddenly appears that is similar yet completely different..."

"If Su Bai and Heavenly Physician back then had been subjected to this divine ability, perhaps they would not have been targeted."

It wasn't that Li Fan's True-False Transformation directly affected powerhouses who could traverse possibilities. Rather, it "poisoned" the "materials" for their enlightenment, thus severing their future path in an alternative way!

Of course, this kind of poison, it seemed, could only be inflicted by Li Fan, who wielded "Return to Truth."

"Although I cannot directly confront them yet, this move should be enough to disgust them."

Li Fan was quite satisfied. Perhaps there were crucial details in the cultivation process of [All Selves Unite] that Li Fan did not yet know. But based on Evil Su Bai's past "persistence," every "self" was extremely important. If a "self" in an existing possibility suffered such a fate, for a powerhouse of that level, it would undoubtedly be unacceptable.

"Severing only one individual in a possibility might not completely prevent achieving 'All Selves Unite.' But due to this acquired deficiency, they might be weaker than others by a notch. And it's irreparable."

Li Fan's gaze turned towards the heavens again. As if envisioning the figure of Black Heavenly Physician, his heart began to stir.

"When the end of this life arrives, I can experiment on Heavenly Physician. First, I'll apply the True-False Transformation divine ability, then deliberately send him outside the wall. Let's see how Black Heavenly Physician, who will arrive suddenly, will react."

Li Fan sent away the ten experimental subjects. He then stabilized his understanding of the True-False Transformation divine ability until his temporary enlightenment reached a bottleneck due to exhaustion.

The minor incident in the Xuanhuang Realm was just a brief moment. Li Fan's attention returned to the starry sky outside the high wall. Due to the inconsistent time flow, approximately thirty-odd days had passed here.

The True-False Transformation divine ability had forcibly interrupted the Profound Coffin's world-crossing. The two immortals in the coffin remained motionless for a long time under this deterrence. And Li Fan, during this period, by interacting with the Demonic Killing Immortal Soul, seemed to have found a way to forcibly open the coffin lid.

Ultimately, the Demonic Killing Immortal Soul, with its power close to the Tribulation of Annihilation, was the most terrifying destructive force in the mortal world. None could compare. Even though Li Fan's current realm was slightly weaker, with continuous erosion, even the Profound Coffin, despite its reputation for world-crossing, could not withstand it. It couldn't even achieve complete isolation.

But Li Fan did not act rashly. Given the divine abilities displayed by the two immortals in the coffin, his Demonic Killing Immortal Soul alone was insufficient to subdue them. Therefore, other methods were needed.

Qian Ruochang was relatively easy to deal with. The Demonic Killing Immortal Soul could isolate the Dao Net. Without the Dao Net's power, he was merely a bit stronger physically.

The difficult one was the Nameless Immortal. Li Fan had previously interacted with him at close range while he was undercover among the new Immortal Hunters and hadn't detected him. Clearly, his strength was likely above Li Fan's. Perhaps slightly inferior to the Starving Immortal in the Immortal Ruins, but likely not by much, as he was a True Immortal who had survived great calamities.

"His tricky part lies entirely in his [Nameless] characteristic. Severing all connections with the world..."

"Therefore, what I need to do is forcibly establish karma with him."

Li Fan's mind flashed through the methods he could utilize. Lights and shadows shifted continuously, finally settling on a chessboard filled with black and white pieces.

"Immortal Domain Fragment..."

Li Fan's eyes flickered. Although Li Fan could only collect faded pieces from fallen players, the presence of the Southern Immortal Pillar in the Immortal Domain indicated deep connections.

"I wonder if he can still ignore it despite carrying the weight of the Immortal Domain."

Li Fan's heart stirred. With a concrete plan, the current challenge was how to send the chess piece out. All of Li Fan's actions now relied on the power of the Unbounded Dreamland. The dream power could reconstruct a body outside the high wall, but it could not construct an Immortal Domain chess piece.

"However, the high wall is meant to restrain beings below the True Immortal level."

"Perhaps it cannot restrain Immortal Domain fragments after all."

After a moment of thought, Li Fan vaguely found the answer. Not all Immortal Domain fragments, but only one was retrieved. Pulled by Li Fan's power, it arrived at a weak point of the high wall. Outside the high wall, the Unbounded Dreamland power had been waiting for a long time to receive it. To prevent unexpected variables, Li Fan's true body also maintained full vigilance, ready to "Return to Truth" at any moment.

On the outskirts of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, beyond the continuous High Wall of the Ruined Realms, Li Fan's phantom manifested. Holding a chess piece between his right index and middle fingers, he looked solemn and then threw it fiercely forward.

Like the desperate gamble of Merchant Immortal Zhou Wang in the past, the chess piece, like a sword, flew from Li Fan's hand. Straight towards the high wall.

Unlike the grand spectacle caused by Li Fan's inducement of the Profound Immortal Boat crashing into the high wall, the Immortal Domain Fragment hitting the high wall was silent.

From the perspective within the high wall, the chess piece seemed to be directly swallowed, disappearing in an instant. And from the perspective outside the high wall...

Li Fan waited for a long time, but still didn't see the Immortal Domain chess piece he had thrown! His expression slightly changed. At this moment, Li Fan's dream power had spread throughout this Annihilation Land. If the chess piece had appeared here after crossing the high wall, he would definitely have sensed it.

But the chess piece had been missing for a long time...

Li Fan activated the dream power he had accumulated and explored outwards from the Annihilation Land. Trying to find his vanished chess piece. But after a long time, there was still no success.

"Even the mark I left on the chess piece has disappeared?"

Li Fan's mood became somewhat grim. Reflecting on everything that had happened in this short period.

"Could it be that the Immortal Domain fragment failed to traverse the high wall?"

Within the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, Li Fan searched the area where the chess piece had disappeared more carefully. No trace was found.

"Could it be the time difference between the inside and outside of the high wall that caused the anomaly? Perhaps I need to wait a bit longer?"

Thinking this, Li Fan patiently waited for a while longer. But another day passed, and the chess piece was still nowhere to be seen.

"Could the problem lie with the high wall itself?"

Within the Annihilation Land, dream power gathered near the high wall where he sensed it. The so-called high wall had no physical form. It only appeared inexplicably when the Great Dao collapsed due to the Tribulation of Annihilation, supporting the heavens from falling, creating a small area of survival amidst a completely destroyed region. It was the space left by the toppling ruins.

Li Fan stared intently at the void ahead. Suddenly he recalled that when the Profound Immortal Boat, under his instigation, made a desperate gamble and crashed into the high wall. At that time, when it seemed to connect the inside and outside of the high wall, the Utmost Darkness Star Sea seemed to have seen something terrifying and fled in panic. Li Fan also felt a sense of being observed, as if by something terrifying, looking through a transparent glass.

"Outside the high wall, the Shining Star Sea, is unaware of the existence of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea. From Qian Ruochang passing by the high wall without entering, it can be seen."

"Therefore, this inexplicable sense of dread. Combined with the mysteriously vanished chess piece..."

A somewhat unbelievable thought suddenly arose in Li Fan's mind.

"Could it be that there is something else *inside* the high wall?"

In this life, Li Fan escaped the high wall in an unconventional way using the Unbounded Dreamland power. But he only saw the inside and the outside, not the middle. This was because the wall was formless and intangible. However, since it could support the Utmost Darkness Star Sea and the surrounding Immortal Domain from being destroyed during the Tribulation of Annihilation. The high wall should not just be a void of laws. It might very well be a physical object, similar to the Nameless True Immortal's leg bone or the Southern Immortal Heavenly Pillar.

However, this physical object was hidden by some special means. Not only Li Fan, but even powerhouses like the Nameless Immortal and Qian Ruochang, who were close to the Nameless True Immortal realm, could not notice it.

"But He Gan Xian is not unfamiliar with the Xuanhuang Realm, and even has contact with Xuan Yuanhong. Could it be that this Nameless Immortal is not the He Gan Xian I always thought him to be?"

Li Fan's doubts arose. However, the most crucial thing now was to determine whether the idea of something "inside the wall" truly existed. The Unbounded Dreamland power enveloped the World-Crossing Profound Coffin layer by layer. Li Fan chose to temporarily set aside the two True Immortals in the coffin and deal with the unexpected matter of the wall first.

"The Xuanhuang Realm and the surrounding vast star domain were originally a secret experimental site for True Immortals of the upper realm. Although it was later abandoned, the high wall as a protective measure should also be part of this experimental site."

"..."

Although his desire to explore was urgent, Li Fan did not act rashly.

"Based on the feeling of being monitored that I had earlier, there might be living beings inside the wall. We must guard against it."

"Furthermore, the high wall might have selective interception. After all, the Heavenly Sword Sect and Merchant Immortal Boat truly passed through the wall. Or perhaps, they discovered something inside the wall?"

Recalling these two, they were not top-tier powers in the star sea. However, after crossing the high wall, they suddenly possessed the strength to hunt True Immortals. Even with the time difference, millions of years of accumulation. It seemed almost incredible.

"If they discovered something in the ruins of the Immortal Realm's experiment inside the wall, then this would make sense."

Thinking of this, Li Fan became truly curious about the "inside of the wall." The lost Immortal Domain chess piece could be retrieved by activating "Return to Truth" at any time; it was not worth worrying about.

"However, being inside the Immortal Domain chess piece and crashing into the high wall might be a good method."

"This matter is of great importance, and I must handle it personally."

Li Fan's true body pondered for a moment, then made a decision. In an instant, the materials for creating a clone appeared before him. He intended to forge a clone, a method he hadn't used in a long time. He had been in the Immortal Realm for some time. After understanding Mind Manifestation of Divinity and learning the secrets of the Shining Star Sea's Dao Net, Li Fan had new ideas about forging clones.

"Qian Ruochang's Dao string bones are an example worth emulating."

"The strength of this clone cannot be weak for exploring the inside of the wall."

Li Fan's mind moved, and various materials instantly fused together as if roasted by intense fire. A human body vaguely took shape.

"Dao Projection can be the heart's divinity." The human body suddenly became transparent, like a mirror reflecting all the Great Daos. Dao light condensed, weaving a network within the body.

"Immortal Domain Fragment can be the body's bones." Li Fan whispered, throwing an Immortal Domain chess piece. The Immortal Domain chess piece continuously unfolded, transforming into a pillar-like entity, slowly integrating into the Dao Net.

Chapter 1460: Li Bueren Destroys the World

A small chess piece could evolve into an Immortal Domain fragment. Fundamentally, the so-called chess piece was the superposition of countless True Immortal inscription characters. True Immortal inscription characters were one of the methods True Immortals used to interpret the Great Dao. In the past, the Profound Immortal Boat, after obtaining an Immortal Domain chess piece, transformed it into the external armor of the Immortal Boat. And now, under Li Fan's continuous urging, the thrown chess piece, adhering to the Dao Net projection in his mind, unfolded and flowed, transforming into a humanoid body. However, even at this stage, it was merely an empty form. The miniature Dao Net and the Immortal Domain fragment were external objects. The connection between them and Li Fan's true body was too weak. Therefore...

Li Fan's true body pointed forcefully at his own brow. The finger's energy seemed to penetrate his entire body. A portion of his divine soul, along with flesh and bone, was directly blasted out, forming a thin but blood-red afterimage outside Li Fan's true body. Enduring the dizziness, Li Fan directed a portion of his body to fly into the body forged from the Dao Net projection and Immortal Domain fragment. Relying on his familiarity with these two elements, Li Fan controlled it with some difficulty, almost forcibly stuffing the blood-red afterimage into it.

This forging process was not just simple clone creation. It also drew inspiration from the process of Crafty Work crafting the Saint Punishment puppet and Tian Yang achieving Xian Kui. Rather than a clone, it was a perfect fusion of a clone and the embodiment of Dao. Furthermore, because the materials used for this forging were too powerful, Li Fan was also concerned about the clone going out of control, recreating the scene of the former Sage Emperor Li Ping. From the outset of the forging, Li Fan had set the tone for this powerful clone. It would have no self-emotion. It would strictly follow Li Fan's commands. If it encountered any obstruction, it would kill them all. If the opponent was too strong, it would temporarily avoid confrontation and follow secretly, seeking a solution... In short, the clone puppet was set as an emotionless task-executing machine. Its only mission was to thoroughly investigate the secrets within the high wall. It even had a command to self-destruct upon mission completion.

The Dao Net projection was a reflection of the Great Dao of heaven and earth, while the True Immortal inscription characters were concrete depictions of the Great Dao. The two had a strong correlation. The blood-red afterimage Li Fan split from his own body was filled with his understanding of the Great Dao. Using this as a bonding point, the three were slowly smelted into one.

"The clone's mind projects the Dao Net, and its body is formed by the Great Dao. Upon birth, it has already reached the minor accomplishment stage of Mind Manifestation of Divinity and Nascent Soul of the Physical Body." "In terms of combat power alone, it is likely far superior to me..." As the powerful puppet gradually took shape, another self, equally powerful, was slowly pulling Li Fan towards that direction, as if a reflection in the water was reaching out to pull him into the water. Like a toddler wielding a heavy sword.

If it were before Li Fan infiltrated the Shining Star Sea and came into contact with the Dao Net, this clone, once it appeared, might have exceeded Li Fan's control and usurped him. But now... Li Fan's expression was calm as he issued Dao Net commands one after another. The Dao Net projection within the clone puppet simultaneously emitted flashing lights, as if responding to Li Fan's actions. The puppet was thus slowly subdued, its imposing aura contained, and it stood still.

Li Fan's action, though seemingly casual, was built upon the accumulation of the Shining Star Sea's research on the Dao Net over countless years. However, Li Fan had adapted it for his own use, applying it to the Dao Net projection within his mind. Compared to the vast Dao Net covering the entire Shining Star Sea, the one within Li Fan's divine sense was admittedly weak. But it already possessed the fundamental properties of a "Dao Net." Coupled with the support of a powerful physical body, this clone puppet would have no difficulty matching True Immortals.

"Even better, the clone puppet has no immortal spiritual energy within it; it is a creation of Great Dao laws. If intentionally concealed, hiding within heaven and earth, it would be like ice melting into water, leaving no trace. Like ordinary objects hitting the high wall, it would not be specially treated and directly released." Manipulating the miniature Dao Net with one's own power is by no means easy. Even with Li Fan's current divine sense strength, he had to divide eight or nine-tenths of his attention to control the clone puppet.

"Actually, it wouldn't be a problem to release it temporarily. As long as it can be brought back under the Dao Net's control in time, he will still act according to the mission objectives I set. But he cannot be in a state of freedom for too long..." "Otherwise, stray thoughts will inevitably arise!" Li Fan understood. Dao Net commands were woven into threads, firmly tetherring the clone puppet. Like a giant beast puppet controlled by Li Fan's threads.

"Heaven and Earth are indifferent, treating all beings as straw dogs." "You don't need to consider all beings in this world; just follow my commands." "Let's call you..." "Li Biren!"

With the final command issued, all the threads merged into the Dao Net projection within the clone's mind, becoming invisible by ordinary means. Li Fan felt a peculiar connection form between Li Biren and himself. Compared to a pure flesh-and-blood clone, it was more distant. But compared to a puppet controlled by mere thought, it was much closer.

Li Biren's expression was like ten thousand years of ice, devoid of any emotional fluctuation. His eyes completely inherited Li Fan's most genuine thoughts—his profound indifference to all beings in the world. Even Li Fan himself felt a slight tremor when he looked into them. Li Biren's body radiated no aura, as if he were part of this world itself. Though bearing the weight of the Great Dao, he was as light as a drifting feather. Without seeing him with his own eyes, even if he were right in front of you, you wouldn't notice him. But once you looked at him, you would never forget him, and a primal fear would arise in your heart, becoming an indelible shadow.

Li Fan did not wish to linger with this purely destructive creation. "Go." He said calmly. Li Biren's figure transformed into a sword, disappearing from the Xuanhuang Realm in an instant. Three breaths passed. He had traversed the entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea and arrived at the foot of the high wall. The Great Dao took form, swimming within the Great Dao. Like a fish in water, it was tens of times faster than Li Fan's sword escape technique. And Li Biren, facing the formless high wall ahead, showed no hesitation. He charged straight towards it. From the moment he set off to the moment he collided with the high wall, Li Biren's entire being remained like a statue, without the slightest change. As if this life-or-death matter had nothing to do with him.

"He didn't appear outside the wall..." "It seems the theory of 'inside the wall' is true!" Li Fan, remaining in the Xuanhuang Realm, combined the search with his dream power outside the wall, and preliminarily obtained the answer he desired. After a while, the image from Li Biren's perspective slowly appeared.

"Fortunately, this high wall cannot completely block the connection between Great Daos." Li Fan did his best to sense the encounters of his clone puppet. Due to Li Fan suppressing Li Biren's self-awareness to the lowest possible level, even though he experienced traversing the high wall, Li Biren himself had no psychological reaction. He merely acted as Li Fan's "camera," observing the scene inside the wall for him.

A magical world that lacked a "sky." What appeared above was a reflection of the ground below. But Li Biren stood on the ground, and the mirror of the sky did not reflect him. This was not due to Li Biren's stealth characteristics. It was because... Li Biren did not belong to this world in the first place! Sensing the invasion of an outsider, this world suddenly changed drastically. The sky and the ground trembled slightly and then moved violently, approaching each other. As they converged and closed in, they aimed to crush this intruder who had suddenly appeared.

Li Biren simply thrust his right hand upwards. His arm instantly expanded into a sky-pillar, forcefully propping up the converging sky and earth. The mirror-like sky continued to press down, unable to advance an inch, emitting creaking sounds. Where the sky and the pillar met, layers shattered due to the immense pressure. However, behind the shattered mirror surface, there was not space to escape to the outside. Instead, there was another layer of mirror!

Li Biren supported the sky with his right arm, while his body detached from his arm and quickly roamed this space, searching for an exit. But this place seemed boundless. Even with Li Biren's terrifying flight speed, he flew for nearly half a day without finding an edge. It was as if the boundaries of this world continuously expanded outwards as he moved. However, while flying, Li Biren recorded the detailed scenes of this world in his mind, finding no repetition.

Li Biren returned to where his sky-supporting right arm was, then grabbed the sky-pillar with his left hand. With a slight exertion, it was as if he grabbed a giant club and yanked it forcefully. The sky-pillar tilted, instantly tearing open a rift in the sky. Li Biren, holding the sky-pillar with his left hand, swung it non-stop. With a whistling sound, the mirror-like sky was shattered into pieces in an instant. He even took a deep breath and swallowed the shattered mirror fragments that were constantly falling from the sky.

The Dao Net projection in his mind flickered, having already analyzed the composition of this mirror-like sky. "Dao as a curtain, blinding the eyes of all beings." "The exit is ahead." Li Biren simply stated the conclusion, without any superfluous thought. Like a giant in a creation myth parting the heavens and earth, Li Biren held the giant pillar and rapidly expanded his figure. In just a moment, he surpassed the shattered mirror-like sky above. Then, regardless of the consequences, he continued to grow upwards towards the sky beyond the sky, smashing through layers of mirror-like surfaces with his head acting as a hammer.

*Boom! Boom! Boom!* When the final layer of deceptive curtain was broken, Li Biren burst out. His figure had returned to its normal size, and he cautiously surveyed his surroundings. "No signs of life." "No fluctuations of Great Dao energy." "Temporarily safe."

Looking back at where he came from, it was just a glass-like transparent sculpture. Due to being pierced and shattered, its original appearance could not be discerned. And around it, there were a total of sixteen other sculptures. "There should be eighteen in total." "One has disappeared." "Among the remaining sixteen, five are shattered, and the rest are intact." Li Biren calmly analyzed as always.

He flashed to the nearest intact transparent sculpture. "Beyond a certain distance, it cannot be seen clearly. Only by approaching the statue can one see its appearance clearly. And the world within the statue." "It's not due to restrictions from formations..." "But it's one of the Dao principles here." Li Biren observed coldly, his eyes seemingly manifesting the miniature Dao Net. He reached out his hand into the void, gently stroking it. In the Dao Net, a new light appeared. It was a Great Dao principle that was not originally in the miniature Dao Net. Li Biren sensed it, captured it, and integrated it into his own Dao Net projection.

After a moment, the light in Li Biren's eyes dimmed. In his vision, the eleven transparent sculptures that were previously unclear had all revealed their true forms. They were, inexplicably, people with different appearances. Or rather, Immortals! "Each sculpture contains a Great Dao of heaven and earth." "It should be the Dao cultivated by the Immortal within the sculpture."

Li Biren approached the sculpture before him and felt the aura of the Dao principle related to [Guard] from it. However, this Dao principle was already recorded in the Dao Net projection, so Li Biren ignored it. He simply pressed his eyes close, peering into the scene within the transparent sculpture. If Li Fan's true body were here, seeing this scene, he would undoubtedly be shocked and his heart would race. But Li Biren didn't even frown. Gazing into the wide-open eyes he saw, he met them head-on: "A corpse." "A True Immortal's corpse."

Li Biren retracted his gaze and moved to the other transparent sculptures. He also observed them closely. Within each sculpture, a True Immortal's corpse was visible. "The Dao they cultivated are all different." "Not the same True Immortal." "I did not see a True Immortal's corpse where I came from..."

Standing before the last transparent sculpture, Li Biren hesitated no longer. He punched the face of the sculpture. The sculpture remained motionless. Not even a tremor occurred. Li Biren's punch, capable of shattering the Xuanhuang Realm, vanished like a clay ox entering the sea, completely blocked. But Li Biren persisted. Punch after punch. Symbols formed on his body, like tattoos, appeared to be contorted True Immortal inscription characters.

"It seems unharmed." "But with every strike, a small part of the sculpture's Dao principle aura is drawn to my body." "One side decreases, the other increases." "It's effective." Li Biren continued to punch relentlessly. The originally transparent sculpture became even more "pale." From a glassy state, it transformed into liquid. Finally, under Li Biren's steady bombardment, it shattered and dispersed. However, strangely, the True Immortal's corpse that Li Biren had seen earlier did not fall out as the sculpture broke apart. Only fragments scattered across the ground. Just like the scene Li Biren created when he broke free earlier.

"The True Immortal corpse I saw was not a true True Immortal corpse." "But the condensation of the True Immortal's comprehension of the Dao principle during his lifetime." "Although the True Immortal perished, these comprehensions were preserved by someone, in some way." Li Biren put a fragment into his mouth. After carefully chewing it, he gave his judgment. "It is beneficial to me." He then opened his mouth wide and swallowed all the scattered fragments of Dao principle comprehension in this place.

Chapter 1461: Standing Still on the Infinite Sea

Li Biren's Dao Net projection in his mind seemed to become clearer. The hasty consumption of knowledge in such a short period did not cause indigestion. The insights from the fallen True Immortals, combined with Li Biren's unique physique's strong resilience, allowed him to accept the True Immortal insights from this place almost entirely without damage.

"This space only contains these transparent statues. Moreover, the boundary of the space does not have the concept of 'before.' There is no path forward, just like the high walls of the star sea."

Li Biren replicated the process, shattering all the remaining transparent statues in this place and devouring them. Then, he intended to break free from the confinement of this space.

Before traversing and leaving, Li Biren sensed that the eighteen statues here had not truly disappeared. Even though they appeared to have been entirely consumed by him, the source of the True Immortal insights that generated the statues still existed.

"With time, they should be able to recover their original state."

"However, it will take at least tens of thousands of years."

Darkness replaced light, and when Li Biren could see again, he was already in a square space. Looking around, he saw similar small block spaces in all directions—front, back, left, right, up, and down. They seemed within reach yet infinitely far away. Most of these block spaces were dead silent. The remaining ones flickered irregularly, appearing strange, while only a minority of the block spaces stably emitted a faint light.

Looking at everything before him, Li Biren fell into contemplation.

"The block spaces bear some resemblance to the cages used to imprison True Immortals in the depths of the Star Sea Dao Net."

"The reason it looked completely dark when viewed from the outside..."

Li Biren then looked at the areas where light flickered for comparison. After a moment, he nodded slightly.

"The life force has completely vanished, a dead zone. There is no need to observe further."

"As for those flickering areas..." He extended his hand to touch and feel them. After a long while, even though his self-awareness was suppressed to an extreme degree, Li Biren still frowned slightly.

"The original observation system has been destroyed, presenting an erroneous state. And the culprit causing the observation failure..."

"The Tribulation of Dao Annihilation!"

Li Biren withdrew his hand. Even though he had only touched the edge of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation from a distance, his finger appeared unnaturally blackened, like strange charred remains. Where it was black, the Dao principles were annihilated, and Dao was no longer Dao.

Li Biren exerted a slight force, and the blackened fingertip turned into ashes, scattering upwards and disappearing into this space.

"Merely approaching the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, the immortal domain body uncontrollably turned into dust."

"..."

"However, the square boundary was able to temporarily firmly restrain the erosion of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation like a dam."

While contemplating, his severed finger regrew. Li Biren stared intently at the square space boundary, trying to decipher its mystery. But the results were minimal. He then turned his attention back to the dozen or so areas in this space that faintly glowed.

After some observation, Li Biren concluded:

"The star sea, with its life force not flourishing, has a situation largely similar to the Utmost Darkness Star Sea..."

"Even the True Immortal inscriptions left by He Gan Xian are rampant here."

Li Biren carefully examined all the light points.

"None of these are the Utmost Darkness Star Sea where the Xuanhuang Realm is located, but unfamiliar starscapes..."

Li Biren looked down at his own position. Or rather, at the small squares which were identical to the thousands of surrounding spaces.

"I broke through the high wall and shattered eighteen True Immortal statues, thus breaking through the curtain of Dao and reaching this place."

"However, what I see before me is not from the perspective of an 'observer,' but I am still within a cage."

"So, the star sea where the Xuanhuang Realm is located is just one of these myriad block cages..."

Looking at the countless blocks surrounding him that should have been shining with life force, Li Biren was momentarily lost in thought. But his self-awareness was weak, and he quickly recovered from his shock, beginning to ponder.

"If that's the case, the high wall doesn't just block one star sea."

"It's just that all these star seas exist in a parallel, juxtaposed manner, unable to see each other..."

Suddenly, Li Biren's mind flashed with the scene of Qian Ruochang finding another Ascension Platform in the ruins not far from the high wall.

"No wonder there are two Ascension Platform ruins despite being close to each other."

"It's because this starscape has been divided and superimposed, all contained within the high wall!"

"Indeed, these are methods beyond human imagination. Even I would need great effort to destroy all these starscapes. Let alone gathering them so precisely, like blocks."

Li Biren was not awed by the divine spectacle before him but analyzed it calmly.

"Such a grand display, using the starscape as a testing ground..."

"...What are they experimenting on?"

"How does one reach the true core area?"

"I am not the first person to cross the high wall. Before me, the Profound Immortal Boat, the Heavenly Sword Sect, and others have all successfully escaped the wall. How did they escape from this cage?"

"No trace of them was found."

"Or perhaps, they did not reach this space?"

Li Biren looked down at his immortal domain body.

"Perhaps it is precisely because of this special body that I have entered this area. Different methods of crossing lead to different outcomes..."

Even the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation could be temporarily resisted. Li Biren, in his current state, could not break through the square boundaries of this experimental field. He did not stubbornly continue but turned back towards his point of origin. In the narrow space where the eighteen statues were located. He began to search again meticulously.

"In the Xuanhuang Realm, when mortals are infected by the Immortal Miasma, cultivators would move mortals to small worlds or heavens and seal them with the Great Immortal Eradication Array. The trials within the array are not something mortals can overcome. Here, to ensure the sealing of the experimental subjects, it is necessary to do what is absolutely necessary, ensuring that only the leaders of this experiment, or the Immortals, can reach the true core location."

Although he still found nothing after searching, Li Biren gradually formed a guess.

"The difference between Immortals and mortals lies, first, in their power. Second, in their infinity."

"My immortal domain body, possessing power, meets the first requirement. This is why I could easily break through the curtain of Dao and see the truth of the experiment. But without the characteristic of infinity, I cannot enter the core area..."

"The Sea of Infinity."

After figuring out the key point, Li Biren did not waste time. He temporarily returned from within the high wall. Returning to the Xuanhuang Realm, he brought the Dao Key Stone Tablet left by King Xuan Yuan, replicated from the Immortal Ascension Platform. Then, he returned in an instant.

"A single stone tablet is not enough."

"Connecting to the Sea of Infinity requires meeting three conditions."

"The immortal spiritual energy unique to a True Immortal. The Ascension Platform, an access route from the Immortal Realm. And the secret inscriptions held by the guarding Immortal officials."

"The stone tablet was replicated from the Ascension Platform by King Xuan Yuan."

"Qian Ruochang of the Shining Star Sea, in order to lure the Formless Immortal, disguised himself as a guarding Immortal official. I have also mastered that True Immortal inscription."

"What is currently lacking is immortal spiritual energy. Unclaimed immortal spiritual energy."

...

Li Fan's thoughts churned. His true body in the Xuanhuang Realm had already made preparations.

"If Scholar Zhu hadn't been so generous before, this time there would have been more trouble."

Not far outside the high wall, near the slumbering Profound Coffin and the sleeping Immortal Hunters. Ma Tiande, also asleep, had his fingertip momentarily covered by a piece of skin that did not belong to him. It lasted only for a fleeting moment before quickly disappearing. However, a wisp of immortal spiritual energy, through the intangible Dao Net, traversed space and arrived at Li Fan.

At the same time, the two Immortals trapped in the Profound Coffin seemed to have sensed something. The long-silent coffin emitted faint, subtle fluctuations, but ultimately dissipated. The two Immortals did not speak again.

Within the high wall, in the space where the eighteen statues were originally located. The appearance of immortal spiritual energy seemed to have triggered something. The surrounding high wall-like boundaries rippled like water, and the hidden objects behind them were about to reveal their true forms. However, perhaps because it was only a wisp of immortal spiritual energy and not a True Immortal's true body, after a series of continuous ripples, it could not be completely lifted.

Li Fan knew that he still needed to act personally. Thus, he no longer hesitated, seizing the moment when the immortal spiritual energy still existed, and began to write on the Dao Key stone tablet. Like Qian Ruochang's possession before, even the movements and time required for each stroke were identical. Soon, with immortal spiritual energy as ink, the mysterious symbol shone on the Dao Key stone tablet.

Although there were no glorious phenomena or auspicious signs, a mysterious power suddenly erupted from the stone tablet. It was not entirely accurate to say that this power came from the stone tablet, as the tablet had merely opened a passage. A path leading to the Sea of Infinity.

Unexpectedly, his soul was drawn into a massive, surging vortex. Beside him, every droplet of water seemed to contain endless, brilliant starry skies. Countless scenes flashed before his eyes, as if experiencing trillions of years in an instant. Such a massive amount of information, though only a forced glimpse, was still a devastating disaster for the being immersed in it. Fortunately, the one accessing the Sea of Infinity this time was a clone puppet whose self-awareness had been completely suppressed. If Li Fan's true body had rashly entered, after being baptized by the droplets of the Sea of Infinity, even with the benefit of "Return to Truth," the immense trauma to his soul would be difficult to recover from in a short time.

Qiao Saidao was trapped in the "Era" device and had experienced millions of reincarnations. Yet, all that he experienced combined was not enough to form a droplet in the Sea of Infinity.

"My mind, attached to the Dao Net, can barely hold on, but not for long."

"Unlike the previous time, entering the Sea of Infinity with the True Immortal skin!"

"After all, it was only one stone tablet from the Ascension Platform, not the entire Ascension Platform. This kind of wave is something that newly ascended Immortals cannot withstand. It must be missing corresponding protective components..."

The scene of Qian Ruochang borrowing the Ascension Platform to seal Immortals flashed in Li Fan's mind. Due to being tainted by the light and shadow data of the Sea of Infinity, the miniature Dao Net that Li Fan's divine sense relied on was also struggling. It seemed to have encountered the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, and the edges of the Dao Net were being submerged by endless waves, ceasing to exist. The Dao Net began to collapse. The Sea of Infinity was about to engulf him.

But Li Fan did not retreat. He was created to explore the secrets within the high wall, and to explore the secrets of the high wall, he had to first connect to the Sea of Infinity and achieve the True Immortal body. To achieve this goal, he could disregard life and death.

"This scene of the Sea of Infinity swallowing the Dao Net..."

"It's actually so similar to the sudden arrival of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, swallowing everything!"

Li Fan's consciousness gradually blurred. At the critical moment of inspiration, the power of his Demonic Killing Immortal Soul, guided by the Dao Net's remaining faint light, finally arrived. The remaining light of the Dao Net, wrapped by the power of the Demonic Killing Immortal Soul, caused the monstrous waves of the Sea of Infinity to instantly subside. As if it had lost its target, the vortex calmed, turning into an endless ocean.

Once again, Li Fan saw the legendary Sea of Infinity. This time, it was not by borrowing the True Immortal's skin, but by personally traversing the vortex with his clone puppet, descending into it!

On the boundless Sea of Infinity, it seemed that no new True Immortals had visited for a long time. It was terrifyingly calm. But occasionally, whirlpools would appear inexplicably on the sea surface, stirring up some water. Li Fan, or rather, Li Fan, saw fleeting figures in these splashed water droplets. They were eons of history accumulated, far longer than the trillions of years he had experienced in the vortex. And this was just a negligible drop in the ocean.

Li Fan looked around. The Sea of Infinity was boundless. Who knew how many histories and beings were gathered here. Words could not describe its magnificence. Li Fan wandered within it, lost in thought. The individual, the True Immortal, the Nameless Immortal, and even the Transcendent beings spanning possibilities. In the face of this creation, their existence seemed to lose all meaning. Time seemed to stand still, and his thoughts seemed to be completely frozen.

After an unknown period, the fluctuation from "Return to Truth" within Li Fan's true body awakened him. It was a very strange emotion. It seemed like surprise. It seemed like nostalgia. There was also sadness. And resentment. A mixture of myriad emotions made it difficult for Li Fan to distinguish whether "Return to Truth" was happy, angry, sad, or fearful.

The calm of the Sea of Infinity was quietly broken. A terrifying deep-sea monster seemed to be stirring beneath the water. The entire sea surface was churned, boiling and stirring up waves. The terrifying power generated by the collision of water droplets even caused the Demonic Killing Immortal Soul's concealment to gradually fail. Like a flimsy life jacket in a storm, it was useless. The Dao Net attached to the divine sense was precarious, on the verge of complete dissipation.

In the next moment...

Li Biren was inexplicably detached from the Sea of Infinity. Everything he had witnessed seemed like an illusion. Only...

Li Biren stretched out his right hand. Although he did not summon immortal spiritual energy, Li Biren knew that as long as he wished, he could communicate with the Sea of Infinity at any time and summon endless power. But he did not dare.

Chapter 1462: Allegory of Mountains and Seas

For Li Biren, a creature of pure destruction, the emotion of "fear" was almost nonexistent. The reason he dared not use the infinite power was due to "instinct."

The moment he had the thought of using infinite immortal spiritual energy, the boundless Sea of Infinity appeared again in Li Biren's mind. The terrifying waves, each containing trillions of years of history, would pour down through the channel he created to connect to the Sea of Infinity, engulfing all things in the world, even the Great Dao of heaven and earth. Nothing in the mortal world could survive. This inexpressible pressure made Li Biren hesitate to press that invisible "button," even though it was within reach.

In addition to the pressure from the magnificent Sea of Infinity itself, what troubled Li Biren even more was the terrifying existence hidden beneath the Sea of Infinity, unseen. Merely their thoughts, triggered by sensing "Return to Truth," could stir up tempestuous waves in the Sea of Infinity.

Since returning to reality, Li Fan had been trying to communicate with "Return to Truth" to gather more information about the Sea of Infinity, but had received no response. Fortunately, Li Fan felt some reassurance that "Return to Truth's" power seemed unaffected in real-time, and he could still activate it at will. It was likely just in a bad mood and unwilling to respond.

However, the sights beheld during this brief journey to the Sea of Infinity forced Li Fan to consider many things. For example, the fact that the Sea of Infinity seemed to be closely related to the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. And that "Return to Truth" likely had a great connection with the Sea of Infinity and was an old acquaintance of the terrifying unknown beings hidden beneath the Sea of Infinity.

"Virtualize everything, return to the origin anchor point."

"Has the Sea of Infinity, which exists above all worlds, also been traced back..."

The extremely heavy, yet unavoidable truth suddenly appeared before Li Fan. Throughout his cultivation journey, as Li Fan's realm improved, his understanding of "Return to Truth's" abilities deepened. From struggling against True Immortals to being able to create separate timeline fragments called [Endless Reincarnations] out of thin air, he seemed to never see the limit of "Return to Truth's" abilities. But today, after using the methods left by the Immortal Realm to ascend and connect to the Sea of Infinity, Li Fan finally caught a glimpse of the limit of "Return to Truth."

"The terrifying beings hidden beneath the Sea of Infinity seem to be old acquaintances of 'Return to Truth.' If they are of the same level, then 'Return to Truth's' tracing power might not be effective against them."

"But to confirm this, I would need to enter the Sea of Infinity again in the next life. However..."

A shadow flashed in Li Fan's eyes. This was the first time since his reincarnation cultivation that he had to face an enemy like himself, capable of escaping the cycle of reincarnation. Especially the experience of nearly "drowning" in the Sea of Infinity, which suddenly put immense pressure on Li Fan.

Furthermore, "Return to Truth's" performance on the Sea of Infinity, those powers that transcended everything in the mortal world, made Li Fan think of the legend of the Creator God that he had heard from Liu Ruchen.

"A powerful Creator God defeated his peers and extracted their power to evolve all beings in the world..."

Liu Ruchen claimed to have read this legend in an ancient book. Li Fan had previously searched Liu Ruchen's memories and indeed found this ancient book. However, when the Medicine King Sect hastily fled the Xuanhuang Realm back then, it wasn't an important item, so it wasn't taken and was lost.

"This legend of the Creator God is not circulated or recorded elsewhere in the Xuanhuang Realm."

"There is reason to suspect that the so-called ancient book might be Sun Piaomiao's personal notes..."

"Liu Ruchen casually flipped through this book, and besides the legend of the Creator God, he only read another allegorical story of a dialogue between a mountain and a sea."

Li Fan recalled what Liu Ruchen had seen back then. In the beginning of ancient times, there were only mountains and seas in the world. They surrounded each other, relying on each other. Initially, the relationship between the mountain and the sea was harmonious, until one day, life suddenly emerged in the sea. This existence was different from mountains and seas, adding much vitality to the sea, and naturally attracted the sea's attention.

At first, the mountain paid no mind. The lifespan of beings in the sea was limited, while mountains and seas existed forever, imperishable. Compared to the nearly endless years of mountains and seas, the creatures in the sea were destined to be fleeting visitors.

But as time passed, the mountain was surprised to find that the number of creatures in the sea not only did not decrease but became even more prosperous. After investigating, the mountain was shocked to discover that it was because the sea could not bear to see the creatures die one after another, so it shared its endless lifespan with them.

The mountain was greatly angered: "Sea! Why did you do this! Why should these little ones be qualified to enjoy the same infinite lifespan as us?"

The sea gently retorted: "Mountain, why not? You and I can exist in this world forever. Even if we share our lifespan with them, it will not make us weaker. Isn't it better for the space between mountains and seas to be more lively?"

The mountain was speechless. It observed the creatures evolving in the sea and then sighed: "Sea, it's not that I am stingy. It's just that once these little ones grasp what doesn't originally belong to them, they will instinctively crave more."

The sea retorted again: "What is 'originally belonging'? Is our infinite lifespan inherent?"

The mountain ultimately fell silent.

...

"It seems to be just a simple allegorical story. But if combined with the chapter about the Creator God, and what I saw in the Sea of Infinity, there might be another meaning. Sun Piaomiao..."

Li Fan pondered for a moment and decided to find that lost ancient book. However, when the Medicine King Sect fled collectively back then, it was considered an act of betrayal by the Ten Sects. The sect was quickly ransacked and looted. In the chaos of that time, no one knew where that ancient book ended up. It might have been burned to ashes.

Li Fan first summoned the stone tablet. Although the stone tablet claimed to be able to record all events that occurred in the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan knew it was limited to the original Xuanhuang Realm. Moreover, transcendent powers like the Fishing Pond could not be recorded by the stone tablet. So, he didn't have high hopes. As expected, it did not find the ancient book from Liu Ruchen's memory.

However, with Li Fan's current control over the Xuanhuang Realm, as long as this book still existed within the Xuanhuang Realm, it could definitely be found. Li Fan did not need to do it himself. With just a single command, the cultivators of the Myriad Immortal Alliance and the Five Elders Association, awakened from their dreams, began searching through their own collections.

Li Fan's attention temporarily returned to his clone puppet, Li Biren. Although he did not summon immortal spiritual energy, Li Biren, after returning from the Sea of Infinity, had already acquired the attribute of "infinity." Coupled with the wisp of immortal spiritual energy transmitted by the immortal skin, it seemed to have passed some kind of verification.

The originally limited space, like a high wall, instantly manifested physically and folded backward. This was a rather strange yet difficult-to-explain visual change. Li Biren felt that this small space was rapidly expanding in all directions. Moreover, due to the increase in the volume of space, a staircase extending diagonally upwards gradually appeared in positions that did not exist before. The expansion of space seemed endless, and the staircase that appeared before Li Biren also seemed to extend upwards indefinitely. There was no end in sight.

Li Biren did not rashly step onto the staircase, but first observed his surroundings. This space was not infinitely extending like the staircase, but after expanding to a certain limit, it gradually showed a peculiar curvature. Although it was still expanding, the rate of increase in space volume had significantly decreased. The space gradually became full, but apart from the faint silver light emanating from the staircase before him, there was nothing else.

To explore the true secrets of the high wall, Li Biren finally stepped onto the staircase. In the next second, Li Biren actually felt as if he had returned to the Sea of Infinity. Lines were moving rapidly forward all around him. The lines were sometimes solitary, sometimes clustered together. Some were simple gray and white, while others were colorful.

Li Biren tried to interact with these lines and discovered that they were like the water of the Sea of Infinity, storing and recording vast amounts of historical and living being information. However, the amount of data was not on the same level as the real Sea of Infinity, and Li Biren could withstand it without pressure. Moreover, the information within the lines was encrypted, and Li Biren could only glimpse vague shadows.

Traveling rapidly through the torrent of lines, Li Biren soon emerged from it. He arrived at the entrance of a dark passage with a faint aura of death. The door sealing the passage had inexplicably been blasted open, with four shattered puppet corpses lying nearby. The puppet parts were scattered all over the ground. Li Biren looked back at where he came from, realizing that this location was the end of the passage.

"No boundary ahead."

"If I want to leave, I need to go through the process of traversing lines again."

Li Biren looked at the fallen puppets nearby. Although they had been broken for who knows how many years, Li Biren could still feel a faint threat from them. He reached out and picked up a piece of debris from the ground. With all his might, he tried to crush it but could only cause further damage.

"The materials used to forge the puppets are not ordinary."

Without choosing to get entangled with these gate-guarding puppets, Li Biren moved his figure and entered the passage.

"Hmm?"

As he flew, Li Biren keenly sensed the difference between this place and the outer star sea. In the mortal star sea, he would merge with the Dao Net and travel along the Dao, crossing the Utmost Darkness Star Sea in just three breaths. But this place seemed to be a dead zone where the Great Dao was not manifest. His connection with the Dao Net felt obstructed by an invisible barrier, becoming much more difficult. The Dao Net projection in his divine sense instantly dimmed. Only certain specific Daos were unaffected, as if the complete Dao Net had been burned away, leaving only a few remnants.

Li Biren's flight speed was greatly reduced, and even his combat power was significantly diminished. But he was not in a hurry. Instead, he became interested in studying this dark passage. For him, simply seeing this place made the trip worthwhile.

"The path before the Myriad Immortal Alliance's Dharma Protector Hall is paved with Spirit Transformation Stones. Within the path, spiritual energy is forbidden, and cultivators can only walk on foot."

"This passage has a similar effect. However, it does not restrict ordinary cultivators, but rather True Immortals who have comprehended the Dao!"

"Moreover, it's not just this passage, but all the buildings here."

Li Biren noted as he walked through the artificially created passage. It had no physical boundaries but only conceptual restrictions like high walls, forcing those who entered to proceed in a specific direction.

"Originally, the walls of this passage should have displayed scenes, but they seem to be damaged and are not rendering."

The passage was not long. By the time he reached the exit, Li Biren suddenly looked back, a feeling arising in his heart. There were no more complications after this. Emerging from the darkness, the only circular light at the exit, Li Biren's eyes landed on a messy, cylindrical hall. The cylindrical hall was towering, its top unseen. It seemed to have been plundered, appearing somewhat empty.

Li Biren followed the faint death aura he had sensed earlier and found a cleared area on the ground.

"This is..."

He rubbed his finger on the ground and brought it before his eyes, revealing a distorted, illusory face. Screaming and roaring, "Save me!" It was only a residual trace, re-ignited by Li Biren's immortal power. He could not communicate with it and could only mechanically repeat words like "Save me," "Escape quickly."

Li Biren shook his head slightly. As he withdrew his immortal power, the distorted face dissipated on its own. After a thorough inspection, there were thirty-seven traces of residual thoughts in the cylindrical hall, and these were only the ones with traces left. As for those that had been completely wiped clean, it was impossible to speculate.

"Judging by the intensity of these residual thoughts, they should all be from fallen True Immortals."

"The reason they are far inferior to the desire for survival in the Utmost Darkness Sea is twofold: first, the difference in strength during their lifetimes; second, the thorough cleansing of this place."

"True Immortals were slaughtered like ants. What happened here?"

Apart from the thirty-seven traces, Li Biren found nothing else in the cylindrical space. And apart from the passage Li Biren came from, there seemed to be no other connections in this cylindrical hall. The investigation had stalled.

After pondering for a moment, Li Biren suddenly looked at the few brightly shining Great Daos in his divine sense miniature Dao Net. A plan began to form in his mind. Li Biren's immortal domain fragment body folded back on itself, transforming into a chess piece, hidden among the other suppressed Dao paths. Only the brightly shining parts remained, harmonizing with the Dao principles of this place. The originally infinitely tall cylindrical hall suddenly contracted to nine feet nine inches. One by one, items appeared, filling the empty hall. And on the cylindrical walls of the hall, Li Biren indeed saw countless block spaces displayed, showing scenes.

Chapter 1463: The Great Void Delineated

These block spaces were precisely the scenes of countless divided star seas juxtaposed that he had seen after breaking through the Utmost Darkness Star Sea. They were still in three states: dark, faintly lit, and flickering.

However, the overview on the circular wall displayed a far greater number of blocks than Li Biren had seen. Li Biren tried to locate the Xuanhuang Realm. After locking onto the light spot representing the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, he also identified the countless block spaces displayed alongside the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

And at the edge of all these block star seas, a coarse white line separated this circle of block spaces from other regions. This white line seemed to be some kind of dividing line. Although visually, the Utmost Darkness Star Sea region and other regions on the circular wall were parallel and unremarkable, it was precisely because of the existence of this white circle that the block star seas within the delineated area were invisibly elevated. Like stars surrounding a constellation, they were clustered in the most conspicuous position.

"This kind of specialness..." Li Biren stared intently at the dazzling white circle.

"Great Void." A word naturally appeared in Li Biren's mind. In the ancient cultivation era, the tangible boundary of the explorable star fields. A void without end, a place of pure nothingness.

From afar, observing the Great Void, Li Biren vaguely sensed its essence. But he could not be sure.

"Although it is a place of complete nothingness, it is fundamentally different from being affected by the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. It appears empty because most Dao principles have disappeared there, leaving only a few Great Dao laws like pillars. Just like this experimental field..."

"Within the scope of these Dao principles, one can see the things hidden and concealed in the experimental field, and avoid being forcibly drained of one's attributes in the Great Void."

Ancient True Immortals sought to advance further by merging with a certain Great Dao in heaven and earth, achieving the Nameless realm. Only by comprehending a certain Dao to an extreme degree could they take this step. Therefore, the cultivation of True Immortals was mostly a deepening of comprehension of a certain Dao. Although the Three Thousand Great Daos is a figurative expression, due to the differences between each Dao, True Immortals were naturally endowed with many different "attributes." For example, the Hungry Immortal, the Xi and Yi Immortal, He Gan Xian, and so on.

This place, and the Great Void, with its pseudo-Tribulation of Dao Annihilation forbidden techniques, could filter True Immortals from the vast sea of True Immortals to select "allies" and grant permission to enter and exit this experimental star field. Identity and background could be fabricated with lies, but stance could not. In other words, if a True Immortal truly sought to infiltrate this place and changed their cultivated Dao path, they would directly become a member of the "faction," and this place would welcome their arrival. Thus, there would be no "infiltration."

"This forbidden technique is a massive screening machine."

"And it does more than just simple screening; once the allegiance is changed, it's likely impossible to turn back."

And the reason Li Biren could enter this place after so many years was due to the heaven-defying method of 'Mind Manifestation of Divinity and Dao Net Projection.' If the various Great Daos in heaven and earth naturally divided True Immortals into different factions, then the Dao Net Projection was 'I want them all,' joining all existing and known True Immortal factions impartially.

This was absolutely impossible in ancient times. Let alone the Three Thousand Great Daos, even cultivating two different Daos simultaneously was extremely difficult. And even if one cultivated multiple Daos, it was ultimately inferior to mastering one Dao to the extreme and achieving the Nameless realm.

"Just as I analyzed before."

"The reason my Dao Net Projection could exist safely is first, the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation occurred, and the Immortal Realm was destroyed. The Nameless True Immortals who merged with the Dao and the Dao, either died or fled, unable to notice this miniature mirror reflecting the Great Dao."

"Moreover, there is the Star Sea Dao Net of Shining Star Sea to cover my sight."

With the destruction of the Immortal Realm and the suspected abandonment of this experimental site, coupled with Li Fan's repeated reincarnations and various factors, Li Fan was able to luckily enter this place. It can be said that without any one of these conditions, he would not have been able to enter.

"Records of the Great Void have existed since ancient times."

"But since the great tribulation descended and the high walls rose, all traces have vanished."

"From what I see now, after the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation broke out and emergency protective measures were activated, the entire experimental block star seas underwent an overall change."

Li Fan stared at the coarse white circle representing the Great Void. It suddenly appeared among the countless small blocks on the circular wall, as if someone had drawn a circle in the vast sea of stars! Highlighting the target to be searched for!

"Although this experimental site has been abandoned for unknown reasons, all its facilities are still in operation, leading to this delineation of the Great Void?"

Li Fan analyzed based on the clues observed. Although he could enter this place due to the special nature of his Dao Net Projection, he only had the authority to "observe," not to "manipulate." Whether it was the divided block star seas on the circular wall or the various objects that appeared in the cylindrical hall, he could not move them at all.

He could not yet determine the exact reason for the delineation of the Great Void, but the fact that the Utmost Darkness Star Sea of the Xuanhuang Realm was among them was enough to make Li Fan wary.

Li Fan tried to reconstruct the secrets hidden behind this experimental space based on the clues he had.

"The Tribulation of Dao Annihilation is suspected to originate from the same source as the Sea of Infinity."

"After I, using an incomplete Ascension Platform, connected to the Sea of Infinity, I discovered that by drawing upon the infinite power within the Sea of Infinity, countless droplets in the Sea of Infinity would pour down through unseen channels, engulfing all things in the world. This premonition was so real that the instinctive fear it brought made even the clone puppet, with its extremely suppressed self-awareness, hesitant to press that button."

"But there are countless True Immortals, not to mention immortal artifacts, immortal servants, and immortal puppets. They use infinite immortal spiritual energy without such concerns. The immortal spiritual energy derived from the Dissolution Disc undoubtedly proves this point."

Li Fan thought so. A sacred power diffused from the Dissolution Disc, enveloping his fingertips in white light. While sensing its infinite nature, he seemed to see the boundless Sea of Infinity again.

"There cannot be a second Sea of Infinity in the mortal world."

"The Immortal Realm initially did not fear the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation much, similar to mortals viewing floods, with True Immortals responsible for guarding against them."

"It is reasonable to assume that the ancient Immortal Realm was fully aware of the consequences of summoning the power of the Sea of Infinity, which would lead to the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. However, the temptation of infinity made True Immortals unwilling to give up using the Sea of Infinity."

"Even, they built things like [Dams] and [Reservoirs] on the Sea of Infinity. All True Immortals did not directly connect to the Sea of Infinity but transferred through the dams and reservoirs built by the Immortal Realm, thus avoiding the terrifying disaster of the Sea of Infinity pouring down and the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation descending upon the world."

"But..."

"The Sea of Infinity is a place of unimaginable grandeur and sanctity. Even Nameless True Immortals cannot compare to a single wave churning in the Sea of Infinity."

"Even though the civilization of the ancient Immortal Realm had developed to the point where they could restrict the Sea of Infinity to some extent, but..."

Li Fan thought again of the terrifying, obscure fluctuations emanating from the depths of the sea when "Return to Truth" stood on the Sea of Infinity.

"Those who play with fire will burn themselves."

"There are no eternally impenetrable dams in the world, and once a crack appears, it is difficult to mend. Moreover, there are countless True Immortals, either accidentally or intentionally, who seek to bypass the restrictions set by the Immortal Realm and connect directly to the Sea of Infinity, just like me."

"Every time this happens, it is equivalent to tearing open another crack between reality and the Sea of Infinity."

"Over time, the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation becoming more intense is a foregone conclusion."

Li Fan's thoughts churned, constantly extrapolating.

"Signs of the tribulation appeared, and one by one, star domains in the Immortal Realm were annihilated."

"'Return to Truth.' This treasure that can reverse fate was also suspected to originate from the Sea of Infinity. Although the Immortal Realm might not have known its specific function, they vaguely guessed that it might be able to completely resolve this world-ending crisis. Thus, they secretly searched everywhere, even extending their search to the lower star seas."

"They deduced the estimated time of 'Return to Truth's' appearance. And 'Return to Truth' was supposed to appear at that time..."

"Appearing in the Xuanhuang Realm, it was discovered by the powers of the Immortal Realm. If it had been controlled by the masters of the Immortal Realm, the Nameless True Immortals, from the beginning, perhaps 'Return to Truth' could have turned the tide and nipped the world-ending Tribulation of Dao Annihilation in the bud."

"However, for some unknown reason, 'Return to Truth' appeared late."

"The Immortal Realm did not wait for this world-saving treasure."

"Although the overall situation remained stable, the emergence of alternative ideas was inevitable."

"Just like what I glimpsed in the memory of that True Immortal. Great figures have their own thoughts, and ants have their own ways of survival."

"True Immortals resorted to their own methods, each seeking their own path to survival."

"Some transformed mortals into immortals, some used nameless bones and immortal heavenly pillars to forge world-saving vessels, Immortal Realm fragments..."

"But no one expected that the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation would erupt early. And its ferocity was far beyond anything before. It was as if all the connection channels between the Sea of Infinity and the mortal world had exploded, and a monstrous disaster suddenly descended."

"Caught off guard, True Immortals, Nameless True Immortals, and even the current rulers of the Immortal Realm, all died like ants..."

Li Fan seemed to see the terrifying scene of the Sea of Infinity pouring down and destroying the Immortal Realm.

"Although many Nameless True Immortals were willing or forced to become pillars to resist the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, how long could they hold on?"

"The Sea of Infinity swallowing the real world is the general trend. Unless they can rebuild the [Dams] of the former Immortal Realm in these brief moments of safety, otherwise..."

Li Fan couldn't help but look at the doomsday countdown on the "Return to Truth" panel.

"The Sea of Infinity seems to span all possibilities."

"The Tribulation of Dao Annihilation is definitely not unique to my [Prime] possibility."

"Or perhaps, after the great tribulation occurred, the Nameless True Immortals of the [Prime] possibility fled at the first sign of danger and went to other possibilities."

"Although they leaped across possibilities, as long as they did not abandon their immortal spiritual energy, their connection with the Sea of Infinity would always exist. Moreover, reaching the realm of merging with the Dao as a Nameless True Immortal is not something that can be abandoned at will."

"The Tribulation of Dao Annihilation follows like a shadow, engulfing the world..."

Even with Li Fan's current deduction ability, comparable to the Dao Transformation Stone Mother, he felt a splitting headache. Dealing with a single possibility was manageable. Converging numerous clues, he could deduce countless possible answers and verify them, selecting the one closest to the truth. But once other possibilities were involved, the difficulty of deduction suddenly increased exponentially. First, Li Fan knew nothing about the state of other possibilities, having too little information. Second, for every additional possibility, the number of variables involved in deduction doubled. Theoretically, with infinite possibilities, even thousands of Dao Transformation Stone Mothers working together would be insufficient.

"However, with the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation raging to this day, the remaining possibilities in the mortal world are likely far from infinite. With a remaining lifespan of over seven million years..."

"Perhaps 'lingering on borrowed time' is a more appropriate description."

Li Fan's thoughts raced to the extreme. Suddenly, his vision went black, and he was forced to stop deducing. His attention temporarily shifted from the Immortal Realm and the truth of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, returning to that strange experimental site.

"The original purpose of this place was supposed to be to 'guard' for [Return to Truth]."

"However, because 'Return to Truth' ultimately did not appear as expected, this place was officially abandoned by the Immortal Realm."

"But only on the surface."

"Some minor figures from the Immortal Realm did not completely give up and leave. However, their goal was likely not 'Return to Truth'."

"But merely to find a glimmer of possibility for survival in the face of the imminent Tribulation of Dao Annihilation."

"The technique of delineating the [Great Void] definitely involved the assistance of Nameless True Immortals..."

"But why did these people all disappear suddenly?"

"Judging from the remaining traces, there were definitely quite a few True Immortals gathered here."

Li Biren once again investigated the experimental site, trying to uncover more secrets. His gaze swept around and suddenly focused on an item that had inexplicably appeared in the cylindrical hall. It was a strangely shaped human俑 statue. Like a hidden hermit in the court, it stood quietly there, yet almost escaped Li Biren's attention. If not for its unique style, so similar to something Li Fan had encountered before, Li Biren might have truly overlooked it.

Chapter 1464: Compassionate World Reincarnation Sect

This kind of concealment technique, which could only be discovered if one knew the item possessed a unique property, was characteristic of Sun Piaomiao's遗物. The statue before Li Biren, similar in style to the few遺物 Sun Piaomiao left on the Profound Immortal Boat, reminded him.

"Sun Piaomiao's遗物 almost all had unique functions. The humanoid puppet could increase 'Return to Truth's' charge by double. The Three-pronged Tree granted 'Return to Truth' an extra simulation opportunity. And the bronze immortal crane, after being destroyed, would transmit a secret message to the ear."

"Tianluo Era, Year 213. Beginning with Shangzhang Dayuanxian and Zuo E'er Fenghuang, ending with Yong Chi Fenruo and Yan Mao Xuan Yi..."

Li Biren thought this way and slowly approached the humanoid statue. The items that inexplicably appeared in the hall seemed related to the experiments in this experimental site. Although they had viewing permission, their main bodies were not in the same time and space as Li Biren, making them only observable from afar and uncontactable by any means. Only this humanoid statue, due to the connection Li Fan had with other of Sun Piaomiao's遗物, could Li Biren vaguely touch it.

His finger seemed to probe into a layer of icy mist, rather than feeling the statue's physical form. Even with this vague sensation, Li Biren felt the same profound and mysterious feeling as when he encountered Sun Piaomiao's遗物: "If the main body were here, perhaps it could absorb it directly using 'Return to Truth,' ignoring the restrictions here. However, this place is rumored to have been built specifically to capture 'Return to Truth.' Before fully understanding this place's secrets, the main body would never venture into such a dangerous place."

He had to find another way. Although an initial connection had been established with the humanoid statue, further operations were impossible. All forms of energy, and even divine sense, could not affect this statue that existed between reality and illusion.

After trying in vain, Li Biren recalled Sun Piaomiao's various actions. Then, the secret message resurfaced in his mind.

"Tianluo Era, Year 213..."

*Buzz buzz buzz!* The moment this sentence reappeared in Li Biren's mind, the puppet emitted a heavy sound, as if a machine that had been sealed for many years was activated again. The humanoid statue seemed to shift from虛 to實 (void to real), its previously lowered hands slowly rising to its chest. Extending its right hand, it pointed towards the center of the circular wall.

The scene of countless block star seas displayed on the cylindrical hall changed drastically as the puppet pointed. The circular wall flickered rapidly between light and dark. Like a book with pages being quickly turned forward, or like a video being played in reverse. The extinguished life force turned into dark, silent starscapes, and then brightened again. The flickering block star seas also gradually stopped their movement and became stable. The few areas where life force still existed suddenly erupted, transforming from faint points of light into brilliant starscapes.

Unknowingly, Li Biren was surrounded by a vast sea of life. The entire star sea monitored by the experimental site seemed to have returned to the time before the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. The star sea's light and shadow were leaping and shifting. Finally, at a certain moment, it abruptly stopped. After a pause, the scene on the circular wall resumed normal playback.

The scene changed extremely rapidly. Even with Li Biren's divine sense strength, fully deciphering and identifying everything within it was somewhat strenuous. However, after a moment of observation, Li Biren quickly realized. What he was seeing was a repeatedly played recorded scene.

"This is not reversing time and returning to the era before the Great Tribulation. It is through this humanoid figure that the monitoring data recorded by this experimental site has been retrieved."

"Tianluo Era, Year 213..."

"So the following segment should be..." Li Biren recited the latter part of the secret message in his mind again. "Beginning with Shangzhang Dayuanxian and Zuo E'er Fenghuang."

The humanoid figure moved again according to this instruction. Its previously lowered left hand also slowly rose. This time, it was not a simple point, but like drawing the circle of the Great Void, it outlined a range within the repeatedly played scene. Li Biren saw that not only was a portion of the recording of Tianluo Era, Year 213, truncated from the beginning, but also, with this stroke, ninety percent of the block star seas on the circular wall disappeared. The brilliant sea of life suddenly dimmed.
