Li Biren continued to recite the last sentence of the secret message. "Ending with Yong Chi Fenruo and Yan Mao Xuan Yi."

The looping recorded scene was further shortened. According to Li Biren's calculation, Tianluo Era, Year 213, originally represented about a thousand years in the Xuanhuang Realm. But after the screening of the two commands, the time range was greatly reduced. Li Biren watched the repeating scenes and calculated that this segment was about fifty years long. Similarly, this time it was not just a precise lock on the time range. The humanoid figure waved its hand again, parting the starscape. This time, only three block star seas remained brightly lit. The originally inconspicuous three small blocks occupied the entire circular wall. The events that occurred in these block star seas during this period were replayed in rapid succession. And among them, one star sea was extremely familiar to Li Biren. It was the Utmost Darkness Star Sea where the Xuanhuang Realm was located!

With a slight movement of his mind, Li Biren attempted to probe into the recorded scene before him. This time, there was no resistance from protective forces, as if he were truly wandering in the star sea. Li Biren quickly located the Xuanhuang Realm.

"No Immortal Dao Ten Sects."

"No Xuanhuang Cult."

"Wild God, Samsara, Divine Wood. This is from an ancient era when the Immortal Realm still existed. The Great Tribulation had not yet appeared, and cultivation sects could still communicate with the Immortal Realm."

For fifty years of time, Li Biren could not observe everything that happened on the Xuanhuang continent in detail. He could only focus on certain unusual events.

"The Wild God Sect reached its peak in summoning Wild Gods in the fifth year. A total of twelve different Wild Gods appeared simultaneously, suppressing all opposition. In the Xuanhuang Realm, they were unrivaled. However, in the forty-third year, one of the Wild Gods suddenly lost contact with the Wild God Sect. This was something unprecedented in the history of the Wild God Sect."

"Although a new Wild God was reconnected eight years later, this incident caused great worry to the sect leader and elders of the Wild God Sect."

"Compared to the Wild God Sect, the Samsara Cult appeared much more low-key. The Samsara Cult does not establish great Samsara in the Xuanhuang Realm, but establishes small Samsaras within individuals. With the Samsara Undying Body, one can repeatedly reincarnate and be reborn. Although each reincarnation results in the loss of cultivation, certain crucial memories are preserved."

"And the pursuit of continuous reincarnation and rebirth is not to ascend to immortality, but rather..."

Li Biren narrowed his eyes. The ultimate cultivation of the Samsara Cult's secret techniques, which could not be known through surveillance, was unknown. But the actions of that Samsara Cult sect leader were indeed suspicious. Besides always avoiding surveillance by connecting to the Immortal Realm, Jiang Lianshi often sat in meditation on the top floor of a tall pavilion in the Samsara Cult. The top floor had only one large hall. Tens of thousands of paintings by Jiang Lianshi himself were hung there. These paintings seemed to be all drawn by Jiang Lianshi himself. In each painting, Jiang Lianshi had different expressions, attire, and actions. Besides painting, Jiang Lianshi spent his time facing tens of thousands of his own portraits in this pavilion. Throughout the entire process, there were no fluctuations of spiritual energy. But as a bystander many years later, Li Biren still felt a strange sensation from this bizarre cultivation scene. Sometimes, he even had the illusion that in a certain moment, all the paintings in the pavilion came to life.

Within fifty years, Jiang Lianshi did not achieve any breakthrough. The entire Samsara Cult remained low-key and silent. There was only one instance of action: a Divine Wood Sect elder came knocking, wanting to borrow the Samsara Cult's treasure, the [Ten Thousand Year Pearl]. According to the Divine Wood Sect elder, the Ten Thousand Year Pearl could promote the growth of the Divine Wood Sect's Divine Wood without side effects. He sincerely requested it but was rejected by Jiang Lianshi in one word. The Divine Wood Sect elder pleaded several times, but the result was the same. Enraged, he attempted to seize it by force, but was pointed at the center of his brow by Jiang Lianshi. The elder, over sixty years old, seemed to reverse through time, returning to infancy. Not only was his cultivation lost, but his mind also regressed to childhood. Jiang Lianshi did not take the elder's life but ordered someone to send him back to the Divine Wood Sect, along with a talisman he personally wrote. A seemingly ordinary yellow paper, on which was drawn a crude eye. The Divine Wood Sect received this talisman, apologized to the Samsara Cult, and expressed their gratitude, offering equivalent gifts. Jiang Lianshi politely declined and strictly ordered his disciples to minimize interaction with the Divine Wood Sect.

...

"Jiang Lianshi's cultivation..." Li Biren had observed Jiang Lianshi for fifty years. Even with his current vision, he could not fully fathom it. On the surface, he seemed to be merely at the Dao Integration realm, but that single finger that could reverse time was already very telling. Considering the Samsara Cult's ability to reincarnate and cultivate continuously, Jiang Lianshi had likely lived for an unknown duration. Furthermore, the tens of thousands of self-portraits hanging in the pavilion's top floor made Li Biren think of the word "possibility." "Could the Samsara Cult's ultimate secret involve their own selves in other possibilities? Although they cannot cross over, they can subtly connect?"

Li Biren became increasingly curious about Jiang Lianshi's ultimate fate. However, the recorded scene was fixed at this fifty-year period, making it impossible to pry further.

Within these fifty years, besides the events in these powerful sects, something else happened in the ancient Xuanhuang Realm that deserved Li Biren's attention. In the thirtieth year, in the southeastern corner of the Xuanhuang Realm, a True Immortal allegedly descended to the mortal world. That large area of distorted light and shadow made it impossible to see the details clearly. Furthermore, this True Immortal was not alone but had someone to greet him in the Xuanhuang Realm. The one responsible for the reception seemed to be merely a mortal. For the first thirty years, he lived as an extremely ordinary village elder. But in the thirtieth year, he suddenly left his wife and children and went into the deep mountains. He set up a reception ritual. After completing this, he returned to his village as if nothing had happened. Just half a year later, he died. The True Immortal who was received seemed to have escaped the unseen surveillance and disappeared thereafter. What Li Biren found particularly noteworthy was that the place where the mortal lived was very close to the location of the Fishing Pond. However, there was no trace of the Fishing Pond in this recorded holographic image. Therefore, it was not yet possible to determine if the "Fishing Immortal" was involved behind the scenes.

"This period of time does not include the Medicine King Sect or Sun Piaomiao's existence."

"What did he want to reveal by leaving this secret message through the bronze immortal crane? Or did he himself not understand, and only roughly pinpointed the time frame?"

Li Biren's gaze temporarily shifted away from the Xuanhuang Realm. He looked towards the outside of the star sea. It had to be said that the ancient cultivation era was vastly different from the present. Life was abundant, and strange phenomena often appeared in the star sea. Li Biren finally understood why there were always rumors that when star sea anomalies erupted, even True Immortals had to retreat.

"To some extent, the outbreak of star sea anomalies would interfere with the connection between True Immortals and the Sea of Infinity."

"Without the characteristic of infinity, True Immortals might not be able to escape unharmed amidst these strange and unpredictable anomalies."

In fifty years, the Utmost Darkness Star Sea experienced seven anomalous events that could deter True Immortals. The blurry recorded images recounted these magnificent scenes that had occurred in the star sea historically. Li Biren's divine sense drifted through the Utmost Darkness Star Sea during these fifty years. He secretly noted every anomaly in the cultivation world.

"As expected, the Xuanhuang Realm is unique."

"Regardless of anything else, its connection with the Immortal Realm alone makes it extraordinary compared to ordinary cultivation worlds."

"Moreover..." Li Biren clearly sensed that the "spirituality" of beings in other cultivation worlds seemed much weaker compared to the Xuanhuang Realm.

Chapter 1465: Really Guiding

The so-called "spirituality" was a unique quality that Li Fan, his true body, began to perceive in cultivators and beings after comprehending the divine ability [True Form is False]. It was a comprehensive judgment of mindset, talent, origin, luck, and all other factors, related to the probability of that being transcending possibilities. In the past, Li Fan's perspective was focused only on the common people of the Xuanhuang Realm. Those he contacted in the Shining Star Sea were among the top talents. Moreover, their numbers were too small to make a judgment. Now, with Li Biren's observation scope expanded to the entire experimental star sea, the Xuanhuang Realm was just one of countless stars, and the data volume had increased tens of millions of times. Li Fan suddenly discovered a fact: "Among the vast sea of cultivation worlds, the aptitude of beings in the Xuanhuang Realm is definitely among the best."

The cause of this difference in the average aptitude level of cultivation world beings was unknown. "But the True Immortals in the experimental site must have discovered this peculiarity. It is reasonable for them to regard the Xuanhuang Realm as a primary object of observation."

Among the entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea, Li Fan was most concerned about the Profound Merchant Immortal Boat. At this point in time, the Profound Merchant Immortal Boat had already begun to travel between various realms. Due to the boat's unfixed location, sometimes even venturing near areas where star phenomena erupted, the experimental site's records of the Profound Merchant Immortal Boat were not continuous. During certain periods, observation of the Profound Merchant Immortal Boat was completely lost. Shortly after, the Immortal Boat would "jump" to another location in the star sea. Inside the Immortal Boat, there also seemed to be some method capable of interfering with the experimental site's recordings. The images were very unclear, intermittent as if the signal was lost. In Li Fan's exploration, it was as if he was hitting a wall everywhere, completely unable to fully grasp what was happening inside the Profound Merchant Immortal Boat.

"It is said that the Profound Merchant Immortal Boat discovered the fact that beings in various realms were being raised like livestock, and therefore abandoned the idea of settling in one realm, choosing instead to constantly roam the star sea in hopes of escaping this fate. To some extent, they have indeed achieved this."

"According to the current claims of the Profound Merchant Immortal Boat, they likely possess an Immortal artifact, or a method usable only by True Immortals, to achieve such a miraculous effect."

Following the routine, Li Biren recorded all suspicious events that occurred within the Profound Merchant Immortal Boat during these fifty years. Just as he was about to examine the other two block star seas besides the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Biren suddenly felt as if he had overlooked something. Pondering, his consciousness returned to the fifty-year recording of the Xuanhuang Realm. This time, he focused not on the prominent, dazzling beings but on the ordinary masses. Li Biren discovered that some of the faces were eerily familiar. At this recorded point in time, Li Fan did not yet exist. The reason Li Biren found some faces familiar was that they had appeared in the countless frozen corpses within the Reversed Life and Death Great Array of the Heaven of Death and Life, as one of the corpses.

"Not just these. Even one or two of these faces still exist in the current Xuanhuang Realm?" With a thought, Li Fan's true body locked onto two individuals within the Unbounded Dreamland Paradise. They were originally mortals who began their cultivation journey only after the Dreamland Paradise enveloped the entire Xuanhuang Realm. And in the experimental site's records, these two also existed as unremarkable mortals in the ancient Xuanhuang Realm.

"..." Four faces, spanning eons of time, overlapped pair by pair before Li Fan's eyes. Even with Li Fan's current power, capable of destroying the Xuanhuang Realm with a wave of his hand, he couldn't help but feel a chill. He recalled the mortal who suddenly deviated from his normal life path in the recorded footage, as if he had become a different person, to receive the True Immortal.

"These mortals are likely just NPCs created to fill the Xuanhuang Realm and be used for endless reincarnation. At crucial moments, they can even receive special instructions to complete tasks assigned by True Immortals..."

"This method of control is not achieved through any divine abilities or spells, but is likely embedded deep within the core of these mortals." Before ascending to Immortality, Li Fan could barely create something using the "Form of Living Beings." Therefore, he had no doubt that the True Immortals of the Immortal Realm in the past had the ability to mass-produce living beings.

"These created living beings are recycled. This indicates that the experimental site also considered the problem of consumption. Due to the enormous base number, each reincarnation cycle, centuries or even millennia pass in the world, and almost no one can even notice."

"Even if discovered by chance, it can be explained as a coincidence, making it difficult to confirm."

"Only someone like me, who spans two time periods and has complete knowledge of the appearance of all beings in the Xuanhuang Realm, can make a definitive judgment."

"Not only will everything that happens be recorded, but even the environment of the cultivation world and most beings are pre-set. Truly worthy of being an experimental site..."

"It's just that I don't know if other cultivation worlds, besides the Xuanhuang Realm, are also like this." The other realms have all been destroyed. Li Fan cannot verify. But likely, their situations should be similar to the Xuanhuang Realm.

"The maintenance of the experimental site is definitely related to the unstable ring and the Nine Star Red Pearls in the ancient Xuanhuang Realm formation that I discovered previously."

"The Nine Star Red Pearls are missing, suspected to have been taken away."

"Traces of the 'Return' technique were left at the scene."

"If it were an insider from the Immortal Realm retrieving it, there would be no need for such trouble. Therefore, it should be an outsider."

"Judging from the residual pattern of the Nine Star Red Pearls I saw before, and the recorded data in this experimental site, the Nine Star Red Pearls should contain all the life data of beings that have existed in the Xuanhuang Realm..."

In Li Fan's mind, countless different faces flashed rapidly. A question suddenly arose in his mind. If those mortals were NPCs created to fill the void, then what were the cultivators who were active in the history of the Xuanhuang Realm, those glorious figures, even peerless powerhouses known throughout the ages?

"Not only are there frequent geniuses in the history of the Xuanhuang Realm."

"All True Immortals who have ascended in the past have left no records. Either they were deliberately erased, or they all achieved the Nameless realm and spontaneously disappeared from the world's records."

"If it's the former, it's fine. But if it's the latter..." Nameless True Immortals, even though they died like ants during the calamity of the Immortal Realm's destruction, each's advancement required merging with the Dao. Their numbers could not be too large. Moreover, this was based on countless, immeasurable cultivation worlds in the lower realms. Even if the Xuanhuang Realm was exceptionally blessed with spiritual energy, it was impossible to produce so many Nameless True Immortals frequently. Like a bolt of lightning cleaving through the mist. A thought inevitably arose in Li Fan's mind: "Perhaps Nameless True Immortals descended to the lower realms in some way. Using themselves as bait, trying to attract and capture ['Return to Truth']?"

Li Fan's thoughts raced. "This supreme treasure from the Sea of Infinity, capable of reversing the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, would surely attract even Nameless True Immortals. If it were me, knowing about this experimental site in the lower realm, I would also find a way to get involved, even if it meant sneaking in. "After all, it's just an avatar, and it can be done casually. If they actually managed to capture it?"

"But how could ['Return to Truth'] be so easily lured out? They were destined to fail."

"Those who can cultivate to the Nameless True Immortal realm undoubtedly have extraordinary talent. Even if they emulated themselves as bait for the sake of realism, they might not have the memories of their main bodies. But returning to the True Immortal realm should not be a problem."

"As an experimental site, theoretically, it is impossible for experimental beings to escape through ascension. However, these True Immortals from the Immortal Realm are naturally exempt from the restrictions. Some might even be existences that the experimenters themselves cannot afford to offend. Thus, they would naturally choose to let them go willingly."

Li Fan suddenly recalled Mo Ruban's description of King Xuan Yuan's memories. "King Xuan Yuan was able to successfully ascend to Immortality because the Immortal Official in charge of the lightning tribulation happened to die during the Immortal Realm's destruction calamity, allowing him to narrowly ascend to the Immortal Realm. According to King Xuan Yuan himself, that lightning tribulation was never intended to let any cultivator pass."

"King Xuan Yuan was already the greatest figure in the Xuanhuang Realm's history. In fact, since starting his cultivation path, he was suspected to have had the assistance of the Fishing Pond. Even so, facing that ascension lightning tribulation, he still had no chance of winning."

"It seems that under normal circumstances, escaping from this experimental site is impossible."

Li Fan's expression darkened, yet he felt a sense of relief. Fortunately, the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation had descended and destroyed the Immortal Realm. The True Immortals fled in all directions to save their lives, no longer bothering with this experimental site.

"Otherwise, even with the benefit of ['Return to Truth'], I would likely be like a bird in a cage, or a fish in a net..."

Thinking of this, Li Fan suddenly paused. Reflecting carefully: "Or perhaps, the True Immortals' calculations back then were not wrong. 'Return to Truth' did indeed appear in this delineated experimental site. But..."

"Perhaps they did not anticipate that ['Return to Truth'] has its own consciousness. How could such a method fool 'Return to Truth'?"

"Thus, it never revealed itself and waited..."

"Not only was the Immortal Realm destroyed and the experimental site ruined, but it also waited for a suitable, unique vessel."

With this conjecture, "Return to Truth," which had been dormant since returning from the Sea of Infinity, finally fluctuated again. However, the emotion it conveyed this time was somewhat baffling to Li Fan.

"A bit of certainty."

"And a bit of amusement."

"This..." Li Fan's expression remained calm, even shamelessly wanting to ask for more guidance. Having spent hundreds of reincarnations with "Return to Truth," Li Fan could perceive almost any subtle change in it. Li Fan keenly noticed that since returning from the Sea of Infinity, and possibly interacting with "Return to Truth's" old acquaintances, "Return to Truth" had gradually become more "active." Previously, it only responded lazily under extreme circumstances. But now...

This time, in response to Li Fan's sincere request for guidance, "Return to Truth," which had always been indifferent, actually provided an answer. Li Fan himself was caught off guard by this result. After a moment of stunned silence, he searched for "Return to Truth's" guidance. His true body and the clone puppet, Li Biren, showed no changes. The change existed... in the time segment called [Endless Reincarnation] that Li Fan had created in this life. True Venerable was trapped within, having experienced nine thousand three hundred and sixty-three reincarnations. No matter how he tried, he could not alter the outcome of the Xuanhuang Realm's destruction. Therefore, after the eight hundredth attempt, True Venerable finally chose to give up. He gave up all pursuits. From the beginning of each reincarnation, he resigned himself to await the destruction. Gradually, he even felt that this might not be so bad. Anyway, no matter how it was destroyed, he would return to the initial time point. So, in a sense, didn't he mean immortality? With this realization, True Venerable's passivity became even more justifiable. He lived his days in a daze. He never noticed that the speed of his reincarnation was getting faster and faster.

In Li Fan's view, under the disturbance of "Return to Truth," the speed of reincarnation in this time segment was drastically accelerated. True Venerable, trapped within, could not perceive it, but Li Fan could see the cycle of evolution happening tens of millions of times per second. True Venerable, completely resigned, gave up struggling in each reincarnation. Samsara, therefore, lost its variability. Each time was identical to the last.

... Staring intently at True Venerable in his reincarnation, Li Fan's expression became somewhat unusual. Because he saw that True Venerable's spirituality was being gradually stripped away with each increase in the number of reincarnations. It was as if Li Fan was constantly using the divine ability of True Form is False. Ultimately, his spirituality was completely lost, and his future path was severed!

Li Fan's mind roared. "When true becomes false, and false becomes true."

"The divine ability of True Form is False can reduce a cultivator's spirituality."

"And isn't each activation of my reincarnation equivalent to True Form is False?"

"Moreover, this True Form is False was even personally activated by 'Return to Truth'..."

Li Fan trembled inwardly and conjured a water mirror before himself. He had observed the spirituality of all beings. But he had never observed his own. With trepidation and fear, Li Fan looked at himself. The familiar, extremely familiar face and body. This time, upon closer inspection... To his relief, what he feared did not happen. Even... Li Fan's expression became somewhat strange. He stroked his chin and suddenly realized. What was "Return to Truth's" guidance? Was it the reason Li Fan, as the vessel, was unique? Why was he chosen from among countless beings?

Li Fan gazed at his own face. His spirituality did not seem particularly outstanding. But he had a strange feeling. His own spirituality was incomparably profound. Even after being stripped away by repeated reincarnations, it had not changed much.

"If the ability to withstand True Form is False is also a form of aptitude..."

"Perhaps this aptitude of mine is the top-tier in the world."

"Unlike other cultivation aptitudes, this is what 'Return to Truth' truly values."

Chapter 1466: Shoulder the Dao Annihilation Tribulation

After experiencing a hundred cycles of reincarnation, my spiritual essence remains undiminished. Even a Nameless True Immortal might not compare to me. After realizing my uniqueness, Li Fan couldn't help but feel a surge of joy.

He attempted to communicate with "Return to Truth" again, but it was like a stone sinking into the sea, receiving no response. After a long while, Li Fan’s turbulent emotions finally calmed. Naturally, a greater question began to surface in his mind.

My spiritual essence is perhaps rare, or even unique, in the mortal world. What is the reason for this characteristic? Li Fan directly thought of his identity as a "transmigrator." But was it truly so, and why was a "transmigrator's" spiritual essence so different? If there were other "transmigrators," would they also exhibit the same characteristics as him? Furthermore, there was an even deeper layer to consider: What was the "purpose" of "Return to Truth" attaching itself to Li Fan?

These questions were beyond Li Fan’s current ability to explore. Suppressing all turbulent thoughts to the deepest part of his heart, Li Fan thought: At the very least, my relationship with "Return to Truth" has become outwardly closer. Since it returned from the Infinite Sea, it has become more 'lively,' which is a good thing. If it can guide me once, it can do so a second time. And the guidance of "Return to Truth"... It surpasses the enlightenment gained by directly facing the Great Dao!

While the main body gained substantial benefits, the clone puppet, Li Biren, showed no emotional change due to these discoveries. His mission was to thoroughly investigate matters within the high wall. The situation was still shrouded in mist, so how could he afford to relax?

Based on the current clues, it can be determined that this place was originally part of the Immortal Realm's experimental facilities. The purpose of the experiment was to find a way to counter the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. This experimental site naturally possessed certain methods for defending against the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. Although abandoned for unknown reasons, it transformed into the high wall when the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation erupted, saving countless star seas within the experimental site from complete annihilation. Similarly, the experimental site's mission dictated its highly covert nature. Internal defenses were sufficient to trap the living beings within the experimental star seas. Externally, it needed to consider the probing of powerful beings at the Nameless realm and above. No wonder Qian Ruochang of the Shining Star Sea and the "Nameless Immortal" approached the high wall as if they saw nothing. It was not that they did not want to, but that they could not. It could even block the gaze from other possibilities to some extent.

The meaning of Sun Piaomiao's message remained unclear for now. Li Biren decided not to dwell on it for the time being. I discovered the peculiarity of the high wall because the Immortal Realm chess piece was captured by the high wall and disappeared into thin air. Since that is the case, why not return to the origin of the matter and track the current location of that chess piece ... The Immortal Realm chess pieces left by Sun Piaomiao had mutual resonance. However, due to the high wall, this resonance was severed. Even though Li Biren's body was forged from an Immortal Realm chess piece, and he was within this experimental site, he still couldn't sense the presence of his "kindred."

After a moment of thought, Li Biren decided to return to the Utmost Darkness Star Sea for now, leaving the Medicine King Cauldron chess piece in the Xuanhuang Realm to prevent the fragments from reassembling and the Immortal Realm from re-emerging. Then, from his body, he separated faint silver limbs resembling a net or an arm, violently "entangled and tightly bound" all the remaining chess pieces onto himself. Then, he fiercely charged towards the high wall again. The moment he entered the high wall, Li Biren felt an immense suction force from the outside. The Immortal Realm chess pieces within his body, uncontrollably, swiftly flew towards the source of the suction. Li Biren did not resist this force; in fact, his body transformed back into its original chess piece form, flying towards the unknown with his "brothers."

Indeed, unlike entering as an intruder, this time the entry was through a different path. Li Biren seemed to be hurtling through countless block star seas above the experimental site. Then, he traversed the Great Void, which served as the boundary of all star seas. He arrived in a space that was both familiar and unfamiliar. It was familiar because it seemed to be the same place as the cylindrical hall Li Biren had previously visited, just located at the very top of the cylinder, in a place invisible from the bottom. Upon arriving here, the suction force on the Immortal Realm chess pieces disappeared. Li Biren, in his chess piece form, observed his surroundings. He discovered that the eleven chess pieces that had mysteriously disappeared before and were now brought along, were all quietly floating in formation. Six of them had inexplicably merged together, appearing seven-colored like the ones Li Fan had seen before. The remaining five were tightly clustered together, waiting for Li Biren's final piece to join them. From the chess pieces not far away, Li Biren sensed an urge to return. However, perhaps because the crucial Medicine King True Cauldron piece was missing, or perhaps because this was the true core area of the experimental site with some unknown restrictions, Li Biren felt that the attraction of the chess pieces had not yet reached the point of being uncontrollable. Maintaining his stability, he surveyed his surroundings. Only then did he suddenly notice that five blurry figures were quietly standing around him. Li Biren's heart immediately tensed, and he retreated rapidly, assuming a battle stance. However, he found that no matter how fast he moved, these five figures always circled him, keeping him in the center. He could neither approach nor distance himself. The five ethereal figures were like the azure sky to the beings living on the ground. An eternally unstable distance was maintained between them. Fortunately, these ethereal figures seemed to have no offensive capabilities, behaving like inanimate objects, showing no reaction to Li Biren, the intruder. Li Biren first gathered all the Immortal Realm chess pieces, then observed the five ethereal figures, confirming that there was no immediate danger. They were faintly beyond my perceptual abilities, hence I didn't notice them at first. It was only when I truly observed and paid attention that I could discern their existence... The words "Nameless True Immortal" suddenly popped into Li Biren's mind. This scene was strikingly similar to what Li Fan had spied upon in the Shining Star Sea: Nameless True Immortals serving as living stakes to build the Dao Net. The Immortal Heavenly Pillar in the Immortal Realm was also made from the leg bone of a Nameless True Immortal and possessed a certain degree of resistance to the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. It was not unbelievable that Nameless True Immortals were also used as building materials within the high wall. However, Li Biren instinctively felt that this place was different from the Dao Net and the Southern Immortal Heavenly Pillar. "Using Dao as pillars, this is the ability displayed by the five ethereal figures, and it should be correct." "The key lies in..." Li Biren frowned slightly. "It's the same Great Dao!" For a True Immortal to ascend to the Nameless realm, they needed to merge with the Dao. And among the Three Thousand Great Daos in the world, each was different, and there could be no repetition. Therefore, it was impossible for two Nameless True Immortals to achieve enlightenment through the same Dao path. Not two, let alone five appearing at once! "From different possibilities?" Li Biren was shocked, but he quickly dismissed this idea. He had witnessed the aura of powerful beings who could traverse possibilities. Although these five ethereal figures were strong, they were far from comparable. "Therefore, there is only one answer." "These five ethereal figures are manifestations of the same Nameless True Immortal." "Not like flesh and blood, such as the leg bone in the Southern Immortal Heavenly Pillar, but merely their ethereal projections." Li Biren's heart trembled. "To erect walls and withstand the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation with just five ethereal projections?" "What realm is this?" The five ethereal figures, like stars, circled Li Biren. Their faces were indistinct, and it was impossible to tell if they were male or female. Yet, like divinities in myths, they inspired solemnity and reverence. This was the natural emotion of lower beings when encountering superiors. "I once speculated that beneath the ruins of the Immortal Realm lay a martyred Nameless True Immortal, using himself as a pillar to block the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation from the Immortal Realm." "But now, this Nameless being before me doesn't need to sacrifice himself. By merely projecting five ethereal figures, he achieves the same feat..." Li Biren's shock was beyond words. It was evident that the being who left these five ethereal figures was among the strongest of all Nameless True Immortals. This form of strength, compared to the ability to traverse possibilities, was different. Li Biren could not judge which was superior. But he knew that their performance was equally awe-inspiring. "In Su Bai's memories, facing the monstrous Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, Evil Su Bai could only flee in disarray." "But in the [Primordial] possibility I inhabit, there is such a peerless expert who resists the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation with his own ethereal projections." "Perhaps they chose different paths?" "Where is this expert now? Was he originally in charge of this laboratory's plan?" Various questions arose in Li Biren's mind. "If there were more such experts, the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation might not be so difficult to deal with." Li Biren gazed at the five ethereal figures, thinking that if more powerful beings existed, the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation might not be so formidable. The ethereal figures, capable of becoming immortal pillars and resisting the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, should be infinitely close to the Dao itself. Yet, though they were within reach, Li Biren could not comprehend the Great Dao they represented. It was as if this Dao was not within the scope of his current understanding and interaction with the Great Daos of heaven and earth. Seeing without seeing, hearing without hearing, knowing without knowing! "Either this being is from another possibility; the Dao he merged with does not exist in the [Primordial] possibility. To me, it is a completely unfamiliar existence, hence I cannot comprehend or perceive it at all." "Or perhaps..." "This being's realm has already reached consummation. Leaving the confines of this world with the Dao he merged with, he walks alone!" Li Fan had previously conjectured: that Nameless True Immortals merged with the Dao and then fled, drawing away the Great Daos that once served as pillars of heaven and earth, thus shattering the load-bearing walls of the building, leading to the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. But later, after encountering many Nameless True Immortal realm experts, and fortunately entering the Infinite Sea to witness the subtle connection between the Infinite Sea and the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, his guess became doubtful. However, upon directly facing these five ethereal figures, he had truly encountered a Nameless True Immortal who had "stepped outside of the Three Realms and beyond the Five Elements." "Coming from another possibility, yet sacrificing himself to help resist the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, such a possibility is slim. He could have fled alone." "This being should be a native inhabitant of the [Primordial] possibility." Li Biren observed and attempted to use his divine sense to illuminate the Great Dao represented by these five ethereal figures. But the mirror of his mind, capable of illuminating the Great Daos of heaven and earth, remained empty when facing these five ethereal figures. "Does this being still exist in the current possibility?" "If he has already departed, and only left behind ethereal projections with such effectiveness..." "Then it is truly terrifying." Of all the things and beings Li Fan had encountered so far, only the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation and the Infinite Sea inspired such dread. And those who could contend with them, besides "Return to Truth," were these unknown powerful beings. Although they were weaker than "Return to Truth," they still showed Li Fan the upper limit that cultivators could reach. After the fruitless attempt at illumination, Li Biren stopped wasting his efforts. "These five ethereal figures must be the core of the high wall." "Such an important area must have a reason for attracting the Immortal Realm chess pieces. However, we still cannot find the trigger method." Remaining here, Li Biren could only manifest in the form of an Immortal Realm chess piece; otherwise, he would soon be expelled. "Since there has been no change for a long time, is it because the Immortal Realm chess pieces are not yet complete?" This thought soon surfaced in Li Biren's mind. After some deliberation, Li Fan, the main body in the Xuanhuang Realm, finally handed over the Medicine King Cauldron to the clone puppet. The Medicine King True Cauldron, collected by Li Fan in this life without alarming the Hungry Immortal, had its occupants from the Medicine King Sect naturally placed in the Land of Unbounded Dreams, contributing to the dreamland's construction. The Medicine King True Cauldron reverted to its original form: a simple, unadorned white chess piece. Li Biren re-integrated it into the center of the high wall, where the five ethereal figures resided. Li Fan, the main body, maintained extreme vigilance, ready to "Return to Truth" at any moment. Li Biren also prepared to reassemble his body and evolve into an Immortal Realm. However, the development of events was somewhat beyond Li Fan's expectations. Even with all the chess pieces complete, the Immortal Realm did not unfold in the space where the five ethereal figures were located. Instead, an unseen force seemed to be restraining the formation of the Immortal Realm. But as Li Fan had predicted, when the Immortal Realm chess pieces gathered here, anomalies occurred in the surroundings. Like foreign objects falling into water, causing ripples. The faces of the five ethereal figures distorted amidst these ripples, becoming somewhat clearer. Their gazes were all fixed on the chess pieces in the center. It was as if the heavens and earth were pressing down upon them. Li Biren's Immortal Realm chess piece-formed body momentarily struggled to bear the pressure. "This is..." "With all the chess pieces gathered, they have earned the attention of the Nameless True Immortal, finally worthy of their notice!"

Chapter 1467: Guarding the Hill Immortal

Along with the appearance of the five ethereal figures' faces came faint, exceptionally calm words. It seemed not spoken to Li Biren, the intruder, but a pre-recorded message.

"The Virtuous Sage Shouqiu Immortal pays respects to the enlightened Sage Houdu."

"Having both attained the Nameless realm and aimed for transcendence, yet the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation lurks. We cannot shirk our responsibilities."

"By chance, we obtained this excellent method, using projections to replace the body, capable of resisting endless calamities."

"We share it with you..."

The five ethereal figures spoke in unison. What followed was not ordinary sound, but like a carving knife engraving the method directly onto Li Biren's body, surrounded by the ethereal figures. There was no pain, not even any abnormality, as if it were forgotten memories that had always belonged to him, re-emerring. It skipped the entire process of contemplation, learning, and mastery. To know was to have achieved supreme mastery!

However, Li Biren felt a tinge of regret. The reason the five ethereal figures were actively imparting the pháp môn was that all the chess pieces of an entire Immortal Realm had arrived. In terms of status, it was almost equivalent to a Nameless True Immortal. Therefore, the Shouqiu Immortal regarded all the chess pieces as a unified whole. The engraving and imprinting were performed on this entirety.

What Li Biren received was only a small part. But this secret method, which could only be cultivated at the Nameless True Immortal realm, was enough to broaden his horizons!

"This method is called [Shouqiu’s Wandering Notes]."

"On the edge of the vast ocean, there is a humble hill, nameless."

"Virtuous Sage Shouqiu guarded the hill for one hundred and twenty-three epochs. Witnessing the ebb and flow of the tides, the rise and fall of life. Each time he felt something, he recorded it. As time passed, the wandering notes gradually formed..."

Li Biren sifted through the "memories" in his mind. Simple words seemed to depict a lonely figure, who for one hundred and twenty-three epochs, had guarded the vast ocean’s edge. Standing on the nameless hill, gazing at the endless ocean. A scene of coexisting with the tides.

"This Shouqiu Immortal, capable of shouldering the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation with five ethereal projections, his strength and realm are certainly not as simple as the self-deprecation in his wandering notes."

Li Biren let out a long sigh, seemingly breaking free from the ancient years brought by these few lines.

"Sun Piaomiao’s previous transmission contained descriptions of the Tianluo Epoch. Epoch should be the calendar and commemoration used by the Immortal Realm. I just don't know how many years in the Xuanhuang Realm correspond to one epoch in the Immortal Realm."

"But regardless, one hundred and twenty-three epochs must be an extremely long period of time."

"And the sea and hill that required such a long time to constantly guard certainly cannot be ordinary seas and hills."

Li Biren suddenly recalled the allegory of the mountain and sea from the book suspected to be left by Sun Piaomiao.

"If the sea represents the Infinite Sea, then what does the mountain represent..."

The wandering notes left by this Shouqiu Immortal, Virtuous Sage, not only simply imparted the method of leaving ethereal projections but also meticulously recorded the entire thought process and experience of Shouqiu Immortal in comprehending this method. This method was not achieved through sudden enlightenment one day. It was refined through accumulation and infinite contemplation. Receiving this method, Li Biren felt as if he had "transmigrated" into the body of the former Shouqiu Immortal, re-experiencing the vicissitudes of one hundred and twenty-three epochs with his body, soul, and thoughts. Even if he only faced the mountain and the sea every day.

The seemingly infinite data almost drowned Li Biren. Fortunately, he bore this burden with the other Immortal Realm chess pieces. With his super physique, which was a projection of his divine sense Dao Net and fragments of Immortal Realm law, he could barely endure it.

"No wonder Shouqiu Immortal's ethereal projections only appeared when facing Nameless True Immortals. It wasn't that he was stingy and unwilling to impart this method to other Immortals, but rather that those below the Nameless realm could simply not bear it!"

Carried along by the torrent of Shouqiu Immortal's thoughts, Li Biren seemed to return to the Infinite Sea. Each drop of water around him contained billions of years of history.

"According to Shouqiu Immortal, the sea’s encroachment on the mountain has existed since the beginning of time. But like the tides in the mortal world, they fluctuate, with varying strengths. Since he began guarding the sea from the hill, its momentum, although constantly fluctuating, has been on an upward trend in scale. In fact… it is far from reaching the estimated 'climax.'"

"Shouqiu Immortal discovered this trend in the twentieth epoch. For the next hundred epochs, he confirmed this viewpoint."

"He had issued warnings to the world long ago, but alas, his words carried little weight?"

"This..." Li Biren felt greatly puzzled upon hearing this. However, the subsequent account of Virtuous Sage Shouqiu Immortal's life provided the answer. It turned out that at that time, Shouqiu Immortal was still an "ordinary" True Immortal. He had not even attained the Nameless realm. Thus, his words were naturally ignored.

But in the eighty-eighth epoch, Shouqiu Immortal’s accumulated efforts finally led him to the Nameless realm. However, he did not boast about it, but continued to silently guard the hill and observe the sea. At that time, the Immortal Realm seemed to have encountered a calamity, and all the Immortals in the Immortal Realm were too preoccupied to pay attention to this guardian of the distant sea. The entire Immortal Realm seemed to have forgotten him.

Until one day, the waves surged, crashing over the hill.

...

Breaking free from Shouqiu Immortal’s seemingly plain yet profoundly magnificent life, Li Biren began to focus on the method of [Ethereal Projection Carrying Dao].

"According to Shouqiu Immortal, as he sat on the hill gazing at the sea, the surging waves seemed to represent the countless Great Daos in the world."

"Each wave, in reality, was one and the same with the rhythm of the Great Dao."

"A person standing on a mountain peak, like a giant rock. Daily struck by the sea waves, it would be worn down. But simultaneously, between the mountain and the sea, it would leave its own unique mark."

..."

Shouqiu Immortal's wandering notes were extremely obscure and difficult to comprehend. Even with Li Fan's hundred lifetimes of reincarnation and countless experiences, he found it difficult to understand in a short time.

"If not for my 'Return to Truth' and my personal experience in the Infinite Sea, even if I obtained this method, I would be completely lost, perhaps even dismissing it as a joke!"

"Because this method is vastly different from the cultivation systems in the world," Li Fan realized.

But the magic of Shouqiu Immortal's wandering notes lay here. Even if the recipient could not comprehend its profound mysteries, because the five ethereal figures actively engraved it, the recipient could wield the [Ethereal Projection Carrying Dao] technique as if it were their own, without any obstacles.

"Completely without need for self-loss, merely extracting traces left in history and the Great Dao, transforming them into ethereal projections to bear the weight of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation..."

"This divine ability is indeed beyond imagination!"

Moreover, Li Fan sensed that the [Ethereal Projection Carrying Dao] technique had more than just the single effect of resisting the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. Or rather, carrying the Dao was just one of the many effects of this divine ability.

"Immune to a hundred calamities, all spells ineffective, eternal life..."

"Besides these, the most crucial is [Transcendence]!"

"It is the fundamental method to step outside of the Great Dao of this world."

By extracting all traces left in the mountains and seas in the past, it was also a process of severing all connections with the world. Then, with a solitary body, unbound by the net of the Great Dao...

Li Fan's heart trembled, a sense of yearning rising within him.

Just then, Shouqiu Immortal's transmission journey reached its conclusion. All of [Shouqiu’s Wandering Notes] had been fully imprinted. The five ethereal figures left by Shouqiu Immortal, Virtuous Sage, actually bowed slightly towards Li Biren in the center, offering a礼.

Then their bodies vibrated and slowly dissipated, returning to their previous state of silently bearing the Dao.

Li Biren's expression was solemn, and he respectfully returned the礼. He knew this was Shouqiu Immortal’s hope that future sages would also leave behind ethereal projections to carry the Dao, hence the bow.

"Shouqiu Immortal's ethereal projections may not be limited to this place within the high wall."

"After leaving these Dao-carrying ethereal projections, where is he now? Has he already left the current possibility?"

Recalling that despite the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation ravaging, the lower star seas still retained their vitality, Li Fan suddenly understood. And Li Biren’s ability to traverse possibilities beyond the mountain, Li Fan had no doubt of.

"Regardless, being able to leave behind some Dao-carrying ethereal projections, and leaving behind a profound and miraculous salvation technique for later generations, Shouqiu Immortal has certainly lived up to his responsibilities."

"Worthy of the name [Virtuous Sage]."

After a long period of contemplation, Li Biren finally came back to his senses and looked at the surrounding Immortal Realm chess pieces. After being engraved by Shouqiu Immortal, these chess pieces seemed different from before. Originally, these Immortal Realm fragments merely floated quietly, exuding a heart-palpitating aura. But now, they had returned to their original state, appearing unremarkable. So much so that anyone careless would overlook them.

"Or perhaps, it is more appropriate to describe it as 'gradually detaching from this world.'"

Li Biren's heart suddenly felt a sense of alarm. He had not forgotten that during the "Return to Truth" event, the leg bone of the Nameless True Immortal from the Immortal Realm seemed to have sensed something and flew towards it.

"The Nameless realm cannot be simply measured by life and death."

"Even though it was just a leg bone, and still in a fragmented state, but who knows what might happen after receiving [Shouqiu’s Wandering Notes]."

Li Biren tentatively picked up one of the white chess pieces. Then, disregarding everything else, he transformed his body from the Dao Net chess piece projection into his original form. A repulsive force struck, and Li Fan, carrying the Medicine King True Cauldron, fell from the uppermost space of the circular hall.

Chapter 1468: A Cycle, An Immortal Emperor

Falling from the space of Shouqiu Immortal’s ethereal projections, unlike directly intruding from the outside, the sights seen within this circular hall also differed. It seemed that sensing Li Biren’s residual Shouqiu Immortal legacy, the circular wall of the hall changed again. Besides the blocks representing countless monitored star seas and the white circle of the Great Void, there was also a figure closely resembling Shouqiu Immortal. Standing with his hands behind his back, facing away, he gazed down at the star seas below. Li Biren’s spirit jolted, and he attempted to probe it with his divine sense. After a moment, he realized: “This is not the Shouqiu Immortal, but someone like me who has received the inheritance of [Shouqiu’s Wandering Notes], hence the similar aura.” “However, judging by the degree of ‘Shouqiu’ state manifested by this figure…” “This person has likely received the complete wandering notes inheritance at the Nameless True Immortal realm, not like me, who took a shortcut.” However, this figure left by the Nameless True Immortal was not for carrying the Dao. It seemed to be merely recording an image. It had been hidden within this experimental space inside the high wall, only activated when it sensed Li Biren’s similar ‘Shouqiu’ aura.

“Immortal Emperor Zhaiyang, who held office, recently passed away.” “It has been a full epoch since the [Lan Ke Dao Field] was founded…” “What an exceedingly long period of time. So long that even with my immortal body, my past memories have become somewhat blurred.”

This voice did not come from the figure before Li Biren, but from the distant heavens, as if conversing with the figure from another realm. “When Immortal Emperor Zhaiyang first ascended the grand ceremony, I was merely an immortal servant in the Lie Tu Star Domain. Seven million, six hundred twenty-four thousand, six hundred and thirty-eight years have passed, and I have already risen to the Nameless realm.”

The figure spoke with emotion, not looking in the direction of the voice from the heavens, but continuing to gaze at the many star seas within the experimental site. “You remember so clearly. As expected of one who received Shouqiu Gong’s inheritance…” The voice from the heavens carried a strange emotion, a mixture of envy and schadenfreude. “Shortly after Shouqiu Gong departed, you already knew. It seems this place is indeed not clean…”

The figure snorted coldly. “That was Shouqiu Gong!” The voice from the heavens immediately became sharp. “At that time, the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation surged, and countless star domains were instantly submerged. The number of wrongfully dead was immeasurable. Immortal Emperor Zhaiyang led all the Nameless Immortals to personally confront it, but ultimately could only retreat again and again. Fortunately, Shouqiu Gong descended from the heavens and, with his own power, repelled the world-destroying tide… What a magnificent presence! Immortal Emperor Zhaiyang, upon meeting Shouqiu Gong, had to address him as a junior. Not to mention the countless True Immortals who were saved, who regarded Shouqiu Gong as a reborn parent. Even if he disliked being disturbed, how could Shouqiu Gong’s every move be concealed from the Immortals of the heavens? If the Lan Ke Dao Field were not a secret place, perhaps your receiving Shouqiu Gong’s inheritance now would have become known to the world!”

Listening to the somewhat sarcastic words, the figure did not refute. The voice from the heavens continued: “Immortal Emperor Zhaiyang reigned for seven million years, not a long lifespan, but it was our limit. Yet Shouqiu Gong lived for over a hundred epochs, experiencing over a hundred Immortal Emperors! Don't forget, among them was the [Infinite Immortal Emperor] with a lifespan of nine million nine hundred ninety-nine thousand nine hundred and ninety-nine years! Shouqiu Gong’s might is unimaginable! Qingyin, now that you have attained the Nameless realm and received the inheritance, let alone being able to live for over a hundred epochs like Shouqiu Gong without perishing, you should at least have a lifespan comparable to the Infinite Immortal, without a doubt…”

The Nameless True Immortal, named or titled [Qingyin], interrupted the voice from the heavens: “Shouqiu Gong left behind Dao-carrying ethereal projections in the Dao Field. If you are truly envious, why not descend to the lower realm and visit in person? Although not as good as Shouqiu Gong’s direct disciple, it is still close.”

The incessant voice from the heavens abruptly stopped. After a long pause, it chuckled and said: “Disciple of Shouqiu Gong is not so easy to become. We True Immortals, our lifespans are equal to the Dao. We come from the Dao and return to the Dao. When the Dao rises, it rises; when the Dao falls, it falls, following the will of heaven and earth, which also conforms to the principles of the world.” “A lifespan of millions of years is already quite long. Like Shouqiu Gong…” “Hehehe, having someone like Qingyin is enough.”

Qingyin said coldly: “Enough. If you have something to say, say it directly. After Shouqiu Gong left, I lost track of him. If you want to inquire about him from me, don’t even think about it.”

The voice from the heavens changed quickly, getting straight to the point: “Immortal Emperor Zhaiyang has fallen, and Heavenly Luo Immortal Emperor has just ascended. Some things from the previous epoch will likely be discarded. This Lan Ke Dao Field will also likely be decommissioned. Qingyin, you should prepare yourself.”

Qingyin seemed stunned, then asked in a deep voice: “That thing… after searching for so long, are we just going to abandon it? Although it didn’t appear within the estimated time, who knows if we wait a little longer and it will appear.”

“…This matter is complicated and cannot be explained in a short time. Simply put, besides the change in administration by Immortal Emperors Zhaiyang and Heavenly Luo, it is also related to Shouqiu Gong. Shouqiu Gong’s might repelled the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, causing a subtle shift in the overall perception of the Immortals in the Immortal Realm. During the Zhaiyang Epoch, the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation raged everywhere, causing countless True Immortals to die. Immortal Emperor Zhaiyang led the Nameless Immortals of all domains in person, but ultimately could only retreat again and again. At the most difficult time for the Immortal Realm, Shouqiu Gong descended from heaven and, with his own power, repelled the world-destroying tide. This made the Immortals realize that the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation seemed not unstoppable. Moreover, it is said that Shouqiu Gong also left behind multiple inheritances in the Immortal Realm. Anyone who attains the Nameless realm has the opportunity to become Shouqiu’s disciple. Qingyin, you say, when one’s own strength is sufficient, why would they seek help from external things?”

Qingyin remained silent for a long time. After a while, he said in a low voice: “During the Zhaiyang Epoch, all beings were pessimistic and negative, and the Immortal Realm was filled with gloom. Countless True Immortals chose to end their own lives. But in today’s Heavenly Luo Epoch, the situation has completely reversed… However, with all the True Immortals being so confident, I’m afraid it’s not a good thing.”

The voice from the heavens clearly disagreed and chuckled: “Then let us wait and see! I am merely reminding you out of goodwill.” “Of course, if you insist on preserving this Lan Ke Dao Field, it’s not impossible. I can also help a bit. But in the future, you will need to be more discreet, so as not to be discovered by other True Immortals. Heh heh, if something happens later, don’t implicate me. The newly ascended Heavenly Luo Immortal Emperor is not as benevolent as Zhaiyang.”

Qingyin cupped his hands: “Brother Ling, rest assured.”

As if time had frozen at this moment. Light and shadow shifted, and countless years passed. This day, the True Immortal named Ling and Qingyin met again, not through voices from the heavens, but personally arriving at this Lan Ke Dao Field. The recorded light and shadow of the True Immortal named Ling continuously distorted and fluctuated, even affecting Qingyin’s body.

“Damn it, these people in the Immortal Realm are really crazy now. The Heavenly Luo Immortal Emperor is the craziest of them all!” “I feel something is wrong, so I decisively fled first. But I estimate that the lower star sea won’t be safe for long either. My brother and I need to make plans early.”

The True Immortal named Ling paced back and forth, seemingly very anxious. Qingyin, as always, was calm. But compared to the previous recorded light and shadow, his body exuded a more mysterious and transcendent aura, becoming more and more similar to Shouqiu Gong. “I am Shouqiu Gong’s disciple and have received his inheritance. I cannot lightly leave.” “However, I have a premonition that Shouqiu Gong, he might have already left this world. I might be able to follow his footsteps and pursue him.”

The True Immortal named Ling looked sideways, staring intently at Qingyin, and was shocked: “Are you saying… that rumor is true?” He became even more anxious, his steps quickening, murmuring: “Crossing the sea by boat, going to another possible world. Ultimately roaming the Infinite Mortal World, achieving complete and utter transcendence and freedom. The sea may perish, but I remain. The mountain may collapse, but I remain at the summit…” “Qingyin, you must take me with you!”

Qingyin said calmly: “You and I have been sworn brothers since we were insignificant. If I can achieve [Minor Transcendence], how could I not take you with me? However, I have Shouqiu’s inheritance. If I wish to leave, I must first give Shouqiu Gong an explanation.”

“An explanation?” Ling seemed puzzled. “Shouqiu Gong imparted the pháp môn, asking us to leave behind ethereal projections to carry the Dao and resist the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. In the past, doing so was acceptable. But time has passed, and things are different now. The surging tide of Dao Annihilation is several times fiercer than in the previous epoch. Shouqiu Gong, with his profound attainment, might be able to resist with his ethereal projections. But for us juniors…” “It’s all in vain. It could even harm ourselves by being caught in the tide of Dao Annihilation. Even if some are willing to sacrifice themselves to condense projections, it would be like a drop in the ocean for the current Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.”

The True Immortal named Ling nodded in agreement: “The Heavenly Luo Immortal Emperor has gone mad. He’s doing it on the principle of ‘success or death.’ And yet, he can still attract a large group of people to go mad with him. Alas, it’s all Shouqiu Gong’s fault for giving them illusions!”

Qingyin remained noncommittal, not mentioning Shouqiu Gong. He continued to speak of his own predicament: “The matter of condensing projections, although I am unwilling, my duty remains. It’s not something that can be dismissed just by saying no.” “Although Shouqiu Gong has departed, the restrictions he left behind are still something we cannot ignore.” “This is the price of accepting Shouqiu Gong’s inheritance. When Shouqiu Gong imparted the technique back then, he actually made it very clear to me. But the pháp môn of transcendence was too tempting. And at that time, the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation seemed to have been completely suppressed, hence I readily agreed.” Qingyin seemed quite helpless.

“Heh, truly times have changed.” The True Immortal named Ling merely commented casually, then began to think seriously. “Still need to fulfill the duty of carrying the Dao… Let me think.” After a long while, he suddenly clapped his hands: “I have a plan!”

At this critical juncture, light and sound suddenly dimmed together. Li Biren’s vision froze again for a moment. After continuing to play, the final recorded image was shown. Qingyin himself and his condensed Dao-carrying ethereal projection stood facing each other. The True Immortal named Ling said with a look of triumph: “Qingyin, how is my plan of ‘substituting the peach with the plum’? Since we cannot bear the real Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, let’s first create a miniature version that your strength can withstand. The current situation is already riddled with holes; one more or less won’t matter!” “Seal that hole, and you will have given Shouqiu Gong an explanation, by leaving behind ethereal projections to carry the Dao!”

Qingyin silently looked at his own ethereal projection before him and sighed: “Countless lives in two star domains have died because of you and me… It truly was not my intention.”

“Why bother with so much! If they didn’t run, they would have died sooner or later anyway. By fulfilling you and me to achieve minor transcendence, it’s also doing something useful before death!” The True Immortal named Ling said dismissively.

Qingyin nodded silently. He gently pointed at the Dao-carrying ethereal projection before him, and the ethereal projection immediately broke through the void, disappearing without a trace. Qingyin was momentarily lost in thought. Shortly after, he looked up towards a certain direction and spoke again, his tone filled with a hint of joy: “With all fetters severed, I can depart.” For some reason, Qingyin inexplicably glanced towards Li Biren’s probing direction for the last time. After completing this gaze across time and space, the recorded figure completely dissipated.

…

After a long time, Li Biren finally came back to his senses. The recorded footage left in the experimental site, the conversation between the two presumably Nameless True Immortals, contained too much implicit information. “Epoch. Immortal Emperor Zhaiyang, Immortal Emperor Heavenly Luo.” Li Biren had not expected that the epochs of the Immortal Realm were not of fixed duration, but were determined by the reign of the acting Immortal Emperor. “Seven million years is not a long life. True Immortals are indeed not the same species as mortals.” “And that Shouqiu Immortal, or Shouqiu Gong, actually lived for over a hundred and twenty-three epochs…” A rough calculation yielded a staggering number.

“Also, the True Immortal Ling mentioned that lifespans are equal to Dao, but later said that a lifespan of millions of years is already very long. What is going on? Could it be that the Great Daos in heaven and earth only have a lifespan of millions of years? How is that possible?” Li Fan, whose divine sense now illuminated the Dao Net, had never perceived any lifespan limit for the Great Daos of heaven and earth. “The records in the experimental site should not fabricate falsehoods in this regard.” “Unless…” Li Fan’s heart suddenly moved. He thought of his previous speculation that the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation and the Infinite Sea originated from the same source. “The Tribulation of Dao Annihilation destroys the Dao, and the surviving Daos gradually shed their inherent restrictions.” “The Great Daos of heaven and earth, under the baptism of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, have changed and become stronger than in ancient times?” Li Fan could not be sure. Or perhaps, the rise and fall of Dao was an inherent attribute of Dao itself. But no matter what, the limit of millions of years for True Immortals, and even Nameless True Immortals, was somewhat disappointing to Li Fan. It was still far from his ultimate goal of true immortality, which he had imagined before he officially began cultivating. “However, Shouqiu Gong, who lived through a hundred calamities and over a hundred Immortal Emperors without perishing, is already close to the ultimate goal I desire.”

Chapter 1469: The Fox Borrows the Tiger's Might

Shouqiu Gong's power inspired yearning. However, Li Fan was not overly concerned about the restrictions that came with receiving Shouqiu Gong’s inheritance, as mentioned by Qingyin. Firstly, although Shouqiu Gong was implicitly the strongest known existence, Li Fan still didn't believe he surpassed "Return to Truth." Secondly, it was Li Biren, the clone puppet, who obtained and cultivated [Shouqiu’s Wandering Notes]. If necessary, he could be sacrificed to settle the debt. It had nothing to do with Li Fan himself.

"There are still some doubts in the video left by Qingyin."

"For example, why did Qingyin specifically leave this recording in the experimental site? His final glance towards the viewer was clearly intentional."

"Sun Piaomiao, and that True Immortal who was responsible for guarding the Xuanhuang Realm back then, still do not fully understand the specific relationship with this so-called [Lan Ke Dao Field]..."

Too many secrets were lost forever due to the descent of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation and the destruction of the Immortal Realm. Li Fan did not intend to delve into everything. "Although I cannot fully uncover the secrets of the high wall, having obtained Shouqiu Gong's inheritance and Qingyin's recognition, my 'access rights' within this experimental site are much higher than a mere tourist."

Qingyin's projection dissipated, and Li Biren stood again in the circular hall, quietly comprehending. The various objects that had previously ignored him now seemed to be somewhat touchable and manipulable. Besides the humanoid statue that called up the historical records of the experimental site, the object that resonated most strongly with him was a dark red wooden armchair.

Li Biren gently stroked it, feeling the faint aura of Shouqiu Immortal’s ethereal projection. "It seems Shouqiu Gong once sat in this chair."

Li Biren also tried sitting in it. Boom! The scene and vision suddenly changed. As if leaving the core circular hall of the experimental site, it floated out of the countless monitored block star seas. Ascending upwards, it arrived outside the experimental site!

Li Biren saw a familiar starscape. It was the narrow Annihilation Land outside the Shining Star Sea. He could even vaguely glimpse the prosperous starlight within the Shining Star Sea from afar! Zooming in, he could focus on a single point and observe in detail the World-Crossing Profound Coffin still hovering in the starscape, as well as the newly recruited Immortal Hunters asleep in the Land of Bliss!

Because he had previously carefully observed the World-Crossing Profound Coffin from his own perspective, this time, when inspecting it from another angle, Li Biren instantly noticed a difference between the two situations. The first sensation was one of awkwardness and regret, as if a flawless creation had gained a flaw!

“This is the scar I inflicted on the World-Crossing Profound Coffin using the [True Form is False] divine ability. I myself could not clearly see it, yet from this perspective, this imperfection is clearly visible…”

Forcing down the discomfort, Li Biren continued to examine the Profound Coffin. The surrounding starscape and the Great Daos of heaven and earth seemed to turn into undulating waves. And in this vast ocean, the World-Crossing Profound Coffin was like a small boat. Although it could not avoid being tossed about by the storms, it could still calmly weather endless storms and waves. If not for that scar.

"With this scar I caused, it’s like a crack in the hull of the ship."

"Seawater seeps in through the cracks. If you still want to cross the sea with it, the final outcome will inevitably be sinking to the bottom of the sea."

His gaze seemed to jump across the river of time, seeing the future. This was not based on deduction, but a scene that directly appeared before Li Biren's eyes.

“This… is what truly powerful beings see on a daily basis?”

Li Biren now understood. What he was seeing should be from the perspective of the "high wall" itself. Even with other True Immortals’ restrictions and formations, the core foundation of the high wall was still the five Dao-carrying ethereal projections left by Shouqiu Gong. By borrowing the power of these five ethereal projections through the implicit connection with the wooden chair Shouqiu Gong once sat in, it was possible to a certain extent. It could resist the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation and shield the gaze of the Nameless.

The value of the ethereal projections left by Shouqiu Gong needed no further explanation. With their power, Li Biren could not only see the imperfection of the Xuan Coffin at a glance but also vaguely discern the principle by which the Xuan Coffin could traverse the world. Just as Li Fan had previously speculated.

The boat, which seemed capable of traversing the endless ocean, was not particularly outstanding in its material. But it seemed to be composed of countless overlapping shadows. Each additional layer of overlap increased its stability. With layer upon layer added, it could better ignore the winds and waves.

“This… should be the same principle as Black Heavenly Physician and Evil Su Bai hunting their alternate selves, right?”

Li Biren somewhat obsessively watched the overlapping shadows on the Profound Coffin, his gaze seeming to follow them, looking towards other possibilities. But precisely because he had caused that scar before, the current Profound Coffin was deviating from these overlapping shadows. Initially, there was only a negligible deviation. But Li Biren saw that as it swayed with the external storms, the difference was constantly increasing with the passage of time! His probing gaze was also distorted and obstructed, making it impossible to truly see into other possibilities. Not even a shred of light and shadow.

Li Biren secretly lamented. “If the World-Crossing Profound Coffin were intact, perhaps we could truly see the path to other possibilities?”

Compared to the Profound Coffin itself, the method used to seal it seemed crude in contrast. Like rough ropes tied haphazardly on a flawless white wall. It was indeed sturdy. But with the help of the high wall, or rather, the gazes of Shouqiu Gong’s Dao-carrying ethereal projections, Li Biren could easily see the key to unlocking these knots.

“So, at Shouqiu Gong’s level, they have attained universal understanding. No matter what divine abilities or techniques you use, from a superior position, I can see through them at a glance.”

Li Biren was captivated for a moment, then a thought suddenly arose in his mind. “I wonder if, besides ‘seeing,’ one can also borrow more power from Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projections?”

Once the idea arose, it could no longer be suppressed. He strained his mind, recalling the contents of [Shouqiu’s Wandering Notes] left behind, sensing the aura of Shouqiu Gong left on the Grand Tutor chair. It was as if he saw again the lonely figure of Shouqiu guarding the sea and standing eternally alone. In that instant, Li Biren seemed to return to the core of the high wall, to the place where the five ethereal figures were located! Standing amidst the ethereal figures, being collectively observed. Li Biren felt immense pressure. This time, it was not about receiving an inheritance, so the ethereal figures seemed to have no active defenses, as if directly facing the mountain and the sea, and Shouqiu Gong on the mountain and sea. Li Biren felt as if his body were being pressed into the Grand Tutor chair beneath him. Not just physically, but also mentally.

敏锐ly sensing that Shouqiu Gong’s five surrounding ethereal figures seemed to be drawing closer to him, Li Biren decisively sprang up from the Grand Tutor chair. Like falling from the clouds to the mortal world, his boundless vision was compressed back into a small space. Li Biren felt a moment of discomfort. Fortunately, his subjective will was weak, and he quickly readjusted.

“Indeed, the power of the ethereal projections can be borrowed.”

“However, the ethereal projections are primarily for bearing the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, and not much power can be borrowed. Moreover, it is a double-edged sword.”

“The gap between it and Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projections is too vast. Even if Shouqiu Gong has no ill intentions, rashly using it would inevitably lead to assimilation.”

This was the conclusion Li Biren reached after analysis.

Meanwhile, in Li Fan’s main body, the joy far surpassed Li Biren’s. “After escaping the Utmost Darkness Star Sea and encountering beings like Dao Net, Immortal Hunters, and Nameless True Immortals, I have always been treading carefully, constantly guarding against these powerful beings finding their way to the Xuanhuang Realm through connections.”

“But now…”

Li Fan’s main body suddenly stood up, looking in the direction of the high wall, overjoyed. Just now, he did not detect the assimilation trend that Li Biren perceived on his main body. This meant that even if using Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projections had negative consequences, it would not affect him.

“Shouqiu Gong could single-handedly resist the monstrous Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. Even the Immortal Emperor of the Immortal Realm bowed to him as a junior…”

“The more power from his ethereal projections I can borrow, the stronger I become.”

“In other words, in the vicinity of this high wall, even if a Nameless True Immortal were to appear, I would not fear him!”

Li Fan had not felt this excited in a long time. With "Return to Truth," all treasures in the world seemed to have lost their great value to him. Theoretically, as long as he wished, no matter how precious or rare an item, he could turn it into an infinite amount. But Shouqiu Gong's ethereal projections were not precious due to their quantity, but because their very existence was their greatest value, similar to "Return to Truth!" It was like finding a heaven-defying item in a game. Li Fan couldn't wait to try it out.

His gaze turned to the Profound Coffin floating quietly outside the high wall. “You two have rested long enough.”

“It’s time to put you to work and test the quality of Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projections!”

Borrowing Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projections indeed carried immense negative consequences, and even excessive use could precipitate the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. However, these were no longer within Li Fan’s considerations!

Li Biren, having received Li Fan’s command, rested briefly before sitting back on the Grand Tutor chair. At the same time, "Ma Tiande," who had been slumbering in the Annihilation Land starscape, suddenly opened his eyes. Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection’s vision and the sight of this body slowly merged.

The World-Crossing Profound Coffin, which was originally impenetrable and could not be opened, now felt as if it could be instantly broken. Ma Tiande revealed a meaningful smile and lightly flicked his finger towards the "knot" in his field of vision. The knot, entangled in myriad strands, was thus easily untied. With a muffled roar, the coffin lid also shifted open. Qian Ruochang and the Nameless Immortal within the coffin were clearly stunned by this sudden change. Without any hesitation, they unleashed their full potential, attempting to escape the coffin.

The moment they leaped out of the World-Crossing Profound Coffin, Li Fan also clearly saw their true appearances. First, Qian Ruochang. In normal vision, he was a burly, muscular man, holding a giant pillar, strong and fierce. But from Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection’s perspective, Qian Ruochang was not even considered "human." He was a mass of qi. Or perhaps, a polymer of Dao. Just like the silver bones that Li Fan had spied upon earlier, which were very similar to the Dao Net, Qian Ruochang's entire body was directly formed by aggregated and manifested Dao threads. Only the core within the body manipulating Qian Ruochang’s form was a normal human soul. It was like a miniature Dao Net overlaid on the outside of a human soul.

“No wonder Qian Ruochang felt strange to me.”

“What is this? Dao Incarnation? Or a Dao Net mech?”

This method of Qian Ruochang could indeed allow a mortal body to exert the power of the Great Dao. Under the Nameless realm, even True Immortals would be hard-pressed to defeat him. But the drawbacks were also extremely obvious. Without connecting to the Infinite Sea, or even truly connecting to the Great Daos of heaven and earth, every bit of power consumed could not be replenished. Even if the miniature Dao Net possessed infinite power, it could not last forever. More importantly, the soul wrapped by the miniature Dao Net was constantly being squeezed by the Dao strings, as if being sliced by a thousand blades. The level of pain was unimaginable. This was not something that could be endured simply by having a strong will. Under such pressure, the soul was destined to be shattered into countless fragments. A powerful soul and strong will only served to slow down the process.

“Even with divine abilities like my Infinite Cyclic Void, it would be useless.”

“Based on Qian Ruochang’s current soul strength, he could only last for about three hundred years at most.”

“For mortals, this is considered a long life. But for the True Immortal realm, it is too short.”
