Li Fan looked at the Nameless Immortal. He was known for severing all connections with the world. But from Li Fan's current perspective, this was far from the truth. If everyone in the world was a projection of the Great Dao of heaven and earth from a certain angle, rich and three-dimensional, then this Nameless Immortal had, as much as possible, pared himself down to a "thin bamboo pole," minimizing his interaction with the Great Dao. Admittedly, he seemed to have severed ties with all things in the world. But in essence, it had nothing to do with "nothingness." It was somewhat close to the Dao of "solitude" and "loneliness."

“The culmination of this Immortal’s cultivation is not the profound and mysterious Dao of Nothingness, but rather transforming oneself into a law of the world, becoming a part of the Great Dao of heaven and earth, yet remaining independent of it.”

“The moment of consummation is the time of minor transcendence.”

“As expected of a True Immortal who has survived to this day!”

Having discerned the true nature of this "Nameless Immortal" at a glance, Li Fan couldn't help but praise him. The benefit of observing from above with Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection's gaze was self-evident. All sorts of demons and monsters would reveal their true forms at a glance. While Li Fan was observing, Qian Ruochang and the Nameless Immortal, as if having already planned it, unleashed their escape techniques and headed in different directions simultaneously.

Li Fan increased the power of his borrowed ethereal projection and glanced again. The undulating Great Daos in this region of the annihilation land were instantly frozen. Qian Ruochang and the Nameless Immortal, like insects trapped in a net, were immobilized!

Chapter 1470: The Strongest Three True Immortals

Whether it was True Immortals or Qian Ruochang’s Dao Net outer form. They were all essentially relying on the power of [Dao].

At this moment, facing Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection, whose understanding of [Dao] far surpassed theirs, all divine abilities and methods became useless.

In Li Fan’s sight, the Dao principles in this annihilation land’s starscape, which were not very dense, were instantly attracted by Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection. Like a massive vortex suddenly appearing in the ocean, it claimed absolute priority.

Qian Ruochang and the Nameless Immortal were inevitably affected. For now, they could only uncontrollably struggle. If they remained in this distorted vortex of Dao for too long, they risked “losing their Dao”!

Watching the two Immortals struggling helplessly, Li Fan's heart surged with emotion. “Perhaps this is also due to the fragility of this starscape, having suffered the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. But the main reason is that Shouqiu Gong’s true strength has reached an unfathomable level. Thus, even borrowing a small portion of the power from his five ethereal projections was enough to instantly suppress two True Immortals!”

While Li Fan was contemplating, Qian Ruochang and the Nameless Immortal, who were restrained, were already sweating profusely. They considered themselves top-tier experts within their respective factions. Yet, they were so easily manipulated by this mysterious figure!

Both their minds raced, pondering the possible origins of this mysterious figure.

It was at this moment that Li Fan discovered he could vaguely perceive the inner thoughts of these two True Immortal-level beings. Unlike the ambiguous, general emotional trends observed through methods like Heavenly Physician's [Diagnostic Pulse], this was a direct presentation of scenes unfolding in their minds!

Although not every scene was perfectly clear due to the fluctuations of their thoughts, this true ability to “peer into the mind” greatly shocked Li Fan. Keep in mind that the objects of this “mind-peering” were not mere mortals or weaklings, but genuine True Immortals! Moreover, Qian Ruochang and the Nameless Immortal were both approaching the Nameless realm!

“Roughly speaking, before transcending, they are still creations of Dao. Whether it’s their every move or their thoughts, they cannot escape the Great Dao of heaven and earth. The clearer their understanding of Dao, the more clearly they can perceive the changes of living beings within Dao.”

“Their strongest desires trigger the most obvious fluctuations. If a powerful being like Shouqiu Gong were to appear before me, and I instinctively invoked ‘Return to Truth’ to restart, I would likely be discovered instantly, repeating the events with the Heavenly Physician.”

“No wonder, when Black Heavenly Physician had not yet arrived, I still felt an extremely strong premonition. If I hadn’t decisively ‘Return to Truth’ early on, perhaps…”

Feeling a sense of lingering fear, Li Fan did not dwell on the emotion of fear. Instead, he naturally sought ways to avoid being mind-read as his immediate priority.

“Being perceived is due to causing changes in Dao. Like dropping a pebble into calm water, even the slightest disturbance will cause ripples. If one wishes to avoid this…”

With the blessings of Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projections, Li Fan could seek solutions at the fundamental level. He soon discovered the most suitable, almost tailor-made method for him.

“As long as I am alive, fluctuations in my thoughts are unavoidable.”

“Shouqiu Gong watched the sea for a hundred epochs. Even with all my encounters, my understanding of Dao will never surpass his. Beings like Black Heavenly Physician, who can traverse possibilities and devour their alternate selves, are definitely beyond me. To disguise myself before them? Difficult, difficult, difficult…”

“The only feasible method is to conceal the fluctuations caused by my divine sense within the macrocosm. The ripples caused by a single drop of water falling into a pond are very noticeable. But in the vast ocean, spontaneous fluctuations, not caused by external factors, are almost impossible to detect.”

“Transforming the mind into divinity, projecting the Dao Net!” A sharp light flashed in Li Fan's eyes. “The more my projected Dao Net resembles the true Great Dao of heaven and earth, the stronger my concealment will be. My current level…”

Ma Tiande cooperated, deliberately indulging in his thoughts. Under the gaze of Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projections, what he thought was captured for the most part.

“It seems that I am still far from being able to conceal my thoughts before transcendent beings,” Li Fan had a very clear understanding of his true strength and did not feel discouraged.

His attention returned to the thoughts of Qian Ruochang and the Nameless Immortal.

Unlike the continuous scenes captured from Li Fan’s mind, the insights gained from these two were intermittent.

Qian Ruochang's mind flashed with the True Immortals he speculated possessed the combat power of Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projections. Their appearances were unknown, their names were only heard through the highest secret lists of the Immortal Hunters. The three figures that Qian Ruochang was most certain of were the ones most clearly observed.

The first was [Good Transformation]. This True Immortal could conceptually twist and transform all harmful actions by the True Immortal forces against the Shining Star Sea into beneficial ones. He was active at the beginning of the struggle between the Immortal Hunters and the True Immortals. The Immortal Hunters repeatedly suffered heavy losses, but from top to bottom, they felt as if they had won a great victory each time, showing no sense of crisis, but becoming even more blindly optimistic. Yet, the reality of the Shining Star Sea grew worse. Ultimately, the Shining Star Sea was reduced to a small patch of territory for survival. It was only at the last moment that someone enlightened them, and they finally realized the truth. The benefits of Good Transformation were not limited to influencing the overall battle. It also manifested in the extreme threat posed by the individual True Immortal [Good Transformation]. After failing to twist the overall situation, the Good Transformation True Immortal once single-handedly charged into the fray, attempting to end the battle alone. Even in front of the crowd of Immortal Hunters, he slaughtered his relatives and friends. Those influenced by the Dao of Good Transformation felt no anger, but instead excitement and praise, as if being killed was a great happiness and liberation. Good Transformation moved as if in an unhindered realm, slaughtering freely. If he hadn't been stopped at the last moment, the Shining Star Sea would have ceased to exist long ago.

Upon reaching this point in his mind-peering, Li Fan couldn't help but frown slightly. “This True Immortal [Good Transformation] is indeed terrifying. Compared to Jiang, the promulgator of ‘All things are like me,’ his ability seems even more domineering. At the very least, if ‘I’ were to slaughter my relatives and friends, I would instinctively stop him. But under the influence of the Dao of Good Transformation, one could probably only laugh and applaud.”

“Every time the Good Transformation True Immortal is involved, Qian Ruochang’s mental fluctuations are so intense. It is evident that this Good Transformation left a significant psychological shadow on the Immortal Hunters.”

“Although Good Transformation is powerful, the Immortal Hunter who intervened twice at the last moment to break the power of Good Transformation seems to be slightly superior. However, it seems as if they were deliberately erased. Every time Qian Ruochang thought of this person, he subconsciously skipped over them, obtaining almost no useful information.”

“Judging by this power, could it be that powerful hand that forged the Dao Net?”

Li Fan continued to observe the next True Immortal. The cultivation of this Immortal was [Chaos]. The strength of most Immortal Hunters relied on the Dao Net to unleash their power, but this True Immortal’s cultivation of the Chaos Dao could disrupt the Great Dao of heaven and earth, restoring it to the primordial darkness before the separation of heaven and earth. Wherever this Immortal went, even if he stood still, the combat power of the Shining Star Sea would be greatly reduced. And perhaps because the Chaos True Immortal caused too much destruction to the starscape when he took action, the True Immortal faction also had reservations. This Chaos True Immortal did not appear many times in person, but each appearance caused great trouble for the Immortal Hunters.

As for the last True Immortal Qian Ruochang’s mind thought of… “Is it said to be the one who forged the [Reverse Flow Boat]?” Li Fan’s heart trembled slightly. The Reverse Flow Boat was a creation superior to the World-Crossing Profound Coffin among the three methods of escaping the world. It could traverse the river of time and return to the past. Regarding this True Immortal, Qian Ruochang’s thoughts were also very few. Many of his considerations were fleeting glimpses. Li Fan, in the moment of capturing these thoughts, instinctively had Li Biren increase the power of borrowing from the ethereal projections. In just an instant, he was able to see more. The True Immortal who forged the Reverse Flow Boat, internally referred to as [Reverse] by the Immortal Hunters. After the Reverse Flow Boat was forged, did [Reverse] indeed board the divine boat and travel to the past? This became a mystery with the complete disappearance of that group of True Immortals. But judging from various clues accumulated by generations of Immortal Hunters, this True Immortal who seemed to have mastered the power of reversing time might still be alive. Because as the Dao Net grew stronger and the Immortal Hunters counterattacked, the True Immortal faction gradually fell into disadvantage. However, each time the True Immortals were in a desperate situation, they would miraculously resolve the crisis. Excluding the possibility of an inside traitor, and based on other important evidence, the Immortal Hunters had basically concluded that this [Reverse] Immortal existed.

… “Reverse.” If Li Fan, who had mastered "Return to Truth," still had any interest in any Great Dao principles in the world, it would undoubtedly be this power of reversing time. What was the specific difference between it and the "True Form is False" of "Return to Truth"? More importantly, if Li Fan mastered it, could he return to and anchor himself one year in the past? Unfortunately, this [Reverse] was truly mysterious. Even among the Immortal Hunters, they could only infer its existence from various clues. As for anything else, they knew nothing.

Compared to Qian Ruochang’s various speculations, the Nameless Immortal’s mind was much simpler. All his thoughts pointed to one possibility. [Dao Inscribing Immortal]! Judging from the scenes flashing in the Nameless Immortal’s mind, he had seen the original [Dao Book] left by the Dao Inscribing Immortal when he was still in the Immortal Realm. Therefore, he could clearly recognize the power of the Dao Inscribing Immortal. Thus, after his cultivation reached fruition, when he was easily suppressed like a plaything, his first reaction was that the other party was the Dao Inscribing Immortal.

“The Nameless Immortal also heard rumors that the Dao Inscribing Immortal had died.”

“However, he had always dismissed them.”

“Interestingly, the Nameless Immortal had also heard of Shouqiu Gong’s reputation. As for why he didn’t guess it was Shouqiu Gong…”

“Even though Shouqiu Gong’s power is supreme, he would not do such cruel things to the weak.”

Li Fan couldn't help but shake his head slightly. Peeking into the minds of True Immortals allowed Li Fan to experience the feeling of the world’s strongest beings. But it was not without side effects. Li Biren's body gradually exuded a dense ancient aura of weathering the mountain and sea. Moreover, countless block experimental spaces, including the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, emitted faint rumblings, as if signaling the imminent arrival of a great tide.

With the ubiquitous perception of the Unbounded Dreamland, Li Fan further sensed that a wisp of Dao Annihilation black energy inexplicably generated in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

“Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projections are like a great dike holding back the flood. Now that I’ve used only a portion of it, the endless flood is inevitably seeping through.” Li Fan had anticipated this, but he hadn't expected the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation to arrive so quickly.

With a thought, Li Biren sprang from the Grand Tutor chair. His body trembled uncontrollably, attempting to break free from the aura of mountain and sea, to minimize the impact of Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projections.

And without the deterrence of Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projections, Qian Ruochang and the Nameless Immortal could now move. However, they did not leave immediately. Looking at Ma Tiande's smiling expression, they instinctively felt cautious. After hesitating for a moment, they both bowed in unison. They believed that the powerful being who could suppress them in an instant would not toy with them without reason.

At the same time, Qian Ruochang looked at the “newly ascended Immortal Boat” before him, a hint of strangeness flashing in his eyes. “Presumably, the body has been taken over and controlled.”

“Does this World-Crossing Profound Coffin truly cross worlds?” Li Fan, manipulating Ma Tiande’s body, skipped the pleasantries and directly asked.

Qian Ruochang and the Nameless Immortal were slightly stunned.

“It can indeed cross worlds,” Qian Ruochang quickly replied with certainty.

The Nameless Immortal added: “It is said that this coffin was forged from the remains of a transcendent expert, hence it can traverse the Infinite Sea and reach the other shore. This is why I risked danger and dashed into it at the last moment.”

“I didn’t expect to fall into the trap.”

Qian Ruochang sneered: “It can’t really be called a trap. If you hadn’t appeared, I would have truly crossed worlds.”

Li Fan remained noncommittal towards their bickering. Even without mind-peering, he could sense some sense of loss in the Nameless Immortal’s heart. It was likely because, through some method, he had determined that the "senior" Li Fan was portraying was not the Dao Inscribing Immortal.

Ignoring their petty thoughts, Li Fan simply imitated Shouqiu Gong’s posture, standing with his hands behind his back, and sighed. “With the great calamity upon us, where is truly safe?”

“Crossing worlds, crossing worlds, is merely deceiving oneself, moving from one shallow depression to another.”

Qian Ruochang and the Nameless Immortal seemed unsurprised by Li Fan’s words.

“We will find the true other shore.” The Nameless Immortal’s tone was inexplicable.

“Yes. Unfortunately, with only seven million years left, it may not be enough,” Li Fan added the same sentiment.

Once again, Li Biren borrowed the power of Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projections. With a gentle wave of his hand, he collected the World-Crossing Profound Coffin. Facing Li Fan’s blatant plundering, Qian Ruochang and the other two did not dare to show any unusual expression.

From their words, Li Fan guessed that perhaps regarding the great calamity in the mortal world, the Shining Star Sea and the True Immortals knew more. But they might not know the specific deadline for the mortal world. As expected, the mention of seven million years caused undeniable shock in both of them.

Chapter 1471: Passing Down the Marvelous Method on Behalf of the Duke

"The great tide surges, the destruction of the world is imminent, and no one can escape.”

“At most, it’s just a difference between dying sooner or later. In a sense, our ending is no different from the True Immortals who died tragically in the past." Li Fan, using Ma Tiande's body, let out a strange, chilling laugh.

He then scrutinized Qian Ruochang and the Nameless Immortal with extremely peculiar eyes, making them inexplicably uneasy.

“From your memories, I’ve seen brutal conflicts and killings.”

“I thought that by now, with the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation having developed to this extent, those below would have united. I didn't expect…”

“Hahahaha!”

Ma Tiande looked at the Nameless Immortal with extreme indifference.

Even though it was only the gaze of a mortal body, it made the True Immortal’s heart skip a beat.

That expression, which despised all things in heaven and earth, and even billions of True Immortals, was not something that could be faked!

Back when the Heavenly Luo Immortal Emperor inspected the various domains, he had also had the fortune to see him from afar.

Although the Heavenly Luo Immortal Emperor was all smiles, his core remained aloof and arrogant, looking down on all beings.

This was consistent with the subtle demeanor that this mysterious senior unintentionally revealed!

“Watching memories, I…”

Recalling the inadvertently used words in his conversation, the Nameless Immortal’s heart was suddenly filled with a bold guess.

“Not all ruling Immortal Emperors of the Immortal Realm remained on the throne until their deaths.”

“Throughout the long history, there were still one or two who retired early, shedding all their burdens and floating freely in the world. They were called the Hidden Emperors of the Immortal Realm.”

“Could it be…”

As the Nameless Immortal’s thoughts raced, Ma Tiande spoke again: “The True Immortals at the peak of all beings have now degenerated to the point of being hunted like prey.”

“It's truly a disgrace on my part.”

“What use is there in remaining in the world? It’s better to dismantle it to offset the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. Coincidentally, the pillars of this star domain seem to be a bit loose.”

Before he finished speaking, the power from Shouqiu Immortal's ethereal projection descended again.

The Nameless Immortal’s face instantly turned pale.

He felt a pair of invisible giant hands fiercely grasping his cultivated Dao path,

and at the same time, they were fiercely tearing at it.

Originally, by cultivating the Dao of ‘Isolation,’ he had already achieved a great degree of separation from other Dao paths in heaven and earth. But now, under the effect of these invisible giant hands, he actually had the tendency to be forced back!

To him, the Great Dao of heaven and earth was like a spiderweb. It had taken him thirty thousand years to painstakingly sever the connection and escape. Now, he was to return to the starting point in an instant!

Even if his understanding of the Dao of Isolation remained, it would still take at least a thousand years of re-organization to escape from the entanglement of the Dao web again.

What even more terrified the Nameless Immortal was Ma Tiande’s remark, “It’s better to dismantle it to offset the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.”

Although he had not yet attained the Nameless realm, due to the uniqueness of his cultivated Dao path, he was like a pillar of isolation. Theoretically, he could indeed be used as a foundation to resist the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.

And judging from his current experience, this “Hidden Immortal Emperor” in front of him did not seem to be joking!

Feeling his body becoming heavier and heavier as he returned to heaven and earth, the Nameless Immortal could no longer maintain his composure and cried out in terror: “Your Majesty, spare my life! Your Majesty, spare my life!”

Hearing this, Qian Ruochang’s expression changed. All his previous speculations were overturned, and his suspicion towards the mysterious figure before him deepened.

“I have long since ceased to concern myself with worldly affairs.”

“This title of ‘Your Majesty’ is too much to bear. I cannot accept it.”

“The destruction of the Immortal Realm? The ruling Immortal Emperors bear the primary responsibility. Your Majesty…”

“Hmph!”

The Nameless Immortal’s words seemed to anger the other party even more.

From Qian Ruochang’s perspective, the True Immortal’s body, which was originally unclear and just a blurry silhouette, now began to become gradually clearer from various parts of his body due to the distortion.

However, it was not the color of normal heaven and earth, but a strange black and white shadow.

“Senior, please calm your anger! Even if this crude immortal body dies, it will be useless in resisting the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.”

“The Shining Star Sea captured several Nameless beings, but instead of warding off calamities, they wove the Dao Net to hunt us…” The Nameless Immortal reacted quickly. Before the pressure on him increased further and he could no longer speak, he quickly changed his tune.

Hearing this, the Hidden Immortal Emperor did indeed loosen his grip.

But his words remained indifferent as he reprimanded, “No wonder you are always at a disadvantage. After fighting for so long, you still don’t know the true purpose of the Dao Net. ”

Ma Tiande glanced at Qian Ruochang.

Qian Ruochang felt as if his Dao Net outer form was instantly caught in a storm.

His body, woven from countless Great Daos, actually felt like it was beginning to fragment in a short period of time.

Fortunately, this storm did not last long, and after the Hidden Immortal shifted his gaze away, Qian Ruochang was almost drained.

But fortunately, he survived in the end.

“You can explain to this fool.”

A cold voice came.

Qian Ruochang hesitated for a moment, but after meeting the indifferent gaze, and recalling his powerlessness just now,

his heart skipped a beat. He finally opened his mouth and said, “Hunting True Immortals is to strengthen the Dao Net, not to weave the Dao Net for the sake of hunting Immortals. Do not overestimate yourself and put the cart before the horse!”

“In the past, when the Immortal Realm was destroyed, countless True Immortals fled to the lower realms to find new paths. Among them, some were willing to become pillars to resist calamities, and some chose to protect themselves.”

“And there were those who, despondent, wished to flee and survive.”

“It was they who took the lead, uniting with other Immortals, who proposed the [Three Methods of Seeking Refuge]: the Profound Coffin of World Crossing, the Reverse Flow Divine Ship. And the ultimate method of transcendence…”

“They left cleanly, but left a bigger mess for us descendants!”

Qian Ruochang’s tone carried a hint of resentment.

“Among those who fled, there were not lacking Nameless beings. If they had followed the normal path of transcendence, they would have left behind remains, ethereal projections, precious items, etc., which could barely serve as support. But they did not do so at all.”

“Rather than saying they lacked the ability, it’s more like they were unwilling!”

“This place is merely the remnant starscape they abandoned!”

Qian Ruochang looked at the Nameless Immortal and said coldly.

ωwш ¸¸c○

The Nameless Immortal wanted to retort, opened his mouth, but didn't know what to say.

Because, strictly speaking, he was also among the abandoned.

“We, the abandoned children, naturally have to choose to save ourselves.”

“Fortunately, among the True Immortals of the past, not all of them were heartless and unjust. We joined forces, using Nameless Immortals as bones and True Immortals as strings. We wove this Dao Net, waiting for the day when the heavens fall, to leave a sliver of hope for the living beings in the world!” Qian Ruochang’s tone was proud.

“The idea is good. Unfortunately, the net is still too weak now,” Li Fan suddenly interjected.

This was not an empty statement.

It was based on Shouqiu Gong’s memories, after seeing the “mountain” that guarded the sea for a hundred epochs, he was giving his honest assessment of the “net” woven by the mortals of the Shining Star Sea.

If the Dao Net of the Shining Star Sea had spread near the high wall, Li Fan could have completely used Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection to tear open a large hole in it.

Even, if the Dao Net’s power had gotten closer, he could have dismantled the core pillars of the several Nameless True Immortals within the Dao Net and used them as pillars within the high wall. It was not impossible.

In fact, Li Fan was somewhat tempted.

If there were other Nameless True Immortals to act as pillars to resist the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, he would undoubtedly be able to utilize more of Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection’s power.

Li Qianlong did not dare to refute Li Fan’s “belittlement.”

He could only say somberly: “Although it cannot withstand the tides of ten thousand lifetimes, it can barely provide a place for survival.”

“It’s better than doing nothing.”

Li Fan said this not out of anger, but with a hint of admiration: “If the Immortal Realm were still here, it would be acceptable to allocate some resources to you to strengthen the Dao Net.”

“Your method, although a bit crude, can make waste useful.”

He had just peeked into the Nameless Immortal’s mind again, seeing his speculation about his ‘Hidden Emperor’ identity.

Therefore, he continued to play the part.

In simple words, he treated True Immortals as ants.

This made Qian Ruochang and the Nameless Immortal even more terrified.

If it were mere arrogant words, it would not have terrified them so much. But combined with the strength to manipulate them like toys with a flick of his hand…

It undoubtedly proved that this senior was not exaggerating.

“I remember there was a Hidden Emperor who seemed to be just as unpredictable and tyrannical.”

“After he inexplicably retired, all the Immortal Domains wildly celebrated.”

Before the Nameless Immortal could think further, Li Fan turned around and asked, “I remember that before Shouqiu Gong departed, he passed down the method of [Ethereal Projection Carrying Dao] to the world.”

“It’s a pity that this method is only suitable for the Nameless realm. And not all Nameless True Immortals can successfully leave behind an ethereal projection for inheritance. This Dao Net is indeed more effective than Shouqiu Gong’s method.”

Hearing the Hidden Immortal Emperor mention Shouqiu Gong, Qian Ruochang did not react much.

The Nameless Immortal’s heart, however, trembled.

Because he felt that the Hidden Immortal Emperor’s gaze, which was both near and far, was once again falling upon him.

“Perhaps, the two can be combined.”

“Only those who are Nameless can carry the Dao. This is because ordinary True Immortals lack sufficient comprehension of the Dao. And among the Immortals, few share their enlightenment with each other. But now, there is something called the [Dao Net] in the world. Interesting…”

“Have you heard of the method of [Ethereal Projection Carrying Dao]?”

The Nameless Immortal’s body trembled slightly, and he repeatedly shook his head: “I have heard of it. But my talent is dull, and I am destined to be without the inheritance of Shouqiu Gong.”

“Watch closely!”

Within the high wall, Li Biren’s body suddenly erupted with countless cracks.

These were signs of the Immortal Realm fragments being crushed by an immeasurable, enormous pressure.

And Li Biren’s appearance became even more similar to Shouqiu Gong.

Facing such a perilous situation, Li Biren showed no fear. Just like Shouqiu Gong facing the great tide of Dao Annihilation.

He took out one of the Immortal Realm chess pieces remaining in the ethereal space and used it to mend his shattering body.

At the same time, he poured all the inheritance of [Shouqiu’s Wandering Notes] that he had received into the Nameless Immortal’s body.

Although not personally passed down by Shouqiu’s ethereal projection.

Shouqiu Gong’s insights were vast and boundless. Even after being diluted by Li Fan, they were still like a vast ocean that ordinary True Immortals could not fathom.

Moreover, Li Biren’s Mind Manifestation of Divinity and Dao Net Projection's acceptance ability was not much weaker than the Nameless realm.

Coupled with the fact that the inheritance utilized the power of Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection.

Even though what the Nameless Immortal comprehended was incomplete, he would only think it was due to his own lack of ability, not that the inheritance itself had problems.

Judging by the Nameless Immortal’s current entranced and deeply shocked expression, it was clear.

Chapter 1472: Compassion Against Dao Annihilation

The Nameless Immortal’s strength was indeed worthy of being a powerhouse among the surviving True Immortals of the Shining Star Sea. He accepted Shouqiu Gong’s [Ethereal Projection Carrying Dao] method much more smoothly than Li Biren.

He did not experience much substantial impact, and most of the time, an expression of obsession and enjoyment was revealed.

Compared to Li Biren's makeshift, half-baked True Immortal, the inheritance of [Shouqiu’s Wandering Notes] was clearly more suitable for a true Immortal.

In Qian Ruochang’s eyes, the aura emanating from the Nameless Immortal became more ethereal and unpredictable at a speed visible to the naked eye.

It seemed that his strength had achieved a qualitative breakthrough in this short period.

This made Qian Ruochang secretly shocked, and at the same time, he couldn't help but feel envious.

After an unknown amount of time, the Nameless Immortal finally emerged from Shouqiu Gong’s vast and profound thoughts.

“Thank you, Senior, for the grace of imparting the technique,” he said earnestly.

This statement was sincere. Shouqiu Gong had disappeared long before the destruction of the Immortal Realm. If not for this Hidden Emperor’s generosity, how would he have had the chance to witness such a wondrous method?

“The concept of the Dao Net is indeed ingenious. Using the Nameless as bones and True Immortals as strings, it can indeed create a net to save the world. It’s a pity that there are too few True Immortals surviving now. You yourselves would not be willing to sacrifice yourselves willingly into the net. ”

“After the conflict, the remaining True Immortals, the number of those who enter the net, may not be enough to support the Dao Net to its expected strength.” Li Fan’s voice echoed quietly in the dead silence of space.

Perhaps because of the recent transfer of techniques, it was slightly different from before.

However, Qian Ruochang did not pay much attention to these details; he was more concerned about what the mysterious senior was saying at the moment.

“This aligns with the hidden worries within the Governing Council. As expected of a senior expert, you saw the fatal flaw of the Dao Net at a glance.” Qian Ruochang was once again filled with awe.

Li Fan continued, “You can pass on this [Shouqiu’s Wandering Notes] for me. Regardless of the past or identity, as long as one is willing to leave behind an ethereal projection, it works. The ability of the ethereal projection to carry Dao is no less than that of the main body. If the True Immortals still surviving in this star sea were to collectively cultivate and leave behind Dao-carrying ethereal projections in the Dao Net…”

“You two do not only have one path of mutual destruction.”

Hearing this, Qian Ruochang finally understood the true meaning of the [Ethereal Projection Carrying Dao] secret technique. The conflict that had lasted for a long time seemed to have finally seen hope of an end. His heart was filled with inexplicable excitement.

As for the Nameless Immortal’s excitement, it surpassed Qian Ruochang’s.

This was not only because he saw the possibility of reconciliation between the two sides, but also because he could personally pass on Shouqiu Gong’s secret technique…

Even though many years had passed, the name Shouqiu Gong still held a weight among the True Immortals of the Immortal Realm that ordinary people could not match.

Especially the Heavenly Luo Immortal Emperor, who had spread his ambitious boasts throughout the Immortal Realm, claiming to thoroughly resolve the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation and simultaneously establish an transcendent [Eternal Immortal Dynasty]. The result, however, turned out to be a cause for the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.

It made the surviving True Immortals of the Immortal Realm miss Shouqiu Gong, who had repelled the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation with his own power.

If Shouqiu Gong were still here, why would the Immortal Realm have been destroyed?

This was a question often brought up by all the Immortal Sects of the Immortal Realm.

And now, he could actually pass on Shouqiu Gong's secret technique…

What an honor this was!

Compared to hiding in the Profound Coffin of World Crossing and fleeing in despair, he clearly preferred to undertake this duty.

Furthermore, with this ethereal projection carrying Dao method, if it could be combined with the Dao Net technique, perhaps it could truly turn the tide and create a salvation boat in the desperate Tribulation of Dao Annihilation!

The Nameless Immortal’s heart trembled, almost unable to resist the urge to immediately travel and promote this matter.

“Since I have already passed on the method, Shouqiu Gong’s entrustment back then has been fulfilled.”

“How you two will proceed next…”

“Hehehe, it doesn't have much to do with me anymore.”

“Let’s leave it at that.”

“You two may withdraw now.”

Just as Qian Ruochang and the Nameless Immortal were deep in thought, Li Fan unceremoniously issued the order to leave.

And this statement made both of them keenly aware of the peculiarity.

“Hidden Emperor Senior has not revealed his true form. Now he is ordering us to leave…”

“Could it be that his true body is hidden here, but due to some reason, he cannot appear in the world?”

The strength displayed by the Hidden Emperor Senior was unfathomable.

And what could restrain him…

In this world, it was probably only the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation!

A thought occurred to both of them simultaneously: “Could it be that this Hidden Emperor Senior is using himself as a pillar to bear the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation?”

This was not a random guess, but there were precedents in history.

However, those Nameless True Immortals who had sacrificed themselves to temporarily block the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation had basically been corroded by it and perished.

Unlike this Hidden Emperor Senior, who could still act to some extent while bearing the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation…

In history, perhaps only Shouqiu Gong could achieve this!

And the words that followed from the Hidden Emperor Senior further confirmed their guess: “Still not leaving? Do you expect me to escort you out?”

“Hehehe, it wouldn't hurt me to stretch my muscles. I’m just afraid that the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation in this star domain will no longer be stoppable!”

The words “Tribulation of Dao Annihilation” caused subtle fluctuations to emanate from the surrounding starscape simultaneously,

causing a sense of dread in their hearts, as if a great disaster was imminent.

This place was originally a survivor site affected by the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, and with the occurrence of these fluctuations, it seemed as if heaven and earth were about to collapse again.

The instinctive warning of danger could not be faked.

Verifying their hypothesis, Qian Ruochang and the Nameless Immortal looked at the Hidden Emperor Senior, who had already departed from “Ma Tiande,” with complex expressions, bowing respectfully in unison.

Then, they both retreated from this starscape.

As for the newly recruited Immortal Hunters who were still slumbering…

The Hidden Emperor Senior had not given any orders, so they dared not ask for them.

Moreover, compared to the gains from this expedition, these juniors were completely unimportant.

“Immortal Hunters…”

“Perhaps their name will change from now on.”

In Qian Ruochang’s mind, a figure of supreme authority flashed.

That person could be said to be the one who personally created the original Dao Net.

Although he seemed to be extremely cruel towards his peers, True Immortals, and even Nameless True Immortals,

Qian Ruochang understood in his heart that he still harbored some affection for the Immortals.

Otherwise, if he had personally intervened, this war would have ended long ago, and the Governing Council would not have accepted the allegiance of those True Immortals who had transcended to mortality.

These people seemed honest, but in reality, they all had ulterior motives and were completely unstable factors.

“Shouqiu Gong. I seem to have heard this name before. I just don’t know who he specifically was.”

“However, if this method of ethereal projection carrying Dao is true… for that person, it would be a great thing.”

In the Nameless Immortal’s mind, various figures who could be allied with flashed incessantly.

The True Immortals, who had been killing each other all along, suddenly turned to cooperate with the Shining Star Sea.

Although this was theoretically the best choice, the hatred of many years could not be cast aside so easily.

To avoid more meaningless deaths, he had to act quickly.

…

With their minds racing, the two left the star domain where the high wall was located.

And Li Fan also withdrew from the thoughts he had been probing.

Using the ethereal power so frequently, Li Biren’s condition was now dire.

He had no choice but to absorb another Immortal Realm chess piece as a supplement.

It was manageable for the clone puppet, but what was worse was the infiltration of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.

Not only in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea where the Xuanhuang Realm was located.

In this experimental field, three out of ten block star seas that had survived and still had vitality had begun to develop black energy of Dao Annihilation.

The fluctuation of the great tide of Dao Annihilation was not something Li Fan had fabricated to scare Qian Ruochang and the others.

This kind of fluctuation, even with the power of Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection, could not be faked.

“If we use it a few more times like this, it might truly lead to a sudden collapse of the world.”

“Unless we can find a Nameless Immortal to share part of the pressure.”

Li Fan thought this way and couldn't help but cast his gaze towards the remaining Immortal Realm chess pieces in the ethereal space.

“When the chess pieces gather, the Immortal Realm appears, and the Southern Immortal Heavenly Pillar emerges.”

“The core of this Heavenly Pillar is the bone of a Nameless True Immortal. At that time, it appeared in the Xuanhuang Realm and caused the world to instantly collapse.”

“But perhaps in Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection space, it cannot be so presumptuous.”

“Bearing the name of Heavenly Pillar, it should also execute the duty of a Heavenly Pillar.”

Li Fan had already made a decision in his heart.

Things always had two sides. As Li Biren frequently used Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection power, his body suffered severe damage from bearing energy far beyond his limits.

However, at the same time, as Li Biren’s appearance became more and more similar to Shouqiu Gong, his manipulation of ethereal power became more and more skillful.

“Living Nameless True Immortals could be suppressed with a single hand, let alone a mere bone.”

Li Fan naturally knew the consequences of playing with a tiger.

Shouqiu Gong was the strongest being he had encountered so far.

Even though he had transcended long ago and gone to other possibilities, just as Black Heavenly Physician and Evil Su Bai could sense their alternate selves in other possibilities, Shouqiu Gong could certainly sense, to some extent, the misuse of the ethereal projection he had left behind.

The reason he was willing to take this risk was because of Shouqiu Gong’s display of “virtue.”

Leaving behind this ethereal power was to help the beings of this world resist the great calamity.

Borrowing and suppressing Nameless True Immortals to increase resistance was also in line with Shouqiu Gong’s original intention.

“Moreover, the Immortal Realm of the Primordial possibility had already been destroyed for tens of thousands of years. If Shouqiu Gong truly cared about this world, he would have returned long ago to check on it.”

“If he has not appeared yet, he would be even less likely to appear due to such a minor disturbance.”

Of course, these “gambles” were not the primary reasons.

Fundamentally, it was because Li Fan possessed the confidence of ‘Return to Truth.’

Even if Shouqiu Gong came from another possibility, Li Fan was confident that he could ‘Return to Truth’ and retreat.

In the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, the faint fluctuations became more frequent.

It was like fierce waves constantly crashing.

A scene of precariousness, as if a great edifice was about to collapse.

“There is no time to delay.”

“If we fail, we can only ‘Return to Truth’.”

“Anyway, we have already gathered enough valuable information,” Li Fan’s eyes flickered.

When Qian Ruochang was finally pushed to his limit, his mind finally showed a flaw.

Li Fan captured the shadowy figure behind the Dao Net.

Although the specific identity was still unknown, a faint shadow was left behind.

If they were to meet again in this star sea, Li Fan would be able to recognize it in an instant.

Of course, this was under the premise of borrowing the power of Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection.

The main body gathered the thirteen Immortal Realm chess pieces, including the Medicine King True Cauldron, which was missing from the Immortal Realm, and sent them into the experimental field’s ethereal space.

At the same time, after leaving behind an item, he quietly departed.

He arrived in the Xuanhuang Realm, ready to activate ‘Return to Truth’ at any moment.

And Li Biren, once again sat on the Grand Tutor’s chair, concentrating his divine sense, watching his body crumble inch by inch.

Only faint starlight, like a net, remained, leaving an empty chair.

This was because he had detached his divine sense projection Dao Net from the Immortal Realm chess pieces and was using it to manipulate the ethereal power.

“The upper limit of controllable power has been sharply reduced again.”

“However, the Immortal Realm’s unfolding is within the ethereal space, which is already sufficient.”

Li Biren had a preliminary judgment.

Without a physical body, only existing as divine sense, it did not have too much of an impact on him.

Instead, without the constraints of a physical body, he vaguely felt that the various Great Daos reflected by his divine sense were even clearer.

A total of thirteen Immortal Realm chess pieces gathered together.

Among them, six had previously merged into a colorful one.

After Li Biren invested them this time, another six merged with each other.

Coupled with the Medicine King True Cauldron, the crucial catalyst…

An Immortal Realm reappeared!

However, compared to the earth-shattering event when it appeared in the Xuanhuang Realm before, in this ethereal space, under the simultaneous gaze of the five Shouqiu Gong ethereal figures.

This unfolding of the Immortal Realm appeared so calm and uneventful.

It did not resemble a corner of the former Immortal Realm, but rather a common mortal cultivation world.

However, when the Southern Immortal Heavenly Pillar appeared in the center of the Immortal Realm, it still caused a slight tremor.

Li Biren even vaguely sensed that Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal figures seemed to have turned their gaze towards it.

The ethereal space was under the suppression of Shouqiu Gong’s power.

The stone tablet could not absorb external objects.

It just stood there quietly.

At this moment, Li Biren threw in the item that the main body had left behind.

One stone stirred a thousand ripples!

The calm stone tablet trembled violently.

Cracks appeared all over it, as if something was about to break free from within!

And what was floating above the stone tablet was Li Fan’s, taken from the ‘Return to Truth’ space,

another nameless True Immortal bone that had followed him in his illicit crossing!

Two identical bones appeared at the same time.

It seemed to have triggered some mysterious and unfathomable change.

Ripples surged through the ethereal space ceaselessly.

Shouqiu Gong’s gaze tilted and concentrated further, the light shifting and changing.

The Immortal Realm stone tablet exploded, and the stable Immortal Realm space instantly became turbulent.

Various lights and shadows twisted and warped.

And in the center of the countless fragments, it was precisely two identical bones, overlapping!

The fusion of Nameless True Immortal bones did not result in only one remaining, like the fusion of two identical rare items.

Instead, it was as if new tissue was growing on the original bone!

Chapter 1473: Primordial Bone Pillar

Just as if the fallen Nameless True Immortal had been reborn from a withered bone.

Light flickered and transformed, and a blurry human figure appeared from the overlapping True Immortal bones.

The Immortal Realm surrounding the figure distorted entirely in its vicinity, as if this Nameless being was repelling all the Great Dao laws that constituted the Immortal Realm.

And Li Fan, borrowing the power of Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection, could vaguely see that the Nameless being was not completely repelling them. After clearly separating itself from the Immortal Realm’s Dao, it was silently transforming everything it came into contact with. And integrating it into itself.

Perhaps "absorbing" is not an appropriate description. "Transforming" is a more fitting term.

The disappearing parts of the Immortal Realm were not absorbed by the Nameless Immortal figure. Instead, under the influence of an unfathomable power, they became beings of nearly the same essence as that figure.

All of this was exactly the same scene as when Li Fan had witnessed the first unfolding of the Immortal Realm and the appearance of the stone tablet without words.

All things return to their origin, returning to the unwritten stone tablet; the evolution of the Dao, tracing back to the origin of the Dao!

At this moment, Li Fan clearly saw the Dao that this Nameless Immortal figure had merged with.

“[Primordial].”

The weight of these two words needs no further explanation.

It could re-establish heaven, earth, fire, and wind, returning a world to its initial state.

The Southern Immortal Heavenly Pillar, originally meant to resist a certain Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, transformed into a vortex source that devoured the Immortal Realm after revealing its true form.

The speed of the Primordial Immortal’s manifestation was faster than Li Fan had anticipated.

What made Li Fan’s heart tighten even more was that as the Primordial Dao in this space increased, the Nameless Immortal’s figure began to blur again, as if it were about to escape this ethereal space at any moment.

Even with Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection’s gaze, it was becoming difficult to grasp the exact location of the [Primordial].

Knowing that delay would lead to complications, Li Fan no longer hesitated.

On the Grand Tutor’s chair, it was as if billions of supernovae erupted simultaneously. Li Biren’s divine sense projection Dao Net instantly turned into a dazzling white light.

And within the ethereal space, a pair of tangible giant hands suddenly descended.

Descending from the ethereal to the real, they fiercely grasped the [Primordial] located in the center of the collapsing Immortal Realm.

The rigidity lasted for only a few breaths before the outcome was quickly decided.

And in this confrontation, Li Fan also glimpsed some of the details of both parties’ powers.

Primordial was the beginning of the Dao. Although sacred and elusive, it was still a manifestation of the Dao’s power.

And the power of Shouqiu Gong seemed closer to [Mountain and Sea]. Even the [Primordial], which held a transcendent position among the Three Thousand Great Daos, had to obediently be bound.

“Even if this skeleton only represents a part of the power of [Primordial], what it resisted was only Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection.”

“The changes observed at this moment are enough to show that Shouqiu Gong’s strength is superior to [Primordial].”

“Shouqiu gazing at the sea…”

Resisting a calamity that could even annihilate the Dao with his own power had clearly surpassed the ability limit of a “cultivator who understands the Dao.”

“The one who guards the sea is only the mountain.”

“But what exactly does this [mountain] refer to?”

The great commotion caused by the Primordial ethereal projection’s descent was suppressed silently.

Under Li Biren’s precise manipulation, it was compressed into a solitary stone pillar along with the remaining Immortal Realm fragments and the unwritten stone tablet.

Then, it was hurled towards the region within the experimental starscape inside the high wall where the black energy of Dao Annihilation appeared most frequently.

The effect was immediate.

The unsettling, hidden fluctuations disappeared instantly, as if they had never existed.

The black energy of Dao Annihilation, which would not disappear inexplicably and only intensified, also began to dissipate like water without a source.

“As expected of [Primordial], occupying an absolutely crucial position among the countless Great Dao laws in heaven and earth. Its effect in supporting the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation is even better than I imagined.”

“No wonder it was chosen as the material to construct the Southern Immortal Heavenly Pillar,” Li Fan observed the [Dao Pillar].

After its initial manifestation, after only a few breaths, it had now, like ice melting into water, merged into the Great Dao of heaven and earth.

Mortal eyes could not see it.

Even Li Fan’s main body could only vaguely perceive that something was wrong with that space, but could not investigate further.

Only by borrowing Shouqiu Gong’s gaze could he thoroughly investigate.

“Besides the Southern Immortal Heavenly Pillar, other Immortal Pillars might also contain Nameless skeletons no less significant than [Primordial].”

“These should be the remnants left behind by True Immortals who transcended in the past.”

Li Fan had uncovered many secrets from Qian Ruochang and the Nameless Immortal’s memories.

When True Immortals transcend and break free from the shackles of the Great Dao of heaven and earth, the Dao they merged with no longer exists in this possibility.

This was also one of the reasons Li Fan had previously speculated about the occurrence of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.

But clearly, these experts who cultivated to the pinnacle of True Immortal were not entirely indifferent to the lives of their fellow beings.

“According to Qian Ruochang, before they transcended and left, they would leave behind remains, ethereal projections, precious items, etc., which would bear part of the responsibility for the thiếu hụt Great Dao.”

“The ones within these Immortal Heavenly Pillars should be the remnants left by True Immortals who transcended in the past.”

“However, compared to Shouqiu Gong’s method of [Ethereal Projection Carrying Dao], this method of leaving behind remains seems…”

Li Fan pondered as he observed the stone pillar, recalling the phenomenon of the Primordial skeleton seeming to have its own consciousness and wanting to ‘Return to Truth’ with him, and the fact that after two identical skeletons overlapped, a 'Primordial' figure manifested.

“Unlike the ethereal projection carrying Dao, which is an existence completely independent of oneself. Even if it can be discarded for a time, but…”

Li Fan pondered thoughtfully: “After transcending the limited possibilities, there is the great transcendence of the ‘unification’ of countless possibilities, which is true transcendence.

“To take this step, one probably still needs to reclaim the things they left behind.”

Li Fan realized this in his heart.

Perhaps this was the reason why some transcendent True Immortals were unwilling to leave behind items to suppress the Dao.

While Li Fan was contemplating, the side effects of using Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection power had been completely eliminated.

The two Primordial bones, serving as Immortal Pillars, had indeed shared some of the pressure of carrying the Dao, just as Li Fan had guessed.

Li Fan vaguely sensed: “If quantified, it is equivalent to about one and one-third of the power of the [Primordial] bone that can be freely utilized by me.”

“We only need to consider the directional changes Li Biren is undergoing, and we don’t have to worry about the sky suddenly collapsing, and the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation descending upon the world.”

“Of course, as time passes, the pressure of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation will only increase, and the power that can be used will gradually decrease.”

However, Li Fan was already very satisfied with the current outcome.

“In other words, if I can capture another Nameless True Immortal to act as an Immortal Pillar, I can then release a portion of the power.”

“Until all of Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection power is unleashed.”

Li Fan was daydreaming when the dire situation of Li Biren’s divine sense projection instantly brought him back to reality.

Continuously using Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection power had inflicted damage on Li Biren far exceeding his limits.

Li Fan focused his divine sense on the Dao Net projection. In a momentary trance, he seemed to see the figure of Shouqiu, with his back turned, gazing at the boundless sea.

After breaking out in a cold sweat for no reason, he finally escaped from the illusion.

“Even if Shouqiu’s ethereal projection has no ill intentions, using it so frequently is like applying immense external force. The clone is uncontrollably undergoing internal deformation.”

“Analogously, when Heavenly Physician Black relied on my clone to descend into the world, it was the same principle.”

Knowing that he could not rush things, Li Fan temporarily ceased the idea of continuously using Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection.

“Unless an uncontrollable situation arises.”

“Now, we must trace the source and restore the clone to its original appearance.”

This was not a difficult task for Li Fan.

With the main body as an anchor, he could compare and gradually strip away the influence brought by Shouqiu Gong, like cutting flesh from bone.

It was simply troublesome and time-consuming.

“After completing the restoration, I still need to find a way to strengthen the clone’s ability to withstand pressure.”

“Otherwise, even with the power of Nameless beings, the time I can utilize is limited.”

Regarding this, Li Fan already had a vague idea.

Shouqiu Gong’s power seemed to originate from the mountains and seas.

Those who can control mountains and seas can only be mountains and seas themselves.

And Li Fan happened to have something associated with the “sea” within him.

“The power of the Demonic Killing Immortal Soul.”

Even though he could freely wield this mysterious power by merging with the Heavenly Dao Immortal Soul, Demonic Killing,

Li Fan had not fully grasped the essence of the “Demonic Killing Immortal Soul” power before.

However, after obtaining Shouqiu Gong’s thousand-epoch insights from gazing at the sea, Li Fan vaguely understood something.

In Li Biren’s divine sense, the Dao Net projection seemed to be roughly torn apart, distorted, and deformed. It was even temporarily disconnected from the connection with the main body.

Li Fan was not in a hurry. He sat steadily in the central command, restoring the Dao Net projection slowly while infusing wisps of Demonic Killing Immortal Soul power into the restored divine sense of the clone.

“Black energy is a precursor to the imminent Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.”

“Like ripples formed by seawater crashing against a mountain.”

“Or perhaps, a phenomenon of the intermingling of mountains and seas,” Li Fan’s eyes gleamed.

As wisps of dark ink were infused, the originally pure and dazzling Dao Net projection seemed to be covered with a dark black border.

Although it still reflected all the Great Daos,

it was somehow different from before.

In Li Fan’s instinctive perception, this projected net had become a bit “sturdier.”

But Li Fan did not rush to experiment.

Instead, he repeatedly sketched, as if constantly outlining with a brush.

In Li Biren’s divine sense, through countless repetitions, the divine sense completely transformed from虚 to实.

His entire body seemed to be formed by the projection of the Dao Net.

And the power of the Demonic Killing Immortal Soul served as the flesh filling it.

A brand new body finally came into being under Li Fan’s meticulous craftsmanship.

Li Biren clenched his fist. Although his body was no longer made of Immortal Realm fragments and seemed weaker in power,

he distinctly felt that he had become more “resistant to blows.”

Looking at the residual black energy of Dao Annihilation in the starscape of the experimental field,

Li Biren’s expression was emotionless. He opened his mouth wide and directly swallowed these dissipating black energy clouds into his abdomen.

The surging black energy, capable of destroying all living things in the world, churned within Li Biren’s stomach.

Li Biren only felt a searing pain.

However, his body itself did not dissipate.

If it were the Immortal Realm fragment body from before, it would not have had such a powerful effect.

“As expected.”

The verification in his heart was confirmed. Li Fan experienced the tumultuous sensation within his clone’s stomach.

“The collision of mountains and seas.”

His thoughts seemed to return to the vast and long twelve epochs recorded in [Shouqiu’s Wandering Notes].

Looking at the vast ocean water incessantly crashing against the mountain below.

Each collision brought about some kind of change in the mortal world.

“It’s a pity. Shouqiu's inheritance was shared by other Immortal Realm chess pieces, otherwise I should have been able to glimpse the true meaning of mountains and seas.” After observing and comprehending for a long time, there was still no result.

Li Fan had to reluctantly withdraw from that mystical state.

Mountains and seas were clearly not things of the mortal world.

Even merely visualizing being there brought about corresponding changes to Li Fan.

The most direct was his lifespan.

After entering the Half-Immortal realm, Li Fan’s lifespan was infinite, equivalent to that of the mortal world, seven million three hundred sixty thousand years.

Although not a fixed number, it would change with Li Fan’s actions, but it was limited below the ten thousand level, in the thousands, hundreds, tens, and units.

However, now, this lifespan had suddenly and drastically decreased.

It was reduced by one-third instantaneously!

Li Fan stared at the number, his expression becoming somewhat subtle.

“Logically speaking, the stronger my strength becomes, the higher the possibility of saving the entire mortal world.”

“Theoretically, this lifespan number should skyrocket.”

“Why did I, after glimpsing the mystery of mountains and seas, have the lifespan of the entire mortal world’s future existence decrease?”

Li Fan was utterly perplexed.

But clearly, this was not a good omen.

Li Fan did not stubbornly continue.

“The secrets of mountains and seas seem to be beyond my reach at the moment.”

“Let’s first perfect the clone’s body and increase its capacity to withstand pressure.”

“If I can fully unleash the power of Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection, it should be enough for me to roam this broken possibility.”

Currently, for Li Fan, the power of the ethereal projection within the experimental field was like a weighing scale. To borrow Shouqiu’s power, he first had to place an equal weight on the other side.

“What I can currently mobilize without pressure is only one and one-third of the [Primordial] bone’s power. The Primordial Dao path, the Immortal of Ten Thousand Daos. Even if it is just a remnant skeleton, it should not be much weaker than an ordinary Nameless True Immortal.”

“If all else fails, I can still unleash more of Shouqiu’s power.”

Li Fan pondered about his next target for hunting.

The number of Nameless True Immortals with known identities was not large.

Li Fan first turned his gaze towards the Immortal Ruins outside the Xuanhuang Realm.

Besides the Hungry Immortal, who was vaguely approaching the Nameless True Immortal realm, there was also the remnant left by the previous Hungry Immortal below her, used to support the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.

Although the Hungry Immortal was being carelessly trampled by Hei Bao, unaware of it herself.

However, with Li Fan’s current strength, planning for her still required careful consideration.

And Li Fan not only wanted to capture True Immortals with current strength.

He even wanted to greedily capture the True [Hungry Immortal] who had attained the Nameless realm.

Chapter 1474: Bullying the Starved Immortal Through Influence

The Starving Immortal had been in seclusion and attained enlightenment within the Immortal Ruins for a long time. Based on her performance after awakening from her previous reincarnation cycle when facing the unfurled Immortal Realm and the voiceless stone tablet, she was not far from reaching the Nameless realm, perhaps just a single step away. Whether she could become a Nameless True Immortal made a colossal difference for Li Fan, akin to the chasm between heaven and earth. "If she doesn't attain the Nameless realm, no matter how close in strength she is, I cannot easily turn her into a pillar to support the Dao. Thus, I cannot free up the power of Shouqiu Gong's ethereal projection." "Perhaps I can help her..." Countless scenes flickered before Li Fan's eyes as he began a rapid deduction. In the past, the Starving Immortal in the Immortal Ruins was a terrifying existence utterly beyond Li Fan's reach. Li Fan still remembered her fearsome power that could destroy the Xuanhuang Realm with a single glance. Even though she was easily captured by Cat Treasure and even severely tormented by Evil Su Bai without her knowledge, the Starving Immortal was still not someone Li Fan, at the Half-Immortal realm, could contend with. But now, after mastering the power of Shouqiu Gong's ethereal projection, she had suddenly become less invincible. "The Xuanhuang Realm is still of great use to me, and it cannot be easily destroyed." "But if she were to attain the Nameless realm, the resulting fluctuations would inevitably destroy everything around it..." After careful consideration, Li Fan had made up his mind. In the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, lights bloomed like scattered stars. Li Biren projected his Dao Net body and returned to the Utmost Darkness Star Sea. Essentially a projection of the Dao Net, it had no physical form. Wherever the Great Dao reached, it could manifest its form, so even while seated on the Grand Tutor's chair and manifesting in the star sea within the high wall, there was no impact. The body formed by the Dao Net projection, hidden in reality, silently merged like snow melting into water. Li Fan's main body rose and gazed across the distance at Li Biren's Dao Net body below the high wall. His own divine sense, through the ubiquitous Unbounded Dreamland Paradise, instantly enveloped the Xuanhuang Realm layer by layer. The main body and the clone, two perfectly identical divine sense Dao Net projections, resonated with each other. The same nodes within the Dao Nets began to naturally fuse together. "Rise!" Endowed with the immense force of Shouqiu's ethereal projection, Li Biren, using the connected Dao Net projections as ropes, let out a low roar and yanked forcefully towards the direction of the Xuanhuang Realm. The Xuanhuang Realm, enveloped by the Dao Net projection, trembled slightly in an instant. Then, inch by inch, it was pulled away from the attraction of the Immortal Ruins! The escape plan from the Immortal Ruins, which the entire Xuanhuang Realm's cultivators had been unable to achieve even with their full strength, was now completed by Li Fan alone. This was the vast difference between a Nameless True Immortal and an ordinary cultivator! At this moment, outside the Xuanhuang Realm, countless Immortal formations emerged. The Xuanhuang Realm seemed to descend into a dense mist, transitioning from solid to ethereal, becoming indistinct. This was a concealment method Li Fan adopted to avoid alarming the Starving Immortal prematurely. As it turned out, the Starving Immortal, engrossed in her enlightenment, cared little about such matters. The departure of the Xuanhuang Realm went completely unnoticed by her. The Dao Net's traction method, while appearing slow, was relative to the size of the Xuanhuang Realm. If converted to a cultivator's flight speed, it was equivalent to traversing ninety-nine Xuanhuang Realms in a single breath. Though slow, it was fast. Soon, without much trouble, the Xuanhuang Realm successfully escaped the Immortal Ruins' suction. All obstacles on its path were disregarded by the power of Shouqiu's ethereal projection, comparable to a Nameless True Immortal. Even the residual black Dao Annihilation energy from the experimental site's spatial tremors was dealt with by Li Fan. The speed of travel through the void increased. Incredibly smoothly, after more than ten days, the Xuanhuang Realm had arrived in a safe starry sky. Apart from the surrounding deathly silence, there were no other flaws. Perhaps sensing the change in its environment, transformations began to occur within the Xuanhuang Realm, such as nascent shoots of the Root of Nothingness and new flows of earth veins, like a dying patient suddenly regaining vitality. The tide had turned, and the situation was now reversed. The fragments of other cultivation worlds, previously implanted by the Heavenly Physician like cancerous growths, now became nourishment for the Xuanhuang Realm's rebirth. The yellow color representing the Xuanhuang Realm's own power sounded the charge of counterattack, rapidly expanding outwards from the core Xuanhuang region. As the actual controller of the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan naturally witnessed all these changes. "Previously, to resist the Immortal Ruins' suction, the Xuanhuang Realm had to constantly divert a portion of its power. Now that it's away from the Immortal Ruins, this power has been liberated." "This is just like how I am now mobilizing Shouqiu's ethereal projection." The rapid resurgence of life within the Xuanhuang Realm was somewhat beyond Li Fan's expectations. He looked at Li Ningqing, also known as Yan Fajue, who was still leisurely traveling through mountains and rivers within the Xuanhuang Realm. Li Fan's granted holiday had long ended, but he hadn't recalled her, as if he had forgotten about it. After working continuously for several thousand years, Li Ningqing clearly hadn't had enough rest. She pretended to have forgotten and didn't return to Li Fan on time. Initially, she was very anxious, but seeing that so much time had passed without any reaction from Li Fan, her worries gradually faded. Spending her days in leisure, exploring various secret realms within Xuanhuang, was incredibly enjoyable. As a creation of the former Immortal Realm, relying on her keen spiritual sense, she had indeed discovered several hidden places overlooked by Li Fan. However, they were mostly abandoned or damaged, with little value. Therefore, Li Fan continued to indulge her, planning to settle accounts with her after thoroughly investigating the Xuanhuang Realm's situation. "If I didn't have Shouqiu's ethereal projection power, which I can manipulate with such fine detail, I wouldn't have to rely on this little girl." Li Fan shook his head slightly. The immense power of Shouqiu's ethereal projection, comparable to a Nameless True Immortal, was absolutely effective in combat. But for searching within the Xuanhuang Realm, perhaps before finding anything, the Xuanhuang Realm itself would be unable to withstand it and might disintegrate. Li Fan had no intention of destroying his own base for now. Setting aside the various changes within the Xuanhuang Realm after its separation from the Immortal Ruins, the clone Li Biren, step by step, finally arrived above the Immortal Ruins. Unlike ordinary True Immortals, the clone puppet's current body was entirely formed by the projection of the Great Dao, perfectly integrating into this world. Without using Shouqiu's ethereal projection power, it was almost impossible for others to detect him. However, the Starving Immortal should not be underestimated. Li Biren's Dao Net projection body, compared to the absolute silence of the Great Dao in this desolate starry sky, still had some differences. As if sensing something, the golden shackles on the Starving Immortal began to emit faint sounds. Li Biren also sensed a suction force emanating from the Starving Immortal. She instinctively wanted to devour Li Biren, this delicious morsel, into her belly. Li Biren did not resist, allowing his body to drift, accelerating towards the Starving Immortal. When he was only three zhang away from the Starving Immortal, Li Biren's heart stirred slightly. "Indeed, down below..." "There is the aura of a Nameless True Immortal." It was very well concealed by the Starving Immortal, perfectly blending with the fluctuations generated by her own enlightenment. If not for being this close, and if Li Biren, as a Dao Net projection, were not supremely sensitive to the Great Dao of heaven and earth, it might have truly been overlooked. With the Starving Immortal's skeletal body in sight, Li Biren suddenly accelerated. In an instant, he closed in on her. The Starving Immortal finally sensed something and abruptly opened her eyes. At the same time, Shouqiu's ethereal projection power descended upon Li Biren's body. In a flash, Li Biren, using the suction force that the Starving Immortal had not yet withdrawn, pointed a finger at her glabella. It was not a wise instruction, but a forceful infusion of Shouqiu's immeasurable might, channeled through the Starving Immortal's suction. The Starving Immortal's emaciated body instantly swelled like an inflated balloon. Not becoming plump like normal flesh and blood, but expanding in a grotesquely distorted manner. The swelling was uneven across her body, making the Starving Immortal at this moment resemble a terrifying monster from the abyssal depths. Even her two eyes were of different sizes; the larger one occupied half her face, while the smaller one was so compressed that only the pupil remained. However, both were staring intently at Li Biren, who had suddenly appeared. Their eyes held shock, confusion, and then boundless rage. But soon, all of this turned into terror. For she finally discovered that the immense power being infused was not something she could possibly consume. At this rate, she might actually "explode." And it wasn't just her immortal body. The Starving Immortal felt that her painstakingly cultivated Path of Starvation was also being gradually occupied by this intruder with brute force. It was as if a cuckoo had hijacked its nest, not only forcefully entering her home but also driving her out completely! "Wuwuwu..." In her terror and rage, the Starving Immortal instinctively resisted. It was fine if her immortal body was destroyed, but her Dao path being encroached upon was absolutely unacceptable. The Starving Immortal struggled with this inexplicable intruder for control of the Path of Starvation. However, she had not yet attained the Nameless realm. Although she was only a step away, this Dao path did not yet truly belong to her. Initially, the Starving Immortal could barely maintain her territory using the familiarity she had cultivated over time. But gradually, horror dawned upon her: the Great Dao of Starvation was actually starting to lean towards the intruder! From occupying ninety-nine percent of the space in the room to being pushed into a corner, it took only a few breaths. The Starving Immortal was momentarily stunned. She realized that the reason for the intruder's efficiency was not only their immense power but, more importantly, their profound understanding of the Path of Starvation. Hence, they could naturally compete for ownership of the Path of Starvation and emerge victorious! "This... How is this possible?" This realization was as devastating to the Starving Immortal as the destruction of her immortal body and the seizure of her Dao path. "Clearly..." "The bones of a Nameless True Immortal of Starvation are beneath me!" "There is no place in this world where this Dao path is denser." "Where did he attain enlightenment?" Unable to muster any resistance, the Starving Immortal fell into despair and confusion. But for some reason, the intruder, who should have soon occupied the entirety of the Path of Starvation, suddenly stopped midway, halting at the last moment. The Starving Immortal dared not make any rash moves, only observing silently. Simultaneously, she gathered her strength for a desperate counterattack. Duels over a particular Dao path in the Immortal Realm were not uncommon, and the outcome was always irreconcilable. Therefore, the Starving Immortal harbored no illusions. However, what baffled her was that the intruder seemed to have genuinely stopped just before the final step. It was as if they could have easily driven her out of this room with a single gesture, yet they did not. After a considerable time, something even more unexpected happened. The figure of the intruder actually shook its head slightly. And then, step by step, it withdrew from the room! The Starving Immortal regained complete control of the Path of Starvation! With her strength largely restored, she was overjoyed. Returning to reality from the struggle over the Dao, the Starving Immortal warily watched the figure not far away. The immense power that had been infused was inexplicably gone. The Starving Immortal's immortal body quickly returned to normal. She retracted the golden chains and, facing the mysterious person before her, attempted to communicate. "Immortal friend..." "What is the reason for this?" After a long silence, a cold voice replied, "This Dao is too weak. Merging is pointless." This answer was far beyond the Starving Immortal's expectations. She was slightly stunned, and her mind went blank for a moment. Those eight words were not difficult to understand. The other party disdained the Path of Starvation as too weak. Therefore, even with a hundred percent certainty of successfully attaining the Nameless realm, he voluntarily withdrew. But... how was this possible? Was there truly such an arrogant person in the world? The Starving Immortal's heart was filled with confusion and shock. The difference between attaining the Nameless realm and an ordinary True Immortal was like the difference between heaven and earth. In the past Immortal Realm, True Immortals could freely establish their own immortal residences in a starscape, enjoying endless energy and resources. However, they were still under the jurisdiction of the Immortal Realm. They dared not disobey the orders of the ruling Immortal Emperor, as if they were citizens of the Immortal Realm. Only at the Nameless True Immortal realm did they ascend to the status of "officials." Not only could they govern a star domain, but they could even argue directly with the ruling Immortal Emperor without punishment. Fundamentally, the source of True Immortals' infinite immortal power was firmly controlled by the Immortal Emperor. With a single decree, he could revoke their access to the Infinite Sea. Without the attribute of "infinite," a True Immortal would not even be a match for their own immortal servants or puppets. And True Immortals who had savored the taste of infinity would not easily relinquish it. Thus, under the rule of the governing Immortal Emperor, there were basically no rebels. The greatest goal for a multitude of True Immortals was to merge with the Great Dao and ascend to the Nameless realm. It was said that Nameless True Immortals could, to a certain extent, break free from the Immortal Realm's control, access the Infinite Sea on their own, and thus achieve true freedom. Therefore, regardless of their strength, attaining the Nameless realm was an irresistible temptation for all True Immortals in the world. But now, someone had passed through the gate of the Nameless realm without entering? The Starving Immortal stared at the figure not far away, full of shock. "If you wish to merge, then merge." "However, there are still some imperfections in your enlightenment." While the Starving Immortal was in a daze, the other party spoke again, elaborating on his own understanding of the Path of Starvation, all of which was conveyed with vivid detail. The Starving Immortal's own understanding and the other party's insights matched, filling her heart with both shock and joy. She was shocked that the other party's comprehension was indeed superior to hers. She was pleased that with the other party's additions, she was not far from taking that final step!

Chapter 1475: The Orthodoxy of True Hunger

Without considering anything else, the Hungry Immortal immediately immersed herself in the other party’s guidance.

Based on her years of secluded cultivation experience, enlightenment inspiration often appeared like a spark, suddenly flashing. If she did not comprehend it quickly, it would soon disappear into the vastness of her thoughts.

Not expecting the other party to offer guidance a second time, the Hungry Immortal seized the current opportunity and focused on comprehending the Dao.
