Admittedly, the Hungry Immortal’s comprehension of the Dao of Hunger was extraordinary after cultivating for thousands of years in seclusion.

Shortly after sitting down again, wisps of profound aura fluctuations emanated from her body.

It was exactly the same as the Nameless traces beneath her!

“It seems that promoting her to the Nameless realm is much easier than I thought.” Li Fan mused inwardly.

Although Li Fan had long spied upon the word ‘Hunger’ on the land of the Immortal Ruins, given his own aptitude, even with the insights gained from countless reincarnations, his comprehension of the Dao of Hunger would never surpass that of the Hungry Immortal at this moment.

The reason he could guide the Hungry Immortal to enlightenment with just a few words was because Li Biren, with Shouqiu Gong’s immense power, synchronously explained what he observed from the Nameless Dao traces beneath the Hungry Immortal to her.

This bird’s-eye view directly pointed to the core, naturally far superior to the Hungry Immortal’s closed-door cultivation.

Li Biren’s guidance was equivalent to giving her a push from behind.

For the Hungry Immortal, who was already just a step away from the finish line, she fundamentally didn’t need anyone’s help to attain the True Immortal realm through her own efforts, it would just take longer.

Perhaps the Hungry Immortal would gradually realize this later, but at this moment, immersed in the process, she had no time to ponder this truth and was solely focused on comprehending the Dao.

Li Biren retreated to the side, observing in secret.

Her body, which had become plump after being infused with power, became withered again after the Hungry Immortal’s enlightenment.

It was like withered bones, clearly indicating that she had entered the state of comprehending the Dao of Hunger.

Immersed in the Dao of Hunger, she instinctively desired to devour everything around her.

The immense suction force that had temporarily disappeared due to Li Biren’s appearance suddenly reappeared from the Hungry Immortal, and it was even more violent than before!

In the entire starscape, only the Immortal Ruins land and Li Biren standing upon it remained motionless.

Everything else instantly slid uncontrollably towards the Immortal Ruins, which had transformed into a central vortex.

Within the Xuanhuang Realm, the newly revived vitality, due to this immense suction force, instantly became as fragile as a candle in the wind and was on the verge of annihilation!

Fortunately, Li Fan manifested his Dao Net projection and protected the entire world.

And pulled the Xuanhuang Realm towards the boundary of the star sea again, attempting to distance it from the Immortal Ruins.

“Compared to before, this sudden surge of suction force is far stronger.”

“So, it was actually the Hungry Immortal deliberately restraining herself earlier…”

Li Fan frowned as he looked in the direction of the Immortal Ruins.

As if to confirm his conjecture.

“Crackling…” Crisp metallic sounds suddenly appeared in the silent starscape.

It was the golden chains binding the Hungry Immortal tightening further.

While gripping the Hungry Immortal, they seemed to be controlling her ravenous desire to devour everything in the world.

“Only in extreme hunger can one truly comprehend the Dao of Hunger.”

“A self-abusive cultivation method akin to asceticism…”

The golden chains tightened, even digging into her shriveled flesh, making eerie creaking sounds as they rubbed against the bones.

But the Hungry Immortal did not tremble throughout the entire process.

She silently endured the pain brought about by her own desires and suffering.

The Dao of Hunger was like a ferocious beast trapped in a cage, roaring to break free, yet firmly bound within this body.

This method of controlling oneself through denial had actually caused the Hungry Immortal's enlightenment efficiency to gradually climb!

Li Biren observed all the changes happening to the Hungry Immortal. He tried to put himself in her shoes and slowly tasted the essence of it.

“The more one is tormented by their Dao and sinks into it, the more they can comprehend its principles.”

“This method of enlightenment…”

“It is somewhat similar to the reverse cultivation method of the Heart Curse of the Xuanhuang Immortal Path. Could it be a method inherited from the Immortal Realm?”

When Li Biren began to observe and ponder, he noticed the difference in the flow of time between the inside and outside due to the reappearance of the Immortal Ruins’ suction force.

Before he could react, three months had already passed in the Xuanhuang Realm.

Outside the high wall, thirty years had already passed!

And this time difference was still widening!

Fortunately, during these thirty years, nothing happened that required the use of Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection power to resolve. Qian Ruochang and the Nameless Immortal from the Shining Star Sea visited several times to report on the progress of their cooperation.

Li Fan merely played dead, blandly replying, “Understood,” and said nothing more.

Qian Ruochang and the other two did not dare to disturb him and withdrew wisely.

…

Having just been in thirty years ago, he instantly found himself thirty years later.

Countless scenes experienced by the main body sequentially appeared in his mind.

The vast difference in the perception of time made even Li Biren feel somewhat unaccustomed, with a faint sense of dizziness. The Dao Net body also showed a slight distortion, only perceptible to himself, as if distorted by looking through bubbles.

Li Biren first attempted to curb the change in the flow of time caused by the immense suction force.

However, this was not an attribute of the Dao of Hunger,

but a natural phenomenon that existed in the mortal world.

Even with the power of Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection, it could not be completely eliminated. It could only be used to minimize the impact of the Immortal Ruins’ suction force on the outside world.

In Li Biren’s eyes, the giant vortex formed by the Immortal Ruins was devouring everything in the world.

And what he had to do was to build a dam outside the vortex to prevent anything from entering the vortex.

Just like the high wall separating the inside and outside of the experimental field!

“Still!” Li Biren silently chanted.

His Dao Net body, like countless stars, began to shine again.

It was like a giant rock standing before a raging tide. But contrary to common sense, there were no splashes of waves. Instead, as had happened in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, the blocked suction force converged at the foot of the high wall.

With Li Biren’s utterance, the suction force that had ravaged the Utmost Darkness Star Sea for tens of thousands of years was easily confined within ninety-nine zhang of the Hungry Immortal.

Li Biren had a premonition that he could continue to compress and push inward to create a “second high wall.” But this might interfere with the Hungry Immortal’s final enlightenment.

Therefore, he stopped at the right time.

The suction force, like surging waves, condensed and did not disperse. It gathered and intertwined beneath the high wall.

Li Biren vaguely seemed to see the scene of Shouqiu Gong gazing at the mountains and seas. He couldn’t help but be stunned.

The reason for this strange phenomenon, where the suction force from the Immortal Ruins was blocked and gathered, Li Biren was beginning to understand today.

“The power of Immortals comes from the Infinite Sea.”

“And the high wall, that is, the power of Shouqiu Gong’s ethereal projection, partly comes from the [Mountain] that accompanies the Infinite Sea.”

“Mountains and seas originate from the same source. They are not completely opposed, hence they can attract each other to a certain extent.”

“Therefore, in a sense, the anomaly occurring at the border of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea is a projection of what Shouqiu Gong saw in the past.”

Standing on the edge of the second high wall, Li Biren’s mind was filled with various insights.

Without the interference of the Immortal Ruins’ suction force, the flow of time within the Utmost Darkness Star Sea finally returned to normal.

But the beings within the star sea remained unaware of this drastic change.

Only Li Fan looked towards the center of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

Having previously been connected to the origin of the star sea’s truth, he could vaguely sense its joyful emotions. This was not solely due to the disappearance of the threat from the Immortal Ruins, but also seemed to stem from the synchronization with the external star sea.

Li Fan temporarily ignored it and looked at his ‘Return to Truth’ panel.

As the flow of time inside and outside the high wall returned to normal, the number representing the lifespan limit of the mortal world flashed and quietly changed.

However, the change was not significant.

It was merely reduced from seven million three hundred sixty thousand years to seven million two hundred thirty thousand years.

“This is not the effect of my establishing the second high wall, but rather the flow of time in my environment has changed.”

“In other words, the time difference between the inside and outside of the high wall is insignificant to the lifespan of the entire mortal world.”

“However, by what method does ‘Return to Truth’ calculate the lifespan displayed?”

Li Fan was somewhat puzzled.

Getting bogged down in such questions was destined to yield no results. Therefore, Li Fan decisively chose to directly ask ‘Return to Truth’ for guidance. Coupled with the precedent of previous guidance, ‘Return to Truth’ did not respond with silence this time.

A massive amount of light and shadow data instantly surged into Li Fan’s mind.

His brow throbbed, and Li Fan instinctively chose to view it selectively.

It seemed that knowing Li Fan’s current ability was insufficient to fully comprehend the casually transmitted image, so this light and shadow itself had been reduced.

He could not see the details clearly, only the vague direction.

“This is…”

“Using my current strength as a fixed template, and assuming immortality as a premise, simulating the maximum possible outcome.”

Although slightly convoluted, Li Fan quickly understood what ‘Return to Truth’ intended to convey.

He carefully gazed at the continuously flashing light and shadow. Seven million years of time passed like a fleeting moment, lasting only thirty-three breaths.

Finally, all light and brightness vanished, leaving behind neither light nor darkness.

It disappeared directly from Li Fan’s mind.

And when Li Fan tried to recall the specific content of the image he had just glimpsed, he found that no memory remained.

He only vaguely remembered that ‘Return to Truth’ had once shown him a simulated scene.

“The annihilation of the mortal world…”

“The so-called lifespan limit is measured and calculated from the perspective of me, the carrier of ‘Return to Truth’.”

“There are infinite possibilities for the future, but the current simulation and deduction is based on my current strength as the main perspective.”

“In this simulation, although I will not die, my strength and cultivation will not improve at all. I can only watch the changes in the mortal world as a bystander…”

Li Fan narrowed his eyes.

He couldn’t help but think of the change in the mortal world’s lifespan panel when Black Heavenly Physician broke through the high wall.

The number rapidly increased from over seven million years until it seemed infinite.

“In that simulation of ‘Return to Truth,’ although I would not die, I would still fall into Black Heavenly Physician’s hands.”

“Nameless True Immortal bones could also cross over with ‘Return to Truth,’ so Black Heavenly Physician could surely do the same. Therefore, my ending was likely not pleasant. Perhaps I became like Yan Fafang…”

“And with the help of ‘Return to Truth,’ Black Heavenly Physician could almost save the mortal world from disaster.”

Having understood the reason behind this, Li Fan couldn’t help but let out a cold snort.

His belief remained the same.

It was absolutely impossible to save the mortal world by sacrificing himself alone.

“The mortal world only has meaning because of my existence. If I perish, even if the mortal world can remain immortal through all tribulations, what does it have to do with me?”

“Moreover, in ‘Return to Truth’s’ calculations, even if Black Heavenly Physician obtained the ability of ‘Return to Truth,’ the lifespan limit of the mortal world still had a specific number.”

“Instead of infinity!”

“Even if this number is incredibly vast, to the point of being unimaginable, it will eventually face its doomsday.”

“Since the outcome is unchanged, whether it is seven million years or seventy billion years…”

“It makes no difference.”

I don’t know if it was the inexplicable influence of the simulated scene ‘Return to Truth’ had shown him, but Li Fan felt that his spirit had hopefully elevated even further.

He could even calmly disregard the vast number representing the mortal world’s possible lifespan in his memory.

It was as if he had truly experienced those long years, only to ultimately face the finality of destruction.

Even, in the depths of his heart, an uncontainable, firm thought emerged.

Only in his hands could ‘Return to Truth’ ultimately change the mortal world’s destined destructive ending.

Completely escaping the fate of Dao Annihilation.

This confidence came without any basis.

As time passed, it slowly faded.

After Li Fan fully recovered, even he felt that his previous thought was a bit too arrogant.

But after careful consideration, he vaguely guessed that he must have seen something in those more than seven million years of simulated light and shadow.

Therefore, such thoughts arose from the bottom of his heart.

Li Fan felt reassured.

When he wanted to verify his guess with ‘Return to Truth,’ ‘Return to Truth’ once again fell into silence.

But Li Fan was not annoyed.

“Silence, not denial.”

Having interacted with ‘Return to Truth’ for such a long time, Li Fan could roughly infer its emotions at times.

Silence was sometimes a form of answer.

Having confirmed that he was the legitimate heir of ‘Return to Truth,’ Li Fan was in high spirits.

Returning to his senses, he looked towards the Immortal Ruins above again.

Li Biren, using his body as a wall, blocked the suction of the Immortal Ruins, while also minutely sensing the changes in power generated by the Hungry Immortal’s enlightenment.

“Because of the change in the flow of time caused by this power, the last time the Hungry Immortal enlightened, it lasted for ten thousand years in the Xuanhuang Realm.”

“This time, with this breakthrough, it will definitely not take that long.”

“And…”

Li Biren observed that due to the existence of the “second high wall” he had personally built, the accumulated enlightenment suction power beneath this high wall had, to some extent, offset the impact of the Hungry Immortal on the outside world.

This greatly reduced the time difference between the inside and outside of the second high wall.

While waiting for the Hungry Immortal to emerge from seclusion and for him to complete his harvest, Li Biren first looked at the Immortal Ruins land beneath him.

Besides the ruins scattered everywhere, the giant character [Hunger] was the most conspicuous.

“The source of this ‘Hunger’ character’s manifestation…”

“It comes from the remnant of the previous Nameless True Immortal who attained the Dao of Hunger beneath the Hungry Immortal.”

Chapter 1476: Shadow of the Nameless Immortal

The Shadow of the Nameless Immortal

Li Biren peered, attempting to discern the traces of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation upon it.

Shouqiu Gong had gazed upon the mountains and seas for over a hundred epochs. Whether it was the mountains or the seas, he had become intimately familiar with them. Now, with Shouqiu Gong’s power, Li Biren truly sensed a hint of familiar aura upon the colossal character 'Hunger' etched on the Immortal Ruins.

"Whether the previous Hungry Immortal died by Dao Annihilation, or whether he became a pillar by transforming his body to resist the world-destroying tribulation from the Immortal Realm, one thing is certain: he must have had close contact with Dao Annihilation."

"Though his body perished, his Dao remained. The current Hungry Immortal discovered the mysteries of this place. The temptation to ascend to the Nameless realm was too great, so she willingly risked great danger, rather than fleeing like other True Immortals, and sought enlightenment here."

"In truth, it wasn't that dangerous."

"From an external perspective, the Immortal Realm had been destroyed for a long time. But from the Hungry Immortal's viewpoint, what she experienced was likely less than a day. Moreover, with the remnants of a Nameless True Immortal serving as a pillar here, if the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation were to erupt again, the Immortal Ruins would likely be safer than other places in this star sea."

"If it were me, I would have made the same choice," Li Biren concluded.

Although he was determined to help the Hungry Immortal achieve the Nameless realm, Li Biren had no intention of simply ignoring the Great Dao of 'Hunger,' as he had claimed earlier.

The Dao of Hunger, capable of altering the flow of time in its surroundings, was certainly not 'weak' in any sense.

Li Biren hid within the dwelling representing the Hungry Immortal's Dao path, observing the Hungry Immortal's figure, increasingly filling the space, as she achieved enlightenment.

He meticulously recorded the entire process.

"If my guess is correct, after the Hungry Immortal achieves the Nameless realm, all these recordings of mine will cease to exist. It's comparable to the simulated deduction that just occurred in my mind. However, there's a slight difference. Even if I 'Return to Truth,' that simulated deduction, along with its ultimate annihilating outcome, will not be recalled."

"But in the Hungry Immortal's case..."

"If she perishes, or if I were to move on to the next life, and no one has yet attained the Dao of Hunger, the recordings will reappear."

"By mastering the legacy of the previous generation's Hungry Immortal and the complete enlightenment process of the last Hungry Immortal, as long as one’s talent is not too poor, one can directly attain the Nameless realm in a short period! It's not necessarily this woman alone who is capable."

Li Biren, with a calm heart, recorded every detail meticulously.

Until the dwelling of the Great Dao of Hunger could no longer accommodate a second person.

A mysterious fluctuation suddenly arose in the heavens and earth.

The second high wall, personally constructed by Li Biren, collapsed without warning.

It wasn't that the Hungry Immortal suddenly turned hostile, but rather that the fluctuations caused by her ascension to the Nameless realm naturally led to this event.

The high wall, replicated by Li Biren, could block the Hungry Immortal during her enlightenment, but it could no longer contend with an existence that had already attained the Nameless realm.

At the same time, Li Biren sensed that a piece of memory in his mind had been inexplicably erased.

However, his mission remained firmly etched in his mind.

The aura, like an abyss and a sea, emanating from ahead, reminded him that before him stood a Nameless True Immortal.

And he was his hunting target!

The process of ascending to the Nameless realm was not yet complete, and the optimal moment for action had not arrived. Li Biren accumulated his strength, ready to strike at any moment.

In the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, it was as if a colossal meteorite had fallen, stirring up monstrous waves that swept outwards. In the face of this mighty force, all remnants in the star sea could not maintain their stability on their own.

Relics and fragmented realms were swept away like dust being crushed.

Finally, they crashed against the boundary of the star sea, where the high wall stood.

Rumble!

The reverse suction force, accumulated over tens of thousands of years beneath the high wall, served as a buffer. Many relics and fragmented realms managed to halt their momentum in time. However, many still collided with the high wall.

The projection of Shouqiu Gong, transformed into a towering embankment, stood unyielding. All the artifacts turned to dust upon impact, like pebbles striking a rock.

The high wall did not even tremble in the slightest.

It even firmly contained the fluctuations brought about by the Nameless Hungry Immortal.

The performance of the high wall greatly reassured Li Biren.

Shouqiu Gong's power was indeed trustworthy.

Concurrently, amidst the tempest and rain caused by the ascension to the Nameless realm, Li Biren also noticed that in the basin where the 'Form of Living Beings' resided beneath the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, inexplicable changes also seemed to be occurring simultaneously.

With Li Biren's current strength, even though the anomaly was extremely weak, it could not escape his observation.

"It seems that, like me, it has silently recorded the birth fluctuations of the Nameless Hungry Immortal?"

This outcome surprised Li Biren.

However, the recording methods used by the two were still different.

Li Biren's recording was complete and comprehensive, while the Form of Living Beings in the basin had, by leveraging the impact generated during the birth of the Nameless Hungry Immortal, rewritten itself to a certain extent.

It was as if pressing down firmly on an ink pad, leaving behind the fingerprint of the Nameless True Immortal. Information about the Nameless True Immortal, which could not have been recorded otherwise, was preserved.

In the basin, the Life River, which had been silent for a long time, suddenly began to boil due to the changes in the Form of Living Beings.

Corresponding to the grand spectacle of the Nameless True Immortal's descent in the star sea, it echoed.

Drawing upon almost all its stored vitality, a figure corresponding to the Hungry Immortal quietly appeared in the center of the Form of Living Beings pattern.

"Shadow of the Nameless Immortal."

"Interesting."

Li Biren's thoughts raced: "According to information previously gathered, this Form of Living Beings was constructed by Xing Wuque, the Heavenly King of Profound Heaven."

"Although Heavenly King of Profound Heaven possessed unparalleled talent, he was merely a Half-Immortal realm at the time of his disappearance. He should absolutely not have possessed such a method capable of imprinting the shadow of a Nameless True Immortal. Therefore, there is a high probability that the issue lies with Xing Wuque."

"Exhausted, almost soul-scattered, leaving behind only a damaged mask..."

If Xing Wuque were simply a native cultivator of the Xuanhuang Realm, with cultivation and strength inferior to Heavenly King of Profound Heaven, he would certainly not have been able to construct such a Form of Living Beings.

But when combined with the fact that the Xuanhuang Realm, as a former staging ground for 'Returning to Truth,' might have had a Nameless True Immortal avatar infiltrate it...

Everything became logical.

"Among the Twelve Heavenly Kings, how many are truly innocent?"

The hunting target was the Nameless Hungry Immortal, so Li Biren temporarily shifted his gaze away from the shadow of the Nameless Immortal in the basin.

The waves gradually subsided, and the anomaly was about to disappear.

The Utmost Darkness Star Sea had the good fortune to witness the birth of a Nameless True Immortal.

But for Her, it might also be misfortune.

For at the moment the Hungry Immortal attained enlightenment, she had completely occupied the Dao of Hunger. Therefore, the remnant of the previous Hungry Immortal beneath her lost its original divine properties, becoming a piece of ordinary material.

On the land of the Immortal Ruins, the character 'Hunger' first dimmed to deathly pallor.

Then, after a moment, it revived and reappeared.

But it had a new owner, gradually merging into the Hungry Immortal's body.

Rumble!

A faint roar of world-ending destruction seemed to come from beyond the heavens.

This was due to the sudden absence of the Nameless remnant, which had originally served as a pillar, causing the erosion of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.

It was like a small hole appearing in an indestructible dam. Although the hole had not completely penetrated the dam, the tides from the outside had already surged in.

If Li Biren were to return the power borrowed from Shouqiu Gong's projection at this moment, with the addition of the Primordial bone and the five projections of Shouqiu Gong. It would be enough to resist the onslaught of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.

But Li Biren did not act rashly.

He even resisted the power retrieval from Shouqiu Gong's projection.

He never forgot his hunting target.

He was waiting for the optimal moment to strike.

And the Hungry Immortal did not disappoint him.

Perhaps inheriting the duty from the previous Hungry Immortal, or perhaps an instinctual act in the face of disaster.

Facing the surging tide of Dao Annihilation, the Nameless Hungry Immortal casually unleashed a portion of her power to temporarily fill the void.

At the same time, she transmitted a message to Li Biren: "Fellow Daoist, hurry and leave. This place cannot be lingered in for long."

Even after achieving the Nameless realm, she still addressed Li Biren as 'Fellow Daoist.' Firstly, it was because Li Biren had helped her enlighten, thus she felt indebted. Secondly, it was because Li Biren's displayed power, though strange, was no weaker than hers. Therefore, her attitude was very friendly.

But the subsequent actions of the other party greatly exceeded her expectations.

Li Biren's body first became momentarily still, then instantly exploded and scattered.

Transforming into a vast silver Dao Net, it accepted the power of Shouqiu Gong's projection with complete tolerance.

Even louder than the roar of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, a thunderous sound echoed in the ears of the Nameless Hungry Immortal.

Within this silver Dao Net, she vaguely saw a towering figure standing with his hands behind his back.

Like mountains and seas.

Even though she had become one with the Great Dao as heaven and earth, compared to him, she was merely like an ant living between the mountains and seas.

That figure bore some resemblance to her 'benefactor.'

But he was even more like...

That person from the ancient legends of the Immortal Realm.

"Shouqiu Gong?!"

The Nameless Hungry Immortal's body and mind trembled, and she was momentarily stunned.

At this moment, the vastness of mountains and seas pressed down upon her.

Only when the ocean's tide rushed towards her and the mountains loomed overhead did the Nameless Hungry Immortal snap out of her shock.

She had no time to question why, but instinctively she prepared to resist.

Even if the other party was truly the great figure who had saved the Immortal Realm, she would never passively accept her fate!

"Hunger."

"I am so hungry..."

A deep, ghost-like voice emerged from the midst of the mountain and sea tide.

It seemed to have come from the Hungry Immortal.

Or perhaps, it came from a mysterious existence beyond the Great Dao.

The power Li Biren was preparing to use to imprison the Nameless Hungry Immortal was all swallowed by the other party as food.

Facing the immense power of mountains and seas, the Hungry Immortal remained undaunted.

She wanted to swallow mountains and drink seas, turning everything in the world into her own sustenance!

Like a giant whirlpool devouring all things, the figure of the Nameless Hungry Immortal became indistinguishable.

Even Li Biren, in his Dao Net form, felt a subtle distortion under this terrifying suction force.

The power of the Hungry Immortal after achieving the Nameless realm was indeed somewhat beyond his expectations.

But with just this much power, she intended to overturn the heavens and earth...

Li Biren, in his other body seated on the Grand Tutor's chair, bowed slightly to the five projections of Shouqiu Gong.

Instantly, a portion of power was drawn from the five projections.

This was the maximum amount Li Biren could borrow, as calculated, under the condition that the high wall would not collapse under the pressure of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.

Approximately equivalent to the power of two and a half Nameless True Immortals!

Consequently, the force binding the Nameless Hungry Immortal instantly doubled, exceeding all previous levels.

The mountains and seas, which already felt boundless, now appeared as mere pebbles and drops of water.

The expansion of the mountains and seas seemed to have no end or limit.

Her initial ambition and determination to swallow mountains and drink seas faltered upon discovering this terrifying reality.

The endless hunger was almost filled.

More critically...

The Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, which they had initially intended to ward off and leave shortly after, had intensified.

The combined effect of these two factors trapped her, rendering her immobile for the moment!

Moreover, it seemed to have discovered her as a potential breakthrough point. The Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, as if possessing sentience, began to attack her.

At this moment, the pressure she endured from Dao Annihilation was many times greater than in other parts of this star sea!

Not only the Hungry Immortal,

but Li Biren also noticed this change in the battle.

As the Hungry Immortal bore more pressure, Shouqiu Gong's projection had to bear less.

Therefore, he could borrow more power.

With further escalation, it was equivalent to the power of three Nameless True Immortals erupting simultaneously.

Already on the verge of collapse under the threat of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, the Nameless Hungry Immortal

was like a bird in a cage, unable to escape.

Li Biren's Dao Net body transformed into ropes.

Binding the Hungry Immortal.

Tightening and locking, while simultaneously 'nailing' her into this starscape.

Bang! Bang! Bang!

"No!"

"We beg Shouqiu Gong for mercy!"

Sensing the opponent's intention, the Hungry Immortal cried out in terror.

A Nameless True Immortal becoming a Heavenly Pillar.

This was not a secret in the Immortal Realm.

At least, the Hungry Immortal had known about this matter for a long time. When she was cultivating in the past, she had even personally witnessed the foundation laying of a Heavenly Pillar.

She never imagined that today, she would have to repeat such a fate!

However, despite all her unwillingness, she could not change this reality.

The scene before the Nameless Hungry Immortal's eyes grew increasingly dim.

She could no longer see the starlight and mountains and seas.

It was as if she were slowly sinking to the bottom of an endless sea.

All she felt around her was eternal darkness and ever-increasing pressure.

...

The moment the Nameless Hungry Immortal's body disappeared from the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

A Nameless Heavenly Pillar was successfully erected by Li Biren in this world.

However, the faint sounds of Dao Annihilation still echoed, and Li Biren decisively returned the power borrowed from Shouqiu Gong's projection.

The Primordial bone, the Hungry Immortal Heavenly Pillar, and the five projections of Shouqiu Gong.

The combined dam formed by so much power was by no means something that the current Tribulation of Dao Annihilation could breach.

After attempting and finding it futile, the surging tide abruptly retreated.

Li Biren checked his Dao Net body.

Due to the constant use of Shouqiu Gong's projection power, it showed signs of vaporizing.

Fortunately, the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation did not last long. Within a few deep breaths, Li Biren had already returned to normal.

"The Tribulation of Dao Annihilation ebbs and flows, as expected."

"And it seems to have no discernible pattern."

"During the brief period when a loophole is discovered, it can suddenly become surging and immense."

"As if..."

"It possesses its own offensive consciousness."

Chapter 1477: The Past of the Starving Immortal

The Past of the Hungry Immortal

"When there's a flaw, it relentlessly pursues and attacks, never ceasing until victory."

"If the plan fails, it temporarily retreats to accumulate strength..."

Li Biren recalled the subtle feelings he experienced while confronting the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation just now.

Just as all living beings in the world could perceive the approaching storm to varying degrees, the premonition of the approaching Tribulation of Dao Annihilation also seemed to be deeply ingrained in the instincts of living beings.

Even long after the great tide had retreated, Li Biren still felt the unease in his heart completely dissipate.

Slowly regaining his senses, he looked at the 'Heavenly Pillar' now standing in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

Unlike the ruins formed by the superposition of two Primordial bones, the pillar before him was truly formed by a Nameless True Immortal who had attained enlightenment.

With the appearance of this Nameless Heavenly Pillar, the sky seemed to become even higher and more distant.

And it also became 'safer.'

The invisible oppressive feeling in his heart vanished, as if he had arrived in the legendary 'Immortal Realm.'

"It's naturally not comparable to the true Immortal Realm, which can draw energy from the Infinite Sea, but calling this place an 'Immortal Domain' would not be an exaggeration."

The heavens were high and the earth was vast. The Great Daos manifested between heaven and earth became even clearer. More importantly, the Utmost Darkness Star Sea within this high wall had now gathered three significant items: Shouqiu Gong's projection, the Primordial bone, and the Hungry Immortal Heavenly Pillar.

While Shouqiu Gong's projection affected all experimental spaces within the high wall, the other two were exclusive to the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

The appearance of each of these items had, invisibly, elevated the 'momentum' of this star sea.

With the presence of all three, the Utmost Darkness Star Sea had been elevated to a point where it could temporarily look down upon the Dao Annihilation tide below.

"Living within this realm, one's innate potential is far superior to that of other regions. In simple terms, everyone is a gifted individual, a prime candidate for seeking immortality and the Dao. Furthermore, it was a surviving land after the baptism of Dao Annihilation. Under such natural conditions, those who can cultivate here are inherently exceptionally talented..."

Li Biren raised his eyebrows slightly: "The Utmost Darkness Star Sea is like the sacred lands and dojos of ancient cultivation legends. Regardless of their strength, anyone who emerges from it is bound to possess earth-shattering cultivation talent."

"If the path to immortality had not been severed, and if the Immortal Ascending Platform officials were not obstructing them, it would likely not be difficult for the entire realm to ascend."

"What a pity..."

"Now, it is merely a high ground, a single boat amidst the world-ending tide."

With the convergence of three powers comparable to Nameless True Immortals, only Li Fan, through continuous reincarnation and information gathering, could complete such a meticulous plan.

In essence, the Utmost Darkness Star Sea could now be called the safest region in the entire [Primordial] possibility.

Even if the entire possibility were engulfed by the Dao Annihilation tide, the Utmost Darkness Star Sea could serve as a high ground, holding on for a period of time.

As for Li Fan, who considered the Utmost Darkness Star Sea his lair, he naturally felt even more at ease. It was like being in a meticulously protected doomsday safe house.

Let the ice seal the world outside, and the turbulent waves rage.

I stand firm and unmoved!

While Li Fan's main body felt invigorated, his clone, Li Biren, quickly detached himself from this sense of satisfaction and busied himself calculating the specific benefits gained from the Hungry Immortal's transformation into a pillar.

"Originally, I could unconditionally and without side effects utilize the power of one and one-third of the [Primordial] bone."

"But after suppressing the Hungry Immortal..."

"The result is not equivalent to the full power of a Nameless True Immortal, but rather the remnant of the previous Hungry Immortal must be subtracted."

"Approximately equivalent to two and one-fifth of the Primordial bone's power."

Having roughly completed the quantification calculation.

This result did not entirely exceed Li Fan's expectations.

Although the Primordial bone was powerful, representing the fundamental Dao of the beginning of all things, it was ultimately only two remnant bones, not a complete entity.

Under such circumstances, it could still nearly match the power of a newly ascended Nameless True Immortal. This was enough to illustrate the terror of its full state.

"Judging from the Hungry Immortal's performance in her previous battle, she still possessed the strength to swallow mountains and drink seas when facing Shouqiu Gong's projection. Even upon initial ascension, she was undoubtedly not among the weaker Nameless True Immortals. And now, I can freely utilize the power equivalent to two Nameless True Immortals..."

"In this star sea, I truly have no opponent."

Although the power used was entirely borrowed from Shouqiu Gong's projection, it did not diminish Li Fan's delight.

"The Immortal Realm was destroyed, and the Immortals fled. With such strength, it almost means invincibility."

"It's a pity it's limited to the vicinity of the high wall."

"Furthermore, I can replicate this feat, attract and suppress other Nameless True Immortals again, and further develop the power of Shouqiu Gong's projection! The upper limit is when all five of Shouqiu Gong's projections are fully utilized by me!"

"That is the power capable of resisting the monstrous Dao Annihilation during the destruction of the Immortal Realm..."

A hint of wistful longing flickered in Li Fan's eyes.

However, he was not blinded by this unparalleled immense power.

After all, it was only temporary borrowing, not his own true strength.

"However, it is not something that cannot be used as my tool."

This successful suppression of the Nameless Hungry Immortal had, in practical terms, validated the extent of the energy Li Fan could mobilize.

At this level, he no longer needed to be so cautious.

"The Utmost Darkness Star Sea, the few blind spots within the Xuanhuang Realm, can finally be resolved all at once," Li Fan's eyes flashed with a sharp glint.

However, before taking action, Li Fan carefully compared the Primordial bone and the Hungry Immortal Heavenly Pillar in the starscape.

Although both were used as pillars to resist Dao Annihilation, their performances were entirely different.

The Primordial bone, already within the unwritten tablet and the Southern Immortal Heavenly Pillar, seemed to have accepted its fate or been tamed. It simply bore the brunt of everything silently, with all light and phenomena contained. It looked like an ordinary, broken stone stump.

But the Hungry Immortal Heavenly Pillar had been forcibly bound by external force.

The Hungry Immortal's consciousness still existed.

Li Fan could not only sense the monstrous resentment surrounding the Heavenly Pillar but could also clearly hear the Hungry Immortal's constant stream of curses.

Li Fan acted as if he heard nothing, continuing to observe with a slight smile.

He extended a wisp of divine sense, making contact with the Hungry Immortal Heavenly Pillar.

Boom!

As his divine sense trembled, the Great Dao of 'Hunger,' stretching across heaven and earth from top to bottom, stood before Li Fan in exquisite detail.

As if all her secrets were laid bare, exposed entirely to Li Fan. The Hungry Immortal, sealed within the Heavenly Pillar, was stunned for a moment.

Then, even more furious curses welled up.

However, the most she could do was this.

She was completely unable to stop Li Fan's intrusion.

"Though I can perceive the Dao, I cannot comprehend it in the slightest."

"The Dao of Hunger has already been attained by someone else. It has as if disappeared from this world."

"How can I comprehend something that belongs to another?"

Li Fan sighed faintly.

What he regretted was not just the Dao path of Hunger before him.

But it was evident that amidst the great tribulation of the Immortal Realm's destruction and the flight of the Immortals, countless Great Daos were missing.

"It's like my divine sense projection only reflects a small part of the Dao Net. What remains in the Primordial possibility are just scraps..."

"The Great Dao is incomplete, and the world is imperfect."

"Even so, the world I see is so magnificent. It's truly hard to imagine what a truly complete Great Dao world would look like..."

This was a common fantasy for any cultivator, and Li Fan was no exception.

He was momentarily lost in thought before the Hungry Immortal Heavenly Pillar.

After a long time, Li Fan's gaze shifted from yearning to determination.

"One day, I will witness the complete Dao of Heaven."

"That day will come."

Besides observing the Dao of Hunger within the Hungry Immortal Heavenly Pillar, Li Fan could also vaguely glimpse the Hungry Immortal's past life.

However, due to her attainment of the Nameless realm and the consolidation of all her past experiences, these imprints of memory were all covered by the Great Dao of Hunger.

It was like hiding behind a layer of Dao's outward appearance.

Without dismantling the Hungry Immortal Heavenly Pillar, Li Fan could not fully examine it all at once.

He could only slowly, inch by inch, peel it back for inspection.

Besides combating the Great Dao of Hunger, Li Fan's probing also had to contend with the Hungry Immortal's own struggling consciousness.

The Hungry Immortal's resistance seemed to be extremely intense, even more so than when she fought Li Biren earlier, as she seemed to be instinctively resisting Li Fan's gaze.

"If I had known this would happen, why bother in the first place!"

Li Fan let out a cold snort. Not only did he not withdraw, but he pressed further.

Breaking through the defenses of the Great Dao of Hunger.

He glimpsed a segment of the Hungry Immortal's past life, during her youth before she even became a True Immortal.

The Hungry Immortal was not a cultivator who ascended from the lower realms but had lived in the Immortal Realm since her birth. She was an appendage to a True Immortal.

Although labeled as an 'immortal servant,' the Hungry Immortal had never once seen the nominal 'master' she was assigned to since her creation.

Even with the Immortal Realm's infinite resources, they, as servants, did not need to provide tribute to their master. The Hungry Immortal heard that her master disliked liveliness and preferred solitude. Although they, the immortal servants, were created and bestowed upon the master, the master had never inquired about them.

Instead, they were settled in his own fiefdom.

Having such a 'master' was naturally a blessing for the immortal servants.

The immortal servants lived extremely freely. They were protected by a True Immortal master from above, and there was no need to worry about anything.

However, such leisurely days did not last long.

One day, the young Hungry Immortal personally witnessed the world-ending Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.

Her master's domain, her homeland, named [Singing Immortal Realm],

was instantly destroyed in the face of this terrifying tribulation.

If not for her reclusive True Immortal master appearing at the last moment to save her, the Hungry Immortal would have likely perished in the tribulation back then.

"Carefree and untroubled..."

"Hmph!"

The Hungry Immortal only remembered her master letting out a cold snort as he watched the Immortal Realm in the distance being annihilated, after casually saving them.

After that, his figure faded and disappeared.

After that, the Hungry Immortal never saw her master again.

It was only after this that the Hungry Immortal finally learned her master's name.

[Non-action].

...

The moment Li Fan glimpsed these two words from the Hungry Immortal's memory, it was as if he had touched something he shouldn't have. He encountered strong resistance from the Hungry Immortal.

Even the Hungry Immortal Heavenly Pillar trembled slightly. Under the powerful repulsion, Li Fan's consciousness was directly ejected.

Since there would be ample time to deal with her later, Li Fan did not force the issue this time, deciding to be content with what he had gained.

Let the Hungry Immortal calm down first.

"Nameless Immortal..."

His expression grew somewhat solemn as he recalled, in the Hungry Immortal's memory, what he had seen.

Although not as leisurely and elegant as Shouqiu Gong, and the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation he faced was not as vast as the one that threatened the entire Immortal Realm.

But that was the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation nonetheless!

Li Fan, who had recently come into contact with it, knew very well how terrifying this tribulation was.

"To be able to save his servants while facing the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, and successfully escape."

"The strength of this Non-action Immortal is not weak either. It's just that the young Hungry Immortal's memory is still somewhat vague. I don't know if he had truly reached the Nameless realm."

The reason Li Fan had this doubt was that the Nameless beings he had encountered all possessed a peculiar trait. They merged with the Dao, standing alone between heaven and earth.

But that Non-action Immortal did not give Li Fan that feeling.

However, if he hadn't reached the Nameless realm, how could he have resisted the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation?

"Perhaps it was because of merit and reward... Interesting."

Thinking of how there were many such figures in the past Immortal Realm, some who perished in the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, and some who abandoned their realms and fled. Li Fan felt a strange emotion arise in his heart.

"But it's just a decaying world."

It was foreseeable that the possibilities the Immortals fled to in the past were likely far more vibrant than the [Primordial] possibility Li Fan currently inhabited.

"Fortunately, it has been verified that figures who disappeared in the [Primordial] possibility may still exist in other possibilities."

"So I will not be eternally unable to meet them."

The events and objects he had encountered recently, such as Shouqiu Gong, Primordial Dao, Non-action Immortal, etc.

Made Li Fan feel as if he had glimpsed a heaven beyond the heavens, and a person beyond people. His mind, rare for him, became active, and a spark of excitement arose.

It was like playing a game for a long time and suddenly discovering vast hidden maps and characters. He instinctively felt a desire to explore and yearn for more.

"Although I am currently only at the Half-Immortal realm, I will surely, one day, traverse across possibilities and witness such wonders."

"When the seas change and the rivers flow, true heroes emerge. When the world faces annihilation, true heroes of the world are revealed."

"The Immortals in other possibilities might be even more spectacular than what I've glimpsed in the Primordial. Hehehe..."

Li Fan thought silently.

Then, he calmed his thoughts and returned his attention to his clone, Li Biren.

After some calculation and adjustment, he could now operate Shouqiu Gong's projection power with relative precision.

The first target to be dealt with was naturally the Grand Magister Tian Du, whom Li Fan considered a thorn in his side!

With a single thought, Li Biren returned from the center of the star sea to the Origin Dao Province within the Xuanhuang Realm.

The moment he stepped into this province, he felt a force rapidly retreating.

"Sorrow... Dao Annihilation."

A faint chanting voice from the heavens suddenly sounded.

Li Biren narrowed his eyes, noticing that the two figures, one large and one small, seemed to be attempting to escape before him.

Chapter 1478: The Origin of Ink Kill

The Origin of Ink Slaughter

Or to be precise, it was the smaller figure that, by enveloping the chanting spirit projection – the so-called Grand Magister Tian Du – was trying to escape from Li Biren.

"A thousand souls shifting, a hundred spirits turning."

"Infinite, boundless, blameless."

...

The profound sounds echoed, and Li Biren found that the two figures were indeed gradually fading, attempting to evade his immense power.

Li Biren felt a strange sensation. Although the two were within his grasp, his desire to capture them was not as strong as before.

He even developed an indifferent sentiment towards his prey.

It was clear that even Li Biren's Dao Net body could not resist the influence of the chanting sound.

Unfortunately, while this profound sound had the divine effect of avoiding calamity, it was not an omnipotent wish-granting machine.

By merely channeling a bit of Shouqiu Gong's projection power, Li Biren instantly broke free from the encirclement of the chanting.

No longer resonating from the heavens and entering the soul, it was merely like the buzzing of mosquitoes, easily ignored at any time.

Li Biren reached out and grasped, and the child-like projection, the Grand Magister Tian Du, was instantly silenced, like a rooster whose neck had been grabbed.

However, to Li Biren's surprise, the chanting spirit projection beside the Grand Magister was barely affected. It merely rippled like water, swayed slightly, and continued.

And influenced by the profound sound beside him, Li Biren keenly sensed that the Grand Magister he held tightly in his hand was slowly escaping from his grasp.

This escape had nothing to do with power.

It represented a trend.

Like a conceptual law: avoid calamity, be blameless.

Li Biren had a feeling that even with the power of the two Nameless True Immortals he could wield, he could not disregard this conceptual trend.

Even...

Perhaps even if all five projections of Shouqiu Gong unleashed their full power, he might stand a chance.

If Li Biren had used his full strength from the beginning, he might have truly allowed the Grand Magister to slowly escape from his hands.

Fortunately, in his eyes, the Grand Magister was only at the Half-Immortal realm. When he first made his move, he only channeled a very small portion of his power. When he realized he couldn't change the trend of his prey slipping away, he gradually increased the strength of his grip.

Not by direct suppression.

But by trend against trend!

Li Biren's available power had an upper limit. Eventually, the Grand Magister would succeed in escaping with the help of the chanting spirit projection.

But until then, he was like he had been struck by a immobilization spell, frozen in place.

Immovable!

Li Biren slowly approached. After shielding himself from the influence of the chanting profound sound, he finally saw clearly the Grand Magister Tian Du, who was famous in Xuanhuang Realm history.

He truly resembled a young disciple of a sage, dressed simply, with a youthful face, like a child. But his eyes were dark and deep, as if he had seen through all the principles of the world, its rise and fall. A serene aura enveloped him. Even as Li Biren drew near, his expression remained unchanged.

He even acted as if he didn't see Li Biren at all.

Li Biren didn't address him for the moment, but first turned his gaze to the chanting profound sound beside the Grand Magister.

After encountering the Dao Net, Shouqiu Gong, Primordial Dao, and others, his horizons had broadened immensely.

Observing from such close proximity, he could naturally see what this illusory projection truly was.

"A remnant after transcending and departing..."

"It's just that this remnant, instead of being used as a pillar to prop up Dao Annihilation, has continued its original Dao path."

"No wonder the Grand Magister Tian Du, no matter what happened, remained indifferent and refused to leave with this illusory projection."

A strange light flashed in Li Biren's eyes.

"After the minor transcendence to the Nameless realm, the Dao He merged with should have disappeared from the world. But if a remnant remains, after many years, a new manifestation of this Dao might appear in the world."

"It's equivalent to starting anew from infancy. Compared to evolving from nothing, it’s countless times faster!"

Li Biren stared intently at the illusory projection, trying to penetrate the chanting profound sound and see its true essence.

"Avoid calamity when there is calamity."

"Preach scriptures when someone seeks guidance."

Recalling the various rumors about the Grand Magister Tian Du in the Xuanhuang Realm, a thought slowly surfaced in Li Biren's mind.

"It's not about responding to every request, but about evolving oneself based on external changes."

"Going with the flow, exploring all possibilities."

"This is..."

"The Dao of Illusionary Life!"

This was a Dao path that had long since disappeared in the Primordial possibility, leaving only this new remnant within the illusory projection.

The Dao path of Illusionary Life was clearly not inferior to [Primordial] or [Non-action]. After observing it for a few moments, Li Biren had already gained a lot.

At this point, he realized that a new Dao path represented not just a single Dao, but also allowed for glimpsing a chain of related Dao shadows!

Even though most of these Daos no longer existed in this world.

But as they were all among the Three Thousand Great Daos, by leveraging his comprehension of the Dao, he could 'fill in the blanks' for these 'lost Daos'!

"Grand Magister Tian Du is truly fortunate. This [Illusory Life Dao Image], even in the Immortal Realm, would be a treasure sought after by all Immortals. Yet he, a mere Half-Immortal, has possessed it for tens of thousands of years." Li Biren couldn't help but sigh.

The reason the Grand Magister Tian Du had remained in the Origin Dao Province, unwilling to leave or emerge, was fundamentally because he could not control the coming and going of the [Illusory Life Dao Image]. Until he had completely refined and mastered it, he could only follow it step by step!

"So I was wrong before. Knowing that this chanting profound sound was miraculous, I subconsciously spent too much energy on it. I shouldn't have targeted the Illusory Life Dao Image, but only captured the Grand Magister himself."

"If it doesn't perceive any threat or calamity, it naturally won't evolve its avoidance techniques."

With a thought, Li Biren adjusted the distribution of restraining force. All his efforts were focused on the Grand Magister Tian Du, who resembled a child.

The Grand Magister's expression, which had always been calm and composed, finally changed.

"After all, I have been meditating by the Illusory Life Dao Image for so many years, so there is some use for it," Li Biren sensed that there was indeed a faint, almost imperceptible connection between the Grand Magister and the Illusory Life Dao Image.

The technique applied to the Grand Magister inevitably affected the Dao Image as well.

However, the avoidance power manifested as a result was significantly weaker than before.

This meant that Li Biren had more time to slowly deal with the Grand Magister Tian Du.

However, regardless of the secrets hidden within the Grand Magister Tian Du, they were ultimately no match for the Illusory Life Dao Image. Therefore, Li Biren was not in a hurry to interrogate him, his attention remained focused on the Dao Image.

After a long while...

"The Dao of Illusionary Life, in simple terms, is the ultimate evolution of 'survival of the fittest'."

"Transforming all disadvantages into advantages. Theoretically, it might even be able to evolve a countermeasure against the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation."

"However, this is only theoretical. The prerequisite is not being devoured by Dao Annihilation before evolving the characteristic."

Li Biren pondered this, and suddenly thought of Mo Sha in the Xuanhuang Realm.

"Mo Sha has an intricate connection with Dao Annihilation."

"Perhaps it was an attempt by the experimental field to completely resolve Dao Annihilation. However, Dao Annihilation encompasses all things, and there is fundamentally nothing related to it in the world..."

Recalling the Illusory Life Dao Image, and why it had appeared in the Xuanhuang Realm.

Li Biren shifted his gaze towards Yuan Dao Province below.

"The successful creation of the World's Soul - Mo Sha - should have involved some infusion of Illusionary power."

"This infusion of power did not disappear even after the Illusionary Nameless trascended and departed. It still exists within the Xuanhuang Realm."

"This is the only source of Illusionary power in the [Primordial] possibility besides the Illusory Life Dao Image. It is precisely because of this connection that the Dao Image came here."

Li Biren's thoughts raced, and his Dao Net divine sense swept across the land of Yuan Dao Province and the deep underground.

Since being inexplicably swallowed by ten years of time, Li Fan had never set foot in Yuan Dao Province again. Even after reaching the Half-Immortal realm and mastering the Unbounded Dreamland Paradise, he had avoided this province due to the existence of the Grand Magister.

Therefore, this place was a complete blind spot for him.

Now, with the power of Shouqiu Gong's projection assisting him, the shadows in the blind spot were finally swept away.

Thirty-three thousand Zhang underground in Yuan Dao Province.

A strange space, seemingly independent of the Xuanhuang Realm.

A cluster of ink-like darkness resembling a heart, pulsed incessantly.

Each of its beats was extremely peculiar.

It was not a fluid, continuous motion, but rather a series of intermittent images, as if in a frame-by-frame sequence.

As Li Biren's divine sense drew closer, he felt an increasing sense of familiarity.

This was brought about by his main body harmonizing with the World Soul - Mo Sha - of Xuanhuang Realm.

Li Biren approached cautiously, without disturbing it, continuing to observe.

He already knew what the object before him was.

"Although Mo Sha is the World Soul, it is not an inherent, original entity of the Xuanhuang Realm."

"It was modified and created artificially."

"Unlike other World Souls, the Mo Sha law did not integrate into the Xuanhuang Realm's heaven and earth."

"This area beneath Yuan Dao Province is the separate source from which Mo Sha originated."

The ink-like shadow seemed extremely vigilant towards the approach of foreign objects. Upon discovering Li Biren, it became agitated.

In the intermittently shifting images, the ink shadow churned.

Li Biren felt that if he were to get any closer, he might be attacked.

Although he was not afraid, it might interfere with the subsequent investigation into the origin of Mo Sha.

Therefore, Li Biren decisively stopped.

"This matter requires the main body to handle it."

Li Biren suddenly reversed course and returned to confront the Grand Magister.

Meanwhile, Li Fan's main body concentrated the power of the Mo Sha Immortal Soul within him, differentiating a figure.

It descended rapidly, heading straight for the location Li Biren had previously identified, and saw the cluster of ink-like shadows.

Compared to its vigilance towards Li Biren, the ink shadow clearly regarded Li Fan as 'one of its own.'

It mistook him for Mo Sha World Soul carrying out a mission for the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao.

But Li Fan still sensed countless faint, curious observing intentions.

As if questioning Li Fan's individuality.

Although he had ascended to the Immortal Soul realm, his essence was still Mo Sha power.

Li Fan eventually integrated safely into the ink shadow.

Compared to the Illusory Life Dao Image seen earlier, he observed even more closely.

Surrounded on all sides by ink, Li Fan found himself in an ocean of ink.

His heart was devoid of joy or sorrow, merely calmly observing.

"Hmm... the Path of Destruction originating from Dao Annihilation."

"The power of Transformation from the Illusory Life Dao Image."

"Besides these two..."

Like sipping a fine tea, Li Fan meticulously savored it.

Clearly, it was another Dao path that had already disappeared from the current possibility.

Although Li Fan had never encountered or understood it before.

But because it had a strong connection with the [Dao of Illusionary Life], Li Fan had vaguely glimpsed traces of its Dao in the lost Dao shadow he had previously observed.

"If the Dao of Illusionary Life is the extreme evolution of 'Transformation'."

"Then this Dao is its opposite."

"Eternal Order..."

Li Fan stared intently at the center of the churning ink ocean.

As a creation capable of destroying and devouring all things, what exactly maintained Mo Sha's existence?

Amidst the entanglement of destructive and transformative powers, it was precisely because of an unchanging power that served as a connecting link that [Mo Sha] could exist in the world.

"Transformation. And Permanence."

"These two opposing forces, coming together."

"The restraint originates from the source of destruction in Dao Annihilation."

A hint of surprise flashed in Li Fan's eyes: "Illusionary Life, Eternity."

"These two Daos are not inferior to Primordial. They once joined forces for an experiment..."

Eternity served as the foundation of existence, while Illusionary Life provided the support for evolution.

Through an unknown period of evolution within this ink shadow, Mo Sha came to be today.

If the experimental field were still in its normal state, Mo Sha might have been even more miraculous and closer to the goal the experimental field intended to achieve.

But the experimental field had been abandoned for unknown reasons. Furthermore, due to various circumstances, the Xuanhuang Realm, the crucible for Mo Sha's evolution, had been in a state of self-preservation for many years.

It was simply unable to support Mo Sha's next stage of evolution.

Only when Li Fan, in his previous life, propelled the Xuanhuang Realm to ascend to the Immortal Domain, did he bring a new variable to this long-stalled experiment.

After a period of observation and hesitation, the ink around Li Fan seemed to confirm Li Fan's 'advancement.' It churned spontaneously, as if trying to emulate him.

They wanted to become like him!

But after all, it was a change brought about by propelling an entire realm to ascend. If the surrounding ink wanted to emulate it, wasn't it that simple?

Like a group of boisterous children, they churned incessantly but could never find the right method.

Li Fan observed this scene and suddenly had an idea.

"The accumulation is sufficient."

"What is lacking is only energy."

And Li Fan had no shortage of this.

With a slight movement of his mind, the vast feedback energy from the Xuanhuang Realm's ascension to the Immortal Domain in his previous life, channeled through the Mo Sha avatar, was poured into this mass of ink.

Although from an external perspective, the shape and size of the ink cluster remained unchanged.

Only Li Fan, who was inside, could see the earth-shattering changes.

Skiping the intermediate process of Xuanhuang's ascension to the Immortal Realm,

knowing the outcome that the ink had presented, they could directly emulate it!

Chapter 1479: One Dao, One Ladder

One Dao, One Step

Amidst the layers of black shadows, Li Fan felt countless 'selves' being continuously replicated.

This shadow mass, hidden deep beneath Yuan Dao Province in the Xuanhuang Realm, was collectively evolving rapidly towards the realm of the Mo Sha Immortal Soul.

Empowered by the characteristics of [Illusionary Life] and [Eternity], they could ignore the threshold of becoming Immortal and directly cross the boundary between mortal and immortal.

From mortal to Immortal!

Immersed in the vast ocean of ink, Li Fan clearly saw the effects of these two Daos.

Illusionary Life provided infinite evolutionary power, extending infinitely through extreme numbers and quantities, until the shackles of immortality were broken.

Eternity, on the other hand, served as an immensely solid foundation. No matter how much the internal and external aspects changed, it stood firm and unmoving, like the land upon which even a skyscraper thousands of feet high must be built.

In the interplay of change and permanence, ten thousand years passed in an instant.

Finally, when a new strand of ink broke through all difficulties and descended upon the world, its transformation soon benefited other parts of the ink mass.

The Xuanhuang Realm, a mortal body, miraculously gestured forth an Immortal Soul!

As the energy consumed by Mo Sha's ascension was entirely provided by Li Fan from beginning to end, Mo Sha's 'parents' in this life were Li Fan. It was merely borrowing the Xuanhuang Realm's 'womb.'

However, as the birthplace of an Immortal Soul, after Mo Sha ascended, the subtle connection cultivated over tens of thousands of years between it and the Xuanhuang Realm still brought some feedback to the Xuanhuang Realm.

But compared to the transformations that would normally occur after the Xuanhuang Realm's ascension, the changes brought about by Mo Sha's earlier ascension were less pleasant.

Previously just one of the many World Souls, it now occupied an absolute dominant position. As Mo Sha transformed into an Immortal Soul, it also imposed some of its characteristics upon the Xuanhuang Realm, forcefully and without refusal.

Thick layers of dark clouds inexplicably rose, shrouding the entire Xuanhuang sky. On the ground, black winds occasionally swept past, as if Mo Sha had descended, and wherever the wind passed, everything turned into tiny black particles.

The Xuanhuang Realm, where the threat of the Immortal Ruins had been eliminated and vitality had been restored, suddenly transformed into a gloomy, netherworld of impending doom!

Fortunately, the vast majority of living beings were slumbering in the Unbounded Dreamland Paradise, protected by Li Fan's power. Mo Sha, being Li Fan's 'kin' and 'parent,' showed some deference. It did not directly clash with the Paradise.

Li Fan could vaguely sense the fluctuations of extreme anger from the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, yet it dared not speak. Even the power of an entire realm was no match for the current Mo Sha Immortal Soul. The Xuanhuang Realm's Heavenly Dao could only endure for now, accumulating strength from the benefits of Mo Sha's ascension.

But Mo Sha seemed unwilling to stop there.

While not directly attacking the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, it extended its tentacles towards the various World Souls within the Xuanhuang Realm.

Originally manifestations of countless different laws, the World Souls appeared in myriad forms. However, as Mo Sha Immortal Soul encroached upon them, their forms gradually showed streaks of Mo Sha patterns. And their manifestations of power in the world all carried the destructive characteristics of Mo Sha.

Even World Souls that were not inherently very aggressive, such as Scarlet Flame, became terrifying and formidable.

"If this darkened Scarlet Flame were ordered to boil the sea, perhaps the clouds would wither in a single night."

Mo Sha did not merely invade.

As the ink color gradually dominated the Xuanhuang Realm, within the profound shadows surrounding Li Fan, different 'Mo Sha Immortal Souls' with various properties were differentiated.

Although their essence remained the same, they possessed certain characteristics of other Daos in the world.

The overall harmony remained, while at the same time bringing about a different kind of vitality.

...

Observing all the changes between Mo Sha and the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan felt a subtle premonition.

"Perhaps, this Xuanhuang Realm, modified by the Mo Sha Immortal Soul, possesses a certain degree of survivability against the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation."

"Perhaps, the current level of modification is simply not enough. But compared to its original state, its resistance to Dao Annihilation has undoubtedly increased significantly."

"Is this what the experimental field initially intended by implanting Mo Sha's power?"

Although the current Xuanhuang Realm appeared somewhat grim and terrifying, in the context of the entire mortal world facing annihilation by the Dao Annihilation tide, it seemed more 'suitable' for survival.

"It's like a simple stone cave hidden underground in a cultivation wasteland is more suitable for survival than a magnificent palace on the surface."

"If this model of the Xuanhuang Realm were to be popularized throughout the mortal world..." Li Fan narrowed his eyes.

"Even if it still couldn't prevent the end of everything being submerged by the Dao Annihilation tide, perhaps after the tide receded, one or two islands might survive. In a sense, it could be considered a method of saving the world."

"But it would be conditional on Mo Sha 'baptizing' it first."

Li Fan felt the writhing myriad shadows around him and couldn't help but shake his head slightly.

Not all cultivation realms could easily withstand the changes brought about by the Mo Sha Immortal Soul like the Xuanhuang Realm.

Putting aside the special nature of the Immortal Realm as an experimental field.

Even for the exceptionally special Xuanhuang Realm, without Li Fan's protection and the bond formed by tens of thousands of years of Mo Sha gestation within him, the Xuanhuang Realm would have suffered severe damage during the Mo Sha baptism.

Let alone other normal cultivation realms in the mortal world.

"If this cluster of shadows were released, perhaps even the Shining Star Sea, reinforced by the Dao Net, could not withstand its weight."

"It might be able to resist for a time, but in the face of the Mo Sha Immortal Soul with its [Illusionary Life] characteristic, it would eventually be blackened inch by inch."

Having previously delved into the core of the Dao Net and gained a thorough understanding of both Mo Sha Immortal Soul and Dao Net power, Li Fan concluded after deduction.

"Compared to him devouring and absorbing it himself, allowing it to evolve naturally would better unleash its characteristics."

Li Fan observed the various Mo Sha shadows that had evolved around him, examining each one carefully.

His own Dao Net was created by harmonizing with Mo Sha. If he could simultaneously master these infiltrated laws, he could easily replicate them one by one.

Looking around, Li Fan seemed to glimpse his possible next path.

"The greatest obstacle for True Immortals in comprehending the Dao is that one cannot cultivate multiple Daos simultaneously."

"Even with heaven-defying cultivation techniques like the [Infinite Heavenly Pillar Divine Art], one can at most merge two or three Daos. But if I use Mo Sha Immortal Soul as my foundation..."

"All Three Thousand Great Daos, within my grasp!"

Li Fan saw the Dao Net, stretching infinitely from the heavens to the earth, being slowly stained by Mo Sha emanating from an unknown source.

He instinctively looked at his palm.

Amidst the countless writhing black particles, as his comprehension deepened, different Daos seemed to differentiate.

Although they were all common Daos he had comprehended through his past cultivation experiences, such as the Five Elements, Azure Wind, Blue Flame, etc., with each new aspect Li Fan felt himself becoming stronger in an instant.

"The reason I can easily achieve what countless past sages and saints could not is because the Dao of [Mo Sha] did not originally exist in this world."

"Its fundamental core is Dao Annihilation. It is the Infinite Sea."

"Transcending the Great Daos of the mortal world! Thus, it is not bound by the mortal world's restrictions on cultivating multiple Daos!"

"All the Daos seen in the mortal world can be comprehended and utilized."

Looking at his increasingly vivid Mo Sha body, Li Fan felt a sense of enlightenment.

"Mo Sha is like this, so what about..."

"[Returning to Truth]?"

The ink churned, and Li Fan finally returned his thoughts to his core essence.

"By means of Mo Sha, infiltrating all Daos in the world."

"One Dao, one step at a time. When all the mortal world's Daos are mastered. Perhaps I will be one step away from [Transformation between True and False]..."

Li Fan's Mo Sha body exploded outwards, completely integrating into the newly formed Mo Sha Immortal Soul of the Xuanhuang Realm.

He wanted, first and foremost, to transfer these Daos mastered by the new Mo Sha Immortal Soul.

...

The main body had gained immensely. In the backdrop of a dying Immortal Path and decaying Dao, he had finally found a path most suited to him.

Meanwhile, Li Biren, sensing the changes in the main body, looked at the Grand Magister Tian Du, who was still within the [Illusory Life Projection], and a plan began to form in his mind.

A trace of ink emerged from his fingertip.

It then transformed into a wisp of black energy, slowly flying towards the Grand Magister Tian Du.

Merging into the chanting sound, it quickly disappeared without a trace, like a drop of water into a vast lake.

But the ink did not vanish.

Instead, it reversed the color of the entire lake!

The Illusory Life projection rippled, attempting to expel the encroaching ink.

But every ripple it produced actually provided an opportunity for the Mo Sha to invade.

Within the illusory projection's body, a shadow quietly occupied the forehead.

Since being locked onto by Li Biren, the Grand Magister Tian Du, whose expression had always been calm and composed, finally changed.

Although he still appeared as calm and collected as ever.

Li Biren could tell that he was merely pretending to be calm.

"Mo Sha is indeed more effective than my Dao Net's brute force."

Li Biren thought this, and channeled a wisp of Mo Sha Immortal Soul power into himself.

Like countless stars suddenly dimming, plunging the heavens into silence.

But after a few breaths, beneath this dark starry sky, a greater vitality emerged.

Enhanced by the Mo Sha characteristic, Li Biren, although unable to directly match the Illusory Life projection, could, to a certain extent, disregard its influence.

Amidst the surrounding chanting sounds, he moved step by step, ardundously forward.

Slowly but firmly, he finally reached the Grand Magister Tian Du.

With a grip on the Grand Magister's throat, amidst his increasingly terrified expression, he dragged him forcefully out of the protection of the Illusory Life projection!

"You..."

The Grand Magister still wanted to speak, but the dark Dao Net had already tightly enveloped him.

Wisps of ink poured in from the top of his head.

The Grand Magister's eyes instantly lost their pupils, turning completely black.

His struggling movements gradually ceased.

Li Biren was using Mo Sha to infiltrate the Grand Magister's cultivated Dao path.

Originally, Li Biren thought that since the Grand Magister had guarded the [Dao of Illusionary Life] for millennia, he must have also cultivated the Dao of Illusionary Life.

However, when Li Biren, with Mo Sha's infiltration, entered the Grand Magister's core, he realized something was wrong.

"Unlike the Hungry Immortal, whose time was distorted by cultivating the Dao of Hunger, experiencing ten thousand years while actually living only a few days. This one has literally been contemplating the Illusory Life projection since the Heavenly King of Xuan period."

"Such a long period of time, constantly by the side of the [Illusory Life Projection], even if he were a pig, his comprehension of the Dao of Illusionary Life wouldn't be so poor. But this Grand Magister..."

"He relied almost entirely on the projection for protection, without exception. His own demonstrated ability to avoid calamity was almost negligible."

Although Li Biren, with the power of Mo Sha Immortal Soul, had entered the Grand Magister's core.

What he saw was too 'sparse.'

Not only the Dao he comprehended, but also his experiences and memories.

It was completely unlike the Grand Magister Tian Du who presided over Xuanhuang for tens of thousands of years as expected.

Li Biren glanced around. He instinctively sensed something was amiss.

Looking at the empty surroundings. He suddenly remembered the scene glimpsed in the high wall experiment field, with countless block star seas arranged side by side.

"Perhaps, this is just one of the Grand Magister's inner realms?"

Li Biren had a feeling.

Infinite ink then erupted from his body.

Within moments, it completely submerged this place.

Then, under immense pressure, it began to penetrate towards other areas.

Boom! Boom!

As cracks appeared, the vast ink tide surged towards the surface beyond the Grand Magister Tian Du's manifested form.

As if suddenly entering a world full of living beings.

Countless figures floated all around.

Although their faces were all the same, they were undoubtedly all Grand Magister Tian Du!

"These people... look somewhat familiar."

Li Biren saw some familiar acquaintances among these figures.

They were the mortals and cultivators living in Yuan Dao Province.

Lan Yu, Dugu Xi, Dugu Shi, Feng Mu, etc.

They currently had various expressions: some were furious, some were horrified, and some were indifferent.

"The living beings of Yuan Dao Province are all transformed from Grand Magister Tian Du?"

Li Biren's first thought was this.

But he quickly reacted, realizing it was incorrect.

Because the current living beings in Yuan Dao Province were still living unaffected on the land of Yuan Dao Province. There was no abnormality even though the Grand Magister had been captured.

Li Biren recalled the strange phenomenon in Yuan Dao Province where ten years of time were mysteriously consumed.

In an instant, he understood.

"It's not that ten years of time have truly disappeared. It's that all the living beings within it are in a state of stasis."

"Only the Grand Magister himself is still active."

"During these ten years, he made copies of all the living beings in Yuan Dao Province within his own body."

"And the purpose..."

Li Biren seized the figure of 'Lan Yu.'

"Although not the real Lan Yu. But..."

Li Fan could still perceive the aura of comprehension of the [Dao of Life and Death] from him.

Even more profound than the actual Lan Yu he had seen before.

Li Biren looked at the countless different Grand Magisters floating all around.

Each one comprehended a different Dao path!

Chapter 1480: Four Saint Lords of the Immortal Realm

One Dao, One Step

“To comprehend the Three Thousand Great Daos with the strength of one person. The Grand Magister’s thoughts actually overlap with mine to some extent.”

Looking around, Li Biren felt a touch of surprise, and also some confusion.

The Grand Magister’s inner world was a manifestation of all living beings,

and also the embodiment of countless Great Daos appearing between heaven and earth.

The countless beings copied by the Grand Magister had become vessels for the manifestation of Great Daos.

Li Biren looked at the myriad faces arranged around him, and for a moment, he almost felt as if he were in the Dao Net itself.

In fact, conceptually speaking, the Grand Magister alone was indeed comparable to a "Dao Net."
