However, whether it was in the meticulousness of the beings comprehending the Dao, or the number of Dao principles, there was still a vast gap compared to the Dao Net Li Fan had seen in the Shining Star Sea.

“These myriad Dao paths are all manifested through different living beings. But…”

Li Biren shifted his gaze from Lan Yu to another mortal from the Origin Dao Province.

On him coalesced the aura of the Great Dao related to “painting.”

The intensity of the aura fluctuations was such that it was utterly impossible for a mere mortal to possess!

“The shadows copied by the Grand Magister have a far greater comprehension of the Dao than their original forms…”

Li Biren's gaze shifted to where the projection of all beings was focused.

In the depths of the cosmos, within the Shadow of Illusionary Life.

Li Biren suddenly understood: “So that’s how it is. The Shadow of Illusionary Life represents the ultimate transformation. It not only adapts to the times but can also produce various different reactions based on the different living beings it encounters.”

When the Ten Great Immortal Sects of the Immortal Realm’s disciples entered Tiandu and saw the Shadow of Illusionary Life, each person’s vision and hearing was filled with different cultivation techniques. But without exception, they were all profoundly related to what they had previously learned, as if tailor-made for them.

The disciples of the Ten Great Immortal Sects thus concluded that the Grand Magister must have originated from the Immortal Realm, and that the teachings they received were Immortal Realm heritage techniques.

“The Immortal Realm… what mortal methods could there be? Compared to Immortal techniques, the true inheritances of the Ten Great Immortal Sects are still far too lacking!”

“They would never have imagined that the so-called heritage was merely a different evolution naturally produced by the [Shadow of Illusionary Life] after coming into contact with them, like a mirror!”

“The Grand Magister placing them inside to behold the [Shadow of Illusionary Life], and later periodically freezing the living beings of Origin Dao Province, was likely for the sake of the Dao manifestations reflecting in this mirror.”

Thinking of this, Li Biren couldn’t help but look at this Grand Magister Tiandu with renewed respect.

Possessing a supreme treasure that directly led to the Nameless realm, yet unlike the Starving Immortal who directly comprehended the Dao of the treasure, he instead used it as a tool, attempting to put all the Great Daos in the world into his grasp…

And the Grand Magister was actually just a mere Half-Immortal.

Such actions could only be described as arrogant and overconfident.

But Li Biren knew very well that the Grand Magister, facing a supreme treasure of the Nameless realm, still managed to suppress his inner greed and remained steadfast for ten thousand years, never changing his original intention.

He was by no means a fool.

“He must have his reasons for doing this.”

Li Biren did not press the interrogation for the moment, but instead looked at the Grand Magister, who had accumulated knowledge for ten thousand years, and the different Dao paths that had manifested through the Shadow of Illusionary Life in various living beings, and actually gave a rare smile.

“His strength is insufficient. He is merely doing the work for others.”

“I shall accept this generous gift.”

With this thought, torrents of ink erupted from Li Biren.

Like tentacles, they successively dyed all the myriad Dao manifestations within the Grand Magister.

As Li Biren had deduced, within each figure was a comprehension of a different Dao path.

They were like fruits condensed over tens of thousands of years, extremely enticing and fragrant to cultivators!

Li Biren unceremoniously took them all for himself.

As the ten thousand Dao manifestations were swallowed by Li Biren, within Li Fan’s main body, within the boundless ink ocean of the Slaughter Immortal Soul, different water droplets gradually began to appear.

This was exactly the same as what happened when Mo Sha infiltrated the Xuanhuang Realm previously.

The Grand Magister’s comprehension of the Dao over ten thousand years, combined with Li Fan’s own comprehension gained through countless reincarnations.

Countless ink droplets representing different Dao paths differentiated themselves from the Slaughter Immortal Soul.

While bringing vitality to the Slaughter Immortal Soul, they also provided a path for it to transform into different Great Daos.

Feeling the drastic changes occurring within his body, Li Fan’s heart stirred, and a flickering flame, red with black edges, appeared in his palm.

“Ink Slaughter as the core, Scarlet Flame as the manifestation.”

“This flame…”

Li Fan flicked his finger, and the black flame instantly turned into a thread, flying out of the Xuanhuang Realm and colliding thunderously with the Heavenly Pillar formed by the Starving Immortal in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

Without even a ripple, the Heavenly Pillar stood unmoving.

After all, it was formed by a Nameless True Immortal capable of resisting the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. Li Fan’s main body was still only at the Half-Immortal realm. Although Mo Sha was peculiar, it was utterly insufficient to harm the Starving Immortal Heavenly Pillar.

Li Fan was not surprised, raising his eyebrows slightly, and sensing a subtle, unremarkable black scorch mark on the Heavenly Pillar.

“To merge with a Dao using a Nameless Immortal body, the strong repulsion towards other Dao paths, and yet it couldn’t completely eliminate Mo Sha.”

“Furthermore, along that black trace, Mo Sha’s erosion continues. Although slow, it is persistent.”

“If time is infinitely extended, even a towering Heavenly Pillar might eventually be breached.”

“And this is only the beginning…”

Li Fan had a premonition that as he continued to infiltrate more Dao paths, Mo Sha’s erosion ability would only grow stronger.

“It’s as if, though these different Dao paths are distinct, they still have certain commonalities. The more Dao paths infiltrated, the more commonalities are grasped.”

“Using these as keys, one can eventually overcome all obstacles.”

The thought of Li Fan infiltrating the Three Thousand Great Daos with Mo Sha had only just been conceived, yet it had already taken root and sprouted.

In addition to his own accumulations, a greater part of it was thanks to the Grand Magister’s tens of thousands of years of accumulation.

As the torrents of ink completely submerged the Grand Magister’s inner world.

Li Fan also detected some characteristics of the Grand Magister’s comprehension of the Dao.

Unlike the Dao Net’s nested structure with countless nodes, the Grand Magister ultimately centered around himself.

Myriad Dao manifestations encircled him in the center.

As if he were an emperor being worshipped by all Great Daos in the heavens!

However, now, with Li Fan’s intervention, this majestic emperor had become a solitary figure.

Li Biren confronted the true Grand Magister.

Surrounded by countless original copies of himself, the Grand Magister Tiandu, trapped in a desperate situation, unexpectedly showed no signs of dejection, fear, or anger.

His exterior, like a naive and innocent young disciple, remained calm. He was merely constantly calculating something with his fingers.

Finally, seeming to achieve no results,

he shook his head and chose to give up.

He then asked in a faint voice, “Where does Fellow Daoist come from?”

“Naturally, I come from where I came from,” Li Biren replied coldly.

Seeing that Li Biren was unwilling to reveal his origins, the Grand Magister asked no further questions.

Instead, he began to negotiate: “I will cede the [Shadow of Extreme Simplicity] and allow me to leave. Is that acceptable?”

“Extreme Simplicity?” Li Biren pondered for a moment.

Then he coldly stated, “If I kill you, this Shadow of Illusionary Life will also be mine.”

Upon hearing this, the Grand Magister looked somewhat disheartened, but not out of fear of Li Biren’s killing intent. Rather, it was due to the different appellation Li Biren used for the illusory shadow: “So you see it as Illusionary Life.”

“There is no difference,”

The Grand Magister shook his head. “Before the birth of heaven and earth, there was chaos and boundlessness, and then Extreme Simplicity initially emerged.”

“Afterward, all things began to arise and multiply.”

“Extreme Simplicity is the ultimate power of change in the world. If Extreme Simplicity were still Extreme Simplicity, the world would not have become what it is today.”

“The Great Dao itself is in decline. Extreme Simplicity transforming into Illusionary Life… Heh, I was deceived in the past.”

Li Biren narrowed his eyes, listening to these somewhat cryptic remarks.

“Even if the Great Dao were not in decline, if the true Dao of [Extreme Simplicity] were placed before you, with your mere Half-Immortal cultivation, what could you possibly do?”

Seeing that Li Biren did not act rashly, the Grand Magister was happy to live a little longer.

“The Dao of Extreme Simplicity already has its master. That is precisely my Master.”

“Although Master has departed, leaving only a residual shadow in the world, it is not something I can covet. I merely used Master’s divine might to comprehend the Dao paths of the world.” The Grand Magister spoke leisurely, not appearing like someone facing imminent death.

“Do you think that by fabricating a fictitious master, I would not dare to refine you?” Li Biren snorted coldly.

The Grand Magister chuckled dismissively and pointed to his Daoist robe: “I have worn this disciple’s attire for countless years, just as I did when I served Master. I have not changed it for a long time, so how could it be fabricated?”

“Whether you believe it or not. You need not worry. Even if you kill me, Master will not exact revenge for me. In the past, Master left behind a residual shadow, intending to prop up the collapsing heavens of the Immortal Realm. Unfortunately, before I could deliver the residual shadow, entire Immortal Regions were already engulfed by Dao Annihilation. Watching Master’s residual shadow, I then became greedy…”

“How could someone who can transcend be unable to control even their own residual shadow? Your lie is too crude, Li Biren commented.

The Grand Magister glanced at Li Biren, his tone inexplicably strange. “When I say Master departed, I mean ‘passed away,’ not ‘transcended.’ Although Master possessed heaven-defying divine abilities, since he chose to die, naturally no spiritual consciousness would remain.”

Li Biren was stunned upon hearing this.

What the Grand Magister said was indeed somewhat beyond his expectations.

“To merge with [Extreme Simplicity] and die so easily?” His tone was filled with disbelief.

“Easily… Hehehehe.”

The Grand Magister chuckled without answering, instead changing the topic: “Indeed, if Master had wished to continue living, there would have likely been methods to extend his life. But Master simply did not wish to!”

“Who in this world wishes their Master to pass away more than I? After all, as long as he was alive, even the ruling Immortal Emperor of the Immortal Realm would have to treat me with utmost respect and courtesy.”

“And once he died…”

“Hehehe.”

The smile on the Grand Magister’s face appeared somewhat sinister and twisted.

“In that case, your Master must have been an unparalleled expert in the Immortal Realm. How does he compare to Shouqiu Gong?” Li Biren ignored the other party’s strange expression and directly asked.

“Shouqiu Gong.” The name pulled the Grand Magister out of his resentment. For a moment, he seemed lost in thought.

Then, he slowly said, “Master and Shouqiu Gong never met.”

“Master was an acknowledged expert in the Immortal Realm, while Shouqiu Gong lived in solitude in the wilderness, suddenly rising to fame.”

“I also asked Master about Shouqiu Gong, and he said…”

The Grand Magister suddenly paused, intending to create suspense.

Li Biren, surprisingly, resisted the urge to ask and simply stared coldly at the Grand Magister, waiting for his next words.

After a period of stalemate, the Grand Magister felt it was uninteresting and said, “Master simply said five words: ‘Responsibility-free is naturally strong.’”

“I don’t know what it means specifically.”

“Anyway, until he passed away, he never mentioned that Shouqiu Gong again.”

Li Biren carefully savored these five words: “Responsibility-free is naturally strong.”

After a long while, he suddenly asked again, “How many powerful beings like your Master were there in the Immortal Realm back then?”

The Grand Magister’s expression became contemplative. “There were only three in the entire Immortal Realm who could sit and discuss the Dao with Master.”

“Of course, this does not include Shouqiu Gong.”

“Master would sometimes take me along when he traveled, and sometimes he would roam alone.”

“I remember on one occasion, I asked Master who among the Four Sacred Monarchs was the strongest. Master did not answer, but merely smiled and tapped my forehead. He said…”

“Who is the strongest, I do not know. But if you ask who is diligent, it must be the two Sacred Monarchs, [Lianshan] and [Guihai].”

“After Master finished speaking, as if recalling something joyous, he burst into laughter.”

The moment Li Biren heard the words [Lianshan] and [Guihai], his mind instinctively thought of the mountain and sea that Shouqiu Gong had witnessed.

He couldn’t help but ask, “This Lianshan and Guihai…”

The Grand Magister returned from his memories and stared at Li Biren.

Unsure of what he was thinking, he remained silent for a long time before finally answering Li Biren’s question.

“Lianshan, the first immortal in the world.”

“Guihai, who opened the Infinite Spring.”

“It can be said that these two Sacred Monarchs created the eternal prosperity of the Immortal Realm from nothing,” the Grand Magister said solemnly, word by word.

From his demeanor, his reverence for these two Sacred Monarchs was evident.

These few words, to Li Biren, were like thunder.

The Grand Magister’s words were not difficult to understand.

Lianshan was the first immortal in the world.

Guihai was the True Immortal who found a way to connect to the Infinite Sea, thus making immortal power endless.

Someone who had personally witnessed the vastness of the Infinite Sea and could harness its power was definitely at an unimaginable level of strength.

And the name “Lianshan,” when associated with the mountains that opposed the Infinite Sea, was rather thought-provoking.

“Perhaps the mountain was the initial foundation of a True Immortal’s power.”

Li Biren’s mind raced.

The Grand Magister’s background was far greater than he had imagined.

“Besides the three Sacred Monarchs, [Extreme Simplicity], [Lianshan], and [Guihai], what about the remaining one?” Li Biren continued to extract information about the past Immortal Realm from the Grand Magister, who answered all his questions.

“The remaining one…” the Grand Magister pondered for a long time, showing rare hesitation.

“Cannot be spoken of.”

After a long while, he shook his head.

“Master, Lianshan, and Guihai have all passed away. Only this Sacred Monarch still exists in the world.”

“If I mention his name, he will definitely be perceived.”
